la dbab pa bsdu ba/ gzhi bsdu ba/ rnam grangs bsdu ba/ rnam par bshad pa'i sgo bsdu ba dang lnga'o/ /sdom gnyis ni/ theg chen thun mong min pa'i sdom theg bsdus/ theg pa
thun mong gi sdom mngon pa kun las btus pa gnyis so/ /dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i rab tu byed pa sde brgyad de/ brgyad ni nyi shu pa'i rab byed/ sum cu pa'i rab byed/ phung
po lnga'i

rab byed/ rnam bshad rigs pa/ las grub pa'i rab tu byed pa ste rang rgyud du brtsams pa lnga'o/ /gzhan 'grel du brtsams pa mdo sde rgyan gyi 'grel pa/ dbus mtha'i 'grel pa/
rten 'brel gyi mdo'i 'grel pa dang gsum mo/ /spyod pa'i cha ston pa ni/ byang sa'i tshul khrims kyi le'u dang / sdom pa nyi shu pa lta bu'o/ /gsum pa brjod bya don gyi sgo
nas ni/ ji snyed pa ston pa'i bstan bcos dang / ji lta ba ston pa'i bstan bcos dang / thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam ston pa'i bstan bcos dang gsum du 'byed do/
/dang po la'ang phal pa dang / khyad par can gnyis las/ dang po ni/ lugs kyi bstan bcos shes rab brgya pa dang / skye bo gso thig dang / 'dul ba lung gzhi las 'byung ba'i
brtag pa brgyad dang / brtag pa bco brgyad la sogs pa lta bu ste/ de dag kyang mngon mtho'i rgyu yin la/ thar pa'i rten du'ang 'gro srid de/ shes rab brgya pa las/ mi
yi chos lugs legs spyad na/ /lha yul bgrod pa thag mi ring / /lha dang mi yi them skas la/ /'dzegs na thar pa gam na 'dug / ces gsungs so/ /gnyis pa ni/ rig pa'i gnas lnga'i
bstan bcos las/ nang rig pa'i bstan bcos ma gtogs pa'i snga ma bzhi yan lag dang bcas pa ni gong du smos pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa ni/ rigs tshogs brgyad dang rgyan snang
bden gsum chos dbyings bstod pa la sogs pa chos dbyings zab mo'i don bye brag tu ston pa rnams so/ /gsum pa ni/ rin chen phreng ba dang / gshes spring dang / bzhi brgya
pa la sogs pa skyes bu gsum gyi lam ston pa

rnams so/ /gnyis pa 'bras bu rdo rje theg pa'i dgongs 'grel gyi bstan bcos la gnyis/ rgyud 'grel tshul gyi gdams ngag bstan pa/ de ltar bkral ba'i rgyud 'grel gyi bstan bcos
so/ /dang po la spyir rgyud sde rin po che 'grel pa'am/ bshad pa'i tshul mang du yod na'ang phal cher gdams ngag drug dang / rgyud gsum dang / bdag nyid can gsum dang /
gnas pa bzhi dang / dag pa gsum dang / gsang ba bdun te drug po der 'du bar dran pa'i dbang po rnams bzhed do/ /de'i dang po ni/ 'grel pa pos 'grel bar sla ba dang / dpyod
ldan rnams kyis rtogs par sla ba'i phyir gdams ngag drug gi sgo nas bshad de/ drug ni spyi'i don du bshad pa/ sbas pa'i don du bshad pa/ mthar thug pa'i don du bshad pa
ste gsum dang / de rjod par byed pa'i sgra ni yan lag gi don gyis bshad pa/ yi ge'i don gyis bshad pa/ man ngag gi don gyis bshad pa dang gsum ste/ dpal nam mkha' dang
mnyam pa'i rgyud las/ yi ge dang ni yan lag dang / /bsdus pa'i don dang spyi yi don/ /sbas dang de bzhin mthar thug par/ /rgyud rnams nges pa kho na yin/ /zhes gsungs pa
ltar ro/ /dang po spyi'i don la pha rol tu phyin pa dang spyi'i don du bshad pa ni byang chub phyogs kyi chos la sogs pa de dag mthun par bya ba dang / bskyed pa'i rim pa
spyi ni mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub gnyis ka bsgrub pa la dgos pa'i phyir ro/ /sbas pa la rang byin rlabs kyi sbas pa dang / dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i sbas pa gnyis
so/ /mthar thug pa ni sangs rgyas kyi sa

ste/ de la'ang gnyis/ spyi'i don gyi mthar thug pa ni theg pa thun mong ba la grags pa sa bcu gcig dang / sbas don gyi mthar thug pa ni gsang sngags pa la grags pa'i sa bcu
gnyis pa dang bcu gsum pa'o/ /des na brjod bya'i don gsum la phye na drug tu 'gyur ro/ /de re re la'ang rjod par byed pa'i sgra ni gsum ste yan lag gi don gyis bshad pa/
yi ge'i don gyis bshad pa/ man ngag gi don gyis bshad pa ste tshul de dag gis rgyud don bshad pas mtha' drug tu 'gyur ba yin te/ rje btsun ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pas/
spyi sbas mthar thug rim bzhin yan lag gi/ don gyis bshad pa ji bzhin sgra dang ni/ /nges pa'i don dang dgongs min bshad pa ste/ /de gsum yi ge man ngag gis bshad na/ /rim
bzhin ji bzhin sgra min drang don dang / /dgongs pa'i bshad bya zhes bya mtha' drug dang / /zhes pa ltar te/ de'ang brjod bya spyi'i don gnyis su yan lag gi don gyi tshig
ji ltar byung ba ltar bshad pa ni sgra ji bzhin pa'i bshad pa zhes bya'o/ /brjod bya spyi'i don gnyis su yi ge dang man ngag gi don gyis bshad pa ni ji bzhin ma yin
pa'i bshad pa zhes bya'o/ /brjod bya sbas pa'i don du yan lag gi don gyis bshad pa ni nges pa'i don gyi bshad pa zhes bya'o/ /brjod bya sbas don du yi ge dang man ngag gi
don gyis bshad pa ni drang ba'i don gyi bshad pa zhes bya'o/ /brjod bya mthar thug tu yan lag gi don gyis bshad pa ni dgongs min gyi bshad pa zhes bya'o/ /mthar thug tu
yi ge dang man ngag gi don gyis bshad pa ni dgongs pa can gyi bshad pa zhes bya ste/ 'di dag ni 'jigs bral

rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug bi rU pa yab sras kyi bzhed pa gzhan dang thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams ngag yin no/ /gnyis pa ni/ sems kyi rgyud rgyun chags pa gang zhig gtan la
dbab pa la dgongs nas gzhi dang lam dang 'bras bu'i rgyud gsum gyi sgo nas bshad de/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ rgyud ni rgyun chags zhes bya ste/ /rgyun de rnam pa gsum du 'gyur/
/gzhi dang de yi rang bzhin dang / /mi 'phrogs pa yis rab phye ba'o/ /rang bzhin rnam pa rgyu yin te/ /gzhi ni thabs zhes bya ba yin/ /de bzhin mi 'phrogs 'bras bu ste/
/gsum gyis rgyud kyi don bsdus pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /gsum pa ni/ lus dang ngag dang sems dang rlung ste rgyu bzhi yod pa dang / /dbang bzhi dang lam bzhi dang
'bras bu bzhi dang sku bzhi yod pas rim pa ltar dbyibs kyi bdag nyid/ sngags kyi bdag nyid/ dbang chos kyi bdag nyid/ mthar thug chos kyi bdag nyid de bzhir gnas pa la
dbang chos dang mthar thug chos gnyis gcig tu byas pa'i bdag nyid can gsum gyi sgo nas bshad de/ dpal nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud las/ sngags dang dbyibs dang chos bdag
nyid/ /sbyor ba rnam pa gsum gyis ni/ /srid pa'i nyes pas mi gos shing / /rgyud kyi don la 'jug par bya/ /zhes gsungs so/ /bzhi pa ni/ 'bras bu longs spyod rdzogs pa'i
sku gong bur gnas pa/ chos kyi sku chur gnas pa/ sprul pa'i sku gzugs su gnas pa/ ngo bo nyid kyi sku gzugs las 'das par gnas pa ltar sbyang gzhi dang sbyong byed kyi chos
rnams kyang gnas

pa bzhi bzhi yin pa'i phyir de dag gi sgo nas bshad pa ste/ dpal nam mkha' dang mnyam pa las/ gong bu chu dang gzugs su gnas/ /de bzhin gzugs las 'das pa ste/ /gnas pa rnam
pa bzhi ru ni/ /rgyud rnams nges par kho na yin/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin no/ /lnga pa ni/ rgyu'i rgyud ngo bo nyid kyi dag pa gsum/ thabs kyi rgyud sbyong byed kyi dag pa
gsum/ 'bras bu'i rgyud dri bral gyi dag pa gsum ste rgyud gsum so so'i thad sor dag pa gsum ldan gyi sgo nas bshad pa ste/ dgyes pa'i rdo rje las/ nges par dngos po thams
cad kyi/ /dag pa de bzhin nyid du brjod/ /phyi nas re re'i dbye ba yis/ /lha rnams kyis ni brjod par bya/ /rang rig bdag nyid dag pa nyid/ /dag pa gzhan gyis rnam grol min/
/zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /drug pa ni/ snod min la gab cing sba ba'i don du gsang ba bdun gyi sgo nas bshad pa ste/ dpal kha sbyor las/ gsang ba ni mi gsal ba'o/ /gsang
ba ni de kho na nyid mdor bstan pa'o/ /gsang ba ni sa bon lnga'o/ /gsang ba ni dam pa'i dngos po sbas pa'o/ /gsang ba ni gsang ba'i chu skyes so/ /gsang ba ni lte ba'i
dga' ba'o/ /gsang ba ni thams cad du 'gro ba bsdus pa'o/ /gsang ba ni bde ba mtha' yas pa ste rgyud kyi gzhung gi bshad pa'o zhes gsang ba'i sgra ni bdun pa ste/ brgyad pa
ni brjod du med pa'i mtshan nyid do zhes gsungs pas mtha'i gsang ba gnyis rtogs bya dang rtogs pa'i gnas lugs kyi ngo bor dbyer med pa'i phyir bdun du nges pa nyid do/
/gzhan yang ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa'i rgyud las gleng

bslang ba lnga/ rigs pa bzhi/ mtha' drug tshul bzhi/ bshad pa gnyis/ slob ma brtag pa/ bden pa gnyis te rgyan bdun zhes bya ba'i bshad pa'i tshul de rnams kyang 'di dag gi
nang du ma 'dus pa med par gsungs te/ de dag gis ni 'bras bu sngags kyi theg pa 'grel tshul spyi'i rnam par gzhag pa mdo tsam bstan nas/ bye brag tu ni rgyud sde rin po che
so so'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i rnam par 'grel ba'i tshul mi 'dra ba ci rigs par 'byung ba rnams ni rgyud 'grel so so'i steng du rtogs par bya'o/ /gnyis pa bkral ba'i rgyud
'grel gyi bstan bcos dngos la gnyis te/ rgyud sde so sor 'grel ba'i bstan bcos dang / rgyud sde spyir 'grel ba'i bstan bcos so/ /dang po la bzhi las/ dang po bya rgyud
phyogs kyi rgyud 'grel gyi bstan bcos ni/ bsam gtan phyi ma'i rim par phye ba rgya cher bshad pa sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ dpung bzang gis zhus pa'i rgyud kyi tshig
don bshad pa la sogs pa mang du bzhugs pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa spyod rgyud phyogs kyi rgyud 'grel bstan bcos ni/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i
rgyud kyi 'grel bshad slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa la sogs pa rnams so/ /gsum pa rnal 'byor rgyud phyogs kyi rgyud 'grel bstan bcos ni/ rtsa ba'i rgyud de nyid
bsdus pa'i rgya cher bshad pa ko sa la'i rgyan slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa dang / de kho na nyid snang bar byed pa slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad
pa la sogs pa rnams so/ /bzhi pa rnal 'byor bla med

rgyud phyogs kyi rgyud 'grel bstan bcos ni/ gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po kye rdo rje rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rgya cher 'grel pa byang chub sems dpa'i rdo rje snying pos
mdzad pa dang / dka' 'grel padma can slob dpon mtsho skyes kyis mdzad pa dang / kau mU dI sbyangs dka' zla bas mdzad pa la sogs pa rnams dang / bshad pa'i rgyud rdo rje
gur gyi dka' 'grel intra bhU tis mdzad pa dang / kha sbyor rgyud kyi 'grel pa man ngag gi snye ma zhes bya ba 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa la sogs pa rnams dang
/ bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i 'od spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis mdzad pa la sogs pa rnams so/ /shes rab kyi rgyud dam rnal
'byor gsang mtha'i rgyud phyogs kyi rgyud 'grel la mngon brjod 'bum pa las 'byung ba nyung ngu'i rgyud kyi don rnam par bshad pa byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes
mdzad pa dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa gru gzings slob dpon padma rdo rjes mdzad pa la sogs pa rnams so/ /rnal 'byor chen po thabs rgyud phyogs kyi rgyud
'grel la gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags pa'i lugs la/ sgron ma gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rgya cher bshad pa dang / sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon zla ba
grags pas mdzad pa sogs dang / slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs pa'i lugs la/ rgyud 'grel slob ma la phan pa zhes bya ba la rab tu zhi ba'i ye shes dang bi shwa na mi
tras mdzad pa la sogs pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa ni/ rgyud sde gong 'og de dag las mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i lhag pa'i lha mang du bstan pa rnams kyi sgrub
pa'i thabs dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / smin byed dbang dang / grol byed lam gyi rim pa yan lag tu bcas pa zab cing rgya che ba'i tshogs dpag tu ma mchis pa bzhugs
pa rnams so/ /'dir smras pa/ nyi ma'i rgyud 'khrungs rgyal ba'i 'dzum sgros dang / /gsang gsum byin rlabs rjes su gnang las skyes/ /legs gsungs mjal ba'i rab dga' rgyas
pa'i gzugs/ /shong ba stong gsum snod 'di e ma yangs/ /sbrang rtsi'i rgyal mtshan 'dzum brgya mi bstsu zhing / /lhas rtsen go la'i khyim du mi rgyu bar/ /mdo sngags rgyal
bstan nyin mor byed pa yis/ /yid srubs gnas su brnag dka'i mun pas gtibs/ /de mthus chos min smra ba'i sngo bsangs ma/ /pha mthar bgyid pa kho nas rta bdun pa'i/ /rjes
su 'gro min mngon mtho nges legs kyi/ /lam kun ma bsgribs ston pa 'dis kyang ngo / /lta byed dbang po ya bral skyes bu yis/ /dpyad bya'i gzugs don phra zhib dpyod nus
min/ /de bzhin dgongs 'grel med pa'i bka' gcig pus/ /thub pa'i dgongs don ji bzhin rtogs pa nyung / /legs par phye'o a sho ka'i 'dab ma/ /gong bur yur ba mtshar sdug rkang
pa'i rtses/ /mtha' drug tshul bzhi'i lkog gyur rgyal ba'i bka'/ /dgongs 'grel mkhas pa'i bstan bcos phreng bas so/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs
can rol pa'i chu gter las/ 'jug yul shes pa'i ched du bstan pa'i rnam par gzhag pa'i sarga ste dang po'o/ // /spyi don gnyis pa 'jug sgo

shes pa'i ched du thos bsam la rim gyis slob pa'i tshul la gsum ste/ thos bsam gyi dgos pa bstan pa/ brgyud ldan gyi slob dpon bsten tshul/ thos bsam la rim par slob tshul
lo/ /dang po ni/ 'phags mchog klu sgrub zhabs kyi bshes pa'i spring yig las/ mgo'am gos la glo bur me shor na/ /de dag phyir bzlog bgyi ba btang nas kyang / /yang srid med
par bgyi slad 'bad 'tshal te/ /'di bas ches mchog dgos pa gzhan ma mchis/ /zhes gnas skabs tshe 'di dang phyi ma'i bde don tsam bsgrub pa'i zhar byung gi tshul gyis ma
yin par 'jig rten 'di'i bde 'byor snying po med pa thams cad blos bor nas/ bsgrub par bya ba'i snying po'am gtso bo ni gzhan don du srid zhi'i mtha' la mi gnas pa'i mya ngan
las 'das pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang bsgrub par bya dgos te/ de sgrub pa'i thabs ni bslab pa gsum gyi lam la ma brten par mi 'grub pa'i phyir ro/ /de la'ang thog
mar thos bsam bsgom gsum gcig la gcig ltos kyi tshul du go rim ma log par nyams su bstar dgos te/ mgon po byams pas/ 'di na dang po thos la brten nas tshul bzhin yid la
byed pa 'byung / tshul bzhin yid la byed las yang dag don yul ye shes 'byung / /de las chos thob de yod de las blo gros rab tu skye/ /gang tshe de na so sor rang gir med
na ji ltar nges/ /zhes dang 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis kyang / shes rab rgyas par byed pa thos pa ste/ /de dang bsam pa gnyis ni yod gyur na/ /de las bsgom pa la ni rab tu
sbyor/ /des ni dngos grub bla na med par 'gyur/ /zhes

so/ /de'ang yang dag pa'i ye shes bsgom byung gi yon tan rnams rgyud la bskyed pa la/ thos pa'i don la rnam par dpyod pa'i bsam byung gi shes rab sngon du 'gro dgos so/ /de'i
sngon du'ang sngon chad thos par ma gyur pa'i phyi dang nang gi shes bya'i gzhung lugs gong du smos pa mtha' dag gam/ bye brag tu gang la gang dgos pa'i chos rnams legs
par thos dgos te/ byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod las/ thos pas chos rnams shes par 'gyur/ /thos pas sdig las ldog par 'gyur/ /thos pas don med spang bar 'gyur/ /thos pas
mya ngan 'das pa thob/ /ces dang / skyes rabs las/ gang zhig thos pas yid ni dad gyur nas/ /legs par dga' la brtan pa nyid du 'gyur/ /shes rab skye zhing gti mug med par
'gyur/ /rang gis shes kyang de ni nyo bar rig sa/ /thos pa gti mug mun sel sgron me yin/ /rkun po la sogs mi 'khyer nor gyi mchog / kun tu rmongs pa'i dgra 'joms mtshon
cha yin/ /thabs tshul man ngag ston pas grogs kyi mchog / phongs par gyur kyang mi 'gyur mdza' bo yin/ /gnod pa med pa mya ngan nad kyi sman/ /nyes pa chen po'i dgra 'joms
dpung gi mchog / grags dang dpal gyi gter gyi mchog kyang yin/ /ya rabs rnams dang 'phrad na skyes kyi mchog / tshogs kyi nang na mkhas pa mgu bar 'gyur/ /zhes dang /
spyod 'jug las kyang / rgyal sras rnams la mi slob pa'i/ /dngos de 'ga' yang yod ma yin/ /de ltar gnas pa'i mkhas pa la/ /bsod nams mi 'gyur gang yang med/

/ ces gsungs pas so/ /lhag par rgyal ba'i gdung 'tshob byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can gnas skabs 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyis nyen pa rnams gang la gang 'dul gyi thabs
sna tshogs pa ston pa'i sgo nas smin par bya ba'i phyir dang / mthar thug don gnyis lhun gyis grub pa rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i gnas bsgrub pa'i phyir/ shes bya'i yul
mtha' dag la mi bslab pa 'ga' yang med de/ mgon po byams pas/ rig pa'i gnas lnga dag la brtson par ma byas na/ /'phags pa'i mchog ste thams cad mkhyen nyid ga la thob/ /de
ltar gzhan dag tshar gcad pa dang rjes gzung phyir/ /bdag nyid kun shes bya phyir de la de brtson bya/ /zhes dang / 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi tas kyang / rang blo shes bya
kun la ma sbyangs na/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nam mkha'i mtha' ltar ring / /de ltar dgongs nas rgyal dang de sras kyis/ /shes bya'i gnas kun sbyangs zhes legs par gsungs/
/zhes so/ /des na rgyal ba'i myu gu blo dang ldan pa rnams ni shes bya rig pa'i gnas yan lag dang bcas pa mtha' dag la thos bsam gyi bslab sbyang bya dgos par gsungs so/
/kha cig na re de ni rgyal ba'i sras blo mchog dang ldan pa rnams kyi ngor gsungs kyi deng dus rang cag lta bu'i blo gros rtul zhing brtson 'grus shin tu dman pa'i mthar
thug pa dag la ni ma yin te/ rang nyid kyis nyams su len pa dang gzhan la 'chad pa la sogs pa bsgrub pa'i nus pa phra ba'i phyir zhe na/ rang nyid kyis nyams su len pa dang
gzhan la phan gdags par 'dod pa'i bsam pa sems bskyed kyis zin

pa la ni bslab sbyang mi 'os pa 'ga' yang med cing thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang sgrub pa la dgos pa shin tu che mod/ de skad smra ba po des rang mtshang gzhan la ngom par
zad do/ /ci'i phyir snyam na/ des ni dge sbyor sna re bsgrubs kyang thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam du 'gyur ba lta zhogaphan pa shin tu chung ba'i gyi na nyid du mngon te/ nges
'byung gi bsam pas gtan nas ma zin pa'i phyir ro/ /der gnod byed gzhan yang blun po dang zog po phal cher bslab sbyong dgos pa la ngo tsha bar byed cing / mkhas pa rnams
ni bslab sbyangs ma byas pa la ngo tsha bar 'dzin pas kyang nang rtags phyi rol du ngom pa mngon te/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi tas/ blun po slob par ngo tsha 'dzin/
/mkhas rnams ma bslabs ngo tshar 'dzin/ /des na mkhas rnams rgas gyur kyang / /phyi ma'i don du rig pa bslab/ /ces dang / skye ba snga mar ma bslabs pa/ /tshe 'dir blun par
mthong nas ni/ /phyi mar blun por skyes dogs nas/ /tshe 'dir dka' yang 'bad de mnyan/ /sgom na thos pa mi dgos zhes/ /blun po blo rgya chung ngur smra/ /thos pa med pa'i
bsgom pa tsam/ /'bad kyang dud 'gro'i sgrub thabs yin/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /des na legs par bshad pa ni byis pa'i ngag la 'dug kyang gus pas mnyan pa dgos
ched khyad par can du shes par bya'o/ /gnyis pa brgyud ldan gyi slob dpon bsten tshul la gsum/ slob dpon bsten pa'i dgos pa/ bstan bya'i slob dpon/ de bsten pa'i tshul lo/
/dang po la gnyis/ byis pa blo ldan du gzhug pa'i slob

dpon dang / blo ldan bstan pa la gzhug pa'i slob dpon no/ /dang po ni/ byis pa las dang po pa blo dang ldan pa'i go sar bkri bar byed pa'i thabs ni yon tan thams cad kyi gzhir
gyur pa yi ge'i klog la shin tu byang chub par byed dgos na'ang / de ni slob dpon gyi ngag la ma ltos par rang stobs kyis mkhas par mi 'gyur te/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya
paNDi tas/ byis pa 'jug sgo'i 'grel par/ byis pa blo gsal ba dag gis slob dpon gyi thad du phyin la me tog phul te tshig 'di skad kyis gsol ba gdab bo/ /mkhan po gson cigayon
tan kun gyi gzhir gyur cing / /gsal zhing rdzogs par rab phye la/ /tshul bzhin brjod na don 'gyur ba'i/ /klog gi cho ga bdag zhu'o/ /zhes brjod/ des kyang 'di skad du/
bu gang zhig shes na don 'gyur zhing / /mkhas par gyur na ngo mtshar che/ /nga yis ji ltar bstan pa bzhin/ /bsgrub par 'dod na rjes su gzung / /zhes gsal zhing zur phyin
par tshig smra'o/ /des kyang de bzhin bgyi'o zhes brjod do/ /mkhan pos kyang de ltar legs so zhes smras nas rjes su gzung ba'i tshul sogs rgyas par gsungs pa'i phyir ro/
/de ltar dgos pa'ang rje btsun bsod nams rtse mos/ gang gis yi ge'i bye brag dang / /dbye bsdu 'byung gnas mi shes par/ /sgra klog brjod par mkhas ma yin/ /don yang rnam
par 'khrul par 'gyur/ /zhes yi ge'i bye brag dang / dbye bsdu dang / sgra'i 'byin thabs rnams ma 'khrul zhing zur phyin pa legs par shes dgos so zhes gsungs mod kyi/ de
dag slob dpon mkhas pa zhig med par rang dgar

zhugs pas shes par mi 'gyur zhing ngal ba snying pos dben pa'i phyir ro/ /des na de la mkhas par bya ba la bdun te/ ngo bo gzung dang byed las dang / /nges tshig dbye bsdu
rgyu klog tshul/ /zhes pa ltar las/ dang po ni/ yi ge'i ngo bo skad kyi gdangs 'ba' zhig ste/ rnam 'grel las/ yi ge kun slong shes pa las/ /skye la shes pas sgra skye'o/
/zhes so/ /gnyis pa yi ge'i gzugs ni/ de'i rnam par dbye ba mdo rgya cher rol pa las/ tshangs pa'i yi ge kha roShTA'i yi ge padma'i snying po'i yi ge angga'i yi ge bangga'i
yi ge ma ga dha'i yi ge bkra shis pa'i yi ge sor gdub kyi yi ge sa kA nI'i yi ge sA dha nI'i yi ge A hu'i yi ge rtsub mo'i yi ge 'gro lding ba'i yi ge mon yul gyi yi ge
lho phyogs pa'i yi ge drag po'i yi ge grangs kyi yi ge spyi'u tshugs kyi yi ge rjes su mthun pa'i yi ge dha ra da'i yi ge khyA sya'i yi ge rgya nag gi yi ge hU na'i yi
ge dbus kyi yi ge rgyal gyi yi ge lha'i yi ge klu'i yi ge gnod sbyin gyi yi ge dri za'i yi ge mi'am ci'i yi ge lto 'phye chen po'i yi ge lha ma yin gyi yi ge nam mkha' lding
gi yi ge ri dwags 'khor lo'i yi ge bya rog skad kyi yi ge sa lha'i yi ge bar snang gi lha'i yi ge nub ba lang spyod kyi yi ge byang sgra mi snyan gyi yi ge shar lus 'phags
po'i yi ge 'degs pa'i yi ge gzhag pa'i yi ge rab tu gzhag pa'i yi ge rgya mtsho'i yi ge rdo rje'i yi ge 'phrin yig rab tu spring ba'i yi ge rnam par gzhag pa'i yi ge
chung ngu ma

yin pa'i yi ge bstan bcos bskor ba'i yi ge rtsis bskor ba'i yi ge 'degs pa bskor ba'i yi ge rkang pas bris pa'i yi ge tshig phyi ma gnyis grub pa'i yi ge ji srid tshig phyi
ma bcu grub pa'i yi ge bar ma sgrub pa'i yi ge sgra thams cad kun du sdud pa'i yi ge rig pa dang rjes su mthun pa'i yi ge rnam par bsres pa'i yi ge drang srong dka' thub
kyis gdungs pa'i yi ge gsal ba'i yi ge sa rab tu lta ba'i yi ge sman thams cad kyi rgyu mthun pa'i yi ge snying po thams cad kun bsdus pa'i yi ge ste yi ge drug cu rtsa
bzhir gsungs pa de dag tshang ba bod du ma byung yang da ltar dar srol yod pa tshangs pa'i yi ge lAnytsa na dang / de dang cha mthun pa dha ri ka'i yi ge de'i mgo gyen du
bzed pa na ga ra'i yi ge mi 'dra ba rnams dang / de'i mgo thur du bkug pa klu'i yi ge wartu la dang / 'dra min shes che ba kasmi ra'i yig rigs mi 'dra ba gsum tsam dang
/ gzhan yang gau Da'i yi ge dang / gha hu ra'i yi ge dang / sindhU'i yi ge dang / go la'i yi ge dang / ma ga dha'i yi ge dang / ka ma ta dang / pukkaM dang / rgya mtsho mtha'i
yi ge dang / sindha ka ra srin po'i yi ge rnams 'dri klog gi srol mchis pa ste/ de rnams la dbyangs yig bcu drug gsal byed la ka la sogs pa'i sde pa lnga/ mthar gnas
bzhi dang dro ba bzhi dang kSha yig ste sum cu rtsa bzhi'o/ /gzhan yang rgya dang hor gyi yi ge dang / bod kyi yi ge la slob dpon thu mi sambho Tas mdzad pa'i gzhung sum
cu pa las/ A li gsal byed i sogs bzhi/ /kA li sum cu tham pa'o/ /zhes dang / sa paN gyis yi

ge'i sbyor ba las kyang de dang mthun par gsungs pas dbyangs yig la i u e o bzhi dang / gsal byed la ka la sogs pa sum cur bzhed la/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mos ka nas ha'i
bar gyi nyer dgu ni pha'i yi ge dang / a yig ni ma'i yi ge ste pha ma sum cu zhes bzhed do/ /gsum pa byed pa ni/ thu mi sambho Tas/ bslab pa kun gyi gzhi 'dzin cing / /rig
byed smra ba rnams kyi rgyu/ /ming tshig brjod pa kun gyi gzhi/ /yi ge'i sbyor ba bshad par bya/ /zhes tshul khrims la sogs pa'i bslab pa kun gyi gzhi'ang yi ge la rag
las pa dang / nges brjod la sogs pa'i rig byed rnams dang / sgra dang tshad ma la sogs pa rig pa'i gnas lnga yan lag dang bcas pa smra ba'i rgyu yang yi ge yin pa dang
/ ming dang tshig tu brjod pa kun gyi gzhi yang yi ge yin pas yi ge'i byed las zhes bya ba'o/ /bzhi pa ni/ yi ge'i skad dod la a kSha ra zhes pa mi 'gyur ba'i don to/ /yul
tha dad pa'i skad la 'gyur ba yod kyang dbyangs dang gsal byed mi 'gyur ba'i phyir/ byanydza na zhes pa gsal byed de ming tshig brjod pa gsal bar byed pa'i phyir/ warNaN
zhes pa nus pa dang ldan pa ste/ rjod par byed pa'i nus pa dang ldan pa'i phyir/ de'ang ji skad du/ mi 'gyur ba dang gsal byed dang / /rjod par byed pa'i nus ldan phyir/
/yi ge zhes ni brjod pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /lnga pa dbye bsdu la/ ka lA pa las bcu bzhi rnams dbyangs so zhes dang / ka la sogs pa rnams gsal byed do zhes dbyangs
rnams bcu bzhi dang gsal byed sum

cu rtsa bdun rnams yin no/ /dbyangs yig kyang bsdu na/ mtshungs pa dang mtshungs pa ma yin pa dang / nA min dang nA min ma yin pa gnyis sam/ mtshams sbyor gyi yi ge dang mtshams
sbyor gyi yi ge ma yin pa gnyis rnams su 'du'o/ /gsal byed la'ang sde pa yin min gnyis/ sgra ldan sgra med gnyis su 'du'o/ /tsandra pa las kyang / a i uN/ r-i l-ika?e
o/ ai autsa?/ ha ya wa ra la Na/ nya ma da Na nama?/ dznya bha nya?/ gha Dha dha Sha?/ dza ba ga Da da sha?kha ba tsha Tha tha tsa Ta taba?/ ka pa ya?/ sha Sha sara?/
hala?/ zhes pa'o/ /de dag gi ngos 'dzin ni/ dharmma dA pas/ gcig las gyur pa Na nga nya ba rnams/ /gnyis las Na Sha bzhi las ka tsa dag/ lnga las ra sha ma ya rnams shes
bya/ /drug las la ni bsgrub par bya ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i bar gyi yi ge rnams go bar bya ba'i ched du'o/ /de'i dbye ba la a a u r-i bzhi la thung ngu ring po shin tu
ring po ste gsum gsum/ de dag re re la'ang tsandra go mis yi ge'i mdo las/ mthon po rnams kyis u dAtta/ /dma' bas a nu dAtta'o/ /de dag bar ma swa ri ta'o/ /zhes skad gdangs
mtho dma' bar ma gsum gsum ste sum cu so drug de rnams la sna ldan dang sna med so drug re ste bsdoms pas bdun cu rtsa gnyis/ mtshams sbyor yi ge bzhi la thung ba med
pas ring po dang shin tu ring po gnyis/ l-i la ring po med pas thung ngu dang shin tu ring po gnyis/ de dag lnga po re re la'ang skad gdangs mtho dman bar ma gsum gsum du
phye bas sum cu/ de rnams la sna ldan dang sna med sum cu re bsdoms pas drug cu ste/ gong

gi de dag bsdoms pas dbyangs la brgya so gnyis/ gsal byed la sum cu so gsum yod pa las/ ka gcig pu la yang dbyangs brgya sum cu so gnyis bzhugs te/ bsdoms pa gsal byed bzhi
stong sum brgya nga drug yod do/ /bod kyi yi ge'i dbye bsdu la/ sa skya paNDi tas/ dbyangs dang gsal byed gnyis ka'i rtsa ba a'o/ /de las dbyangs rnams 'byung ba na i u
gnyis 'byung / de dag sbyar ba las e o r-i l-i bzhi 'byung bas bdun no/ /yang de las gsal byed rnams 'byung ba na/ a las ka tsa Ta ta pa ha ste drug 'byung bas rtsa ba'i
phyi mo bcu gsum mo/ /rtsa ba de dag las dbyangs bcu drug dang gsal byed kyi gtso bo bco brgyad 'byung ba'i tshul ni dbyangs thung ngu bdun las ring po bdun 'byung bas bcu
bzhi/ sna ldan nam nga ro dang rnam par gcad pa gnyis 'grub pas bcu drug go/ gsal byed drug po'i steng du i las ya dang / u las wa/ r-i l-i las ra dang la/ aHtsheg drag
can las sha Sha sa/ aM nga ro can dang mthun pa nga nya Na na ma lnga'o/ /de dag las gsal byed kyi nying lag sum cu rtsa gsum 'byung ba'i tshul ni/ kha la sogs pa gnyis
pa rnams ni ka la sogs pa dang po rnams dang khong nas 'byung ba'i sgra sbyar ba'am/ ga la sogs pa gsum pa rnams ni ka la sogs pa dang po rnams dang a'i sgra sbyar ba'o/
/gha la sogs pa bzhi pa rnams ni ga la sogs pa gsum pa rnams dang ha'i sgra sbyar ba'o/ /de dag phan tshun sbyar ba las lo 'dab dang 'dra ba'i yi ge du mar 'gyur ba yin no/
/slob dpon bsod nams rtse

mos/ bod kyi yi ge sum cu bdun/ /sgra yi pha ma sum cur 'dus/ /srog rkyen yan lag yi ge bdun/ /de dag a yi khongs su 'du/ /zhes yi ge sum cu po de yang bsdu na dbyangs a dang
gsal byed nyer dgu po sgra'i pha ma gnyis su 'du zhing / yongs su grags pa'i a ni rang nyid kyis brjod bya rjod byed du rung bas gzhan gyi grogs mi dgos pa'i phyir seng
ge lta bu'i a zhes bya'o/ /de'i dbye ba tshig dang kyog dang shad dang yan lag i u e o bzhi ste/ bdun po ji ltar bsdu zhe na/ a'i dbye ba brgyad las/ dang po tsheg nyid
srog gi a de'i ngo bo yin no/ /de rgya gar la don gyis ston pas mi dgos kyang bod kyi yi ge'i bar du gsal bar byed pa ste/ de nyid las/ rang nyid brjod par mi nus te/ /thig
le chen po yi ge med/ /yi ge kun la 'jug pa'i phyir/ /thig le stong pa yi ge brgya/ /de nyid bod kyis gsal bar byed/ /ces gsungs pas ngag tu brjod pa med kyang bar gyi
sa mtshams gsal bar byed pa la de nyid rag las pa'i phyir/ de bzhin du dang por 'jug pa'i dang kyog dang tha mar 'jug pa'i shad gnyis ni rkyen gyi yi ge ste/ de'ang dang
po ni glang po'i sna lta bu'i a dang / phyi ma ni rnam par gcod pa'i a zhes bya'o/ /i u e o bzhi ni ka la sogs pa'i lus rnams kyi yan lag tu 'gyur ba'i phyir yan lag gi

ni/ /lce rtsa can gyi yin par bshad/ /sogs so/ /bdun pa klog tshul ni/ thung ngu phyi mo gcig pa ste/ /ring po phyi mo gnyis pa'o/ /plu ta phyi mo gsum pa yin/ /zhes gcig

las te/ slob dpon sogs la ma bsten par rang nyid kyis dpe tsam la brten nas chos kyi tshig don zab mo khong du chud par mi 'gyur zhing / brgya lam dpe la bltas pas don go

g.yar ba'i rgyan dang brkus pa'i

nor/ /slob dpon med pa'i rig pa rnams/ /yod kyang gzhan gyis brtsi ba med/ /ces dang / rgyu 'bras bslu ba med pa 'di/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i khyad chos yin/ /ma bslabs pa la
kun mkhyen du/ /'gro na rgyu 'bras ga la bden/ /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /des na legs par 'dod pa'i blo gros can rnams kyis gzhi lam 'bras bu'i gnas skabs thams cad du
bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa ni legs pa'i yon tan thams cad rim gyis 'phel ba'i gzhi yin par shes pa'i ched du/ bshes spring las/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa

sdud pa las/ bla ma mkhas pa rnams la rtag tu bsten par bya/ /ci phyir zhe na mkhas pa'i yon tan de las 'byung / /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /gnyis pa la gnyis/ dge ba'i

sbyor dang rtag sbyor gyi brtson 'grus dang ldan pa/ lung don rigs pas 'byed par nus pa'i rnam par dpyod pa dang ldan pa/ bshad bya'i chos kyi tshul de gdul bya'i blo dang
'tsham par go bde zhing rna bar snyan par smra mkhas pa/ rnyed bkur sogs la ma ltos par sems can rnams la snying brtse ba'i sgo nas tshul bzhin du smra ba'i bdag nyid can
de lta bu'i bla ma dam pa de nyid skyo ba med pas bsten par bya ste yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas yin pa'i phyir ro/ /gnyis pa ni dam pa'i chos 'dul ba las rab tu 'byin

slob ma ni dad pa dang ldan pa zhig ste/ de med na seng ge'i 'o ma snod phal par mi chags pa

ches pa dang 'dod pa dang sems dang ba'o zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /des na chos mnyan pa la dad pa nyid gtso che ste/ dkon mchog ta la'i gzungs las/ dad pa sngon 'gro ma ltar

ba/ bla ma lnga bcu pa sogs las rgya cher gsungs so/ /des na dbang bskur nas sngags kyi sdom pas ma sbrel na/ bla ma de bzang zhing grub thob yin na'ang pha rol tu phyin

ste/ de'ang lus don yod pa'i phyir phyag 'tshal ba dang / bskor ba byed pa dang / mnyes pa'i las bsgrub/ ngag don yod pa'i phyir bla ma'i yon tan brjod pa dang / bstod

byed po dge ba'i bshes kyi drin/ /gzugs can zhig na srid pas ci ste theg/ ring min phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos/ /'grub byed sngags kyi sdom pas skal ba bzang / /sku
bzhi'i sa bon 'jog pa'i slob dpon de/ /dkon mchog gsum las logs shig dmigs su ci/ /e ma skyabs mchog yid bzhin nor bu rnams/ /deng nas byang chub snying po mchis kyi bar/
/'bral med gtsug gi rgyan du mnyam 'grogs par/ /nyin mtshan gsol 'debs gser gyi skud pas btsems/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu
gter las/ 'jug sgo shes pa'i ched du thos bsam la rim gyis slob pa'i tshul gyi sarga ste gnyis pa'o/ // /spyi don gsum pa thos don yid ches ched du chos kyi brgyud rim bstan
pa la gnyis/ bstan pa'i 'jug sgo so thar gyi sdom par gnas pa'i chos kyi brgyud rim/ sdom par gnas pas thos bsam ji ltar byas pa'i chos kyi brgyud rim

mo/ /dang po ni/ chos mngon pa mdzod las/ tshul gnas thos dang bsam ldan pas/ /bsgom pa la ni rab tu sbyar/ /zhes dang / dge slong la rab tu gces pa'i mdo las/ shin tu legs
par tshul khrims gang / /sdom pa'i mi de mdzes pa'i gzugs/ /'dul ba la ni nye bar gnas/ /tshul khrims bslab pa rang yid ches/ /mi de nyi ma gcig la yang / /bsod nams phung
po dpag tu med/ /gsog cig sangs rgyas 'bras bu 'grub/ /ces dang / 'phags pa klu sgrub zhabs kyis kyang / khrims ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i sa bzhin du/ /yon tan kun gyi gzhi
rten lags pa gsungs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ thog mar yon tan phun sum tshogs pa thams cad kyi gzhi tshul khrims kyi bslab pa la gnas pa ste thos bsam sgom gsum gyi dge
ba gang dag bsags pa thams cad byang chub chen po'i rgyur 'gyur ba'i phan yon yod pa rjes su thos pa'i 'grogs bshes dag gis khrid de/ rang lo bcu gcig tu son par 'bri klung
gser dang ldan ma'i rgyun chen po dal gyis gzhol phyogs su gya gyur bgrod pa'i 'gram ngogs yin pas ldan yul zhes grags pa ga la ba der/ dpal sa skya'i lha khang bla brang
gi gdung brgyud dri ma med pa mkhyen brtse nus pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho lta bu la dbang 'byor ba 'jam dpal dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po pa'i zhabs kyis bcags shing legs par bskrun pa'i dgon sde sa dkar bsam 'grub gling zhes btags pa/ de nas brtsams te lha rigs bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs
kun dga' blo gros pa dang / de'i

sku dbon mthu stobs dbang phyug kun dga' bsod nams pa zung gis phebs shing gdan sar mdzad de chos srid zung 'brel gyi phrin las gser gyi 'khor los mdo khams kyi ljongs chen
por dbang sgyur bar mdzad pa'i sa'i thig le de nyid du/ mkhar dkar dmar zhes pa'i bla brang khag gnyis byung ba'i mkhar dmar po'i bdag po drung pa kun dga' rgya mtsho zhes
pa skar nag rtsis dang gso ba rig pa'i gzhung lugs la shin tu mkhas shing / dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po dang / mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa dang / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang shes bya bzang po la sogs pa las sdom pa gsum gyi bka' lung zab cing
rgya che ba thob cing / de dag gi bslab bya rnams la gces spras su mdzad pa de nyid kyi drung du skra phud phul bas/ tshangs par spyod pa'i dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa phog
ste/ kun dga' bsod nams zhes ming du gdags pa bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'og tu tshigs gsum rim nos kyi bstan pa la rim gyis slob pa'i skabs su dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa yang
bskyar du thob pa'i brgyud par bsdoms pa las 'dir zur pa ma dgos so/ /gnyis pa sdom par gnas pas thos bsam ji ltar byas pa'i brgyud rim la gnyis te/ thun mong ba phyi
rig pa'i gnas thos pa'i brgyud rim dang / thun mong ma yin pa nang rig pa'i gnas thos pa'i brgyud rim gnyis/ dang po ni/ theg pa chen po mdo sde rgyan las/ rig pa'i gnas
lnga dag la brtson par ma byas na/ /'phags

mchog ci sems thams cad mkhyen pa thob mi 'gyur/ /de bas gzhan dag tshar gcad pa dang rjes gzung phyir/ /bdag nyid kun shes bya phyir de la de brtson byed/ /ces gsungs pa'i
go rim dang mthun par mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgo las kyang / de yul brda sprod rtog ge dang / /gso ba phyi nang rig ces gsungs/ /gzhan la gzhan dag rnam bshad pa/ /'di yi nang
du 'dus shes bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ log rtog tshar gcod pa brda sprod rig pa sgra dang / rtog ge rig pa tshad ma dang / gzhan rjes su 'dzin pa gso ba rig pa tshe'i
rig byed dang / phyi rol rig pa bzo'i rig byed dang / bdag nyid kun shes par byed pa nang rig pa sde snod dang rgyud sder gtogs pa rnams rim par gsungs pa'i go rim dang
mthun par 'chad pa la/ dang po tshig gi log rtogs tshar gcod par byed pa sgra rig pa thos pa'i brgyud rim la dngos dang / zhar byung gnyis/ dang po la sgra mkhan dbang phyug
go chas gzhon nu kartI ka bsgrubs pas zhag bdun na gzhon nu gdong drug lag na mdung thung thogs pa byung nas gsungs pa'i legs sbyar gyi bstan bcos/ byA ka ra Na'i 'grel
pa 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu thams cad mkhyen pa zhwa lu lo tsA ba rin chen chos skyong bzang pos mdzad pa'i bshad sbyar gzhung don rab gsal dang / de'i 'grel pa karma
pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i kar TIka gi steng nas ri mo'i lag khrid gzhung 'bebs legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi mes po  sgra'i byung tshul
rnams las sum cu rtsa gsum du sgra mkhan sarba dznyA zhes pa byung ba des lha'i dbang po brgya byin la sgra bslabs

zhes 'byung ba de 'di dang gcig par sems so/ /tshangs pa/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin/ drang srong  gzhon nu gdong drug phur bu/ slob dpon dbang phyug go cha/ rgyal po bde spyod
bzang po/ jo bo drag 'byor/ mkhas pa chen po tsandra go mi/ slob dpon dharma dA sa/ mkhas pa ratna ma ti/ paN chen pUrNa tsandraHslob dpon 'chi med seng ge paN chen lakShmI
ka ra/ 'jig rten mig gcig shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ shong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ lo chen mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros dpung rgyan mdzes pa'i tog dpang
lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ sgra bsgyur nam mkha' bzang po/ skad gnyis smra ba thugs rje dpal gyi zhabs/ zhwa lu lo chen legs pa'i rgyal mtshan/
thams cad mkhyen pa chos skyong bzang po/ skyogs ston karma lo tsA ba rin chen bkra shis blo gros ngo mtshar bye ba'i gter mdzod/ dpal khang lo tsA ba dbyangs can snyems
pa'i sde/ sgang ra lo tsA ba 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ smon 'gro paN chen rig gnas rgya mtsho pa tshe dbang don grub/ de sras gnas lnga rig pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang rgyal
rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ rnam gling paN chen dkon mchog chos grags/ chab mdo byams gling gi skad gnyis smra ba kun dga' legs pa/
che tshang mkhas pa gsung rab rgya mtsho/ gtsug lag rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag karmma 'chi med thub bstan rab gsal/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen nam 'byung du rung
ba'i yon tan la smon pa'i tha snyad du/ ngag gi dbang po 'jigs bral phyogs las

rnam par rgyal ba'i lha dbyangs can snyems pa'i lang tsho'i sde zhes btags pa la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na rnam gling paN chen nas/ che tshang mkhas pa gsung rab rgya
mtsho man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na paN chen tshe dbang don grub nas/ ngam ring mkhan po mang yul lo chen tshe brtan rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho man 'dra'o/
/yang na lo chen thugs rje dpal nas/ dpal sdings skad gnyis smra ba grags pa'i mtshan can/ zhwa lu lo chen man 'dra/ yang na thugs rje dpal nas/ stag tshang lo tsA ba
shes rab rin chen/ zhwa lu lo chen man 'dra'o/ /'di bsdus don dang gzhung 'bebs gtso bor sbyar ba'i brgyud pa yin la/ mtha' dpyod gtso bor sbyar ba'i brgyud pa ni/ zhwa
lu lo chen nas/ dpon pad dkar chos skyong / 'brug pa lo tsA ba spyang mo ngag dbang grags pa/ lo chen dbang phyug zhabs/ shong ston sprul pa'i zlos gar sangs rgyas dpal
bzang / smon 'gro paN chen tshe dbang don grub man 'dra'o/ /sgra mdo 'di'i rtsa ba'i 'byung khungs ni indra byA ka ra Na gtso che bar bzhed do/ /rgyu mtshan brgya byin gyis
indra byA ka ra Na zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos byas/ brgya byin gyis sgra bslabs pa'i slob bu drang srong phur bu yin pa'i phyir ro/ /kA lA pa'i nye brgyud ni/ rje btsun
'jam dpal dbyangs/ des rgya gar shar phyogs ti ra ka'i paNDi ta shrI ma Ni ka la lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang du ka lA pa'i bshad pa gnang
/ des bal po shing kun gyi mchod rten la bskor ba mdzad dus/ bo dong lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis zhus/ de las

snar thang lo tsA ba saM gha shrIs zhus/ de las zhwa lu lo tsA ba legs rgyal gyis zhus/ de las zhwa lu skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po chos skyong bzang pos zhus pa man chad
snga ma rnams dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /rgyal ba kun gyi yum gcig 'phags ma dbyangs can mas gnas lnga rig pa'i slob dpon chen po a nu bhU ti swa ru pA tsarYa ste rjes su 'byor pa
rang bzhin bzang po la dngos su stsal ba'i brda sprod pa'i bstan bcos chen po dbyangs can byA ka ra Na dang / slob dpon de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa rab tu bya ba gsal
ldan dang bcas pa'i steng nas dka' ba'i gnad kyi lag khrid thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba'i yum gyur 'phags ma dbyangs can ma/ gnas lnga rig pa a nu bhU ti swa ru pA
tsarYa nas rim par/ 'phags yul nub phyogs ku ru kShe tra bram ze'i rigs su 'khrungs pa paNDi ta pa la bha dra/ go kU la na tha mi shra/ 'dar pa lo tsA ba ngag dbang lhun
grub phun tshogs/ rnam gling paN chen dkon mchog chos grags/ byams gling mkhas pa kun dga' legs pa/ che tshang smra ba'i dbang phyug gsung rab rgya mtsho/ gtsug lag rgya
mtsho 'dzin pa karma 'chi med thub bstan rab gsal/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /!/ /bod kyi brda sprod pa'i bstan bcos chos kyi rgyal po srong btsan
sgam pos 'jam dpal dbyangs kyi rnam par sprul pa thu mi sambho Ta rgya gar du brdzongs te/ paNDi ta lha rigs pa seng ge dang bram ze li byin bsten nas/ legs sbyar gyi brda
sprod la mkhas par gyur pas rgya yig lnga bcu bod yig sum cur gtan la

phab ste bstan bcos chen po brgyad mdzad pa'i nang tshan sum cu pa dang rtags kyi 'jug pa gnyis kyi 'grel pa thams cad mkhyen pa chos skyong bzang pos mdzad pa'i steng nas
legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bram ze li byin/ thu mi sambho Ta nas rim par/ thams cad mkhyen pa chos skyong bzang po/ skyogs ston karma lo tsA ba rin chen bkra shis blo
gros ngo mtshar bye ba'i gter mdzod/ dpal khang lo tsA ba dbyangs can snyems pa'i sde/ sgang ra lo tsA ba 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ paNDi ta chen po smon 'gro tshe dbang don
grub/ de sras 'jam dbyangs dbang rgyal rdo rje nas rim par se ra theg chen gling gi rab 'byams pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang
na lo chen chos skyong bzang po nas rim par/ tshe bhrU~M pa karma 'chi med thub bstan rab gsal/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /gnyis pa ni/ sa skya paNDi tas/ gzhan las gzhan dag
rnam bshad pa/ /'di yi nang du 'dus zhes bshad/ /ces gsungs pas rig pa'i gnas lnga'i nang du rig gnas gzhan thams cad 'dus pa'i lugs la ni/ zhar byung sgra'i yan lag tu
'gyur zhing / rig pa'i gnas chung ba lnga zhes so sor bgrang ba'i lugs la ni/ sgra shes na don la mi rmongs pas rjod byed kun gyi gzhir bzung nas/ de'i steng du sdeb sbyor
shes na tshigs bcad la mi rmongs/ mngon brjod shes na ming la mi rmongs/ snyan ngag shes na tshig rgyan la mi rmongs/ zlos gar shes na skad rigs la mi rmongs/ zhes dpang
lo/ snar thang saM gha shrI/ rin spungs sa spyod sogs mkhas pa 'ga' zhig

sgra lan gnyis su bgrangs pa'i lngar 'dod pa dang / stag tshang lo tsA bas/ skar rtsis snyan ngag sdeb sbyor dang / /mngon brjod zlos gar 'di lnga la/ /rig gnas lnga zhes 'phags
yul na/ /grags pa'i ba dan rlung ltar sgrog/ ces sgra mi bgrangs par dus 'khor gyi rtsis dang dbyangs 'char gyi rtsis rig gcig tu bgrangs pa'i chung ba lnga zhes pa'i
tha snyad mdzad mod/ don la 'gal bar mi sems te/ nges par che chung gi tha snyad de ltar dgos pa'i grub mtha' 'cha' na gong gi mdo sde rgyan gyi lung de la yang ma khyab
pa'i skyon yod par thal/ der sdeb sbyor dang snyan ngag la sogs pa gzhan lnga po rgyal ba'i sras kyis bslab byar ma bstan pa'i phyir ro/ /des na gang ltar yang / rgya
gar rdo rje gdan gyi mkhas pa sgo drug tu grags pa'i ya gyal rtsod dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa'i sdeb sbyor
rin chen 'byung gnas kyis br-itta dzA ti ngo mtshar rtogs byed kyi ri mo dang bcas pa legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ paNDi ta chen po rin chen 'byung gnas/ paN chen
sa dbang bzang po/ shong lo tsA ba mched gnyis/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan pa/ dpang lo chen po/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ lo chen nam mkha' bzang po/ skad gnyis smra ba thugs
rje dpal/ dpal sdings lo chen grags pa'i mtshan can/ 'gos lo tsA ba gsum pa chos skyong bzang po/ skyogs ston karma lo tsA ba/ dpal khang lo tsA ba dbyangs can snyems pa'i
sde/ sgang ra lo tsA ba 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ shes bya kun rig smon

'gro tshe dbang don grub/ de sras paN chen 'jam dbyangs dbang rgyal rdo rje/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ rnam gling paN chen dkon mchog
chos grags/ byams gling mkhas pa kun dga' legs pa/ mkhas dbang gsung rab rgya mtsho/ brda sprod smra ba'i dbang phyug karma 'chi med thub bstan rab gsal/ des bdag bande
tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na zhwa lu lo chen nas/ lo chen pad dkar chos skyong / grangs chen 'jam dpal rdo rje/ smon 'gro paN chen man 'dra/ /!/ /chos kyi rgyal po
sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mdzad pa'i sdeb sbyor gyi bstan bcos sna tshogs me tog gi chun po rig gnas mtha' dag gi gsal byed mkhas pa 'jug pa'i
sgo/ sgra la 'jug pa/ sgra nyer bsdus/ sgra'i gnas kyi gnad bsdus rnams kyi lung rkyang gi brgyud pa ni/ paNDi ta saM gha shrI/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta kun dga'
rgyal mtshan/ 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ rgyal ba na bza' brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon
'dul ba 'dzin pa/ chos rje byang chub seng ge shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin
dkon mchog 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams
pa kun dga' bkra

shis/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rje don grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun grub pa khams ston nam mkha' dpal bzang / des
bdag la'o/ /!/ /ma hA paNDi ta dpal 'dzin sdes mdzad pa'i mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos mu tig phreng ba las/ 'jig rten mig gcig chos skyong bzang pos mngon brjod nye bar mkho
zhing grags che ba che long zhig logs su bkar ba skad gnyis shan sbyar du yod pa/ slob dpon chen po 'chi med seng ge sa mdzad pa'i mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos a ma ra ko
Sha dang / sa paN gyi tshig gter sogs rgya bod kyi mkhas pa rnams kyi yi ge la brten nas dka' ba'i gnad rnams legs par thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ paN chen 'chi med seng ge
slob dpon rab 'byor zla ba/ mkhas pa phun tshogs byed pa/ shong lo mched gnyis/ lo mchog pa/ dpang lo chen po/ lo chen byang rtse/ lo chen nam mkha' bzang po/ sgra bsgyur
thugs rje dpal/ mang thos legs pa rgyal mtshan/ zhwa lu lo tsA ba chen po/ skyogs ston karma lo tsA ba/ dpal khang pa dbyangs can snyems pa'i sde/ de las sgang rwa ba 'od
zer rgyal mtshan dang grangs chen 'jam dpal rdo rje gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las paN chen tshe dbang don grub/ de nas sras 'jam dbyangs dbang rgyal rdo rje/ ngag dbang
blo bzang rgya mtsho/ rnam gling paN chen dkon mchog chos grags/ byams gling mkhas pa kun dga' legs pa/ che tshang gsung rab rgya mtsho/ karma 'chi

med thub bstan rab gsal/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /tshig gi gter gyi lung rkyang gi brgyud pa ni/ gong gi sdeb sbyor sna tshogs me tog chun po'i brgyud pa
dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /'phags pa'i yul gyi snyan ngag mkhan kun gyi gtsug tu mngon par mtho ba/ tshangs pa'i bu mos rjes su bzung ba'i slob dpon daNTi ste dbyug pa can zhabs
kyis mdzad pa'i snyan dngags me long gi bstan bcos lam rnam par dbye ba/ don rgyan sgra rgyan gab tshig dang bcas pa/ de'i bsdus don lo chen chos skyong bzang pos mdzad pa
dang / dka' 'grel thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i dbyangs can dgyes pa'i glu dbyangs dang 'bras spungs sgo mang gi paN chen blo gros nyi

rgyal mtshan/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ dbon pad dkar chos

skyong / grangs chen lo tsA ba 'jam dpal rdo rje/ smon 'gro paN chen tshe dbang don grub/ 'jam dbyangs dbang rgyal rdo rje/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang

na pad dkar chos skyong nas/ spyang mo lo tsA ba/ lo chen dbang phyug lo chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / zhang mkhar paN chen 'jam dpal rdo rje/ rgyal dbang kun mkhyen lnga

khrims rin chen la'o/ /'dir 'ga' zhig slob dpon chos kyi grags pas/ shes rab can ni phyogs kyi glang po ste/ /tsandra go mi brjod pa rnam par dag/ snyan dngags dpa' bo las

rigs pa'i shes byed

snar thang lo chen saM gha shrIs/ daNDI'i bstan bcos dri ma med/ /ji bzhin 'gyed la dpa' bo dang / /skal mnyam blo gros mig thob pa/ /ma nor lam 'di bdag gis bshad/ /ces bshad
pa dang / lam rnam dbye'i skabs su/ de dag dbye ba snyan ngag mkhan/ /so so la gnas brjod mi nus/ /zhes pa 'grel pa rnams su nag mo'i khol po dpa' bo sogs bgrangs pa
mang ba'i phyir ro/ /zlos gar gyi bstan bcos skad rigs kyi dbang gis bod du 'jug chung bas grags chung zhing mkhas pa rnams kyis bshad srol las don gyis thon pa las zur du
nos pa med la/ de la mkho bas paNDi tas mdzad pa'i rol mo'i bstan bcos kyi lung brgyud ni sdeb sbyor sna tshogs me tog gi chun po sogs dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /'phags pa'i yul
na snyan ngag mkhan kun gyi dbus su nyin mor byed pa'i dkyil 'khor ltar gsal ba chos kyi rgyal po dge ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i rtogs pa brjod pa dpag
bsam 'khri shing yal 'dab brgya dang bdun/ de'i kha skong le'u gcig sras zla ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa dang bcas pa'i yal 'dab brgya rtsa brgyad pa chos kyi rgyal po 'phags
pa rin po che'i bkas bskul ltar skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis dpal sa skyar bsgyur ba la slad kyi lo tsA ba zhwa lu pa chos skyong
bzang pos 'gyur bcos dang zhus dag gis legs par bstar ba'i steng nas lung thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston mchog shAkya seng ge chos rgyal dge ba'i dbang po/ de sras zla ba'i
dbang po/ paNDi ta lakShmI kA ra/ shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gcung

blo gros brtan pa/ dbon po chos skyong dpal/ dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bo dong paN chen phyogs las rnam
rgyal/ stag lung zhabs drung ngag dbang  'di dbyangs can mas rjes su bzung bar grags/grags pa/ kun spangs rnam rgyal grags pa/ 'bum rab 'byams pa rin chen chos dbang / rab
'byams chos rje tshul khrims dbang phyug dpal khang lo tsA ba mang thos chos kyi rgya mtsho/ mdo khams pa bla chen yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/
gong dkar ba chos sde ba/'jam dbyangs mkhyen pa'i rtse mo/ mkhyen brtse chen po'i dbon po yin tshe dbang kun mkhyen yang zer/kun bzang rtse pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/
gong dkar drung yig ri grong pa/g.yu lo bkod pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gong dkar zur 'chad pa/dpal 'byor gling pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ gong dkar 'phying ru thod dkar
ba/nor  gong dkar ba/rgyas gling pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ don grub chos  gong dkar ba/gling bstan pa dar rgyas/ dol pa phyogs las rnam rgyal/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub/ gnas gsar ba ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun chen po kun dga' rgya mtsho/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs
par nos so/ /yang na dpal khang lo tsA ba nas/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen pa'i rtse mo man gong ltar ro/ /yang na stag lung ngag dbang grags pa
nas/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ dpal khang lo tsA ba man 'dra/ yang na dpal 'byor gling

pa nas/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rin chen rgya mtsho man gong bzhin no/ /!/ /dpal dus kyi 'khor lo phyi nang gzhan gsum gyi sgo nas gtan la 'bebs pa'i phyi rol shes pa'i
yan lag rtsis skor rnams dus 'khor gyi cha lag tu bgrangs kyang mi 'thad pa ma yin mod/ rig gnas che ba lngar bsdu ba'i tshe sgra rig pa'i 'khor du 'byung zhing / rig
gnas chung ba lngar dbye ba'i tshe skar rtsis rig gnas chung ba'i ya gyal gcig tu mdzad pa khungs dang 'brel ba nas/ padma dkar po'i zhal lung gi dgongs don gtso bor bzung
/ phug pa man ngag lugs kyi phyag len gyis rnam par spras pa'i bstan bcos bai DUr dkar po'i steng nas lnga bsdus/ sgra gcan lo 'pho zla 'pho/ gza' 'dzin/ gza' lnga tshes
dang nyin zhag la spyod pa/ de dag gi myur rtsis kyi rigs mi 'dra ba rnams nyi ldog 'khor lo/ dus sbyor tatkAl dang dum bu drug pa/ zhag gsum gyi rnam par dbye ba/ g.yul
las rnam par rgyal ba las btus pa thor bu rnams dang bcas pa rnams lag khrid du nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa chos kyi grags pa/ de las mkhas grub nor bzang
rgya mtsho dang phug pa lhun grub rgya mtsho gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las mkhas pa chos legs rin chen/ de nas phug nas chos rje dpal mgon phrin las pa nas rim par/ 'di
nas brgyud pa 'ga' zhig btsal dgos/ser theg chen gling gi chu mig spyi khang pa'i rab 'byams pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin
du stsal to/ /yang na yan chad btsal/ bka' blon mkhas pa kun dga'

phun tshogs/ mnga' ris mkhas btsun kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /phug lugs kyi gza' lnga nyin zhag ma myur rtsis re mig rgya mtsho sogs kyi
lag len che phra rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje phrin las pa nas/ mkhas grub dpal gyi seng ge mkhas dbang bkra shis mtshan can/ ldum bu don grub dbang rgyal/ rnam gling
paN chen nam/ lo chen chos dpal bzang po gang rung nas/ rdor grags padma'i mtshan can/ bla mkhyen bsod nams rgyal/ de las bdag gis so/ /!/ /bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rjes su
'brangs pa byed pa'i rtsis kyi lnga bsdus/ sgra gcan/ lo bdag rgyal blon/ kar myong rtsis/ nyi zlar sgra gcan 'jug pa'i rtsis la sogs pa de la nye bar mkho ba'i rigs rnams
legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yan chad kyi brgyud pa btsal/ dpal sa skya'i mkhas pa dge slong lags/ de las rtsis kyi gtsug lag smra ba'i dbang phyug kun dga' rgya mtsho/
mkhas btsun dge ba'i bshes gnyen sangs rgyas chos 'phel/ de las bdag gis legs par nos so/ /yang na sangs rgyas chos 'phel nas/ rtsis rig 'dzin pa kun dga' rgya mtsho/
de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis so/ /!/ /'di de sngon lag len ma thob kyang thob 'gyur dbang gis bris/ dpal gtsug na zla bas gsungs pa'i dbyangs 'char gyi
rgyud le'u bcu pa'i dgongs 'grel mchog tu dga' ba'i sgra dbyangs dang / ngo mtshar rgyan gyi me tog gi steng nas dbyangs 'char gyi phyag len yongs su rdzogs pa nos pa'i
brgyud pa

ni/ thub pa chen po/ lha chen dbang phyug chen po/ dpal rta mgrin mgon po/ de'i sras dpal ldan tshangs lha nA tha/ dpal zla ba kun dga' mgon po/ dpal utpal bzang po/ dpal gsang
ba'i mtshan can/ dpal yi dam bzang po/ dpal a bhi naM gupta ra na/ dpal shangka ra bha dra/ dpal phun sum tshogs 'dzin bzang po/ dpal seng ge go cha/ dpal 'jam dpal
dga' byed/ dpal 'od mdzad/ dpal dza ya A nanda/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ bla ma chos rje/ slob dpon rin chen rgyal po/ slob dpon rin chen dbang phyug bla ma gzhon
nu rin chen/ sngags 'chang lhun grub dpal/ mkhas grub chos rje/ mkhas mchog ArYa de wa/ mkhas dbang sangs rgyas blo gros/ dus zhabs pa chen po dpal mgon phrin las/ mkhas
pa dpal gyi seng ge bla mkhyen g.yu lo ba/ gnyags ban ngag dbang 'jam dpal blo gros/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho yin nam/ de nas brgyud pa gsum
bzhi ma rnyed pa btsal dgos/ de nas smra mkhas ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /!/ /'phags pa'i yul du nag rtsis
zhes bya ba'i tha snyad ma grags la shar phyogs ma hA tsi na'i yul gyi 'gro ba rnams kun rdzob rtsis kyi bden pas 'dul bar dgongs nas/ mgon po 'jam dpal dbyangs kyis rgya
nag ri bo rtse lngar trikSha shing gi lba ba las byis pa'i tshul gyis brdzus te 'khrungs nas legs gsungs bdud rtsi'i sgo 'phar phye bas yul de shin tu dar rgyas su byung
la/ slad kyi tshe

'phags ma sgrol ma'i sprul pa 'un shing kong jos pur rgyal bod du byon dus rten 'brel rtsis kyi gtsug lag rnams spyan drangs pa nas brtsams te bod yul du rtsis dkar nag ces
yongs su dar srol byung ba'i skor la rtsa ba'i rde'u drug gcod 'dral gyi rde'u nyi shu rtsa gcig zhe bdun ma/ bcu bzhi ma/ brgyad ma/ thang shing rtsis/ tshe rtsis/ bag
rtsis/ gshin rtsis sogs zhib tu nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ kong tse 'phrul gyi rgyal po/ lo tsA ba khams pa phra mo sogs nas rim par/ khyung nag shAka dar/
phug pa mkhas mchog ArYa de wa/ mtshungs med sangs rgyas blo gros/ rtsis rig smra ba'i gtsug rgyan dpal mgon phrin las pa/ de nas se ra theg chen gling gi rab 'byams pa
bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis nos so/ /yang na dpal mgon phrin las nas/ mkhas mchog dpal gyi seng ge bla mkhyen g.yu lo ba/ gnyags
ban nang rwa ba ngag dbang 'jam dpal blo gros/ zur chen pa man gong dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /gnyis pa tshar gcod rig pa tshad ma ni/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi tas/ de ltar sgrub
dang sun 'byin gyi/ /rig pa'i gzhung lugs gang gis shes/ /mkhas pa des ni rdzogs pa yi/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi bstan pa 'dzin/ /zhes gsungs pa rigs par smra ba'i khyu
mchog slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa'i tshad ma'i mdo/ shes bya rig gnas lnga'i skabs su bzhi pa tshad ma/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin kun mkhyen g.yag ston
sangs rgyas dpal

dang / red mda' ba gzhon nu dpal dag gi skabs su sa skya dang ngam ring sogs su po ti grags chen bco brgyad kyi rnam gzhag mdzad par/ tshad mdo 1rnam 'grel 2rnam nges 3tshad
ma'i skor/ /'dul ba mdo 4dang mdo rtsa 5'dul ba'i skor/ /kun las btus 6dang mdzod gnyis 7mngon pa'i skor/ /byam8sa chos 9lnga 10dang pha11ra phyin12 dbu ma yi/ /rtsa 13'ju14ga
bzhi15 gsum ches 16zab dbu ma'i skor/ /sde bdun mdo bcas dgongs 'grel rig 17gter dang / /sde snod rgyud sde kun 'grel 18sdom gsum ste/ /pusti grags chen bco brgyad
zhes su grags/ /zhes pa ltar las dang po tshad ma kun las btus pa zha ma seng rgyal bas bsgyur ba le'u drug gi bdag nyid can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub pa'i
dbang po/ dgra bcom pa chos skyob/ me waM gdabyig gnyen/ dpal ldan phyogs kyi glang po/ slob dpon dbang phyug sde/ dpal ldan chos kyi grags pa/ paNDi ta lha dbang blo gros/
paN chen shAkya blo gros/ slob dpon dul ba'i lha/ shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros/ paN chen nyi ma sbas pa/ slob dpon dza ma ri/ dznyA na shrI mi tra/ paNDi ta chos mchog
bram ze shangka ra nanda/ wanggu paNDi ta ngag dbang / kha che paNDi ta shAkya shrI/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge zhang mdo sde dpal/ sde bdun pa dpal
ldan seng ge mkhas pa nor bzang dpal/ mkhan chen brtson 'grus dpal/ g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma/ rong ston shes bya kun rig mkhas pa don yod dpal/ paN chen shAkya mchog
ldan/ sa skya'i las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol

mchog mkhan chen phrin las bzang po/ dpal ldan shAkya bstan 'dzin/ shAkya nor bu kun dga' legs pa/ bshes gnyen rnam rgyal/ smra dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal/ thams cad mkhyen
pa kun dga' lhun grub/ rje btsun sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / chos rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ e waM pa rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bdag
bande tshul khrims chen la'o/ /!/ /rigs pa'i dbang phyug slob dpon chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma sde bdun gyi ya gyal rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad
ma rnam 'grel le'u bzhi pa sa skya paNDi ta'i 'gyur gyi steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa yang dag pa thub pa'i dbang po/ mgon po 'jam dpal dbyangs/ dgra bcos pa
chos skyob/ mkhas pa me waM ga rje btsun btsong kha pa'i gsan yig na me waM ga zhes snang /kun mkhyen gnyis pa dbyig gnyen/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang po/ slob dpon dbang
phyug sde/ rig pa'i dbang phyug chos kyi grags pa/ slob dpon paNDi ta lha dbang blo gros/ slob dpon shAkya blo gros/ paNDi ta 'od kyi blo gros/ paNDi ta shes rab rgyan mkhan
por yang grags/ 'byung gnas sbas pa/ slob dpon dza  tshad ma'i brgyud 'debs su ya mA ri zhes 'byung ba ma dag pa 'dra'am snyam/ma ri/ paNDi ta chos mchog  rgyal rnga
bdun pa'ang zer/slob dpon dul ba'i lha/ 'di gsan yig 'ga' zhig na ma byung ba brtag bram ze shangka ra nanda/ bde byed dga' bar bsgyur 'dug waM gu paNDi ta/ paN chen shAkya
shrI/ paNDi ta su ga ta shrI/ paN chen dA na shI la/ bal po saM gha shrI/ de bzhi

ga las chos rje sa skya paNDi tas gsan/ de nas 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal/ dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhas pa brtson 'grus dpal/ g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma/ rong ston mkhas pa yon tan dpal/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ sa skya'i las chen
ye shes lhun grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog mkhan chen phrin las bzang po/ dpal ldan shAkya bstan 'dzin man gong bzhin no/ /!/ /sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa'i dgongs 'grel

la/ de nas phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/ dpal

'jam

mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos rje don grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun grub pa khams ston nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sa skya
paN chen nas/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ na bza' brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan/
slob dpon 'dul 'dzin pa/ chos rje byang chub seng ge shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /!/ /gsum pa gzhan rjes su 'dzin pa rig pa'i gnas la bzo dang gso ba gnyis/
dang po bzo rig pa ni/ stag tshang lo tsA ba'i rig gnas kun shes las/ bzo la lus bzo ngag bzo yid bzo gsum/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar na/ rig pa'i gnas phal cher bzo rig pa'i
khongs su 'du bar gsungs shing / 'dir bzo rig bye brag pa dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud dang / 'grel chen dri med 'od dang / bde mchog sdom pa 'byung dang / gshin rje'i
gshed nag po rgyud 'grel bcas dang / 'jam dpal rtsa ba'i rgyud dang / bslab pa kun las btus pa la sogs pa nas gsungs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dang / rgyal yum sogs dang
byang chub sems dpa' khro bo khro mo sogs kyi sku'i thig rtsa ci rigs par bshad pa rnams dang / de dag gi bzhed pa ma nor bar ston par byed pa mkhas dbang sman bla don grub
pas mdzad pa'i sku gzugs kyi tshad kyi rab tu byed pa'i gzhung ni/ bod yul 'dir rgya gzhung tshad ldan lta bur khas len dgos pas/ gzhung der de bzhin

gshegs pa'i sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bshad pa/ tshad kyi gzhung du grags pa 'ga' zhig rang bzos bslad pa'i mi 'thad pa'i phyogs dgag pa/ tshad dang mi ldan pa'i sku gzugs
bzhengs pa'i nyes skyon brjod pa/ mdo rgyud kyi gzhung lugs chen po rnams kyi lung gis tshad ldan gyi lugs dgod pa/ tshad de dag dang ldan pa'i sku gzugs bzhengs pa'i phan
yon brjod pa/ sku gzugs bzhengs pa'i lha bzo dang sbyin bdag gi mtshan nyid brjod pa/ de dag lag tu blang ba'i rim par/ ji skad du/ rgyal ba'i sku gzugs thal mo bcu pa
dang / /rgyal sras rnams kyi mtho bcu zhan pa dang / /rgyal yum sogs kyi zhal tshad dgu pa dang / /rgyal dbang khros pa rnams kyi gdong brgyad pa/ /mi'u thung gi lus tshad
mtho drug pa/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar gyi rgyas par bshad pa ste don tshan bdun gyi sgo nas bstan pa dang / de'i rjes su 'brang bar gyur pa dbyangs can lha mos rjes su bzung
ba rta nag ri mkhar ba dpal ldan blo gros bzang pos/ gang phyir gang gis gang la gang ltar 'dri/ /rtags dang skyon yon spang blang ji ltar bya/ /zhes pa ltar don tshan
brgyad kyis bstan pa dang / de dag gi rjes su 'brangs nas 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa'i zlos gar mkhas dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtshos lag tu blang ba'i thig 'debs kyi

cag gi yang mes sprul sku sangs rgyas lha dbang gis mdzad pa'i bskor thig gi 'grel pa mthong ba don

gsal zhes bya ba dang bcas pa rnams kyi steng nas lag khrid dang thos bsam zhib tu nos pa las/ thog mar dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud dang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad
pa'i 'grel chen dri ma med pa'i 'od le'u lnga pa ye shes kyi le'ur gsal bar bstan pa'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ dam pa dang po'i sangs rgyas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo/ rgyal ba
shAkya thub pa/ zla ba bzang po/ lha dbang gzi brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha'i dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ padma dkar po/ 'jam
dbyangs sprul pa tsi lu paN chen/ piNDo A tsArYa/ dus zhabs pa che ba/ dus zhabs pa gnyis pa manydzu kIrti/ sa manta shrI/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng
/ rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de sras shes rab seng ge bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po rin chen rnam
rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ shar pa ye shes rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub/ chos rje don grub rgyal mtshan/

lhun grub/ khyab bdag klu sgrub rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med smon lam lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang brtson 'grus bzang po/ gnas gsar ba kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ dus
'khor bla ma

kun dga' phun tshogs/ de las bdag gis so/ /de dag gi tshad kyi lag khrid dang rgya sman gsar rnying gi lugs srol so so'i khyad par gyi ri mo'i 'gros sogs zhib par nos pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ 'di yan chad btsal/ de nas karma pa dbyangs can bzang po'i zhabs/ sprul sku sangs rgyas lha'i dbang po/ dbon sprul sku dge 'dun 'od zer/ sprul pa'i bzo bo mkha'
ri gdong pa dbon po rgya bo zhes pa/ 'gru dge yag lha bzo/ de las ngag dbang chos 'phel ba/ des bdag la lag khrid du stsal to/ /yang na dge yag pa nas/ de sras karma
chos lung / mkhas btsun chen po sangs rgyas chos 'phel/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par nos so/ /!/ /byang chub phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun gzugs
rnam du shar ba'i thar pa'i grong khyer gzhal yas khang gi tshad ni/ paNDi ta chen po gung ru shes rab bzang pos mdzad pa'i yi ge la brten nas dkyil 'khor spyi'i thig
tshad rta babs snam bu bzhi pa dang / snam bu bcu gcig pa'i thig 'debs dang / bye brag tu rgyud sde bzhis bstan pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams kyi nang thig gi khyad par rnams dang
/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg gi thab thig dang bcas pa thos bsam gyi sgo nas lag len du gtan la bab cing / rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i rnam
bshad zla zer dang / gzhal yas khang gi tshad rnam par gzhag pa dang / kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pas mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi rnam bshad rnams kyi lung
legs par nos shing gzhal yas khang blos slong gi cha tshad rnams

lag len thos bsam gyis gtan la phab pa'i zla zer gyi brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po nas/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon

'di nas bla ma gnyis tsam btsal/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /man ngag lugs kyi
