grub/ des bdag la stsal to/ /!/ /gnyis pa gsung rten ni gong du smos pa'i yig ris rnams las bod du 'dri srol mchis pa'i nang nas lAnytsa na dang / wartu la dang / nA ga
ra dang / sindhu dang / pukkaM dang / dha ri ka dang / kasmI ra dang / 'phags pas mdzad pa'i hor gyi yig gsar la sogs pa lag khrid du byas pa'i slob dpon dang brgyud rim
ni gong gi brda sprod pa'i skabs ltar 'ded pas btub bam snyam mo/ /bod kyi yi ge la slob dpon thu mi saM bho Tas mdzad pa'i yi ge'i rgyun las brgyud de khyung po

g.yu khri dang sum pa gnod sbyin sogs kyis dar rgyas su mdzad pa'i rdzab dang gshar ma'i nang gsel lugs srol cung zad 'dra min mchis pa rnams la'ang sbyangs lor bgyis so/ /!/
/gsum pa thugs kyi rten ni/ rdo rje dril bu la sogs pa phyag mtshan rnams kyi tshad dang mtshan nyid dang / mchod rten la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten brgyad de/ 'di'i
go rim gyi thog ma lha babs nas byas pa sogs mi 'dra ba mang du yod cing / mnga' ris tshul khrims 'od zer gyis/ pad spungs bltams tshe ser skya'i drung du dar/ /byang
chen rdzogs sangs rgyas tshe rdo rje gdan/ /sgo mangs chos 'khor bskor tshe wA rA Na sIr dang / /cho 'phrul cho 'phrul bstan tshe mnyan yod du/ /lha babs yum gyi don mdzad
gsal ldan grong / /dbyen bzlum dge 'dun 'dums tshe yangs can du/ /sku tshe'i bdud las rnam rgyal mchod rten che/ /myang 'das mya ngan 'das tshe rtswa mchog grong / /zhes
srid pa tha ma pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sku bltams ma thag nas phyogs rnams su gom pa bdun bdun bor ba'i sar padma skyes pa sogs bkra shis pa'i rten 'brel dang mthun
par padma sprungs pas thog drangs par mdzad pa ltar legs shing / mchod rten brgyad po de dag gi cha tshad yi ge mang du mthong mod/ yongs su grags pa kun mkhyen bu ston rin
chen grub dang / sprul sku ri mkhar ba dpal ldan blo gros bzang po dang / thar rtse paNDi ta nam mkha' dpal bzang dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas rgya mtshos mdzad
pa sogs yig cha gsar rnying mthong thos byung ba 'ga' zhig la lag len thig

'debs bgyis pa tsam las 'ga' rer lung brgyud ma thos pa dang / thos pa'i rigs ni gzhung bshad dang bka' 'bum so so'i skabs nas 'byung ba ltar las 'dir smos ma dgos so/ /!/
/bzhi pa gzhan rjes su 'dzin pa'i rig gnas gnyis pa gso ba rig pa'i skor la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u drug dang / bshad pa'i rgyud le'u sum cu so gcig dang / man ngag rgyud la
le'u dgu bcu go gnyis dang / phyi ma rgyud la le'u nyi shu rtsa lnga dang / mjug don yongs su gtad pa le'u gnyis te yongs su dril bas le'u brgya dang lnga bcu nga drug
yod pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs  'di de sngon ma thob kyang slad thob 'gyur dbang gis bris/rgyas sman gyi bla bai DUrYa 'od kyi rgyal po/ 'tsho byed gzhon nu/ sman pa
rgyun shes/ nam so skyes/ thang lha 'bar/ rkang gnyis spyod/ 'gro skyong bu/ me bzhi 'jug lug nagargya skyegs sna/ mda' mchog lan tshwa'i lag pa/ dpal ldan phreng ba/ dpal
ldan phun tshogs/ yid las skyes/ nyi ma'i snying po/ zla ba'i snying po/ zla ba'i 'od zer/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ dpal ldan dpa' bo'am pha khol/ paN chen zla ba mngon dga'/
lo chen bai ro tsa na/ chos rgyal mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan/ gter ston grwa pa mngon shes can/thar rtse pa'i gsan yig tu med/ dge bshes dbus pa dar grags/ 'tsho
byed dkon mchog skyabs/ g.yu thog yon tan mgon po/ sum ston ye shes kun dga'/ sum ston 'bum me/ g.yu thog mgon po rin chen/ phag ston shAkya mgon po/ brang ti dpal ldan
'tsho byed/ brang ti

dpal ldan rgyal mtshan/ brang ti pa kun dga' bzang po/ brang ti stag lha dpal/ brang ti rdo rje dpal bzang / brang ti chos rgyal bkra shis/ brang ti lha rje kun dga' don grub/
dge slong nam mkha' dpal bzang / dbon  'di phan chad slar dpyad dgos/nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ dge slong kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhas grub chen
po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ drung 'tsho ye shes mtshan can/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la bka' drin du stsal to/ /smras pa/ tshul khrims la gnas blo gros
can rnams kyis/ /bslab bya thams cad mkhyen pa'i rgyur 'gyur ba/ /gtsug lag bcu phrag rig pa ston pa'i gzhung / /mthong thos tsam gyis bag chag 'jog tshul byas/ /zhes
dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las thun mong ba phyi rig pa'i gnas kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste gsum pa'o/ /!/
/spyi don gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa nang rig pa'i gnas kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim la gnyis/ sdom pa gsum 'khor dang bcas pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim dang
/ de thams cad kyi rgyab brten du lung gi tshogs thos pa'i brgyud rim/ dang po la/ so sor thar pa'i sdom pa'i chos skor thos pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa'i chos skor
thos pa/ rig 'dzin sngags kyi sdom pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim mo/ /dang po ni lhag par tshul khrims kyi bslab pa ston par byed pa 'dul ba'i sde snod kyi brjod
par bya ba'i gtso bo so sor thar pa ste/ de'i mdo

las/ 'di ni lang tsho'i rnam 'phrul ba'i/ /rkang gnyis gzhon nu'i lcags kyu yin/ /mtsho bas zab pa'i 'khor ba las/ /sgrol ba'i brgal thabs 'di yin te/ /'di ni bzang 'gror 'gro
ba yi/ /nges pa'i chu lon zab pa yin/ /'di ni nyon mongs 'pham byed lam/ /rgyal po yi ni 'dren pa mchog / 'di ni thar pa'i grong 'jug pa'i/ /them skas bzhi dang 'dra
bar gnas/ /zhes dang / bshes pa'i spring yig las kyang / khrims ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i sa bzhin du/ /yon tan kun gyi gzhi rten lags par gsungs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gnas
skabs dang mthar thug gi yon tan la sogs pa dge legs rin po che rin thang gzhal du med pa ma lus pa 'byung ba'i lag 'gro'i dbang po'i bsti gnas su nges pa dang / de bzhin
gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa 'dod dgu 'byung ba'i dpag bsam gyi ljon pa rin po che'i rtsa ba'am gzhi ma ni 'di nyid du bstan pas/ yon tan can kun gyi brten gnas su gyur
pa'i bslab gzhi bsrung ba'i rten can du sgrub par byed pa la/ rang lo cher son pa legs par sbyar ba'i skad du sa ra bha wa ste/ stod 'grel gyi skad du zil gnon zhes dang
/ ljongs 'dir dbang thang dang bstun pa'i ming du me pho rta'i lor sgrol byed kyi lha mo nag pas nya ba'i zhag gi phung po'i mar ngo sngon du 'gro ba'i dmar phyogs kyi
gral tshes dge ba'i nyin/ bdag cag gi 'dren pa dam pa tshad med pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje'i bdag nyid/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya seng ge'i lugs bzang sde snod gsum gyi
brjod par bya ba bslab pa gsum gyis thugs

rgyud yongs su gtams shing mkhas tshul rnam pa gsum gyi lam nas tshul bzhin du legs par 'doms pa la bsnyengs pa mi mnga' ba/ dpal ldan ngag gi dbang phyug chen por yongs su
grags shing grub pa/ don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis pa tshul khrims lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas
la mkhan por zhus shing / gzhung lugs rgya mtshor sbyangs stobs kyi gru gzings chen pos brgal te yon tan nor bu'i gter la dbang 'byor pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje gzhal
du med pa'i bdag nyid can/ chos 'dul smra ba'i dbang phyug dbu mdzad sangs rgyas tshul khrims pas las kyi slob dpon/ bslab pa'i gnas la gus pa 'phags pa rta thul gyi
rnam par thar pa 'dzin cing / gcig tu sems can thams cad la bu gcig pa ltar brtse ba'i bdag nyid can chos rje bstan 'dzin lhun grub pas grib tshod pa/ dad pa'i dge 'dun chos
'dul 'dzin pa shAkya chos 'phel la sogs pa kha bskang bar 'os pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun dang bcas pa'i dbus su tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi sdom pa thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ ston pa thub  phun tshogs lumbi na'i tshal du sku bltams/pa'i dbang po/ shA ri'i  rgyal po'i khab shing thag can du 'khrungs/bu/ sras sgra gcan 'dzin/ grong khyer
ser skyar/bram ze  ra DAr 'khrungs pa'i sa ra ha yin/sgra gcan 'dzin/ 'phags pa lho phyogs be ta'i yul du 'khrungs/ klu sgrub/ gu Na 'dis dbu ma rtsa she la 'grel pa mdzad/
mi tra/ rin chen lam 'bras kyi lo rgyus las dharmA mi trar bshad/ bshes gnyen/ dpal ldan chos  dharma pA la ste zla ba'i grong du 'khrungs pa'i bi rU pa yin/skyong gu
Na

pa ti/ chos kyi phreng ba/ 'byung gnas  dran pa nyer gzhag phyi 'gyur gyi paNDi ta/sbas pa/ paNDi ta chen  kha che khri brtan gyi grong khyer pra ba rar 'khrungs/po shAkya
shrI/ mkhan chen rdo rje  jo gdan/dpal/ mkhan  rgyal ba gser khang pa/chen 'od zer  jo gdan dpal bzang po/snye mo bong ra ba/ mkhan chen  jo gdan/bsod nams dpal/yar 'brog
sbrang mda' ba yin/ mkhan jo gdan/ chen bkra  kha cig 'di 'od zer dpal ba'i sdom phrug rtsibs pa shes mgon gyi sdom drug tu 'dod/shis tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje btsun lha mchog seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge paN
chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ 'dul 'dzin shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun kun dga' legs pa/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun
tshogs/ mkhan po chen po thub dbang bstan pa'i nyin byed thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag la bande tshul
khrims rin chen zhes ming dang bcas te e waM gandho la chen por nyi ma phyed yol gyi dus la bab pa na legs par stsal to/ /de ltar rab tu byung nas nyin zhag gnyis kyis
bskal pa'i gral tshes dge ba'i nyin ga la bar bslab pa ma lus pa legs par klog cing ston pa'i mkhan po chen po kun mkhyen shAkya seng ge'i ring lugs 'dab stong gi dga'
tshal bye ba phrag brgya cig car du 'byed pa'i smra ba'i nyi ma chen po gang yin pa de nyid

dang / las kyi slob dpon dang grib tshod pa mkhan po rin po che'i bkas legs par bskos pa/ gzhung lugs rgya mtsho 'dzin cing chos 'dul smra ba'i dbang phyug chen po gong du
bshad ma thag pa'i 'dren mchog chos kyi rje rnam pa gnyis dang / tshul khrims kyi bslab pa mig gi 'bras bu ltar gces par bsrung zhing mdo sngags chos kyi tshul la mkhyen
dpyod kyi kho lag rdzogs shing / ji bzhin smra ba la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa mchog tu mnga' ba khams ston a mgon bla ma rgyal mtshan pas gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon gyi
khur bzhes/ kha skong dad pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chos 'dul 'dzin pa'i mchog gyur gong du smos ma thag pa rnams dang bcas pa'i dbus su/ ldan phrug pa bdag cag tshigs phyi
ma bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i dge slong gi dngos por bsgrub pa'i sdom pa legs par stsal ba'i brgyud pa ni/ bha ga wAnta thA ga taHarha bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa/ te samyaksaM buddhaHshAkya mu niHArYa sha ri pu traH/ 'phags pa shA ri'i bu/su ta sras sgra gcan 'dzin/ rA
hu laHprA bram ze sgra gcan 'dzin/ hma rA hu laH/ shrI nA  dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub/thArYa nA gArdzu naH/ gu Na yon tan bshes gnyen/ mi tra/rin chen bshes gnyen/ ratna
mi tra/ lakShmI bandharmma pA la/ dpal ldan chos skyong / yon tan bdag po/ gu Na pa tiH/ dharmma chos kyi phreng ba/ mA la/zhi ba'i 'byung gnas sbas pa/ shAntA ka ra
guptaH/mkhas pa chen po shAkya dpal bzang po/ ma hA paNDi ta shAkya shrI bha draH/mkhan chen rdo rje dpal bzang po/ ma ho pa dhyA ya badzra shrI bha draH/ ma ho  mkhan chen
'od zer dpal bzang po/pa dhyA ya rasmi shrI bha draH/ ma ho pa

mkhan chen bsod nams dpal bzang po/dhyA ya puNyA shrI bha draH/ ma ho pa dhyA ya  mkhan chen bkra shis tshul khrims/mangga la shI laH/ pUrbba  shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/dznyA
na dhwa dzaH/ dzi na dwi tI ya  rgyal ba gnyis pa dang sgrol kun dga' bzang po/bhaTTA ra kA nanda bha draH/ pa Tu siddha  mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ka shrI mAM badzra/
pa ri dha ra  yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ratna wardhaH/ bhaTTa ra ka su rotma  rje btsun lha mchog seng ge singhaH/ manydzu  'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge
gho Sha buddha singhaH/ ma hA paNDi ta  paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang /ga ga Na shrI bha draH/ manydzu swa  'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/rA nanda puNya ni rA
bho gaH/ manydzu  'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/nA tha lakShmya gra dhwa dzaH/ ma hA  mkhas grub chen po 'dul 'dzin sangs rgyas phun tshogs/pa Tu siddha bi na ya dha
ra buddha lakShmI/ swA khyA to  legs gsungs chos 'dul smra ba'i dbang phyug mkhan po chen po tshul khrims lhun grub dpal bzang po/dharmma bi na ya wA dI shwa ra ma ho pa
dhyA ya shI la ni rA bho ga shrI bha draH/ te na  des bdag dam pa'i chos kyi skal ba mi dman pa tshul khrims rin chen zhes bgyi ba la yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas
dpal e waM chos ldan gyi dri'i gtsang khang chen por nyi ma shar tsam gyi dus la bab pa na legs par stsal to/ /me saddharmma NA ma hI na su bha gi shI lA ratna nA maM
gu Na ratna syA ka ra sampanna e waM dharmma pa do ma hA gandha ku TI ta tra sUrYo da ya ma tra ya sye dA nIM sampra kA shi tam/ /!/ /kun mkhyen bu ston rin po ches mdzad
pa'i 'dul ba'i las chog rab tu byung ba dang / zhar byung khyim pa la phan gdags pa'i lag len dri ma med pa'i phreng ba'i lung nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bu ston thams cad
mkhyen pa/ slob

dpon bsod nams dpal grub/ mkhas pa nor bzang rin chen/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ stong ra kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ de dbon 'jam
dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ de dbon mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams
pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun chen po bsod nams dbang phyug e waM pa chos 'dul smra ba dpal ldan chos skyong /
des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na bu ston/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ sku zhang grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rje
man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen rab chos rje/ zhwa lu lo tsA ba rin chen chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/
mkhan chen rin chen mkhyen brtse mchog grub/ rmor chen bstan pa'i snang byed kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa
dpal ldan chos skyong bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i
'dul ba'i

las chog gi lung nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang yan kun mkhyen bu ston gyi las chog gi lung brgyud dang 'dra ba las/ de nas shar chen byams pa kun dga'
bkra shis/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa ye shes bzang po/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/
thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /rtsa ba so sor thar pa'i mdo dzi na mi tra dang / ye shes sdes bsgyur ba'i lung
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston mchog thub dbang / 'phags pa  'di la nye ba 'khor byas pa'ang byung /'od srungs/ dgra bcom pa kun dga' bo/ dgra bcom pa sha na'i gos can/ dgra
bcom pa nyer sbas/ dgra bcom pa bha wa nanda/ gsan yig 'ga' zhig tu bha dandaHzhes pa'ang byung /dgra bcom pa me tsa kadagra bcom pa pUrNa ste bdun ni dgra bcom pa/ slob
dpon rta dbyangs/ ku mA ra  gzhon nu rol pa/la Ti/ shrI la  dpal rol pa/Ti/ ha ri  seng ge bzang po/bha dra/ shU ra/ dpa' bo/ba su mi  dbyig bshes/tra/ ba su li  dbyig
len/ste bdun ni rgya gar dbus kyi 'dul 'dzin yin no// 'dus pa bzang po/ sargha bha draH/dbang phyug i shwa ra/ skAndha li/ phung po len/ dge 'dun dbyig saM gha ba su/ pUrNa
mi  gang ba bshes gnyen/tra/ dharma datta/ chos sbyin/buddha de ba/ sangs rgyas lha/dha ra datta  'dzin sbyin/ste brgyad ni kha che'i 'dul 'dzin yin no/ /puNya se nA/
bsod nams sde/saMgha se nA/ dge 'dun sde/puNya nanda/ bsod nams dga' ba/dznyA na

tsandra/ ye shes zla ba/dznyA na se nA/ ye shes sde/a shwa  mya ngan med pa'i 'tsho ba/ka rakShi ta/ sarba  thams cad bsrungs pa/rakShi ta/ dharme  chos kyi mdzod/ka Sha ste
brgyad ni khu sen gyi 'dul 'dzin yin no/ /dharma rakShi ta/ chos kyi bsrungs pa/ka lyA Na rakShi ta/ dge bsrungs/pradznyA rakShi ta/ shes rab bsrungs pa/shrI marga u pa
de sha dpal lam nye bar ston/mokSha  thar pa bsrungs pa/rakShi ta/ ka lyA Na bha dra/ dge ba bzang po/bi dzi ta pra bha wa/ rnam rgyal 'od/saM gha se nA/ dge 'dun sde/shI
la dA sha tshul khrims 'bangs/ya sho  grags pa'i 'bangs/dA shabuddha dA sha sangs rgyas 'bangs/shAkya bha draH/ shAkya bzang po/gu Na yon tan zla ba/ swa maH/ a shwa  mya
ngan med pa'i bshes gnyen/ka mi tra/ shukla mi tra/ dkar po bshes gnyen/shAkya  shAkya bshes gnyen/mi tra ste nyi shu po 'di yu gur gyi 'dul 'dzin yin no/ /shI la mi tra
ni ka ma log gi 'dul 'dzin yin no/ /des sbal ti dgra bcom pa/ skyor mo lung pa bkra shis dpal/ skyor mo lung pa rin chen 'od zer/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan chen
bka' bzhi pa blo gsal/ mkhan chen chos rgyal dpal bzang / paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje grol mchog mkhan chen karma bzang po/ rje shAkya
bstan 'dzin/ shAkya nor bu/ kun dga' legs pa/ bshes gnyen rnam rgyal/ smra dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ drung
chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ shar pa rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag

bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa'i 'dul ba mdo rtsa klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub pa'i dbang
po/ dgra bcom pa nye ba 'khor/ 'phags pa 'od srungs chen po/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ dgra bcom pa sha na'i gos can/ dgra bcom pa nyi sbas/ dgra bcom pa nag po/ dgra bcom
pa dhi dhi kadagra bcom pa legs mthong / phyir 'ong blos mi 'bebs/ slob dpon yon tan 'od/ chos  'di gsan yig ganggA'i chu rgyun min pa gsan yig gzhan 'gar ma byung /kyi
bshes gnyen/ slob dpon shAkya 'od/ paNDi ta seng ge'i gdong pa can/ kha che dzi na mi tra/ paN chen dA na shI la/ lo tsA ba cog ro  ganggA'i chu rgyun na cog ro 'di med
pa'ang byung /klu'i rgyal mtshan/ g.yo dge 'byung bla chen/ mu thu rwa ba dgongs pa rab gsal/gung thang pa/ klu mes tshul khrims byang chub/ gru mer tshul khrims 'byung
gnas/ skyogs shes rab 'byung gnas/ gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ sog  sog chu kha pa/tshul khrims bla ma/ ko khyim pa ye shes bla ma/ nyang mtshams pa rin chen bla ma/ de gsum
char las rgya 'dul ba dbang phyug tshul khrims/ de nas rma tsho byang chub/ yar lung pa'i zur 'chad/bya 'dul ba brtson 'grus 'bar/ chos kyi dbang phyug chos kyi byang
chub/ chos kyi  na bza' 'phred gsol ba/brtson 'grus/ chos  chos dbang nas 'di'i bar zul thu'i mkhan po yin/kyi grags pa/ rin chen dpal bzang / bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon
nu/ mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ thams cad

mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen/ dmar ston rgya mtsho/ rin chen/ byams chen rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas 'phel/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge kong ston
dbang phyug grub pa/ stag phrug kun dga' dpal 'byor/ drung chen thub bstan rnam rgyal/ gling smad rin chen 'byor ldan/ mkhas grub ngag dbang bsod nams rgya mtsho/ mkhan
chen dbang phyug dpal bzang / paN chen ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa bsod nams dngos grub/ mkhan chen ngag dbang don grub/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ rje
sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / chos rje bsam gtan pa/ e waM pa rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis nos
so/ /yang na bya 'dul nas thag ma'i ka ba chen po g.yor po sbal ti dgra bcom pa/ mkhan chen shes rab seng ge bsam yas pa tshul khrims dbang phyug se ba can pa yon tan tshul
khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan bka' bzhi pa blo gsal/ dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen/ dmar ston rgya mtsho rin chen man 'dra/ yang na dmar ston rgya mtsho
rin chen nas/ g.yag ston sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shes bya kun rig kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel man 'dra/ yang na ganggA'i chu rgyun na dmar ston rgya mtsho rin chen nas/
chos rje gzhon nu rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ slob dpon don grub shes rab/ rje lha mchog seng ge shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha'

dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub sogs byung yang rmor chen pa'i gsan yul dang sbrel ma thub/ /!/ /'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po 'phags pa dge 'dun 'bangs kyi slob ma dgra
bcom pa sa ga lhas mdzad pa'i 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa me tog phreng rgyud kha che'i paNDi ta chen po shAkya  paN chen
gsan yig tu pradznyA kIrti'i 'gyur byung /shrI dang khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang / 'od srungs chen po/ kun dga' bo/
sha na'i gos can/ nyer sbas/ dhi dhi kanag po pa/ legs mthong / dge 'dun 'bangs/ dgra bcom pa sa ga lha/ slob dpon  rmor gyi gsan yig na ma Ni ka shrI zhes snang /ma ti
ratna/ kha chen paN chen shAkya shrI/ gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal/ seng ge zil gnon/ rin chen bsod nams seng ge 'um phug gnas rnying pa kun dga' dbang phyug mkhan chen
nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bka' bzhi pa shes rab seng ge bka' bzhi pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon dge ba dpal/ mkhas btsun skal bzang dpal/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/
'jam dbyangs chos rje shes rab rgya mtsho/ chos rje kun dga' dbang phyug slob dpon sangs rgyas dpal grub/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse
paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ rab 'byams phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen
kun dga' lhun

grub/ drung chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ gnas gsar ba kun dga' legs 'byung / chos rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ mkhan chen rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul
khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /sa gsum mnga' bdag 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa'i chos mngon pa kun las btus pa ye shes sdes bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom
ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ rgyal ba ma pham pa/ 'phags pa thogs med/ kha che blo gros brtan pa/ paNDi ta gang ba spel/ ratna a ka ra shAnti/ paNDi ta sa'i rtsa lagapaNDi
ta dA na shI la/ dzi na mi tra/ paNDi ta shI lendra bodhi/ ska ba dpal brtsigs/ cog gru klu'i rgyal mtshan/ zhang  'di la grol mchog gi gsan yig tu mdo sde dpal zhes
snang /ye shes sde ste lo tsA ba ska cog zhang gsum/ de nas nam nad zla ba'i rdo rje/ khu lung dpal gyi rdo rje/ sbas rgyal ba ye shes/ de gsum ga las cog gru rgyal ba ye
shes/ de nas se btsun dbang phyug gzhon nu/ gar mi yon tan g.yung drung / khu ston brtson 'grus g.yung drung / rgya tshul le/ rwa ston khri bzang / li ston chos grags/ brang
ti dar ma snying po/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge shong blo brtan/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ dpang lo blo gros brtan pa/ lo chen byang rtse/
nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ mkhas pa chos dpal mgon po/ gzad pa blo gros rgya mtsho/ mkhas pa don yod dpal ba/ paN chen shAka mchog las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje grol mchog
karma bzang po/ shAkya bstan

'dzin/ shAkya nor bu/ kun dga' legs pa/ bshes gnyen rnam rgyal/ phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ drung chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun
dga' legs 'byung / rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ e waM pa shar chen rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /mkhas mchog dbyig gnyen
gyis mdzad pa'i shes bya gzhi lnga ston pa chos mngon pa mdzod gnas brgyad kyi bdag nyid can paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba'i steng nas
lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ 'phags pa'i gnas brtan 'od srungs chen po/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ dgra bcom pa dbyangs sgrogs/ kha che 'dus
bzang / mkhas mchog dbyig gnyen/ kha che dri med sbas pa/ paNDi ta smr-i ti dznyA na shrI/ mngon pa ba shes rab grags/ rwa zhags zla ba/ mchims zhang btsun/ mchims lha
rje go cha/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge mchims don grub rgyal mtshan/ mchims brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ mchims blo gros brtan pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ mkhas pa yon tan
'od zer/ bshes gnyen chos mgon pa/ skyor mo lung pa blo gros bzang po/ dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen/ dmar ston rgya mtsho rin chen/ 'ga' khang pa bsod nams tshul khrims/
mkhas pa don yod dpal/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje grol mchog mkhan po karma bzang

po/ rje btsun shAkya bstan 'dzin/ shAkya nor bu/ mkhan po kun dga' legs pa/ smra dbang ye shes rnam rgyal/ rab 'byams smra ba phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rje btsun ngag dbang kun
dga' lhun grub/ sangs rgyas bkra shis/ rje gnas gsar ba/ chos rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na dbyig gnyen nas/ mngon pa rang las mkhas pa kha che blo gros brtan pa/ slob dpon gang ba spel/ mkhas pa shAnti pa/ puNya shI la/ rngog
blo ldan shes rab/ mchims lha rje go cha/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge man 'dra/ yang na dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen nas/ rong ston shes bya kun rig gzad pa blo rgyam/
kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rje mi bskyod rdo rje/ dkon mchog yan lagadabang phyug rdo rje/ rin chen chos dbang / sman lung pa blo mchog rdo
rje/ mngon dga' ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ smra dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas dbang sangs rgyas bkra shis/ rje gnas gsar ba/ bsam
gtan phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /smras pa/ nyes med skye rgyu phun tshogs da ltar gyi/
/cho gas tshigs gsum gdams pa rim nos nas/ /gnang bkag bslab pa'i blo mig 'byed pa'i gzhung / /yongs grags bstan bcos mig thur gser ri'i grangs/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos

pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ so sor thar pa'i sdom pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste bzhi pa'o/ // /gnyis pa byang chub sems dpa'i
sdom pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim ni/ blo gros rgya mtshos zhus pa'i mdo las/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dang chos 'dzin dang / /chos sgrub pa dang srog chags snying
brtse ba/ /chos bzhi 'di dag yon tan mtha' med de/ /'di dag mtha' ni rgyal ba mi gsung ngo / /zhes dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa las kyang / byang
chub sems bskyed gyur na skad cig gis/ /'khor ba'i btson rar bsdams pa'i nyam thag rnams/ /bde gshegs rnams kyi sras zhes brjod bya zhing / /'jig rten lha mir bcas pas phyag
byar 'gyur/ /zhes dang / bslab btus las/ sdug bsngal mthar 'byin 'dod pa dang / /bde ba'i mthar yang 'gro 'dod pas/ /dad pa'i rtsa ba brtan bya ste/ /byang chub la ni
blo brtan bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar rang gzhan thams cad srid zhi'i pha rol du son pa'i mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa don du gnyer ba'i blo gros can rnams kyis/ gnas
skabs su lha mi'i go 'phang tsam mam rang don du zhi bde'i mya ngan las 'das pa lhur byed pa'i bsam sbyor thams cad las rgyang bsrings te/ rgyal ba'i myu gu rnams kyi 'jug
sgo chen po 'dir 'jug pa la shin tu 'bad dgos te/ ci'i phyir na/ thub pa'i dgongs pa rab tu gsal ba las/ phan bde'i 'byung gnas rdzogs pa yi/ /sangs rgyas rgyal ba'i
sras las 'khrungs/

/ rgyal sras stong nyid snying rje yi/ /bdag nyid byang chub sems las 'khrungs/ /zhes sogs rgya cher 'byung ba ltar dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bgrod pa gcig
pa'i lam theg pa chen po'i mdo sde zab mo thams cad kyi brjod bya'i snying po/ rgyal ba'i gdung 'tshob byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi 'byung gnas srid zhi'i mtha'
la mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i grong khyer du bgrod pa'i them skas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub kyi mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga ste de la lugs srol gnyis las/
sdong po bkod pa'i mdo dang / nam mkha'i snying pos zhus pa la sogs pa'i rjes su 'brangs nas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis gsungs/ slob dpon chen po klu sgrub nas brgyud pa/
rgyal sras zhi ba lha'i bstan bcos las 'byung ba ltar rgyal ba'i sras po thogs med bzang po dpal gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ston pa bla na med pa thub pa'i dbang po/ a nutta ra mu nindraH/rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs/ bhaTTA ra ka manydzu shrI swa raH/dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub/
shrI nA thArYa nA gArdzu naH/slob dpon 'phags pa lha/ A tsArYA rYa de waH/slob dpon zla ba grags pa/ A tsArYa tsandra kIrtiH/paN chen slob pa'i rdo rje/ ma hA paNDi ta
shiShya badzra/slob dpon dgra las rgyal ba/ A tsArYa dze tA riH/rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ ma hA badzra sa naHa sho ka shrI/chung ba don yod rdo rje/
apanyA mo gha badzra/paN chen bsod nams dpal/ ma hA pa Tu puNya shrIH/ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ wa ri lo tsA ratna kIrti/rje sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/
ArYa ma hA bhU mi paNDa gA nanda garbhaH/slob

dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ A tsArYa puNya graH/rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bhaTTA ra kIrti dhwa dzaH/chos kyi rgyal po sa skya'i mkhas pa chen po/ dharma sya rA dza bhU mi
paNDa ra ma hA paNDi ta/'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan/ ArYa ratna ma ti dhwa dzaH/'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/ mr-i du swa ra khonde shi kaH/byang sems rin chen
mgon/ bo dhi satwa ratna nA tha/rgyal ba'i sras po thogs med bzang po dpal/ dzi na su to྅ saM ga bha dra shrIH/sems dpa' chen po tshul khrims dpal/ ma hA satwa shI la shrI/gzhon
nu rgyal mchog ku mA ra dzi notta ma/'phags sde dpal ldan grags pa/ ArYa se na shrI mAM ya shaH/mkhan chen grags pa rgya mtsho/ ma ho pa dhyA ya ya shassa mu dra/mkhan
chen rin chen grags pa/ ma ho pa dhyA ya ratna kIrtiH/mkhan chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ma ho pa dhyA buddha mangga laM/mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal bzang / ma ho
pa dhyA ye shwa ra shrI bha draH/mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ ma ho pa dhyA ya wa gI sha dharmma ya shaH/mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bkra shis/ ma ho pa dhyA ya mai
tri puNya mangga laM/ sa skya'i lha khang chen mo'i/grub chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ ma hA siddha buddha sA ga ra/ngor mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/
ngorma ho pa dhyA ya manydzu gho Sha buddha lakShmI/byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag theg pa chen po'i rigs kyi skal ba dang ldan
pa btsun pa tshul khrims rin chen la thugs brtse ba chen pos legs par bka' stsal to/ / bo dhi satwa ma hA satwa mangga la bha draH/ te nAtma ka ma hA yA na ku la sya bha
ga bAM bande shrI la ra rnatnaM tsitta ma hA dA yen swA khyA ta/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ sgro mon can pa rin chen dpal bzang / byang sems rin chen mgon po man
'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ bo dong brtson

'grus rdo rje/ khro phu bsod nams seng ge kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che/ rgyal sras thogs med man 'dra'o/ /!/ /byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod la sogs pa mdo sde'i rjes su 'brangs
nas/ 'phags pa mi pham mgon pos gsungs/ 'phags pa thogs med nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon chen po tsandra go mi'i lugs srol/ rgyal ba'i sras po thogs med bzang po dpal
gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas sems tsam lugs kyi sems bskyed thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun ma pham pa/ 'phags pa thogs med/ slob
dpon dbyig gnyen/ 'phags pa grol sde/ btsun pa grol sde/ mchog gi sde/ dul ba'i sde/ seng ge bzang po/ ku sa li che chung gnyis/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ dpal mar
me mdzad/ rgyal ba 'brom ston pa/ spyan snga ba tshul khrims 'bar/ bya yul ba/ rgyal sras  mun sman pa'ang zer/char chen pa/ gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ sangs rgyas sgom
pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims ston/ mkhan chen seng ge skyabs/ mkhas btsun bsod nams ye shes/ byang sems bsod nams grags pa/ thogs med bzang po dpal/ grub chen buddha shrI/
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ mkhan chen ratna shI la/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
'khor lo'i mgon po dbang phyug rab brtan/ 'jam dpal dbyangs ngag dbang chos grags/ sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bsod

nams/ 'di man brgyud pa slar brtag de sras ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug lha khang mkhan chen don grub legs bzang yin nam/ mkhas btsun kun dga' sangs rgyas/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs
sangs rgyas dpal bzang / thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rgyal sras thogs med pa nas/ lo chen byang
chub rtse mo/ lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bo dong paN chen dbyangs can dga' ba/ mkhan chen bsod rgyal/ paN chen shAka mchog paN chen don yod pa/ rje kun dga' grol mchog
mkhan chen karma bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man gong bzhin no/ /!/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sbas don mngon par rtogs pa'i don ma nor bar
gsal bar ston pa rgyal tshab mi pham mgon pos mdzad pa'i bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa paNDi ta go mi 'chi med dang lo tsA ba blo ldan shes
rab kyis bsgyur ba'i steng nas lung nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang zas gtsang sras po/ rje btsun byams pa mgon po/ 'phags pa thogs med/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen/ 'phags
pa rnam grol sde/ btsun pa rnam grol sde/ mchog gi sde/ dul ba'i sde/ mkhan po rnam par snang mdzad/ slob dpon seng ge bzang po/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ slob
dpon yon tan bshes gnyen/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ shar phyogs pa zla ba bzang po/'bum phrag gsum pa'ang zer/ slob dpon bstan skyong / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab/ 'bre

shes rab 'bar/ ar byang chub ye shes/mtshan dngos gzhon nu tshul khrims/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa dkar mo/shes rab 'bum/ dkar chung ring mo/byang chub 'bum/ zhang ye ba/ gnyal zhig
'jam dpal rdo rje/ gzad ring dar ma tshul khrims/ bo dong pa brtson 'grus rdo rje/ khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge lha ston grub pa seng ge tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon/
thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston/ de las thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal dang mkhas pa lung mang po gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma/ rong ston
shes bya kun rig mkhas pa don yod dpal/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ paN chen nam
mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ chos rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ dol chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
lhun grub/ bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhas grub sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen
la'o/ /!/ /yang phar phyin rnying ma 'brom lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon seng ge bzang po nas/ ku sa li che ba/ ku sa li chung ba/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ jo
bo chen po dpal mar me mdzad/ 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ 'brom ston btsan nam mgo bla ma/ 'bre chen shes rab 'bar man 'dra/ yang khu lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ jo
bo rje

nas/ khu chen po lha sdings pa/ rgya rgyal ba tshul khrims seng ge li ston chos grags/ 'bre chen po man 'dra'o/ /!/ /dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dbu ma rtsa
ba shes rab kyi tshig le'ur byas pa paNDi ta ka na ka dang pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/
ArYa de wa/ slob dpon sangs rgyas bskyangs/ dpal ldan zla ba grags pa/ paNDi ta rig pa'i khu byug kha che gzhon nu 'bum/ ha su ma ti/ paNDi ta gser gyi go cha/ pa tshab
lo tsA ba nyi ma grags/ rma bya byang chub ye shes/ rma bya byang chub brtson 'grus/ mtshur gzhon nu seng ge rma bya shAkya seng ge zhang chos kyi bla ma/ sangs rgyas sgom
pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ bcom ldan ral gri/ de gnyis ka las lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ sgra tshad pa rin chen
rnam rgyal/ g.yag sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shes bya kun rig mkhas pa don yod dpal/ paN chen shAka mchog las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje grol mchog bya btang kun dga'
mchog ldan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ dol ba mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ smra dbang
phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ drung chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ rje gnas gsar ba/ chos rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ e waM pa shar chen
rin

chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rje grol mchog nas/ karma bzang po/ shAkya bstan 'dzin/ shAkya nor bu/ kun dga' legs pa/ bshes
gnyen rnam rgyal/ chos rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ dol pa phyogs las rnam rgyal man 'dra/ yang na pa tshab lo tsA ba nas/ thang sag pa ye shes 'byung gnas/ 'brom dbang phyug
grags/ shes rab rdo rje/ ston tshul ba/ bde ba'i lha/ jo btsun pa/ dbu ra ba shes rab dpal/ dharmA shes rab/ shes rab rin chen/ puNya singha/ bag ston bsam bzang / bag
ston gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ rong ston man 'dra'o/ /!/ /'phags pa yab sras gnyis kyi bzhed pa phyin ci ma log par ston pa slob dpon chen po dpal ldan zla ba grags pas mdzad
pa'i dbu ma la 'jug pa pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub pa'i dbang po/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon 'phags pa lha/ slob
dpon sangs rgyas bskyangs/ dpal ldan zla ba grags pa/ kha che gzhon nu 'bum/ paNDi ta gser gyi go cha/ pa tshab lo tsA ba nyi ma grags/ zhang thang sag pa ye shes 'byung
gnas/ 'brom dbang phyug grags/ bla ma shes rab rdo rje/ slob dpon ston tshul ba/ bla ma bde ba'i lha/ jo btsun pa/ dbu ra ba/ shes rab dpal/ dharmA shes rab/ bag ston
shes rab rin chen/ rje bsod nams seng ge bag ston bsam gtan bzang po/ dmar ston gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ rong ston shes bya kun rig don yod dpal ba/ paN chen shAkya mchog
ldan/ rje btsun 131grol mchog pa/ ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ gnas gsar ba mgon po bsod nams mchog
ldan/ mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ smra dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ drung chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga'
legs 'byung / chos rje bsam gtan phun tshogs/ shar chen rin mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan pa/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /!/ /'phags pa lhas mdzad pa'i byang
chub sems dpa'i rnal 'byor spyod pa bzhi brgya la pa tshab lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub dbang / dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub/
slob dpon 'phags pa lha/ paNDi ta zla ba grags pa/ paNDi ta gser gyi go cha/ pa tshab nyi ma grags/ khu mdo sde 'bar/ rma bya byang chub brtson 'grus/ mtshur gzhon nu
seng ge rma bya shAkya seng ge zhang chos kyi bla ma/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyo smon lam tshul khrims/ dbu ma pa byang chub grub/
dbang phyug grags/'di'i mtshan btsal/ mkhan bsod nams mtshan can/ rje grags pa rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ karma dkon mchog gzhon nu/ rong ston thams cad mkhyen
pa/ bla ma don yod dpal/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ thar rtse paN chen/ sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/
bka' 'gyur ba

chen po/ mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ drung chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ rje gnas gsar ba/ chos rje bsam gtan
phun tshogs/ kun mkhyen rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /'phags pa byams pas mdzad pa'i theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan paNDi ta
shAkya singha dang lo tsA ba dpal dang slad kyis lo chen blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang / byams mgon/ 'phags pa thogs med/ dbyig
gnyen/ kha che blo gros brtan pa/ slob dpon gang ba spel/ shAnti pa/ dznyA na shrI/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che sadzdza na/ pa ra he ta/ rngog blo ldan shes rab/
gnyal ba chos blo/ phywa pa chos kyi seng ge gtsang nag pa brtson 'grus seng ge dpal ldan gro mo che/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyi ston shAka
'bum/ skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol po/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab
rgya mtsho/ 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog seng ge shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhan chen dpal ldan don grub/ mgon po bsod
nams mchog ldan/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang
phyug mkhas grub

chen po sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na pa ra hi ta nas/ blo gros grags pa/ mar pa jo 'phan/ mchims ston don grub/ mchims brtson
seng man 'dra'o/ /!/ /yang mdo sde rgyan dang dbus mtha' rnam 'byed chos nyid rnam 'byed ye shes sde'i 'gyur gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ byams pa mgon po/
'phags pa thogs med/ mkhas pa dbyig gnyen/ kha che blo gros brtan pa/ paN chen rig pa'i khu byug daMShTra se na/ mche ba'i sde/bha dra pA da/ bzang po'i zhabs/mar me mdzad/
ganggA dha ra/ puNya shrI/ kha che dgon pa ba/ bram ze sanggha pa/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ rngog lo tsA ba chen po/ ba reg lo tsA ba rgyal mtshan/ ba reg ston skyabs/
skyes bu yon tan dga'/ bla ma bkra shis rdo rje/ sdong khrod 'dul 'dzin/ nyang ro kun dga' rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs dar ma 'od zer/ khro phu tshad ma'i skyes bu/ bu ston thams
cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ g.yag sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan/ don yod dpal/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ las chen ye shes lhun grub/ rje
grol mchog bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang man gong gi mngon rtogs rgyan dang mdo sde rgyan gnyis dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /theg pa chen po'i rgyud
phyi ma de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po ston par byed pa'i mdo zab mo rnams kyis dgongs pa 'grel pa rgyud bla ma'i tshig le'ur byas pa mi pham mgon gyis mdzad pa paNDi ta
sadzdza na dang lo tsA ba

blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba dang / chos dang chos nyid rnam par 'byed pa zha ma seng rgyal gyis bsgyur ba de gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/
byams pa mgon po/ mnga' bdag mai tri pa/ paNDi ta dga' ba'i grags pa/ sadzdza na/ rngog lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab/ khyung rin chen grags/ rgya dmar ba byang chub grags/
gro lung ba blo gros 'byung gnas/ phywa pa chos kyi seng ge 'dul dkar ba/ gtsang pa 'gre sgur/ sdong khrod 'dul 'dzin/ slob dpon dar ma 'od zer/ lho pa gru pa seng ge slob
dpon rig thigs pa/ bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ kun mkhyen g.yag pa/ rong ston shes bya kun rig don yod dpal/ rje shAkya mchog ldan/ rje grol mchog
kun dga' mchog ldan/ brang ti paN chen/ rje dpal ldan don grub/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun
dga' lhun grub/ bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul
khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na byams pa'i chos sde lnga ga'i lung gi brgyud pa bsod nams dbang phyug yan 'dra/ de nas mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul
khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /!/ /A tsArYa shAnta de was mdzad pa'i bslab pa kun las btus pa ye shes sde'i 'gyur la rngog los 'gyur bcos mdzad pa'i steng nas lung thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan

'das thub pa'i dbang po/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ A tsArYa shAnta de wa pa da/ slob dpon e la dha ri/ mi brjed gzungs thob/ dpa' bo'i sde zer/ slob dpon shu raM ga se na/ ku sa li
che ba rin chen bzang po/ thar rtse paN chen gyi gsan yig na 'di gnyis ma byung ba dgos sam mi dgos brtag chung ba rin chen 'od/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ jo bo
dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na/ 'brom chos kyi rgyal po/ po to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan grags/ chos lung pa shes rab grags/ gtum ston blo gros grags/ gro ston bdud
rtsi grags/ zhang btsun rdo rje 'od/ zhang chos kyi bla ma/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/thar rtse ba'i gsan yig tu gro ston gyi rjes su mchims byas nas bar gyi bla
ma gsum med pa zhig byung / mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyo ston smon lam tshul khrims/ bcom ldan rig pa'i ral gri/ skyi stod shAka 'bum/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/
dol po kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ dwags po phyogs las rnam rgyal/skyed tshal 'og mkhan po/ mkhas pa lha dbang blo gros/ rab 'byams dpal
ldan don grub/ kun bzang rtse pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ dpal 'byor gling pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ nor rgyas gling pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ don grub chos gling pa bstan
pa dar rgyas/ dol po smra ba'i seng ge phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun

dga' lhun grub/ de las bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang / skyor mda' ba bsod nams dbang phyug gnyis kyis gsan nam/ de nas mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des
bdag la'o/ /!/ /rgyal ba'i sras po zhi ba lhas mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa le'u bcu pa shlau ka stong phrag gcig gi bdag nyid can 'gyur mang du yod
pa las lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bcos pa'i steng nas lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston mchog shAkya'i rgyal po/ mgon po 'jam dpal dbyangs/ rgyal sras shAnta de
wa/ mi brjed gzungs thob paNDi ta e la dha ri/ grub chen dze tA ri/ zla ba grags pa chung ba/ tsandra kIrti ki tsu zhes legs sbyar skad du'o// jo bo puNya shrI/ bal po ka
na ka pa/ paNDi ta su ma ti kIrti/ rngog lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab/ gro lung pa blo gros 'byung gnas/ cha pa chos kyi seng ge slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje
btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgya mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/
kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ lha mchog seng ge shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang dpal ldan don
grub/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rab 'byams

chos rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ smra ba'i dbang phyug phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen ngag gi dbang phyug kun dga' lhun grub/ rab 'byams sangs rgyas bkra shis/ rje btsun gnas
gsar pa chen po/ chos rje bsam gtan pa/ mkhan chen rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na mi brjed gzungs thob e la dha ri
nas/dpa' bo'i sde/ shu raM ga se na/gser gling pa/ dharma kIrti/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha/ 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ po to ba rin chen gsal sha ra ba yan tan grags/
gtum ston blo gros grags/ gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ ze'u dgra bcom pa man 'dra/ yang na dpal ldan gro nas mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyi ston shAka 'bum/ skyi ston 'jam
dbyangs/ kun mkhyen dol po pa/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa

gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na rngog lo blo ldan shes rab/ zhang tshe spang ba chos kyi bla ma/ nyang bran pa chos kyi seng ge gtsang nag pa
brtson 'grus seng ge dpal ldan gro mo che/ kun mkhyen mchims/ ze'u dgra bcom pa/ mkhan chen grags pa shes rab/ mchims blo bzang grags pa/ gro ston kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ ratna wardha man 'dra/ yang na dpal ldan gro nas/ mchims chen nam mkha' grags/ skyi ston shAka 'bum/grags rgyala'ang
zer/ skyi ston 'jam dbyangs/ kun mkhyen dol po pa/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems
dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rin/ gnyug la  rje btsun ngag dbang grags pa dpal yang zer/paN chen ngag dbang grags pa sogs so/ /yang na rngog
lo nas/ khyung rin chen grags/ stod lung rgya dmar ba/ cha pa chos kyi seng ge 'dzad pa ston skyabs/ mus srad pa chen po/ gtsang po ba bsod nams mdzes/ mkhan po byang chub
dpal man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ gnyug la  rje btsun ngag dbang grags pa dpal yang zer/paN chen ngag dbang grags pa
sogs so/ /yang na rgyal sras zhi ba lha nas/ thams cad rtsegs/ shAkya ma ti/ gu Na puNya/ su ma ti kIrti/ rngog man 'dra'o/ /yang mkhan chen kun dga' tshul khrims nas yar
la gong du smos pa'i bla ma brgyud pa rnams dang ma 'brel bar du bla ma kha cig btsal dgos/ mkhan chen kun dga' tshul khrims nas/ chos rje buddha shrI bha dra/ mkhas grub
sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bka' drin zla bral 'jam dbyangs bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la legs par stsal to/ /!/ /chos kyi rgyal po sa skya paNDi
tas mdzad pa'i rgyal sras lam bzang thub pa'i dgongs pa rab tu gsal ba dang / sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi'i nges gsang bstan bcos sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye
ba gnyis ka'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza'

brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon 'dul 'dzin/ chos rje byang seng ba/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal
tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang po/
byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos rje don grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang / des
bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sdom gsum rab dbye kho na'i brgyud pa ni dpal mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen
pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ mtshungs med nam mkha' sangs rgyas man 'dra'o/ /!/ /sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas kyi sgyu 'phrul rol pa jo bo dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na
la shing rta chen po gnyis kyi gdams pa ma lus pa mnga' ba'i bstan bcos mtha' klas na'ang de'i nang nas/ thogs med sku mched kyi dgongs pa phyin ci ma log pa lta spyod ston
pa sa rgyan gnyis/ klu sgrub yab sras kyi dgongs pa phyin ci ma log pa'i lta spyod rdzogs par ston pa bslab spyod gnyis/ de thams cad kyi yan lag 'chad pa skyes rabs

dang / brjod bya sna tshogs pa ston pas nye bar mkho ba ched du brjod pa'i tshoms gnyis te bka' gdams gzhung drug tu grags pa las byang sa dang mdo sde rgyan gnyis kyi phyi
ma'i brgyud pa gong grags chen bco brgyad du song ba ltar dang / 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sa ye shes sde dang klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur
ba bam po nyi shu rtsa gsum gyi bdag nyid can gyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub pa'i dbang po/ rgyal tshab mi pham mgon/ sa gsum mnga' bdag 'phags pa thogs
med/ sangs rgyas gnyis pa dbyig gnyen/ kha che blo gros brtan pa/ jo bo puNya shrI dhA/ gang ba spel/lo paN gsan yig na 'di gnyis bzhugs kyang mkhyen brtse'i der mi bzhugs
pas brtag ganggA dha ra/ ganggA dzi na ratna/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che sadzdza na/ paNDi ta sa ra he ta/ 'di lo pa'i gsan yig tu btsan kha bo che dang gcig
par mdzad 'dug par dpyad/bla ma blo gros grags pa/ mar pa jo 'phan/ mchims ston don grub/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyi ston shAkya 'bum/ skyi
ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol po/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ de dbon gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ mkhan chen
dkon mchog tshul khrims/ thar lam gsal sgron/ lo pa'i gsan yig na 'di bzhin byung ba tshoms sogs kyi brgyud par dkon mchog tshul khrims dang ratna A ka ra'i bar du bla
ma gzhan mi 'dug cing bla ma'i mtshan mi 'dra bas dpyad/mkhan chen ratna A ka ra/ gnyug la ngag dbang grags pa/ lo pa spyan snga ngag dbang chos

grags/ rje btsun bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ shar chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rtse thang drung chen dpal 'byor bsod nams lhun grub/ pha bong kha pa dpal 'byor
lhun grub/ zur chen chos dbyings rang grol/ kun mkhyen thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ zhwa lu mkhan chen gnas gsar ba 'jam dbyangs bstan
'dzin/ rje phun tshogs legs 'byor/ bka' 'gyur ba chen po ngag dbang rab brtan/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/
dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ sku dbon dam pa rin po che chos grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /'di kha cig mdo sde rgyan sger rkyang
gi brgyud par mdzad pa yod kyang lo phyogs kyi gsan yig tu sa rgyan gnyis thun mong gi brgyud par mdzad 'dug pa 'brel che ba'i nang du btang ba yin la/ yang mdo sde rgyan
sger rkyang gi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ kha che blo brtan nas/ rig pa'i khu byug mche ba'i sde/ bzang po'i zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ ganggA dha ra/ puNya shrI/ kha che dgon pa ba/
bram ze sangga / kha che ye shes dpal/ rngog lo tsA ba/ ba reg lo tsA ba rgyal mtshan/ ba reg ston skyabs/ skyes bu yon tan dga'/ bkra shis rdo rje/ sdong khrod 'dul 'dzin/
nyang ro kun dga' rdo rje/ dar ma 'od zer/ tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon/ bu ston rin chen grub/ nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ red mda' ba gzhon nu blo gros/ rje btsun
btsong kha pa chen

po/ rgyal tshab rje/ gung ru rin byang / gnyal ston pa/ chos dpal rgyal mtshan/ nyi ma grags pa/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ ra tshag pa blo bzang e waM/ rgyal khang rtse pa/ rje
pha bong kha pa man 'dra'o/ /byang sa'i brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ de bzhin gshegs pa thub dbang / byams mgon/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ kha che blo brtan/ gang ba spel/ de las
dzi na mi tra/ dA na shI la/kun mkhyen bu dang mkhan ngag chos pa sogs kyi gsan yig na dzi na mi tra nas grus rgyal ba ye shes kyi bar rnams rim pa bzhin du gnang ba las
sdebs su gsan pa'i gsal kha ma byung yang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang ba nye brgyud ring brgyud kyi khyad yin nam/ indra bhU ti gsum gyis gsan/
de gsum ka las ska ba dpal brtsegs/ cog gru klu'i rgyal mtshan/ zhang ye shes sde gsum gyis gsan/ de gsum las lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje/ nam nad zla ba'i rdo rje/ dbas
rgyal ba ye shes gsum gyis gsan/ de gsum las grus rgyal ba ye shes kyis gsan/ de nas grub mchog gi ye shes/ se btsun dbang phyug gzhon nu/ mgar mi yon tan g.yung drung
/ khu ston brtson 'grus g.yung drung / ra khri bzang 'od/ rgya rgyal tshul/ li ston chos grags/ de gnyis las brang ti dar ma snying po dang / ko ye 'byung gnyis kyis gsan/
de gnyis ka las rog chos brtson/ de nas mchims brtson seng / mchims don ne/ mchims blo brtan/ zhang ston bsod nams rin chen/ bo dong rin rtse/ stag sde ba seng ge rgyal
mtshan/ drang lung ba thugs rje shes rab/ rin chen ye shes/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ rgya ma ba yon

tan 'od/ chos rje bsod nams blo gros/ bka' bcu pa dar ma bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje man gong dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /gnyis pa bslab
spyod gnyis kyi dang po A tsarYa shAndha de was mdzad pa'i bslab pa kun las btus pa ye shes sde'i 'gyur la rngog los 'gyur bcos mdzad pa'i steng nas lung thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ A tsArYa shAnta de wa pA da/ slob dpon e mi brjed gzungs thob/ la dha ri/ slob dpa' bo'i sde zer/ dpon shu raM
ga se na/ ku sa li che ba rin chen bzang po/ thar rtse paN chen gyi gsan yig na 'di gnyis ma byung ba dgos sam mi dgos brtag chung ba rin chen 'od/ gser gling pa chos
kyi grags pa/ jo bo dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na/ 'brom chos kyi rgyal po/ po to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan grags/ chos lung pa shes rab grags/ gtum ston blo gros
grags/ gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ zhang btsun rdo rje 'od/ zhang chos kyi bla ma/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/thar rtse pa'i gsan yig tu gro ston gyi rjes su mchims
byas nas bar gyi bla ma gsum med pa zhig byung / mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyo ston smon lam tshul khrims/ bcom ldan rig pa'i ral gri/ skyi ston shAka 'bum/ skyi ston grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ dol po kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus
chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng

gemus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ dwags po phyogs las  rje phrin las pa/rnam rgyal/ mkhas pa  skyed tshal 'og mkhan po/lha dbang blo gros/ rab 'byams dpal ldan don grub/ kun
bzang rtse pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ dpal 'byor gling pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ nor rgyas gling pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ don grub chos gling pa bstan pa dar rgyas/ dol
po smra ba'i seng ge phyogs las rnam rgyal/ des ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ rje btsun sangs rgyas bkra shis/ gnas gsar pa ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / sa skya pa
ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ sku dbon rin po che chos grub/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /spyod 'jug gi brgyud pa gong grags chen bco brgyad kyi skabs
su gsal ba ltar ro/ /!/ /gsum pa skyes tshoms gnyis kyi dang po slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa'i skyes rabs so bzhi pa lo tsA ba manydzu shrI warmas bsgyur ba'i lung thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rnam 'dren zas gtsang sras po/ mgon po 'jam dpal dbyangs/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ mkhas mchog dpa' bo/ mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ gser gling pa/ jo bo chen
po/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ rgya zur khang pa/ kha mo zi'u pa/ gtsang nag pa/ gro mo che pa/ sangs rgyas sgom pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/
bcom ldan ral gri/ skyi ston shAka 'bum/ skyi ston 'jam dbyangs/ kun mkhyen dol po/ sa bzang ma ti/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / rgyal ba mus pa/ mkhyen

rab rje/ stong rwa ba shAkya don grub/ de dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba chen po byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ grub chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin
bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ rje btsun sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ dpal sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ sku dbon rin po che chos grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang brgyud lugs gcig ni mkhas mchog dpa' bo nas/ 'jam dpal
grags pa/ shAnti pa/ se'u ri pa/ 'jigs med grags pa/ dge 'byung sbas pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che 'bring chung gsum/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ puNya shrI/ steng pa lo tsA ba/ so
'dzam gling rgyan/ lho pa kun mkhyen/ bla ma rgya/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje/ sngags 'chang g.yung ston rdo rje dpal/ rje rol pa'i rdo rje/ lho rin po che grags pa yon
tan/ chos rje grags pa 'byung gnas/ mi pham gnyis pa tshul khrims dar/ spyan snga bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan man sa rgyan thun
mong gi brgyud pa dang gcig yang na slob dpon dpa' bo nas legs ldan 'byed/ zla ba grags pa/ rig pa'i khu byug ku mA ra lakSha/ ha su ma ti/ dza ya A nanda/ khu lo tsA
ba/ legs ldan pa/ gtsang nag pa/ gshen chu skor ba/ gtsang pa jo nag pa/ 'od zer mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs shAkya gzhon nu/ rje rang byung rdo rje man

'dra'o/ /!/ /'di sngar ma thob kyang bka' gdam gzhung drug kha tshang ba'i phyir slar zhu ba'i rtsis su bris/ dgra bcom pa chos skyob kyis bsdus pa'i ched du brjod pa'i tshoms
dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ dgra bcom pa rakShi ta/ dgra bcom pa chos skyob/
dgra bcom pa kr-iShNa'i gos can/ dgra bcom pa sha na'i gos can/ dgra bcom pa nyi ma gung pa/ rgyal rigs thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen/ 'phags mchog klu sgrub zhabs/ slob
dpon ArYa de wa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pa/ ratna A ka ra shAnti/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba/ bar pa/ chung ba/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ dpyal chos kyi bzang po/ dpyal padmo
can/ mkhan po gzhon nu ye shes/ rong pa shes rab seng ge bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma dharma kIrti/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ stong ra ba shAkya don grub/ de dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo
tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub bkra shis bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas man chad gong gi skyes rabs so bzhi pa'i brgyud pa dang 'dra'am
snyam mo/ /'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i mdo

kun las btus pa ye shes sdes bsgyur ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni dbu ma rtsa ba'i shes rab dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /'di de sngon ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyis bris/ 'jig rten
dbang phyug bzang po dpal gyis mdzad pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid yig gi steng nas theg pa chen po'i blo sbyong nyams khrid du legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston
pa thub pa'i dbang po/ rgyal tshab byams pa/ 'phags pa thogs med/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen/ 'phags pa rnam grol sde/ btsun pa rnam grol sde/ paNDi ta gu Na mi tra/ slob dpon
seng ge bzang po/ bshes gnyen gang ba spel/ ku sA li che chung gnyis/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti shargyal ba 'brom/ po to ba rin chen gsal/
sha ra ba yon tan grags/ 'chad ka ba ye shes rdo rje/ se spyil bu ba chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi grags zhes pa'ang byung ba brtag lha spyil bu ba  lha chen po dbang
phyug gzhon nu'am dbang phyug rin po che/ lha lung gi dbang phyug ces grags pa dang 'di gnyis mi gcig pas ma nor dgos/'od zer bla ma/ 'di la ganggA'i chu rgyun du jo bo'i
chos 'byung na byang chub 'od zer dang lo pa spyan snga'i gsan yig na skyes mchog lha chen zer ba snang gsungs/lha sdings pa byang chub 'bum/ lo pa spyan snga pa'i gsan
yig na shes rab 'bum zhes 'dug gsungs/lha sdings dbon po kun dga' rgya mtsho/ thar rtse pa dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse ngag chos gsum gyi gsan yig na 'di gnyis lha sdings
pa yon tan dpal zhes gcig tu bgrangs 'dug kyang ngor chen dang lo pa spyan snga sgrub khang pa gsum gyi gsan yig na 'di bzhin byung bas bla ma gnyis kyi mtshan gcig
tu 'dus pa'i bris nor byung ngam snyam/ tshogs pa'i dbu mdzad

yon tan dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ byang sems bsod nams grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal/ rgya ma ba yon tan 'od/
'phags pa blo 'phel ba/ spyan snga tshul khrims dar ma/ spyan snga bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ rgyal sras bsod nams legs mchog paN chen ngag dbang grags pa dpal bzang / gnyug
la paN chen/spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/
rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa dpal
ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rgyal sras thogs med nas/ mang mkhar ba tshul khrims dpal/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog
sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos rje byams pa chos legs/ mkhan chen rdo rje rin chen/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/
'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang
na slob dpon dbyig gnyen nas/ kha che blo gros brtan pa/ ku sA li che chung gnyis man 'dra/ yang na rgyal sras thogs med dpal nas/ gnyags dbon

bsod nams bzang po/ mtshan ldan zhig mo rang grol/ kun dga' dpal mo/ rje ngag dbang grags pa dpal bzang / lo pa ngag dbang chos grags man 'dra/ yang na rgyal sras rin po che
nas/ mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen grags pa bshes gnyen/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal ba phyag na/ mkhan chen kun blo ba/ gnyug la
paN chen ngag gi dbang po/ ngag dbang chos grags man 'dra/ yang na rgyal sras rin po che nas/ mang mkhar tshul khrims dpal/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog mus chen
sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gung ru shes rab bzang po/ gnyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags man 'dra/ yang na sems dpa'
chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog nas/ ri pa dpal ldan grags/ mkhan chen grags pa rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen grags pa/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas bkra shis/ mkhan chen dbang
phyug dpal bzang / paN chen ngag dbang chos grags/ dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug rmor chen
ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na lo pa spyan snga ngag dbang chos
grags nas/ bla ma dpal ldan chos 'byor/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams man

'dra/ yang na sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ byams chen rab 'byams pa/ kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' chos bzang / mkhas pa lha dbang blo
gros/ rje byams pa phun tshogs/ 'bum mo che pa dpal 'byor shes rab/ ngor sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub man 'dra/ yang na rgyal sras thogs med dpal nas/ grub chen buddha
shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /!/ /rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal gyi dngos slob rje dpal ldan ye
shes kyis mdzad pa'i blo sbyong snyan brgyud chen mo'am/ blo sbyong gsung sgros mar grags pa'i lo rgyus gdams pa dngos dang bcas pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal
ba'i sras po thogs med dpal nas/ 'gro mgon dpal ldan ye shes/ gzhon nu rgyal mchog mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gung ston shes rab bzang po/ gnyug la ngag dbang grags
pa/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun
grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /'di
de sngon ma thob blar thob 'gyur gyis bris/ sum pa lo tsA ba dpal mchog dang po'i rdo rjes rgya gar du byon dus mkha' 'gro ma'i rdo rje'i tshig bzhi pa rje btsun ma sgrol

mas gsungs pa la brten nas thugs rgyud la 'khrungs pa'i/ sum pa lo tsA ba'i blo sbyong snyan brgyud du grags pa kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zin bris kyi steng nas nyams khrid
du legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje phag mo/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ sum pa lo tsA ba/ sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/
rgyal ba brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang
phyug mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ lo pa ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams

mtsho  'dar phyar min/'phrang ba rin chen bzang po/ mkhas grub chos rje/ ri khrod ras chen/ pradznyA bho dhi/ don zhags pa sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'khrul zhig grags pa tshul
khrims/ mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang

po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rin chen/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/
tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra'o/ /!/ /'di ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyis bris/ mkhas pa chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog dang mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan dpon slob gnyis kyis theg pa chen po blo sbyong gi rgya gzhung bod gzhung shin tu gces pa rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i skor la/ mus chen sems dpa' chen
pos mdzad pa'i glegs bam (ka)dkar chagajo bo chen po lha gcig gis rgyal srid spangs nas thar par byon pa'i rnam par (ka)thar pa bla ma'i yon tan chos kyi 'byung gnas zhes
bya ba 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa/ jo bo rjes mnyam med gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa'i drung du byang chub kyi sems 'tshol pa'i slad du dka' ba
spyad nas byon pa'i rnam (ka)thar jo bo chen po nyid kyis gsungs pa/ jo bo chen po a ti shas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i (ka)gzhung rgyas pa mchan  rtsa ba 'di
gnyis la mang nyung yod pas lung so sor gnang ba de ka dngos gtsang ngo / /bcas de las btus pa'i rtsa (ka)ba mchan med gcig 'gor bde legs kun 'byung rin thang med pa'i sku/
zhes yod pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i 'grel pa bka' gdams (ka)yang snying ngo mtshar che'o'i mtha' can/ 'jigs pa'i gcan gzan sna tshogs rgyu ba'i nags khrod du lung rigs
dang rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pa chen po dharma rakShi tas bla ma dam pa'i gsung ltar

bsdebs nas jo bo a ti sha la gnang ba'i dgra bo gnad la dbab pa'i blo sbyong mtshon cha (kha)'khor lo/ ri nag po'i khong gseng na gnas pa'i bla ma dam pa bshad ma thag pas
mdzad pa'i blo sbyong rma bya dug (kha)'joms/ bla ma byams pa'i rnal 'byor pa'i gyer sgom rdo rje'i glu (ga)blangs pas chu bo ganggA'i 'gram du byams pa lha'i rgyal po'i
cha byad kyis gsungs pa jo bo chen pos bod du lkog khrid du mdzad pa/ byams pa'i rnal 'byor pa lugs kyi blo sbyong sems dpa'i rim pa las nyon mongs (ga)pa gtan la dbab pa'i
chos/ blo sbyong sems dpa'i rim pa las bzlog phyogs (ga)gnyen po'i chos/ blo sbyong sems dpa'i rim pa las rang rgyud ngan dma' dbab (ga)pa'i chos/ blo sbyong sems dpa'i
rim pa las zag bcas dge ba'i stobs bskyed (ga)pa'i chos/ gser gling pas jo bo la mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i ched du gnang ba'i (nga)blo sbyong gi rtsa ba nyon mongs lam du blang
ba'i man (ca)ngag nyon mongs pa thams cad la sbyar bar shes par bya ba/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor sbyor dngos mjug (ca)gsum gyis bstan pa spyil bu pa'i zhal nas nga'i snying
phyung nas bstan kyang sha dmar lhog lhog pa kham gcig las mi gda' zhes bsngags par mdzad pa/ yi ge gsum la (ca)brten nas sems can thams cad kyi sdig sgrib sbyong ba/
'di la lung rgyun snang bas dkar chag dang gsan yig na mi gsal ba chad dam snyam/rdo rje sems dpa' la brten nas sha 'khon sbyong ba'i man (ca)ngag rdo rje gdan gyi shar phyogs
nas rnal 'byor ma

gnyis kyis dri ba dris lan gyi tshul gyis jo bo chen po la sems sbyong (cha)bar bskul nas gnang ba'i blo sbyong / jo bo chen pos gsungs pa'i phan yon brgyad dang ldan pa'i
ku sa li'i tshogs (cha)gsog kha che'i paNDi ta chen po shAkya shrIs khro phu lo tsA bar gnang ba'i blo sbyong skyid (ja)sdug lam 'khyer gyi man ngag go'i mtha' can/ grub
thob sum pa lo tsA ba la mkha' 'gro ma dmar sngo gnyis kyis dri ba dris lan gyi tshul gyis gnang ba'i snyan brgyud (nya)blo sbyong 'chi rgyu med pa lags so'i mtha' can/ rigs
gsum mgon po las byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mdzad pa rlabs che bar bstan pa'i kun tu bzang po'i blo sbyong (ta)'khor ba ma stongs bar du 'byung gsung ba'i mtha'
can/ jo bo chen po la byang chub kyi sems ston pa'i bla ma gsum gyi nang nas gser gling pa lhag pa'i lo rgyus dang bcas pa'i blo sbyong thun brgyad (tha)ma zho sha mi
bsri bar phan 'dogs gsung ba'i mtha' can/ thun brgyad ma lag len du byed tshul dge bshes ston pa'i (tha)man ngag la zas la brten pa'i blo sbyong le'u dang po/ dbugs la
brten pa'i blo sbyong le'u gnyis pa/ lus ganggA'i klung gi bye ma snyed du sprul nas rigs drug gi sdug bsngal dang du len pa'i blo sbyong le'u gsum pa/ sha khrag gtong ba'i
blo sbyong le'u bzhi pa/ gtor ma la brten pa'i blo sbyong le'u lnga pa/ 'byung ba la brten pa'i blo sbyong le'u drug pa/ lus yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po cher sprul pa'i
blo sbyong le'u bdun pa/ 'chi kha ma'i blo sbyong gi man ngag le'u brgyad pa rnams/ ltas ngan g.yang du lon pa sogs man ngag bzhi

la brten pa'i blo sbyong ge gas sel (tha)'dod thog tu byed pa yin gyi mtha' can/ brjed pa'i gnas bzhi dang 'chor ba'i gnas bzhi la brten pa'i ma 'ongs pa'i 'gal rkyen spong
ba'i blo sbyong (tha)dpal mar me mdzad nas brgyud pa'i gdams pa/ 'gor dus gsum sangs rgyas kun gyi lam gyi mchog / ces yod pa'i jo bo'i blo sbyong (da)don bdun ma mdo dang
bstan bcos rnams la legs par blta'o'i mtha' can/ blo sbyong yid bzhin nor bu dang lhan thabs bzhi pa che bar yang grags/blo sbyong thun gcig (na)ma zhes pa dpal snar thang
gi mkhan po mchims nam mkha' grags pas mdzad pa/ mnyam med jo bo chen po bod du 'byon khar rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu la spyi chos su (pa)gdams pa/ dpal ldan birWa pa'i
blo sbyong dar paN gyi gsung glo bo lo tsA ba'i khrid yig mnyam med snying rje'i (pha)man ngag dge ba'i bshes gnyen glang thang pa chen pos mdzad pa'i blo sbyong tshig
rkang brgyad ma'i rtsa (ba)ba la 'chad ka bas 'grel pa mdzad pa smon lam yang yang gdab par bya'o'i mtha' can/ de'i zhar byung du a tsa ra gzugs ngan gyi gtam rgyud yod pa/

can/ 'gor byams pa thogs med la sogs dang / zhes yod pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma sde snod thams cad kyi bcud tig pa'i nying (da)khu'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor kun mkhyen thugs ni
brtse ba'i dbang bsgyur cing / zhes

yod pa'i snar thang pa sangs rgyas sgom pas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong tshogs (cha)bshad chen mo/ zhang ratna gu ru'i tshogs chos kyang zer/'dus byas la rtag pa med kyi zhes sogs
rgyal ba yang dgon pas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong nyams len gnad thog (ma)tu skyong ngo'i mtha' can/ jo bo rje lha gcig gi blo sbyong byams snying rje byang chub kyi sems bsgoms
pas na rten 'brel (tsa)snying po zhes bya'o'i mtha' can rnams dang / rten 'brel snying po'i khrid kyang zer/dkar chag tu mi gsal ba blo sbyong (ka)gsung sgros ma'i kha

pa/ byams pa/ gser gling pa/ jo 'brom gnyis/ po to ba/ lcags ri ba/ chos kyi g.yung drung / snye phu rgya sgom/ brag ram pa/ nyan chen pa/ shes rab 'bum/ thogs med bzang po
dpal/ mang mkhar tshul khrims dpal/ sems dpa' gzhon nu rgyal mchog man mtshon cha 'khor lo dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /rje btsun sa skya pa chen pos zla ba drug gi bar du 'jam dpal
dbyangs kyi sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe 'jam dpal dbyangs gtso 'khor gsum pa zhal gzigs pa'i dus su 'jam dpal gtso bos dngos su gsungs pa'i blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral/ de'i
'grel pa rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ sa skya paNDi tas mdzad pa'i 'grel pa/ 'gor rje btsun chen po sa skya pa'i zhal nas zhes yod pa'i zhen
pa bzhi bral gyi gdams pa nub pa rig 'dzin grags kyis mdzad pa/ zhen pa bzhi bral gyi dmigs khrid byang chub sems dpa' rwa lod rdo rjes bskul ba la brten nas kun mkhyen
bsod nams seng ge sa mdzad pa/ khrid yig bla ma kun dga' legs pa'i gsung gis bskul ba la brten nas dge slong kun dga' legs pa'i rin chen gyis zin bris su bkod de chos
kyi rgyal po rdo rje 'chang la gzigs su phul nas dag par byas pa rnams kyi lung khrid legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal dbyangs/ rje btsun brtse ba chen
po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa rin po che
blo gros rgyal

mtshan/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mus chen nam mkha' dbang phyug rje bkra shis
brtan pa/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ mus pa grub pa'i dbang po/ dpal sa skya pa khri chen kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs bsod
nams dbang phyug sngags 'chang bla ma ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa nas brgyud pa 'di rje grol
mchog pa'i khrid brgya'i dbu nas 'byung ba'i khrid yig la rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa dang nub pa rig 'dzin grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge rnams kyis rgyas bkab ste mkhan
chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas rje bkra shis lhun grub pa sogs la stsal 'dug pa de min pa gzhan nas gsan pa'i brgyud pa ni gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por mi bzhugs 'dug pas
'di de'i dbang du btang ba yin/'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang
phyug rje kun dga' mchog grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog rje bstan 'dzin nyi zla bzang po/ lcags zam pa ngag dbang nyi ma/ dge steng bla ma kun dga' dpal bzang /
lcags zam sprul sku kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga'

bsod nams/ de sras ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug de sras sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bka' drin can 'jam mgon bkra
shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /rmor chen pa'i gsan yig las 'byung ba ni/ mus chen nam mkha' dbang phyug yan gong bzhin las/ de nas stong rwa
ba kun dga' legs grub/ de gnyis ka las she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rmor pa grub dbang kun dga' rnam rgyal/ sems dpa' chen po mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang
po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan
chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge nas/ kong ston dbang phyug grub pa/ rje bkra shis brtan pa man 'dra/ yang
na ngor chen nas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug rje dkon mchog 'phel/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus pa dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rnam 'dren mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub
man

'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paN chen/ rwa ston yon tan dpal bzang / glo bo mkhan chen/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /dpal mnyam med dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na'i
thugs dam du mdzad pa'i chos chung brgya rtsar grags pa/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma rgya gar gyi paNDi ta dI paM kA ra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/
1spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma jo bos nai pA la'i yul du grogs po'i don du mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang nag tsho lo tsA'i 'gyur/ 2bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa gser gling
rgyal pos dge slong de wa ma ti btang ba'i ngor jo bos mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng gi 'gyur/ 3dbu ma'i man ngag jo bo dang nag tsho lo tsA
ba'i 'gyur/ 4snying po bsdu ba jo bo dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims 'byung gnas de ba rtsa'i 'gyur/ 5snying po nges par bsdu ba jo bos snye thang du mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid
dang nag tsho lo tsA'i 'gyur/ 6byang chub sems dpa' nor bu'i phreng ba jo bo nyid kyis sgra rang bsgyur du mdzad pa/ 7byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag
tu byas pa 'gyur byang mi gsal ba/ 8'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i glu jo bo dang lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng gis bsgyur ba la slar yang nag
tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas 'gyur bcos mdzad pa/ 9tshul khrims kyi spyod pa'i glu paNDi ta badzra pA Ni dang chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 10chos kyi dbyings su blta ba'i
glu jo bo dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ 11dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag jo bos lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i ngor mdzad pa lo paN de gnyis kyi 'gyur/ 12byang
chub sems dpa' las dang po pa'i lam la 'jug par bstan pa jo bos lha bla ma

byang chub 'od kyi don du mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ 13skyabs su 'gro ba bstan pa 'gyur byang mi gsal ba/ 14theg pa chen po'i lam
gyi sgrub thabs yi ge bsdus pa jo bo dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 15theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs shin tu bsdus pa 'gyur byang gong 'dra/ 16rang
gi bya ba'i rim pa bskul ba dang bcas pa yi ge ra bris pa 'gyur byang gong dang 'dra ba/ 17mdo sde'i don kun las btus pa'i man ngag jo bo dang nag tsho lo tsA'i 'gyur/ 18mi
dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa 'gyur gong 'dra/ 19las rnam par 'byed pa 'gyur gong dang 'dra/ 20ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u jo bo dang dge slong shAkya blo gros
kyi 'gyur/ 21'jig rten las 'das pa'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga 22kha ton dang glegs bam bklag pa'i sngon du bya ba'i cho ga 23pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i sAtstsha gdab
pa'i cho ga 24bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa gong gsal bzhi po de la 'gyur byang mi gsal/ 25sems bskyed pa dang sdom pa'i cho ga'i rim pa jo bo dang dge slong dge
ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur slar yang paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ 26chos tshan nyer drug po 'di rnams dpal dI paM kA
ra nyid kyis mdzad pa yin/ slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa'i cho ga paNDi ta puNya shrI mi tra dang lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/
27dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub

kyis mdzad pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga paNDi ta su rendra bo dhi dang bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 28slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad
pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang yi dam blang ba'i cho ga mkhan po chen po su ma ti kIrti dang lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 29slob dpon mkhas pa chen po

'gyur/ 30des mdzad pa'i sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i spring yig A tsArYA du lo pa dang lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 31slob dpon

slob ma la springs pa'i yi ge lo paN bshad ma thag pa'i 'gyur/ 33slob dpon ma ti tsi  ma khol/tras mdzad pa'i rgyal po ka ni ka la springs pa'i yi ge paNDi ta bidyA kA ra
pra bha dang lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gis bsgyur ba slar yang A tsArYA dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa/ 34slob dpon don yod 'char gyis rgyal po snyan ngag mkhan la gdams pa'i
dri ma med pa'i dris lan rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba paNDi ta ka ma la gupta dang lo chen rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 35'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis dge slong

shu pa/ 51des ba tsha can gyi chu klung gi mdo las phyung ba'i sems can mgu bar bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa bcu gcig pa slob dpon buddha kA ra warma dang lo tsA ba chos kyi
