ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 79dkyil 'khor chen po'i slob dpon ma hA ma tis mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med par sgom pa'i mdo'i rjes su 'gro ba zhes

mtha' can/ gcod yul rgyal sras lam bzang zhes bya ba kun dga'i ming ldan gyis zin bris byas pa'o'i mtha' can/ lam gtor zab mo zhes pa ri khrod 'dzin pa kun dga' rin chen gyis

dga'i ming ldan sprang pos sbyar zhes pa'i mtha' can/ gcod yul nyi ma'i 'od zer zhes bya ba shAkya'i dge slong kun dga' rin chen gyis dkar phyogs skyong ba sgyogs chen gdong
ra'i lha zhol du sbyar zhes pa'i mtha' can/ tshogs las rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba/ bdag cag dpon slob rnams la bkra shis shog ces pa'i mtha' can/ tshogs las rin
chen phreng ba'i zur 'debs zhes bya ba kun dga'i ming ldan bdag gis bkod ces pa'i mtha' can/ tshogs las rgyal ba mnyes byed ces bya ba 'grub par gyur cig gi mtha' can/ lag
mchod ces bya ba a nanda ratnas sbyor ba'o'i mtha' can/ mkha' 'gro sde lnga'i bskang ba rin chen bang mdzod/ zab don thugs kyi snying po'i zhi ba'i me mchod ces bya ba/
las bzhi gang sgrub sngags spel tshig btags zhes pa'i mtha' can/ drag po'i me mchod ces bya ba sems can thams cad la phan thogs par gyur cig gi mtha' can/ zhi ba'i ngar
mi'i ro sreg stong gsum mkha' 'gro'i chad pas chod ces pa'i mtha' can/ cho 'phrul mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba la legs par dpyad cing brtag 'tshal lo zhes pa'i mtha' can/ las
dang po pa rnams kyi nyams len

mdor bsdus dang bcas pa ste de rnams ni drung rin po che nyid kyis mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang tshogs las rin chen phreng ba/ dbang chog 'od kyi phreng ba/ drag tshogs phrin
las lhun grub/ sgrub thabs dngos grub sgo 'byed kyi gsal byed/ sgrub thabs nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba rnams ni mkhas btsun chen po bsod nams grub kyis mdzad pa rnams
dang / zab don gyi snying po'i rgyun gyi nyams len nyung ngu rab gsal zhes bya ba shAkya'i dge slong dharmma bi dza yas mdzad pa/ gcod khrid gdan thog gcig tu nyams su blang
ba'i man ngag gi lung rnams rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni yan chad btsal/ dbang bla kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ ldan ma gcod pa kun dga' rdo rje/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun
dga' rnam rgyal/ drung pa bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ de las bdag gis thos so/ /gzhan yang mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig theg chen lam gyi
gsal 'debs/ theg pa chen po gcod kyi snying po bsdus pa'i lag len/ nyams len mdor bsdus snying po gsal ba/ gcod zab mo don gyi nying khu/ gnyags ston bsam gtan 'od zer gyis
mdzad pa'i dbang bskur byin rlabs rgya mtsho'i zur 'debs/ khros nag lha lnga'i phyag len gyi dogs dpyod/ khros nag bsnyen pa'i kha skong gi sbyin sreg gi tho rnams kyi
lung bcas legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni bka' 'bum gyi lung gi skabs ltar ro/ /!/ /rgya gar dam pa sangs rgyas kyis bod du lan gsum byon pa'i tha mar man ngag 'khyug dpyad
dkar nag khra gsum khams kyi klong thang sgrol mar

mgo na ba/ dpral ba/ migabad kan gyi nad/ dpung pa/ ro stod/ pus mo/ byin pa/ long bu/ rkang mthil na ba rnams gso ba/ rlung / tshad pa/ grang ba/ lus tsha hrab byed pa
rnams sel ba/ skyug pa/ 'khru ba/ gzer nad/ mgo gcod sel pa/ rgyun du gnod pa'i 'dre zhi ba rnams so/ /'khyug dpyad khra bo la/ rta phyugs kyi nad zhi ba/ 'dre byer ba/ 'thab
mo nyung ba/ 'dre gnod thog 'tshag 'od 'khyug zhi ba/ bkra shis shing sa dpyad ngan pa zhi ba/ yams nad chad cing zhi ba/ sa 'dul/ dgra zhi ba/ ngag dang stobs zhi ba/

grol ba/ smyo ba'am kha smras dang nad 'byong ba/ thog bsrung rnams so/ /nag po'i skor la/ 'chi la khad sos pa/ dmag bzlog pa/ dmag byer ba/ gral dpon 'chi ba/ nad kha bsgyur
ba/ dmag dang gnod pa kha smras zhi ba/ gzer gyis 'chi ba/ sngo skam la 'gro ba/ khang pa 'gas pa rnams so/ /zla ba'i 'khyug dpyad la/ dmagabag ma gtong len/ khyim rtsig

pa/ rta/ bong bu/ glang / mdzo/ rtol gsod pa/ bu chung ngu ba/ khyi zug pa zhi ba/ mdze 'ong ba/ khyi thams cad sgo la zug pa/ zhing la lo mi skye ba/ lo tog sngo skam

la 'gro ba/ chang gtad/ pho mo dbye ba/ khang pa bshig pa/ ltas ngan gtong ba/ 'od yong ba/ me 'byung ba/ bya sna tshogs 'bab pa/ gdung thams cad sbrul du 'gro ba/ chu khrag
tu 'gro ba/ khang pa 'jig pa/ rmi lam ngan pa sna tshogs 'byung ba/ zhing sel/ zla mtshan nar mar 'bab pa/ lo tog gtan nas mi skye ba/ ljang pa ser skam du 'gro ba/ zhing

/ zhi byed bstan pa'i nyi ma karma chos grags/ grub dbang nyi zla grags pa/ rje mgon po lhun grub/ sprul sku shAkya rin chen/ chos rgyal gling pa/ mtshungs med da sha

bdag bande

tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /smras pa/ mtha' bral gnas lugs smra bsam yul kun las/ /'das pa shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i don/ /legs par ston pa zab mo gsang ba'i gcod/ /dam
pa'i 'khyug dpyad dang bcas thos pa'i tshul/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gcod kyi skor
thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste drug pa'o/ // /gsum pa rig pa 'dzin pa sngags kyi sdom pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim la bzhi/ bya ba'i rgyud kyi chos skor thos
pa/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi chos skor thos pa/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud kyi chos skor thos pa/ rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim mo/ /dang po

sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun sku mched/ sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ bla ma bsod nams skyabs/ bla ma gzungs kyi dpal/ bla ma dpal ldan

sangs rgyas seng ge rje brang ti pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don

grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med shes bya bzang po/ 'jam dpal grub pa mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul

ldan rdo rje/ dkon mchog 'phel ba man 'dra'o/ /!/ /bde bar gshegs pa bdun gyi sngon gyi smon lam dang sman la sngags kyis gdab pa sogs kyi rjes su 'brangs nas mkhan po

chen rdo rje

shes rab bzang po/ gnyug la ngag dbang grags pa/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /!/ /thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum gyi rjes su gnang ba
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po/ rA hu la gupta badzra/ jo bo a ti shanag tsho lo tsA ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba/ shes rab 'bar/ wa yu ba shes rab tshul
khrims/ lce sgom shes rab rdo rje/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyan ston chos kyi shes rab/ sangs rgyas ston pa brtson 'grus seng ge shangs ston tshul khrims
'bum/ gnyan ston rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje
lha mchog seng ge buddha singha/ mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang
lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/ e waM pa dpal ldan chos skyong
/ des

bdag la'o/ /yang na bla ma gcig tsam btsal nas/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ chos rje kun dga' chos 'phel/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag la'o/
/yang na sangs rgyas ston pa/ grub thob a seng / gser gling pa bkra shis dpal ba/ rdo rje dpal ba/ chos dpal shes rab/ grags pa 'byung gnas/ lo pa tshul dar/ bsod nams
lha dbang / lo pa ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mchog legs rdo rje man 'dra'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas ston pa/ shangs ston pa/ rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag
chen byams pa dpal/ gser gling pa byams pa/ smon lam dbang phyug bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ shes rab bzang po/ gnyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lo pa ngag dbang chos
grags man 'dra'o/ /yang nye brgyud ni/ thugs rje chen po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge ratna wardha man 'dra'o/ /!/ /mi g.yo ba'i rjes
gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ jo bo/ dpal ldan dgon pa ba/ sne'u zur pa/ rtogs ldan bzang mo ba/ lha dge 'dun sgang pa/ sangs rgyas jo bo/ bcu bzhi pa tshul khrims mgon po/ tshes
bcu pa chos kyi rdo rje/ rgyal steng gser khang pa rin chen 'phel/ lo pa tshul dar pa/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang / spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags man 'dra'o/ /yang
lha bzhi'i rjes gnang gi brgyud lugs gcig la/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags nas mus chen nam mkha' dbang

phyug stong rwa ba kun dga' legs grub/ de gnyis ka las she'u lo tsA ba/ de nas mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra'o/ /!/ /gnyis pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi bdag
po'am rig pa'i rgyal po ni 'jam dpal te/ de'ang mnga' ris pa tshul khrims 'od zer gyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog phrin las lhun grub kyi steng nas bya ba spyi'i rgyud nas gsungs
pa'i rigs gsum spyi'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ma hA badzra dhA ra/ badzra pA Ni/ ma hA indra bhU ti/ ma dhya ma/ mr-i
tyu/ nA gArdzu na/ nA ga bo dhi/ kasmi ra dznyA na badzra/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa
skya paNDi ta/ de gnyis ka las do pa dkar ston shAkya grags/ bande lung bde lung zer ba byung / pa kun dga' dpal/ dkar gyi dbon po/gung pa dar ma ye shes/ bag ston gzhon
nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang / gnyags ston byang chub seng ge 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag
tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/

/ yang na/ ngor chen nas/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen lags pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ lo pa ngag dbang chos grags/ she'u lo tsA ba byams
pa kun dga' chos grags/ rje btsun mchog legs rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na ratna wardha nas/ lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra/ yang na brang ti paNDi ta nam mkha'
dpal bzang pa'i yi ge'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud tshul ni/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel yan chad sngar dang 'dra zhing / de nas lha mchog seng ge buddha singha / paNDi
ta nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ nam mkha' bsam 'grub/
des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la e waM thar pa rtser stsal to/ /!/ /'jam dbyangs gang blo ma'i rjes gnang ngam/ 'jam dbyangs ye shes yon tan bzang po'i rigs gtad ces pa
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs  dhI ra pA la zhes pa bod skad du bstan skyong zhes pa ste/ rgya gar gyi paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa yin/ gnyan lo tsA ba'i bla ma yang
yin no/ /dhI ra pA la rngog blo ldan/ gsang phu'i// khyung ston rin grags rgya mar byang chub grags/ /cha pa chos seng gtsang nag brtson seng dang / /dan 'bag dar seng
gnyal zhig 'jam rdor dang / /gzad pa dar tshul dge bshes gra thang pa/ /bla ma bsod rgyal yang rtse rin seng dang / /kun mkhyen bu ston  'di nas bla ma kha cig btsal dgos/mkhan
chen rin rnam pa/ /bla ma bkras rin ngor chen thams cad

mkhyen/ /paN chen grags rgyal bla ma legs 'byung dang / /sa skya lo tsA dkon mchog lhun grub zhabs/ /dkon mchog dpal ldan shar chen byams bkras pa/ /rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen sher rgyam pa/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas
phun tshogs nas/ bsod nams dpal ldan/ mkhan chen tshul khrims lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag tshul
khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na kun dga' bstan 'dzin nas/ mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin stsal to/ /!/ /dam
pa sangs rgyas nas brgyud pa'i 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i seng ge'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal smra seng / pha dam pa/ kha che gu hya/ glen sgom yab sras/ slob
dpon 'od shAkamachog ldan/ skyi ston/ kun mkhyen dol phu pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ ma ti/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ chos rje kun dga' bzang po/ paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge brang ti pa/ paNDi ta chen po nam mkha'
dpal bzang / sgrub khang nas dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa ye shes bzang po/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ de

nas bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ kun mkhyen bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen du bod pa la'o/ /yang na rje lha mchog seng ge shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/
brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun  rtse gdong khri chen/dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ thub bstan mkhan chen ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje/ shar chen ye shes
bzang po man 'dra/ yang na sgrub khang pa nas/ rje ngag dbang brtan pa man 'dra/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub pas mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas legs par thob bo/ /de nyid
kyis mdzad pa'i ril bu'i sgrub pa dang / nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg dang brgyud 'debs rnams kyi lung bcas thos so/ /!/ /ma hA paNDi ta ma ti'i lugs
kyi 'jam dbyangs dkar po'i rjes gnang paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gi yi ge'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ slob dpon ma ti/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ mkhan
chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ sangs rgyas gzhon nu/ mkhan po bsod nams shes rab/ shes rab mgon/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug rje ratna wardha/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam
dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun

tshogs nas mkhas btsun kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs
sa lo/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na ratna wardha/ lha mchog pa/ rje buddha singha / brang ti pa man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa sher
rgyam/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / chos rje dpal ldan don grub man 'dra'o/ /gzhan yang byams pa bsod nams bzang po dang / kun dga' chos 'phel/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/
dpal ldan chos skyong bzhi char las mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang pas gsan/ de las bdag gis mnos te de rnams kyis gsan yul so so dang sbrel lo/ /yang chag lo gsum pa
rin chen chos rgyal las brgyud pa drug ldan byas par snang ste des mdzad pa'i yi ge ra blta'o/ /mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong dang / sangs rgyas dpal bzang pa las sgrub
skor las tshogs rnams kyi lung thob pa ni/ slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi sgrub pa'i thabs ches zab pa kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI dang khro
phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba/ 'jam dbyangs kyi sgrub thabs bskyed rim dang mthun pa'i bstod pa ma tis mdzad pa gnyan los bsgyur ba/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson
'grus kyis mdzad pa'i lo rgyus/ paN chen shAkya shrI'i phyag len ltar khro phu lo chen byams pa'i dpal gyis bsdebs pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rgya ston gyis mdzad pa'i
sgrub skor la rtsa ba'i sgrub pa/ nyes byas 'joms pa/ yon tan sgrub

pa/ rtsod pa bya thabs/ ma sha la brten pa'i las sbyor rnams mkhan po bkra shis lhun grub pa las thos/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa'i las tshogs blo gros
padmo kha 'byed dang bsnyen grub kyi yi ge dang / sbyin sreg rnams kyi lung sangs rgyas dpal bzang pa sogs las legs par mnos so/ /!/ /paNDi ta gser gdugs can gyi bzhed
srol rje btsun 'jam dbyangs dkar po shes rab 'khor lo'i rjes su gnang ba gong ma'i phyag len bzhin thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ paNDi ta gser gdugs
can/ mtshan zla ba'i 'byung gnas sbas pa/rA hu la shrI/ bi ma la shrI/ gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na bi na ya shrI zer/bikSha ta de wa/ gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na bi khya
ta zer ba snang /kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI bha dra/ lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal/ chos rje bsod nams dbang phyug khro phu ba rin chen dbang phyug mkhan chen chos
rgyal dpal bzang / kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang / khro phu ba rin chen 'bum/ gnyags phu ba bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ mkhan chen rin chen bzang
po/ mkhan chen chos grub seng ge sman sdings pa lo chen ratna bha dra/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen/ chos gter dkon mchog legs pa/ e waM sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/
khyab bdag zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku kun dga' bsod nams/ ngag dbang kun
dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims

rin chen la'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang bya tshul rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i ma nor rab gsal sgron ma zhes bya ba'i lung dang bcas pa thos/ /!/ /gsum pa de bzhin gshegs
pa'i rigs kyi yum la thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog bde dga' rgya mtsho dang / bco brgyad 'jam dbyangs chos rjes mdzad pa'i dkyil
chog gi steng nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi yum du gtogs pa bcom ldan 'das ma bsrung ba lnga lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang legs par thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ dpal phyag na rdo rje/ grub chen dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ paNDi ta
don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags
pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam
mkha' mchog grub/ ka bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ de dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun
dga' chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug ngag dbang kun dga' lhun
grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la

stsal to/ /yang na sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje nas/ sku zhang 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan/ de dbon sku zhang bsod nams lhun grub/ sku zhang ngag dbang mchog legs rdo
rje/ de dbon sku zhang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ sku zhang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje
btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ sku
zhang rin chen mkhyen brtse mchog grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na ba ri lo tsA ba nas/ gnyan ston grags/
gnyan rin chen grags/ lha pa'i gnas brtan dkon mchog de sras rngog ston kha'u rgyal/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug rong pa shes rab seng ge 'phags 'od
yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na bu ston nas/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma a mo gha/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rin chen/ chos lung mkhan chen don yod rgyal
mtshan/ mkhan chen kun dga' blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bshes gnyen bkra shis grub mchog ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/
yang na rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ gung pa mgon po rgyal mtshan/ grub mchog ngag dbang rnam rgyal man 'dra'o/ /!/ /'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse'i dbang

phyug gis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs dang brgya rtsa'i chings ltar 'od zer can gtso rkyang gi rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA
ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom
kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ bla ma bsod nams skyabs/ mkhas pa gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ rje ratna shI la/ rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan/ rje nam mkha' dpal ldan/ 'dren mchog snying rje bzang po/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab ngag dbang lhun grub/ byams pa kun dga' lhun grub/
des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /dbang phyug rab brtan pa'i gsung gi gsang ba zhes pa'i gdams pa gzhi 'gro 'dug sogs shar tshe don 'grub pa'i las tshogs kyang thos so/
/!/ /ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje'i yi ge'i steng nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi yum 'phags pa rig pa chen mo'am/ gza' rnams kyi yum gtso 'khor gyi tshom bu la brten
pa'i rjes su gnang ba yi ge'i lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa/ mkhan
po bo dhi sa twa/ 'khon klu'i dbang pos

bsrungs pa/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong / 'khon ston bal po/ 'khon gtsug tor shes rab/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ 'khon kun dga' snying po/ 'khon
bsod nams rtse mo/ 'khon grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'khon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'khon blo gros rgyal mtshan/ gzhon nu dpal grags/ 'phags 'od/ gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen
ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rje lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang
sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun gshegs pa'i rigs
kyi yum gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i rjes gnang lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas phyag na rdo rje dze tA ri/ /rdo rje gdan pa gnyis dang ba ri ba/
/sa skya bla chen rje btsun sku mched gnyis/ /chos rje khu dbon zhang ston dkon mchog dpal/ /brag phug bsod dpal ri khrod blo

gros brtan/ /mtshungs med dpal tshul shar chen ye rgyal dang / /ngor chen kun bzang mus chen dkon rgyal che/ /yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel dang sa lo tsA/ /dkon mchog lhun
grub sangs rgyas seng ge dang / /nam mkha' dpal bzang shar chen kun dga'i mtshan/ /shes rab 'byung gnas kun dga' dpal 'byor dang / /sangs rgyas phun tshogs tshul khrims lhun
grub zhabs/ /de nas mnos pa tshul khrims rin chen no/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs dang / /bstan 'dzin lhun grub bkra shis lhun grub kyis/ /rjes su bzung
ba bdag go yang na ni/ /bstan 'dzin lhun grub dpal ldan chos skyong las/ /legs par thos de tshul khrims rin chen no/ /yang na grub chen dkon mchog blo gros nas/ mus chen
sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams man gong bzhin no/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po nas/ rgyal tshab kun dbang
/ yongs 'dzin/ rje lha mchog pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ brang ti pa/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen sher 'byung man 'dra/ yang zhabs drung rgyal rtse pa la'ang
rje 'dis zhabs drung a mi lags la'ang gsan no/ /rje kun dga' dpal 'byor pas gsan pa 'dra'o/ /!/ /mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis mdzad
pa'i cho ga khrigs rin chen bsam 'phel gyi steng nas 'phags pa kun nas sgor 'jug pa'i 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med pa lha lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang ngam
rigs gtad legs par thob pa'i brgyud

pa ni/ mnyam med thub pa'i dbang po/ jo bo dI paM kA ra/ nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba/ bshes gnyen bya yul ba/ skar chung sbyin pa/ gze pa
don grub ye shes/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon po/ bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ thogs ston shes rab rdo rje/ mes ston grags
pa 'od zer/ bla chen grags pa rin chen/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' 'od zer/ chos rje nam mkha' tshul khrims/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje btsun rdo ring kun spangs
pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ chen po byang ma rin chen bzang po/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang padma phrin las/ mkhyen rab ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub dpal bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims
rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /!/ /sngags 'chang snye mdo shAkya dpal ba'i yi ge'i steng nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtsug tor gdugs dkar lha bcu bdun ma'i
ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang ngam rigs gtad legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar mo/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/
slob dpon bsam gtan bcu pa/ mkhas pa tsandra go mi/ slob dpon gi ra wa ti/ slob dpon rdo rje rnon po/ slob dpon padma lcags kyu/ bram ze rin chen rdo rje/ dze tA ri dgra
las rnam

rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ ldan ma'i skyu ra a skyabs/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/
rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ de las stod lung gad ser ba dang / pho rog pa mdo sde mgon gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka nas khams chen rgan mo lhas pa byang chub dpal/ bla
ma ye shes rin chen/ rje rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma cha rgan pa/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam
rgyal/ sngags 'chang shAkya dpal ba/ rje chos dpal ba/ rje rin chen dpal bzang / mkhas pa lha dbang blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal
bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ mnga' bdag kun dga' lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po/ des bdag la'o/ /rje nyid kyi gsan yig na tsandra go mis mdzad pa'i mdos chog shAkya dpal ba'i dbang chog dang mdos  'di'i lung ma thob/chog gnyis/ lhan thabs
zhwa lu mkhan chen gyis mdzad pa bcas pa'i lung ni/ shAkya dpal/ rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos rje rgyal mtshan bkra shis/ slob dpon dbang chen rgyal po/ bla ma byang
chub bzang po/ mkhan chen rin chen kun ldan/ rig 'dzin kun dga' don grub/ phyi rum dge steng pa byams pa kun dga' 'byung gnas/ khyab bdag rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/
sku zhang rin chen mkhyen brtse mchog

grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /lnga pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi khro bo gshin rje'i gshed dang gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur
ba sogs te/ slob dpon chen po a bha yA ka ra'i bzhed srol chag lo gsum pas mdzad pa'i sreg byed me'i mtshon cha'i steng nas dam pa'i phyag len ltar lung gsum gyi chings
kyi sgo nas khro bo'i rgyal po gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes su gnang ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa sA la'i dbang po/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya
seng ge paN grub a bha yA ka ra/ bhaM ga la'i paN chen shu bhaM kA ra gupta/ de la kha che'i paNDi ta buddha shrI dznyA na dang / grub chen A nanda gupta gnyis kyis zhus/
gnyis ka las chag lo dgra bcom/ de nas chag lo chos rje dpal/ gtsang nag sbug pa mkhan chen dbang phyug  chos rje dpal ba'i gdan sa pa yin/shes rab/ chag dbon bstan 'dzin
dpal bzang / 'jag mon mkhas pa grub chen mangga la shrI/ ti'u ra'i zur khang du bzhugs pa dgung lo brgya bzhes pa/rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ chos rje ye shes dpal bzang
/ de las rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor dang rdo rje 'dzin pa chos skyong bzang po gnyis kyis gsan/ yab sras gsum ga nas chag lo gsum pa rin chen chos rgyal/ bla ma
rin chen rgyal mchog chos rdzong pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ zhwa lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang blo

bzang rgya mtsho/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /de'i rjes gnang bya tshul tho
chung rje nyid kyis mdzad pa dang / rjes gnang gi yi ge sangs rgyas dpal bzang gis mdzad pa thob/ chag los mdzad pa'i sreg byed me'i 'khor lo'i las tshogs la/ lo rgyus phyir
bzlog byad chu bor bskyur ba dang bcas pa'i lung ni/ chag lo/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ she'u lo tsA ba/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang
po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /bstod phrin gyi rab byed ces pa'i lung yang nos so/ /!/ /rin
po che dpal  'di rigs kyi pho nyar bzhag 'os kyang gtsug tor gyi rigs phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir 'dir bris so/ /ldan don grub pas mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas dpal mgon
legs ldan mched gsum gyi rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar mo can/ slob dpon tsandra go mi/
gi ra wa ti/ badzra dakShi/ shu raM ga bha dra/ buddha gu hya/ kha che paNDi ta dkar po/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon
rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ nub pa rig 'dzin grags/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon rin chen
ye shes/ zhang ye ba/ bla ma dkon mchog tshul khrims/ bag ston

gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang pa/ bla ma byang chub seng ge 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ rje dkon mchog 'phel ba/ lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge shar khang pa pradznyA dhwa dza/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag shI la ratna'i ming can la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ mkha'
'gro ma bde ba sbyin/ kha che ratna badzra/ bram ze sadzdza na/ sras mAnydza na pA la/ gnyal ston ye shes dbang phyug dge bsrungs/ gdong sngon pa/ spu ston 'bar thogapho
rog dar ma mdo sde/ thod pa jo 'bur ba/ jo ldan dbang rin/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ ston pa dar ma shAkya/ spur bsod nams dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bag ston gzhon
nu tshul khrims man 'dra'o/ /'di'i rjes gnang dang gtor chog bcas dpal ldan don grub pas mdzad pa'i lung yang nos so/ /!/ /thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis
mdzad pa'i rjes gnang bya tshul gyi yi ge la brten nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi pho nyar bzhag cing 'ga' zhig tu rigs kyi khro bor 'dod pa khro bo'i rgyal po mi g.yo
ba dkar po'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mi g.yo ba/ 'od byed 'byung gnas sbas pa/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ dA na shI la/ yon tan khri/ 'dul 'dzin byang
sems/ rgyal tsha chos dbang / rgyal

tsha gzhon nu grags/ mkhan chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ g.yag ston sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan/ paN chen grags rgyal/ mkhan chen legs 'byung ba/ sa skya
lo tsA ba/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ ngag dbang bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ de las bdag tshul
khrims rin chen gyis legs par thob bo/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ shrI ba blo gros rgyal mtshan/ nub dgon pa sbyin pa grags/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams man 'dra'o/ /yang gong du smos pa'i yi ge de'i steng nas rjes su gnang ba dang / lung gi skor la 'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paNDi
ta dA na shI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa/ mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa'i mi g.yo ba dkar po la brten pa'i shes rab blo 'phel gyi sgrub thabs bcud kyi snying por bkod pa/
des mdzad pa'i spro bsdu/ bogs 'byin/ le brgan te zhal gyi gdams pa gsum/ skyor mo lung gi chos grwar mkhas pa yon tan khris sgrub pa mdzad skabs byin gyis brlabs pa'i
snang ba byung tshul rnams brjed byang du mdzad pa/ de'i yon tan gyi sgo nas bstod pa yan lag bdun ldan ma dang bcas pa rnams rmor chen pas phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa'i lung
/ des mdzad pa'i byin rlabs rjes

gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ khro bo'i rgyal po mi g.yo ba/ paN grub a bha yA ka ra gupta/ A nanda ka ra gupta/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa/ paN chen dA na shI la/ 'jam dbyangs sa
skya paNDi ta/ 'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge bcom ldan 'das ral gri/ slob dpon bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen puNye bha dra/ bla ma dar ma bzang po/ mkhan chen bsod nams
shes rab/ mkhan po shes rab mgon/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun
grub/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ 'dren mchog mchog
legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/
mkhas btsun bkra shis dbang phyug mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog rgya mtsho nas/ dpal sa skya pa ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na dA na shI la nas/ bcom ldan ral gri/ mchims blo
bzang grags pa/ grwa rings pa/ mtshur ston rin chen ye shes/ karma dkon gzhon/ 'dis 'bri khung dpal 'dzin rtsod pa'i sgo nas rmig med du bcom ste dpal 'dzin la klog go

chod cig las mi 'dug gsung skad/rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ mkhan chen ratna shI la/ rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra/ yang na dA na shI la/ 'dul 'dzin byang sems/ mkhas pa lung gi dbang phyug
rgyal tsha lung mang po/ rgyal sras gzhon nu grags pa/ jo nang chos kyi rgyal po/ g.yag mi pham sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan/ paN chen shAkya mchog
ldan/ rje btsun sgo rum pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na nye brgyud ni/ khro bo'i dbang po/ paNDi ta dA na shI la/ de las sa paN dang bcom ral gnyis kyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na
mkhyen rab chos rje nas kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags man 'dra/ yang rjes gnang nye brgyud ni/ khro bo mi g.yo
ba/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar klungs pa mkhas grub seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring kun spangs pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug rje dbang rab man 'dra/ lung rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug nas/ mchod dpon drung pa dkon mchog rdo rje 'chang dbang rab man 'dra/ yang na lung
brgyud lugs gcig ni/ kun mkhyen g.yag pa

nas/ rong ston shes bya kun rig rgyu 'gul paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun
grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug rmor
chen kun dga' lhun grub/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ bkra shis dbang phyug sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ shrI ba blo gros rgyal
mtshan/ sdom brtson sbyin pa grags pa/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra'o/ /shin tu nye brgyud ni/ mi g.yo ba/ g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma man 'dra/ mi
g.yo ba'i sgrub pa mdzad pa'i zhag bdun thog zhal dkar nang du mi g.yo ba'i sku mtheb sor tsam pa mang po byung ba bgegs kyi sprul par mkhyen nas lhag med tu zhal du gsol
bas thul zhing bcom ldan 'das zhal gzigs pa'i lo rgyus snang ngo / /!/ /thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang byed tshul gyi yi ge la brten
nas mi g.yo ba sngon po'i rjes gnang dam pa'i phyag len ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ grub chen dze tA ri dgra las rnam
par rgyal ba/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje
btsun

rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ rgyal ba na bza' brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa
blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog
dkon mchog 'phel ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs mus pa dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang thams cad
mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul
khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ mkhan chen tshul khrims lhun grub man 'dra/ yang
na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ bkra shis lhun grub/ de las tshul khrims rin chen gyis so/ /yang na ngor chen/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo
bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /rigs kyi khro mo ro langs ma dang gzhan gyis mi thub
ma sogs ni ma byung / drug pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi pho nya ni shin tu stobs dang / shin tu rdo rje sogs dang / pho nya mo ni khro mo chen mo dang rab gtum chen mo
la sogs pa ste de rnams kyang

ma byung zhing / brgyad pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi byang chub sems dpa' nye ba'i sras brgyad la sogs pa ste/ gang gi rigs kyi bdag po'i skabs de rnams las gzhan de sngon
ma byung ngo / /rigs sngags 'chang gi sde snod kun gyi gzhi/ /bya rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi lha/ /rgyal ba rgyal ba'i yum dang gtsug tor rig sa/ /khro bor gtogs
pa sde tshan nyi shu gcig / ces dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim
gyi sarga ste bdun pa'o/ // /gnyis pa padma'i rigs la/ dang por rigs kyi gtso bo ni snang ba mtha' yas la sogs pa ste/ 'dir slob dpon dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal zhes
pa dgung lo brgya dang nyi shu bzhugs pa de nyid las brgyud pa/ dpal sa skya pa yab sras kyi gdams pa bya rgyud padma'i rigs tshe dpag med lha dgu ma'i tshe dbang thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ bha ga wAM a pa ri mI tA yurdznyA na/ bcom ldan 'das tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa/garbha sya pA daH snying po'i zhabs/dze tA riH dgra las rgyal ba/bo
dhi bha draH byang chub bzang po/sa mA dhi bha draH ting 'dzin bzang po/badzrA sa nA sho ka shrIH rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med dpal/a mo gha badzraH don yod rdo rje/ba
ri ratna kIrtiH ba ri rin chen grags pa/ma hA gu ru bhU mI paNDa kaH bla ma sa skya pa chen po/puNyA grAH bsod nams rtse mo/kIrti dhwa dzaH grags pa rgyal mtshan/paNDa ra
paNDi tA nanda dhwa dzaH sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/pUrba ka badzra rasmiH shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/mangga laM shuH bkra shis 'od/ai pa kho naShe shi kaH e pa
'khod ston/ma hA

gu ru manydzu gho ShaH bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/bo dhi satwa dzi na dznyA naH byang sems rgyal ye/kIrti lakShmIH grags pa dpal/sru lu dA nanda pra Ni dhaH sru lung kun dga'
smon lam/shI la gu ha kaH brag phug pa/ma ti bI raH blo gros brtan pa/gu ru shrI mAM shI laH bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/dharmma swa mi dznyA na dhwa dzaH chos rje
ye shes rgyal mtshan/badzra dha rA nanda bha draH rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/dzi na yu ba nA nande shwa raH rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug nA ya kA gra ratna wardhaH
'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/swa mI su rottam singhaH rje lha mchog seng ge buddha singhaH sangs rgyas seng ge branti ga ga na shrI bha draH brang ti nam mkha' dpal
bzang /swa mI ga ga na buddhaH de'i dbon/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/bhaTTA ra ka ga ga na shrI bha draH hor se chen gan gyi rgyud/ rje btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang /pa Tu
siddho buddha lakShmIH mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/sarba dznyA na shI la ni rA bho gaH thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/te nAtma bande shI la ratnaM pra
yatstshaH des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to// pA pa Tu siddhi buddha lakShmyaH yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/swa mi dznye ya bha draH rje
shes bya bzang po/ma ho pagdhya shI la ni rA bho ga pUrba batra/ mkhan chen tshul khrims lhun grub sngar bzhin no/ /yang na ba ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge
rgya zhang dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma cha gan grags pa man 'dra/ yang na rgya zhang phug pa/ 'jad pa ri shae pa 'khon ston man 'dra/ yang na grags pa dpal/ chos 'phags
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen seng ge bu ston lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ yang na brag phug
pa/ bla ma dam pa

bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang ma ti/ theg chen pa/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dpal chos pa/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo
sngags 'chang chen po/ brang ti pa man 'dra/ yang na sa lo/ kun dga' dpal ldan/ paN chen man 'dra/ yang na rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong khri chen 'jam dbyangs kun
dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas man 'dra/ yang na brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ brang ti nam mkha' rin chen dang se
chen gan nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kas/ 'dren pa shes rab rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs man 'dra'o/ /de la brten pa'i tshe sgrub kyi gdams pa zab mo
snying gar tshe dpag med gtso 'khor lnga dang spyi bor ye shes tshe dpag med bsgom pa'i tshe sgrub kyi lung ni/ mkhas btsun chen po bkra shis bzang po las thob bo/ de pa'i
gsan yul gang yin btsal bar bya'o/ /!/ /bya ba'i rgyud kyi padma'i rigs su gtogs pa'i tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra zhes grags pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe dpag med/ snying po'i zhabs/ dze tA ri/ bho dhi bha dra/ ting 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson 'grus seng
ge rgya zhang phug pa/ 'jad pa shes rab rin chen/ e pa 'khon ston thugs rje rin chen/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po gzhi thog pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ byang sems rgyal ba
ye shes/ bla ma

grags pa dpal bzang / bla ma chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ sku zhang chos rje nam mkha' mchog grub/
mkhyen rab chos rje/ bsod nams mchog grub/ rje byang gling pa/ rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/gnas gsar ba/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po/de'i dbon po/ grub mchog dbang phyug rab brtan/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang thams cad  a mi lags/mkhyen pa kun dga' bsod
nams bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan/ dpal bzang po/ shar pa bdag chen 'jam mgon ye shes bzang po bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhas grub sangs
rgyas phun tshogs/ de las bsod nams dpal ldan yin nam/ de nas byams pa bsod nams bzang po yin nam/ nam mkha' bsam 'grub gang yin ma nges/ de rjes chos rje bstan pa rgyal
mtshan/ de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis thos so/ /yang na mkhyen rab chos rje yan sngar dang 'dra ba las/ des sgra bsgyur chos skyong bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya
lo tsA/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ rgyal tshab ratna shrI wan/ paNDi ta chen po nam mkha' dpal bzang / sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ a mi lags man sngar
dang 'dra/ yang na sa lo/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa blo gros man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /dkyil chog paN
chen nam bzang

gis mdzad pa'i tho yig 'chi med bdud rtsi'i char 'bebs kyi steng nas mdzad cing / bzlas lung gi skabs su gzungs ring gi bzlas lung bcas pa thos so/ /!/ /ngor chen dkon mchog
lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas grub chen mi tra dzo ki nas brgyud pa'i tshe dpag tu med pa dkar po'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ ston pa sangs rgyas/ lo ke shwa ra/ grub chen mi tra dzo kipaN chen buddha shrI/ chag lo dgra bcom/ grum ston dar ma shes rab/ skrag phug pa shes rab dpal/ grub thob
legs ldan 'od/ chos rje dpal chen bzang po/ ye shes dpal bzang po/ rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs sa lo/ rje dkon mchog lhun
grub/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje btsun nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rje tshul khrims lhun grub/ des
bdag la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen man 'dra/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen gyis grub rgyal
gling pa sa rgyal gyi thugs dam du gnang ba'i tshe sgrub zab mo snga dro mal nas langs ma thag par/ skyabs 'gro sems bskyed mdor bsdus sngon du btang nas/ rang gi snying
sgo nga stong pa lta bu'i nang du padma 'dab ma brgyad pa'i lte ba dang 'dab ma rnams la zla ba'i dkyil 'khor re re'i steng du dbus su sangs rgyas tshe dpag med nas/ nub

byang du mi g.yo tshe dpag med kyi bar lha dgu bskyed nas/ sku re re la dmigs nas gzungs ring tshar re ste dgu bzlas nas 'dod don gsol gdab dang dge ba bsngos pas 'chi ba bslu
ba'i mchog tu 'gyur te/ slob dpon dze tA ri'i thugs kyi yang snying sa skya pa'i gdams pa zhes yod pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ brag phug pa yan chad tshe dpag tu med pa
lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbang gi brgyud pa dang 'dra'am snyam ste dpyad par bya zhing / de nas bdag gi drin chen bla ma bkra shis bzang po pa'i bar btsal/ de las bdag
bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis nos so/ /!/ /bya ba'i rgyud kyi bcangs pa tsam gyis skye ba dran pa'i gzungs sngags yig 'bru lnga bcu rtsa bdun pa byang sgra mi snyan pa'i
tshe'i rang gzungs su grags pa thams cad mkhyen pa zhwa lu lo tsA ba chen pos bslab pa kun las btus pa'i lus bsrung ba'i sngags su bshad pa nyid/ de'i rgya dpe las dngos
su phyung ste dag par mdzad cing / lo rgyus yongs grags su lha'i dge bsnyen zhig gis sgra mi snyan nas dngos su blangs te dgra bcom pa blo gros dpal la gtad pa'i sgra
mi snyan pa'i tshe gzungs la yig cha mi mthun pa sna tshogs 'dug pa las tshe dpag med lhung bzed bsnams pa'i mngon rtogs dang 'brel pa'i tshe dbang la bsdus pa paN chen
nags rin nas brgyud pa sogs kyang yod par grags mod ma thos la/ 'dir sgra mi snyan pa'i rang gzungs zhes yongs grags lo rgyus dang 'brel ba'i sngags dang / rang lus lcags
kyi rdo rjer bsgom pa'i zhal shes dang bcas zhib par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ lha'i

dge bsnyen/ dgra bcom pa blo gros dpal/ lo stong bzhugs/bal po ha ngu tsandra/ lo lnga brgya bzhugs/slob dpon dar ma grags/ lo nyis brgya thub/mnga' ris pa dpal chen rgyal
ba grub/ lo brgyad cur slebs nas kyang lus stobs chung du ma song zer/slob dpon ye shes  lo sum brgya thub/rgyal po/ slob dpon shes  lo nyis brgya lon nas lha sa lan gsum
bskor/rab grags/ dznyA na siddhi/ slob dpon tshad ma'i skyes bu'i gcen yin/bla ma sangs rgyas grags/ rdo rje rin chen/ bka' bzhi pa dpal ldan grags pa/ spyang lung pa gzhon
nu blo gros/ paN chen shAka mchog spyang lung gzhon nu chos grub/ rje btsun grol mchog bar 'dir bla ma 'ga' zhig ma rnyed/ de nas bka' drin mnyam med rdo rje 'chang bkra
shis bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas las kyang sngon gyi lo rgyus dang bcas pa yod pa'i sngags la zhwa lu
lo tsA ba chos skyong bzang pos zhus dag mdzad pa'i steng nas thob kyang de'i brgyud pa slar btsal dgos/ /!/ /lus bsrung ba'i man ngag ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis
mdzad pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thugs sras rin po che yan gong ltar la/ de nas rje bkra shis rin chen/ ngor pa rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rje
sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs sa lo/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ de dbon dpal
mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun

tshogs/ mkhan chen bsod nams dpal ldan/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub las thar rtse pas gsan pa man 'dra/ /!/ /gnyis pa padma'i
rigs kyi bdag po ni spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ste/ de'ang kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sa mdzad pa'i bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi 'phags pa thugs rje chen po bcu gcig
zhal lha so bdun ma'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ jo bo
rje dpal ldan a ti shades lha btsun pa byang chub 'od/ bshes gnyen 'brom ston pa/ rnal 'byor pa shes rab rdo rje gsum la gnang ba las/ 'dir 'brom ston pa/ spyan snga rin
po che/ bshes gnyen bya yul ba/ mus sman pa/ snar thang pa dpal ldan gro mo che/ spyil bo pa stag ston shes rab 'od zer/ dmar ston bsod nams 'phel/ slob dpon grags 'bum/
don zhabs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen grags pa tshul khrims/ mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba
kun dga' chos grags/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ sku dbon ngag dbang mkhyen
brtse rab

brtan/ mchod dpon kun dga' rab brtan/ des rjes su bzung ba lho drung chos rje tshul khrims dbang phyug des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /padma'i rigs kyi bdag po 'phags
pa 'jig rten dbang phyug zhal bcu gcig pa dpal mo lugs kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ dge slong ma dpal mo/ paNDi ta zla ba gzhon
nu/ ye shes bzang po/ bal po pe nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nyi phug pa chos kyi grags pa/ spru pa rdo rje rgyal po/ zhang ston dgra 'jigs/ mkhan chen
rtsi 'dul ba thugs rje byang chub/ 'dzin pa bde ba can pa/ chu bzang pa byang chub 'bar/ rin po che shes rab 'bum/ rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal/ bla ma buddha shrI/
khyab bdag kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje btsun brang ti pa nam mkha'
dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun kun dga' legs pa/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul
khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /lhun grub dpal ldan pa las kyang tshul khrims lhun grub pas gsan pa yin pas de pa'i gsan yul gang yin brtag /
!/ /'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge la brten nas dpal mo lugs kyi 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal gtso

'khor lnga'i rjes su gnang ba dang / rje mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa'i smyung gnas kyi cho ga rjes gnang yi ge'i lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen
po/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i dge slong ma dpal mo/ paNDi ta tsandra ku mA ra/ paNDi ta shrI dznyA na bha dra/ bal po'i paNDi ta pe nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/
grub thob nyi phug pa chos kyi grags pa/ spru pa rdo rje rgyal po/ zhang ston dgra 'jigs/ mkhan chen rtsi 'dul ba thugs rje byang chub/ mkhan chen bde ba can pa/ byang sems
chu bzang pa byang chub 'bar/ rin po che shes rab 'bum pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa bzang po dpal/ grub chen buddhA shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus
chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rmor pa grub chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhyen rab
bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rgyal sras thogs
med nas/ gnyags dbon bsod nams bzang po/ 'phags pa bsod nams dar/ 'phags chen kun dga' bzang po/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /dge slong ma dpal mo lugs kyi
smyung gnas kyi cho ga rgyal sras thogs med pas mdzad pa dang dkon mchog dpal ldan pas mdzad pa gnyis kyi cho ga'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba 'od dpag med/ 'phags
pa spyan ras

gzigs/ grub mchog dge slong dpal mo/ paN chen zla ba gzhon nu/ paN chen ye shes bzang po/ paN chen bal po pe nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nyi phug pa chos
kyi grags pa/ spru pa rdo rje rgyal po/ zhang dgra 'jigs pa/ mkhan chen rtsi 'dul ba/ bde ba can pa/ byang sems chu bzang pa chen po/ chos rje shes rab 'bum/ rgyal sras
thogs med pa/ grub chen buddha shrI/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ kun spangs chos rin/ rdo rje 'chang gis sa bzang 'phags pa las gsan pas kun spangs ma bcug kyang chog go/rdo rje
'chang kun dga' bzang po/ byang sems bsod nams rin chen/ mus chen/ mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun bsod nams dbang phyug rnams gang rung
gis kyang 'thus/ thams cad bcug kyang byin rlabs che/ yongs 'dzin sangs rin/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge mkhas grub grags pa blo gros dang
/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub gang rung / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge 'dren mchog blo gros chos 'phags/ rje kun dga' lung rig sa/ rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen
kun dga' tshul khrims/ rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ 'dren mchog bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rgyal ba'i sras chen dpal ldan chos skyong
/ des bdag la'o/ /gzhan yang bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan pas mdzad pa dang / rje kun dga' lung rigs pas mdzad pa'i smyung gnas kyi cho ga rnams kyi lung ni/ bla

ma gzhan dang gzhan so so nas thob kyang so so'i brgyud pa btsal dgos/ gnyags dbon bsod nams bzang pos mdzad pa'i smyung gnas bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gyi lung thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ gnyags dbon bsod nams bzang po/ 'phags mchog bsod nams dar/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho nas rim par/ mkhan chen brag ston pa/ bla ma shAkya rgyal mtshan/
slob dpon nam mkha' dpal 'byor/ rje dam pa rin po che/ smra dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ mkhas btsun
sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas 'phags pa don yod zhags pa lha lnga'i
rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ e ra pa ti/ rigs ngan gyi rnal 'byor ma/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ rje
btsun lho pa/ zhang nyi phug pa chos kyi grags pa/ drang pho lung pa grags tshul/ skyu ra mkhan po rgyal mtshan mgon/ slob dpon bsod nams grub/ dge bshes kun dga' tshul
khrims/ mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ don zhabs pa sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen shes rab mgon/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ byams pa kun dga' chos

grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngor chen
nas/ gu ge paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / smra ba'i
nyi ma kun dga' bsod nams/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra'o/ /!/ /spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa sa lugs kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
sangs rgyas/ dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom pa/
nyan chen pa/ bsod nams skyabs/ gzungs kyi dpal/ dpal tshul ba/ shar chen ye rgyal/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon rgyal/ kun mkhyen bsod seng / rje ratna wardha/
rje lha mchog pa/ buddha singha / rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pa/ mkhas dbang dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ bla ma dam pa kun dga' legs pa/ 'jam dbyangs
sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ de las bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis mnos so/ /shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas kyis/ shar chen
byams pa kun dga' bkra shis la'ang gsan no/ /skyer sgang pa'i brgyud pa ltar na/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ grub chen rA hu

la/ jo bo rje/ nag tsho lo tsA ba/ phyag sor ba/ shes tshul ba/ lce sgom pa/ skyer sgang pa/ gnyan ston pa/ sangs rgyas ston pa/ shangs ston pa/ khyung po tshul mgon/ ras chen
sangs rgyas seng ge shangs dkar ba rin chen/ rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / grub chen nam rgyal/ rgya sgom legs rgyal/ dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog rje kun dga' rgyal
mtshan/ sngags 'chang chen po dkon  gsang sngags gsar rnying gi sngags 'chang /mchog legs 'dzin/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub man gong dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /'gro ba'i mgon po
'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu nyams su len pa'i sgrub thabs dang / de'i rjes gnang gi chings sgrub thabs brgya
rtsa ltar las ma Ni'i rjes zlos brgya rtsa brgyad kyi bar du byed pa'i rjes su gnang ba snyan brgyud kyi tshul du bzhugs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa'ang kun dga' legs pa yan
chad gtso 'khor gsum pa ji lta ba bzhin yin la/ de nas 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des rjes su bzung ba bande tshul khrims
rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag la stsal to/ /'di dang spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub thabs tshigs su bcad
pa mdo khams shar phyogs mar grags pa rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung yang thob cing 'di gnyis sgrub thabs brgyud tshul bcas gcig pa nyid do/ /!/ /mus chen
dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub

thabs dang / stong ra kun dga' legs grub kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa'i rigs gtad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa thugs
rje chen po/ grub chen rA hu la gupta badzra/ jo bo dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na/ nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba shes rab 'bar/ wa yu ba
shes rab tshul khrims/ lce sgom shes rab rdo rje/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyan ston sbas pa'i  chos kyi shes rab/rnal 'byor/ chos rje rngog brtson 'grus
mkhas grub shangs ston yang zer/seng ge 'gro mgon shangs ston tshul khrims 'bum/ gnyan ston rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang /sngags 'chang
rdo rje gzhon nu/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge mus pa nam mkha'
dpal bzang / mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ mkhyen rab ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen
la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas ston pa/ grub thob a seng / gser gling pa bkra shis dpal/ rdo rje dpal ba/ chos dpal shes rab/ grags pa 'byung gnas/ lo pa tshul dar/ spyan
snga ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mchog legs rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na sangs rgyas ston pa/ shangs ston pa/ rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag chen byams pa
dpal/ gser

gling pa byams pa dpal/ smon lam dbang phyug bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ shes rab bzang po/ gnyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lo pa ngag dbang chos grags man 'dra/ yang nye
brgyud ni/ thugs rje chen po mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge ratna wardha man 'dra/ mus chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i lung yang thob/ yang
na shangs ston nas/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal bzang / 'jag pa blo gros dpal bzang / 'jag chen kun dga'/ rje chos rgyal dpal bzang / mkhan chen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rdo
rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /'jig rten dbang phyug seng ge sgra'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun seng ge sgra/
slob dpon tsandra go mI/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ jo bo nA ro ta pa/ pham thing pa sku mched/ asthu la badzra/ bha ro phyag rdum/ manydza gling pa thugs rje chen po'ang zer/de
gnyis ka las mal lo tsA bas gsan/ de las sa skya pa chen pos gsan/ gnyan gtsug tor/ de'i nye gnas/rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa ye shes 'byung gnas/
shar pa dus 'khor pa/ ye shes rin chen/kun dga' byang chub/ mkhan po rgyal bzang pa/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'dren pa brang ti mkhas
pa/ rje dpal ldan don

grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje mkhas btsun dam pa kun dga' legs pa/ mkhan po chen po buddha lakShmI/ 'dren mchog shes bya bzang po/ mkhyen brtse'i gter chen bkra shis
lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos lcags ri las mi 'da' ba bcu gsum gyi steng du gcig bsnan pa'i klu pa'i gser chos bcu
bzhir grags pa'i ya gyal seng ge sgra'i ngag bsrung 'grol gyi man ngag shin tu zab pa'i mthar thug myong bas thon pa'i lung man ngag dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
'phags pa seng ge slob dpon dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod
nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ bla chen yar sgom se bo/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ rnal 'byor
gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/
rje btsun rdo ring pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mchod dpon drung pa dkon mchog pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ khyab bdag padma phrin las/ 'phags mchog ngag dbang kun
dga' lhun grub/ des

bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /gser chos tshe dpag med sprul sku'i brgyud pa ni gong du song / /!/ /dpal ldan shangs pa bka' brgyud pa'i lugs kyi gsang sgrub skor gsum gyi
nang tshan spyan ras gzigs gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu ma/ mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog lcog

gyis thob bo/ /!/ /thugs rje chen po'i sgo nas mig gsal byed dge ba'i bshes gnyen nyang ston sgrub pos lho brag mkhar chu'i gter nas bton pa/ gter ston dngos kyi rtsa ba

yas/ thugs rje chen po/ padma 'byung gnas/ nyang ston sgrub pa po/ 'gro mgon shAkya bzang po/ ngag gi dbang po/ bkra shis rnam rgyal/ dkon mchog dpal 'byor/ rig 'dzin padma'i

yum ni sgrol ma la sogs pa ste/ 'di bla med du gtogs par bzhed kyang 'dir mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i lung blang dgos pa dang sde tshan gcig tu gzhag pa'i phyir rta mchog

pa/ sangs rgyas sgom pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyo ston smon lam tshul khrims/ rgyang ro byang chub 'bum/ mchims blo bzang grags pa/ gro ston kun dga' rgyal mtshan/

dkon mchog legs 'dzin man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gnyis pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ paN grub wA gI shwa ra/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa
chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal blo gros rgyal mtshan/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug
pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man gong dang 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gsum pa
kha che paN chen lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ bar 'dir bka' bzhi pa

dga' blo gros/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man gong ltar ro/ /yang na kha che paNDi ta nas/ dA na shI la/ gtsang thang pa bla ma ka pa ba/ rtogs ldan grags seng
/ g.ya' bzang pa bsod nams 'od/ bsod nams rdo rje/ gtsang pa blo bzang pa man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs bzhi pa a bha yA ka ra'i lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/

gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan chen

rin chen 'phel/ ye shes 'phel/ kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma byang sems ba/ rgya ma ba yon tan 'od/ shangs dkar ba rin chen rgyal mtshan/ skungs lung pa sangs rgyas 'od/ 'phags
pa rin po che/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs lnga pa gnyan lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ paNDi ta ma ti/ gnyan lo tsA ba
dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ sa skya pa chen po man 'dra zhing / sa chen brgyud par bzhugs phyin de man chad kyi brgyud pa tshang ma ded chog go/ //
bka' babs drug pa dpyal lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ rdo rje gdan pa niska laM kadapyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po/ dpyal a mo gha/ mkhan chen gzhon nu
dpal ye shes/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ rje ye shes dpal bzang / chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba rin
chen rgyal mchog man 'dra zhing bu ston rin po che brgyud par bzhugs phyin de man gyi brgyud pa gong ma rnams kyang 'dir drangs chog go/ // bka' babs bdun pa rngog lugs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ ngag dbang grags pa/ mar pa chos kyi blo gros/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog mdo sde/ rngog kun dga'/ rngog gzi brjid grags pa/

khrus khang lo tsA ba bsod

ma sgrol ma/ karma pa rol pa'i rdo rje/ rje mkha' spyod dbang po/ karma pa de bzhin gshegs pa/ mkhas grub bsod nams 'bum/ bla ma rgyal mtshan/ zhwa dmar ba bzhi pa chos
kyi grags pa/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man 'dra'o/ // /bka' babs dgu pa nags rin lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ paNDi ta ngag dbang grags pa/

tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang brgyud lugs mi 'dra ba gcig la/ 'phags pa rin po che yan gong ltar las/ de nas shAkya 'od zer/ rgyal tsha chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon
tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar klungs pa mkhas grub seng ge rgyal mtshan/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen klu pa bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgya mtsho rin chen/ gong ma
grags pa 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal ba/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng
ge e waM thar pa rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ khyab bdag zhwa lu ba man 'dra'o/ /!/ /sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub
skor dang las tshogs thor bu rnams/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtses phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa'i lung thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge des mdzad
pa'i sbyin sreg gi yi ge chog khrigs ngag 'don bklag chog tu bkod pa tshe dang bsod nams kyi nyi ma bdun 'bar/ des mdzad pa'i tshe khrid skyabs yul zhing khams ma/ bla
ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ bsham dum 'thor gyis song yang 'gal ba med gsungs pa'i mtha' can/ ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa'i sgrol dkar gyi sgo nas 'chi ba bslu ba'i rtog
pa bsdus pa/ des mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang lo tsA ba ba ris bsgyur ba/ yang sgrub thabs/ bum chog gtor chog sgom pa'i srung

'khor rnams chos tshan gcig tu byas pa/ byis pa'i srung 'khor gyi gdams pa yon tan dpag tu med pa/ bar chad zhi byed ltas ngan g.yang du len pa/ slob dpon padma nag pos mdzad
pa'i byad 'grol ba ri'i 'gyur/ klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i gnas dang chom rkun bsrung ba/ ce spyang sngon mo'i lam srung bcas pa'i lung legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zhabs yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ de nas mkhan chen bslab gsum rje/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag zhwa lu pa chen po/ byams
pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa chen po sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des

rje dbang rab man 'dra/ yang ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs sogs kyi brgyud lugs gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab/ rje sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/

pa'i lung dang dmigs khrid

pa/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags
pa rin po che/ shar pa ye shes 'byung gnas/ shar pa kun dga' seng ge bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ gar thig pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma shes rab rdo rje/ grags pa

rta mgrin te/ de'ang paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas jo bo chen po dI paM ka ras yol chos dbang la gnang ba'i rta

ti shayol grub thob chos

dbang / mtha' bzhi grub thob rin po che smon lam pa/ rin po che lam pa/ lha ye shes 'od/ slob dpon legs pa shes rab/ zhang byang chub rin chen/ bla ma byang chub gzhon nu/
mkhan chen byams pa rin chen/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/

don grub yin nam/ de nas bla ma gnyis gsum tsam ma rnyed pas slar btsal/ khang gsar pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des
bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na lha mchog seng ge rje shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse pa man 'dra'o/ /thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi
ge'i lung yang thob/ /!/ /jo bo chen po dpal ldan a ti sha 'phan yul lan pa'i spyil bur bzhugs pa'i tshe bran kha dpal yon gyis tho btsams pa na padma'i rigs kyi khro bor
gtogs pa rta mgrin shwa na bzhis bskor gyi sgo nas btul ba sogs byin rlabs kyi tshan kha shin tu che bar grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba gzhan ma'i rgyas bkab ma yin pa'i

bzang rgya

mtsho/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa rgyas pa'i lang tsho'i
sde/ des bdag skal ldan tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /de'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang she'u lo tsA bas mdzad pa dang / bco brgyad mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs
rjes gnang dang / rgyal dbang lnga pa chen pos mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang yid ches sum ldan bcas pa'i lung rnams thos/ /!/ /ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje'i yi ge dang
/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i yi ge gnyis char gyi steng nas/ rjes ras pa badzra kIrti nas brgyud pa'i rta mgrin dmar po pad dbyug can padma gar dbang gi
rigs su gtogs pa'i rjes su gnang ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal rta mgrin/ u rgyan rin po che/ ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ grub chen ti phu gsang sngags sdong
po/ ras chung rdo rje grags pa/ dbang phyug bzhad pa rdo rje/ sgam po zla 'od gzhon nu/ phag gru rdo rje rgyal po/ skyu ra rin chen dpal/ spyan snga grags pa 'byung gnas/
yang dgon pa thugs kyi rdo rje/ thugs sras spyan snga rigs ldan/ zur phug pa rin chen dpal bzang / 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / chos rje rin chen 'phel/ mkhan chen

dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa/ byams pa ngag

dbang lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na 'ba' rwa ba nas/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge 'jam dbyangs chos kyi
rgyal po/ sprul spu rdo rje rgyal po/ pha rgod bsod nams bzang po/ rdo ring pa chen po man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen rab rje nas/ lo pa ngag dbang chos grags/ she'u lo tsA ba
kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yi ge le tshan gnyis kyi lung yang thos/ /!/ /rta mgrin  'di bya rgyud khro
bor ma nges kyang rta mgrin rnams phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir 'dir bris/dmar po skyer sgang lugs sam gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khro bo'i rgyal

rgyas phun

tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ 'jam
dpal mgon po bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la lan grangs du ma'i bar ro/ /yang na bstan 'dzin lhun grub nas/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag shI la ratna la'o/
/yang na tshar chen nas/ mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos grags rgya mtsho/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ byams pa bsod nams lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /paN
chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang bya tshul gyi yi ge la brten nas byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan la zhal gzigs pa'i padma'i rigs kyi khro

tsha 'od chen/ zhang dbu dkar ba/ zhang lo tsA ba/ zhang byang chub rin chen/ dpal rgyal ba grub pa/ chos rje 'dzin pa rgyal mtshan dpal/ chos rje spang khang pa grags
pa dpal/ sgrub pa po bla ma rin chen brtson 'grus/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ chos rje kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs
'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge rje brang ti pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje brang ti pa nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
dpal bzang / chos rje sangs rgyas dpal

bzang / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bstan 'dzin
lhun grub/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang pa las thob kyang de'i gsan yul gyi bla ma gang yin brtag rgyab
brten lung la sgrub thabs/ nad pa gso ba/ steng gdon gzir ba/ lus bsrung ba/ ser pa bsrung ba/ phyir bzlog pa/ rjes gnang gi yi ge rnying pa rnams dang / thar rtse pa'i yi
ge'i lung bcas thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dkon mchog lhun grub yan gong ltar dang / de nas sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen man gong dang 'dra zhing / bdag gis thob yul dpal ldan
chos skyong las so/ /!/ /padma'i rigs kyi khro mo ni/ thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar rigs kyi khro mo ri khrod lo ma gyon ma ser mo'i rjes gnang thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ brtse chen kun
