chen ye shes/ bla chen sangs rgyas sras/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma bsam gtan grub/ glo bo lo tsA ba shrI wan bo dhi/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI dznyA na/ sa bzang
'phags pa gzhon nu blo

gros/ khyab bdag kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ lha mchog seng ge buddha singha / brang ti paN chen
nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas dbang dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun grub dbang dam pa kun dga' legs pa/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/
mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na mus chen/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge ratna wardha/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang
na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse pa man 'dra'o/ /'di'i sgo nas yul phyogs kyi rims nad gcod pa'i gzungs chog ni/ 'gro mgon
'phags pa'i gsung rab kyi lung brgyud ltar ro/ /!/ /drug pa padma'i rigs kyi pho nya ni/ khro bo spyi gtsug 'bar ba la sogs pa ni ma byung / rigs kyi pho nya mo ni/ 'jigs
med dpal dang dbyangs can ma sogs te/ 'dir 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis snyigs ma lnga dang ldan pa'i 'gro ba rnams phyi rol pa'i lha'i gzugs dang rtags dang
mtshan mas 'dul bar dgongs nas lha thams cad mkhyen pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas dbang phyug sogs phyi rol pa'i lha rnams sku'i cha shas nas
phyung ba'i skabs dbyangs can ma che ba las phyung bar bshad cing nges pa'i don du dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi yum gcig ma yin la/ de yang rigs mang du yod pa'i nang nas shes
rab

bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i lha padma'i rigs kyi pho nya mo ngag dbang lha mo dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i rjes su gnang ba slob dpon dpe med rgya mtsho chen po dang / sum pa lo tsA
ba'i bzhed srol thar rtse paNDi ta nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang kha skong dang bcas pa'i yi ge'i steng nas dam pa'i phyag len 'khrul med
bzhin legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sgra dbyangs lha mo dbyangs can ma/ bram ze phur bu/ bram ze tsandra ka thar rtse pa dang shar pa'i gsan yig na gtum po bde chen
zhes 'di gnyis gcig tu mdzad 'dug kyang ngor chen dang mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na so sor snang ngo / /bram ze bde chen/ bram ze mchod sdong  thar rtse pa dang shar pa'i gsan
yig na 'di gnyis gcig tu 'dug kyang ngor chen dang mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang ngo / /slob dpon seng ge nye ba'i seng ge  ngor chen gyi gsan yig na 'di
bzhin byung zhing 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na u pa singha zhes rgya skad sor bzhag bris 'dug thar rtse dang shar pa sogs gsan yig mang por nyi ma seng ge zer
ba 'dug pa yig skyon shor ram snyam/dpe med 'tsho chen po/ ngor chen gyi gsan yig na 'di bzhin byung zhing mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na dpe med rgya mtsho chen po zhes snang
ba don gcig pa 'dra/ thar rtse pa dang shar pa'i gsan yig na dpe med rgya mtsho chen po so sor phral 'dug pa yig nor byung ngam snyam/sum pa lo tsA ba dpal mchog dang po'i
rdo rje/ kun dga' bla ma/ spyi bo lhas  thar rtse pa dang shar pa'i gsan yig na byang chub bde zer ba 'dug kyang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan thor 'di bzhin snang
ba lo rgyus sogs dang mthun/pa byang chub 'od/ dam pa shes rab/ gru rdo rje seng ge bu ston seng ge 'od/ lha gzhon nu 'bum/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ bla ma rol pa'i
rdo

rje/ karma pa dang mi gcig mkhas pa tsandra shrI/ 'dir sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa'i gsan yig na tshul khrims rgyal mtshan zhes pa lhag po byung / rgyal dbang sogs kyi der ni
med/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal
mtshan/ brang ti paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ dbu mdzad kun dga' dpal 'byor/ 'jam dbyangs sangs
rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ kun mkhyen
dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag shI la ratna la bka' drin du stsal to/ /nye brgyud ni rgya gar nub phyogs kyi paNDi ta sa manta shrIs thugs sras lo tsA ba la gnang ba'i
rgya gar paN chen gyi phyag len 'khrul pa med pa'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ngag dbang dbyangs can ma/ des rjes su bzung ba'i rgya gar nub phyogs kyi paNDi
ta shrI dznyA na bha dra mu nIndra/ paNDi ta chen po sa manta shrI/ sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ bla ma rol pa'i rdo rje man gong dang 'dra/ yang sum pa lo tsA ba
nas brgyud pa'i dbyangs can ma'i rjes gnang dang sgrub skor la/ sgrub thabs dngos/ zhar byung rmi ltas/ gtor ma'i cho ga dang bcas pa/ thun mong ba'i ge gas sel la phrin
las 'chol ba/ grib sel ba/ ting nge 'dzin gyis 'dod chags sel ba/ smyo 'bog sel ba/ 'di las zab pa med pa'i ge gas

sel/ rtags med na spogs chog rdzas kyi chag ge gas sel ba/ nor rgyun ma'i phrag dog sel ba rigs gsum/ lha mo dpal mo'i phrag dog sel ba rigs gsum dang bcas pa/ thun mong ma
yin pa'i ge gas sel la/ ting nge 'dzin la brten nas shes rab 'phel zhing mi 'grib pa/ phongs pa sel ba/ chags pa sel ba/ rnying rlung sel ba rnams dang / sbyin sreg gi cho
ga rtsod pa las rgyal ba/ bsgrub bya dbang du bya ba/ byis pa blo rno bar byed pa/ ril bu'i sbyor ba/ dam tshig me long la brten pa'i zhal shes dang bcas pa bram ze phur
bus mdzad pa'i yi ge sogs/ gzhung man ngag las 'jam dbyangs smon lam dpal ba dang paNDi ta phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi gsung bzhin bkod pa'i lung dang bcas legs par nos
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal yan ring brgyud ltar la/ de nas bla ma gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ rje tshul khrims rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / rje btsun btsong
kha pa chen po/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje bkra shis dpal ldan/ chos rje dpal ldan seng ge 'jam dbyangs legs pa chos 'byor/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ rje thub
bstan pa/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa dge 'dun bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ lha'i btsun pa bsod nams dpal bzang / brag
dgon spyan snga gzhon nu chos dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa snang mdzad rdo rje/ zur 'jam dbyangs chos dbyings rang grol/ 'di nas bla ma gsum tsam btsal/
de nas

mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /sgrub thabs/ spogs chog rtags rtsod pa rgyal ba/ dbang sdud/ dug sel/ byis pa blo rno bar byed pa/ khams 'dus sel ba rnams
man ngag tshigs bcad du bsdebs pa bo dong pa bi dza yas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs tshig lhugaman ngag bying ba/ rgod pa/ 'dod chags/ zhe sdang / mi dga' ba/
sdug bsngal sogs ge gas sel sbyin sreg dang bcas pa/ des mdzad pa'i tshangs pa'i bu mo dbyangs can ma la bstod pa rgyan gyi phreng ba dang bcas pa'i lung nos pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ spyi bo lhas pa byang chub 'od yan sngar ltar las/ de nas 'dzim pa mgon po zla ba'i 'od/ lho pa rin chen grags/ 'dzim mkhan chen bde gshegs/ 'dzim pa rgyal mtshan
dpal/ kun spangs chos grags dpal/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ stag lung ngag dbang grags pa/ paN chen shAkya mchog
ldan/ glang thang spyan snga shAkya rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ rdo rje 'chang
zhwa lu pa chen po/ 'di nas kyang bla ma bzhi tsam btsal/ de nas mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang
na dbyangs can ma/ paNDi ta shI la A ka ra/ tsandra shrI/ gau taM shrI/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ lo chen grags
pa rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ /!/ /thar rtse nam mkha' dpal

bzang gis mdzad pa'i dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung brgyud ni/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan yan gong ltar la/ de nas
paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ 'di gnyis dgos mi dgos brtag shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa ye shes
bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal
to/ /bram ze phur bus mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs ngag gi 'od zer/ drang srong mngon shes can gyis mdzad pa'i las sbyor gyi rtsa ba 'di gnyis kyi lung ni mkhan chen sangs
rgyas dpal bzang / de las dpal ldan chos skyong / de las bdag gis mnos so/ /sgrub thabs 'dod 'jo'i bum bzang las 'byung ba'i dbyangs can dkar mo'i rjes su gnang ba dang /
dpal ldan bsam yas pa tshul khrims blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang sgrub thabs ge gas sel las sbyor dang bcas pa le'u bzhi pa 'od kyi drwa ba/ bstod pa gzhon nu rol
dga' dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ sum pa lo tsA ba yan gong ltar la/ de nas bla brang pa nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen klong chen pa/ mkhas grub chos rje/ sangs
rgyas dbon po/ kun spangs sems can chen po/ bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes/ rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ rje yig pa tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rtse le bsod nams rnam rgyal/
rtse le o rgyan bstan

'dzin/ rig 'dzin mthu stobs rnam rgyal/ rje padma dbang chen/ sdom brtson rin chen dar rgyas/ rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub/ sprul pa'i sku mchog gter bdag gling pa/ de sras
rin chen rnam rgyal/ rdzogs chen pa theg mchog bstan 'dzin pa/ dbon rin po che pa'am nges legs bstan 'dzin pa/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /sgra dbyangs lha mo dbyangs can ma dkar
mo paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rjes su gnang ba thun mong ma yin pa bo dong 'jigs bral gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs las tshogs bstod
pa gnyis bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshangs pa'i bu mo dbyangs can ma/ paNDi ta shI la A ka ra/ tsandra shrI/ gau taM shrI/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bu ston thams
cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bo dong paN chen dbyangs can dga' ba/ stag lung pa ngag dbang grags pa/ paN chen
shAkya mchog ldan/ glang thang spyan snga shAkya rgyal mtshan/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ byams pa bsod nams mtha' yas/ thub bstan mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun
grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas ye shes/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rmor chen nas/ dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang
na rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan

nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ de las byams pa bsod nams mtha' yas/ yangs can mkhan po ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ de gnyis char las mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan
man 'dra'o/ /mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi yi ge'i lung yang thos/ /!/ /rgyud chen krI ya'i chu las skyes pa'i rig sa/ /bde bar gshegs dang bdag po rgyal ba'i
yum/ /khro bo khro mo mngag gzhug pho mor bcas/ /lhag pa lha yi sde tshan nyi shu bdun/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/
padma'i rigs kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste brgyad pa'o/ // /gsum pa rdo rje'i rigs la/ dang por rigs kyi gtso bo ni mi bskyod pa la sogs pa ste 'dir grub
pa'i slob dpon chen po dze tA ris cho ga'i yan lag rnams spyod rgyud ltar bkral ba'i lugs su/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog las sgrib rnam
sbyong gi steng nas rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso bo bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha mo brgyad kyis bskor ba lha dgu'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba nos pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ dznyA na garbha/ dznyA na shAnta/ buddha shAnta/ ngor chen gong dkar ba mkhyen brtse gsum gyi gsan yig na 'dug
rung thar rtse pa dang shar pa'i gsan yig tu mi snang ba chad pa 'dra/buddha gu hya/ ku sa li che chung gnyis/ su warNa Dwi pa dharma kIrti/ dpal dI paM kA ra/ go mi sgom
chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ gnyags ldom bu ba/ spug thams cad mkhyen pa/ chos

kyi rgyal mtshan/ gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na chos kyi tog zer ba 'dug pa tog gi skad dod ke tu rgyal mtshan la'ang 'jug par dgongs sam snyam/bya rin chen  bla ma bya nag chen
po/'od/mnga' ris glo bo pa yin/ glo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon po/ bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka
shrI dznyA na/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ /rgyal tshab kun dbang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ rje sangs rgyas
seng ge thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / ratnArtha siddhiHshar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar chen ye shes bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/
/yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bar 'dir bla ma zhig btsal dgos/ rje btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag la lhun grub steng gi chos grwar stsal to/ /yang shug rwa ba
kun dga' dpal 'byor las lan cig thob kyang de pa'i gsan yul gyi bla ma gang yin ma nges/ yang na bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan nas/ rje lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng
ge man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog 'phel nas/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse pa man gong bzhin
no/ /yang na jo bo chen po nas/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun sa chen/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ snur ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ snur chos 'phags/ gar thig pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ ma

Ni ka shrI dznyA na man 'dra/ yang na sangs rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs/ dze tA ri/ kha che ye shes rdo rje/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ sa skya pa chen po man 'dra'o/ /!/ /gnyis
pa rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po ni rigs pa mchog dang glang po'i rna ba la sogs pa ste/ 'dir zhwa lu pa shar chen ye shes rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i dkyil chog gsang ba nor bu'i
gter mdzod kyi steng nas slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po'i lugs kyi dpal gsang pa'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje lha nyi shu rtsa gcig gam/ 'di gnyis gang gi dbang thob pa
yin yid la ma nges pas slar khang gsar ba'i gsan yig la brtag lha bcu bdun/ lha gcig rnams kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag
par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ dpal kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha
che rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze sadzdza na/ jo bo te dza de wa/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ g.yor po jo ston rdo rje rtse mo/ pur bsod  gra dol gyi mtshams na
bcur zer ba zhig 'dug pa de nas yin pa chog sgrigs dngos grub 'dod 'jor bshad/nams rin chen/ 'byed phu ba karma bkra shis/ lha rje stag pa jo bzang / gnubs lo tsA ba byams
pa'i dpal/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras lo tsA ba
rin chen rnam rgyal/ chos rgyal nam mkha'i mtshan can/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ sku zhang rdo rje 'chang

mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan
chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal
to/ /yang na mkhyen rab rje/ de las lcags sgog lung pa bkra shis dpal  tshar chen gyi lam yig tu ku sa li'i bla ma dang lam du mjal gsungs pa de yin/'byor dang / 'brog
khang don grub rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka nas 'jam dbyangs byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang na kha che rin chen
rdo rje nas/ kha che dgon pa ba dza ya A nanda/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ zhu ston sa skya pa/ jo btsun grags pa seng ge rgya ston sgrub pa po/ rgya ston grub mchog bla ma
rdo rje dpal/ khro phu sems dpa' chen po man 'dra/ yang na khro phu ba nas/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na grub mchog pa nas/ dpal seng pa/ sprul sku rgyal
tsha/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje dpal nas/ gzhon nu seng ge brag ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de sras kun mkhyen bu ston man
'dra'o/ /spyir/ chu yis dbang bskur cod paN dag/ bya ba'i rgyud la rab tu grags/ /zhes gsungs kyang dmigs kyis bsal ba bya rgyud kyi cho ga chung ba rgya gar nas 'gyur
ba 'ga' dang 'di nyid kyi dkyil chog bzhir slob ma'i dbang lnga phyir mi

ldog pa'i dbang dang bcas pa mdzad mod rnal 'byor rgyud dang 'khrul bar mi bya'o/ /!/ /paN chen ngag dbang chos  ngag chos dang byang gling pa gnyis kyis mdzad pa zhes rmor
pa'i gsan yig tu byung /grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo
rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze sadzdza na/ jo bo te dza de ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba
'phags pa shes rab/ g.yor po jo ston/ pur bsod nams rin chen/ 'jad phu ba padma bkra shis/ stag pa jo bzang / khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa dpal bzang / bla chen bsod nams
dbang phyug khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po rin chen rnam rgyal/ grub pa'i
dbang phyug nam mkha'i mtshan can/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ rdo ring kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug grub mchog dbang phyug rab brtan/ kun mkhyen ngag dbang chos grags/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
dbang phyug mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ thugs sras 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ mang thos bsod nams chos 'phel/ ngag dbang tshul khrims bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang bsod
nams dbang phyug thams cad

mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ a wa dhU tI pa/ jo bo rje/ lo tsA ba rgya brtson
'grus seng ge rong pa 'gar dge'ajad gyang phu ba/ mal lo tsA ba/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paNDi ta/ rgyal tsha chos kyi dbang phyug
rong pa shes rab seng ge bla ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma mgon po 'bum/ bla ma nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ yang na sangs
rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ grub chen dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje sa chen man 'dra/ yang ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i
yi ge'i steng nas phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi rjes gnang bstan 'dzin lhun grub nas/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong pas gsan pa'i brgyud pa ni 'og rnam sras kyi
skabs ltar dang / yang mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub pas chos rje bstan pa rgyal mtshan pa'i ngor mdzad pa'i phyag rdor gos sngon can 'gro bzang lugs kyi sgrub thabs
rjes gnang bcas zur phyung mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub pa yan chad ni rnam thos sras dang sbags sgrub
skabs kyi brgyud pa dang 'dra zhing / de nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang bkra

shis lhun grub/ de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par thos so/ /!/ /thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas 'byung po 'dul byed
kyi rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ a bha yA ka ra/ shu bhaM ka ra/ pU dza ti/ ratna rakShi ta/ gau taM shrI/ kIrti paNDi ta/ yar lung lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ bla ma rgyal mtshan rin chen/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ bka' bcu pa gzhon nu seng ge bla ma mgon po 'bum pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje sangs
rgyas seng ge brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ mtshungs med bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rje lhun grub dpal ldan/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun
grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na lhun grub dpal ldan nas/ ldan ma mkhas btsun kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na lhun grub dpal ldan nas/ sangs
rgyas phun tshogs/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ 'jam dbyangs sher rgyam/ 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ 'jam
dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas

dang 'di gnyis gang rung / shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas phun tshogs man 'dra'o/ /rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i
sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi lung yang thos so/ /'di gur nas gsungs pa'i bla med du bzhed pa'ang yod de/ de'i brgyud pa ni 'og tu 'byung ngo / /!/ /mkhas grub sangs rgyas
phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas so'i sngags 'chang snye mdo shAkya dpal la gsang ba'i bdag pos dngos su gnang ba'i gur nas gsungs pa dang 'brel pa'i phyag
na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi rjes gnang me'i dbang dang bcas pa'i rjes su gnang ba sems dpa' sum brtsegs mar grags pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal phyag na rdo
rje/ sngags 'chang shAkya dpal ba/ bla chen chos dpal ba/ chos rje rin chen dpal bzang / mkhas pa lha dbang blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha'
dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ khyab bdag mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ 'di phyin gyi brgyud
pa ma rnyed pas slar bzo/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na bsod nams dpal
ldan nas/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na lha dbang blo gros nas/ dwags po'i paNDi ta bkra shis rnam rgyal/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang / spyan
snga ngag dbang chos grags

rgyal mtshan/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mchog legs rdo rje khu dbon man 'dra'o/ /!/ /thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang byed
tshul gyi yi ge la brten nas gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje u tsArYa'i rjes su gnang ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje
'chang / gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon padma badzra/ mkhas pa tsandra go mi/ rgyal po dharmA pha la/ bla ma zangs gling pa/ khams
pa a seng / jo sras gnyal pa rin chen 'od/ 'di la gsan yig ganggA'i chu rgyun du bla ma bya nag pa yin 'dra zhes snang /bla ma dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ jo sras stag la me
'bar/ ston grags zho rwa ba/ bla ma don zhabs pa/ bla ma lha rje/ slob dpon chos grags/ e pa 'khon ston/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma rgyal 'od/ slob dpon smra ba'i seng
ge chos rje byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng
ge rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ chos rje bsod nams rab rgyas/ thams cad mkhyen pa sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs bral bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rdo rje
'chang bkra shis lhun

grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang bstan 'dzin lhun grub nas/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / de las bdag gis legs par mnos so/ /yang na ngor
chen kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na khams pa a seng nas/ zhang ston dkon
mchog ru smon mkhar ba/ skyi ston ru zhang / dkon mchog blo gros/ slob dpon chos grags man 'dra/ yang na lo tsA ba mchog ldan nas/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ kun
mkhyen jo nang pa/ bya sder ba byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /yang na mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ ratna wardha/ mus
chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /phyag rdor gtum po khyung lnga'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ 'di gter ma'i lugs yin yang phyag rdor rnams
phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir 'dir bris/chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku phyag na rdo rje/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug sprul sku shAkya
seng ge sprul sku shAkya 'bum/ rin chen byang chub rdo rje/ chos rje stag pa ba/ zur dben pa chos bzang bla ma/ mnyam med bde legs rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung
gnas/ mkhas mchog lha dbang blo gros/ rje btsun sangs rgyas seng ge byams pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan
chen lhun grub dpal

ldan/ 'jam mgon sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen bsod nams dpal ldan/ kun mkhyen tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'dzin pa bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag
tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po/ rgyal ba rigs lnga/ padma 'byung gnas/ khri srong lde'u btsan/ mnga' bdag nyang ral nas brgyud de/ sngags
'chang rdo rje bzang po/ rdo ring kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog rdo ring pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos gter dkon mchog legs pa/ mkhan grub
pa man 'dra'o/ /!/ /rdo rje'i  'di 'ga' zhig tu spyod pa'i rgyud du 'jog pa'ang yod/rigs kyi khro bo rnam par 'joms pa mthing nag lha bcu dgu dza ya warma'i lugs sam/ ma
Ni ka badzra'i lugs su grags pa'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil rin chen dbang rgyal gyi steng nas legs par thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / gsang ba'i bdag po dpal phyag na rdo rje/ ngor chen dang thar rtse ba'i gsan yig na mi gsal yang rje mkhyen brtse dang mkhan
chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi gsan yig na snang /rje btsun byams pa/ skal ldan ganggA dha ra/ bram ze slob dpon ma ti badzra/ paNDi ta dza ya warma/ paNDi ta dznyA na
shrI/ lo tsA ba cog gru rab zhi/ bla ma yon tan legs pa/ rje bsam

gtan dbang phyug bla ma don grub ye shes/ rje chos kyi blo gros/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rje dkon mchog rdo rje/ bla ma dkon mchog rdo rje/ bla ma shes rab 'bum/ rong
pa chos kyi mgon po/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ pur bsod nams dbang phyug bya sder ba byang chub rin chen/ bya sder ba byang chub gzhon nu/ bya sder ba byams pa rin chen/ bya
sder ba byang chub/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa
skya lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/
mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen
la bka' drin du stsal to/ /gu ge paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil gyi lung yang nos so/ /!/ /'di de sngon ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyi dbang gis bris/ ngag dbang mchog
legs rdo rje'i yi ge'i steng nas rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po grub chen sa wa ri sa lugs kyi rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa dkar po lha bcu dgu'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang
ngam rigs gtad legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can/ grub chen sa wa ri pa/ dza
wa ri pa/ de wa pUrNa ma ti/ 'gar lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang

po/ gshen ston rin chen dngos grub/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sgang ston shes rab bla ma/ sgang ston shes rab 'bum/ grags pa rdo rje/ go rwa ba dar ma byang chub/ yang rtse
ba rin chen seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhas pa bsod nams 'phel ba/
byang sems rin chen chos rgyal/ mkhan chen rin chen rgyal po/ bla chen chos rig rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsod nams dpal 'byor/ byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mus
chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba mang thos bsod nams dbang phyug chos kyi rje dpal ldan chos skyong ngam bla ma gang rung zhig de las thos par 'gyur ba tshul khams rin
chen zhes bya'o/ /yang na yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge nas/ bla ma rgyal mtshan mgon/ dharmA kIrti/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/
paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ ratna wardha/ lha mchog seng ge buddha singha / mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra'o/ /!/ /thams cad mkhyen
pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa ba ri lugs lha gcig bum gcig gi rjes su gnang ba/ bkru byab bsrung gsum dang

bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon dze tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal ba/ rdo rje gdan pa mya
ngan med pa'i dpal/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin
po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug bla ma rin chen dpal/ bla ma byang chub
gzhon nu/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug rje dkon mchog 'phel

sa lo kun dga' bsod

nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paN chen/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa skya lo tsA ba man 'dra'o/ /!/ /gsum
pa rdo rje'i rigs kyi yum ni mA ma kI dang rigs mchog la sogs te ma byung ngo / /bzhi pa rigs kyi khro bo bdud rtsi thab sbyor sogs dang / rigs kyi khro mo 'dod pa'i rdo
rje ma sogs kyang ma byung ngo / /lnga pa rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nya ni khro bo 'chol pa sogs te/ de'ang sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang / 'jad byams pa bkra shis
lhun grub pas cung zad bsrings pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nya khro bo dme ba brtsegs pa dud kha'i rjes su gnang ba legs par

'byung / bdag chen ngag gi dbang

rgya mtsho yan sngar dang 'dra ba las/ de nas mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal rtse ba ngag dbang bsod
nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ chos rje kun dga' rnam rgyal/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /lnga pa rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nya
mo ni blo gros rdo rje ma dang / rdo rje dril bu ma la sogs pa ste/ 'dir 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang dam pa'i phyag len la brten
nas khro mo dme brtsegs kyi rjes su gnang ba lung bcas

thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ DA ki ma seng ge'i gdong pa can/ gru spang rtse ba rdo rje seng ge chos rje
brag nag pa/ byang sems chen po/ bla ma dngos grub rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsod nams dar/ be phug pa bde legs rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang chos rgyal bsod nams/ de sras
chos skyong bsod nams bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ bla ma gnyis tsam btsal/ de nas mkhan chen sangs rgyas
phun tshogs/ de las mus pa'i dge bshes tshul khrims kyis gsan nam snyam/ de nas drin chen rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la lan
mang du stsal to/ /yang na mkhyen brtse'i zhabs nas/ 'phags mchog byams pa skal ldan bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra'o/ /bya rgyud rdo rje'i rigs
su mthun bsdebs pa'i/ /de bzhin gshegs dang rigs kyi bdag po yum/ /khro bo pho nya dga' ma'i zlos gar gyis/ /dngos grub la gor stsol ba bcu gsum mo/ /zhes dam pa'i chos
thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ rdo rje'i rigs kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste dgu pa'o/ // /bzhi pa nor can gyi rigs la 'phags
pa nor bu bzang po la sogs pa gnod sbyin gyi tshogs rnams te/ 'dir thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang byed tshul gyi yi ge
la brten nas 'phags

pa dzam bha la ser po zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i rjes su gnang ba yi ge de nyid kyi lung dang bcas pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/
gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa a shwa ka shrI/ a mo gha badzra/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ dpal
ldan bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/'di med pa'ang yod/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan
chen bsod nams brtan pa/ bla ma bsod nams skyabs/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub
dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen
la'o/ /yang na yongs 'dzin nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra'o/ /thams cad
mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas 'phags pa dzam bha la nag po zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i rjes su gnang ba yi ge'i lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud
pa'ang bshad ma thag pa ltar

ro/ /!/ /she'u lo tsA ba chen po byams pa kun dga' chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang byed tshul gyi yi ge la brten nas nor can gyi rigs jo bo lugs kyi dzambha
la dkar po 'brug zhon can lha lnga'i rjes su gnang ba thun mong ma yin pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ jo bo chen po a ti shalo tsA ba rgya
brtson 'grus seng ge nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba/ 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ bshes gnyen po to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan grags/ skyo ston
smon lam tshul khrims/ spyan snga bsod nams 'phel/ bka' bcu pa gzhon nu seng ge sribs ri ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ lha phug pa rin chen 'od zer/ bla ma dpal ldan grub
pa/gsan yig ganggA'i chu rgyun du sa skya'i gsan yig na mi gsal yang lo pa spyan snga'i gsan yig tu bar 'dir bla ma kha shas ma rnyed tshul 'dug ces snang / rin po che sangs
rgyas 'od zer/ gtsang pa blo bzang pa/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya bzang po/ 'di gnyis rje bla ma'i gsan yig tu 'byung ba she'u lo tsA ba'i gsan yig nas kha bskang /spyan snga
bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa  buddha lakShmI'i gsan yig tu 'di'i tshab tu ngag dbang mchog legs rdo
rje byung /kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bka'
drin mnyam med rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na kun dga' bstan

'dzin nas/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / de las bdag gis legs par nos so/ /lung la phyi chu sbyin la brten nas bsgrub pa/ nang gtor ma la brten nas bsgrub pa/ gsang ba
ga'u la brten nas bsgrub pa/ thugs rje chen pos spyan nas dzambha la sprul te jo bo la gnang ba'i lo rgyus rjes gnang gi yi ge bstod pa spyan ras gzigs dbang ma/ she'u
lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sgom bzlas rjes gnang byed tshul bcas rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rmor chen pa yan gong dang 'dra la/ de nas
ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas kyis gsan nam brtag de nas rtse gdong sprul pa'i sku rin po che/ mnga' ris pa bsod nams blo gros/ chos rje ting 'dzin rdo rje/
des bdag la stsal to/ /!/ /'dul ba lung las/ rgyal chen sde bzhi po mkha' lding sgra snyan dang sgra chung / klu dbugs dang dbugs chen du gyur pa na bzhi gas sangs rgyas
'od srungs la yon tan shes nas dad de bslab pa'i gzhi bzung nas de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa la 'jig rten skyong bar smon lam btab pa'i mthu btsan pos bstan
pa rin po che skyong ba la 'phags pa'i yul dang gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir yongs su grags shing mkhas grub mang pos chos skyong gi gtso bor mdzad pa'i rgyal po chen po rnam
mang thos pa'i sras 'di nyid kyi gzi brjid ma bzod par lha min gyi dpung phyir log par brten/ lha rnams ngal bsos pas ngal bsos po dang / lha min gyis g.yul bshams pa'i
tshe seng ge khros pa la zhon nas srungs pas gnas srung po

dang / dug sprul chen por sprul nas lha min dbang po ra rgod kyi dmag rnams myos par byas pas lus ngan po zhes sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs mang por grags shing / mu stegs kyi
sprang po nyi ma'i dngos grub sogs bsgral bar dka' ba mang po tshar bcad pas mthu rtsal che ba/ tshe dang dpal 'byor sogs 'dod dgu'i char chen po 'bad med du stsol ba'i
lha mchog 'di nyid kyi chos skor bstan pa snga dar dang phyi dar gyi lo paN rnams las brgyud pa mtha' klas par bzhugs pa las/ thog mar thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngor
chen dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gtor chog rjes gnang bya tshul gyi yi ge rnams kyi steng nas phyag na rdo rje 'gro bzang snying po'i lugs dang rgyal
po chen po rnam thos sras sbags sgrub kyi rjes su gnang ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rdo rje 'chang / gsang ba'i bdag po phyag
na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/te dza de wa/ kha chen dgon pa ba/mtshan 'phags pa shes
rab/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ gsang mtshan dpa' bo rdo rje/g.yor po jo ston/bcur byung / pur bsod nams rin chen/ 'byid phu ba padma bkra shis/ lha rje jo bzang / khro phu
lo tsA ba/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ jo nang paN chen phyogs las
rnam rgyal/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang

po/ paNDi ta chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mtshungs
med dkon mchog dpal ldan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bkra shis/ rje btsun nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ rdo rje 'chang chen po sangs rgyas
phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang dbang dpal ldan chos skyong / de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis lan gnyis kyi bar du mnos so/
/yang na khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge nas/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge kun mkhyen bu ston/ bla ma dam pa man 'dra/ yang na bu ston rin po che/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam
rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub dpal bzang / slob dpon rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ zhwa lu lo tsA ba chos skyong bzang po/ sa skya lo tsA
ba man 'dra'o/ /yang na phyag na rdo rje/ kA ma rU pa/ kahNa pa/ 'gro bzang snying po/ rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze sadzdza na/ kha che dgon pa ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ zhu
ston sa skya pa/ grags pa seng ge rgya ston grub pa po/ dpal yin nam/grub mchog rdo rje dpal/ khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge man 'dra'o/ /der ma zad rgyal po chen po rnam
thos sras kyi bka' srol zab cing rgya che ba'i gdams pa bzhugs pa rnams dus dbang gis chos par rlom pa phal cher mi chos kyi zhar la lha chos 'grub tu re ba'i le lo dang
rnam par g.yeng ba'i dbang gis nub tu nye ba na/ rdo rje 'chang tshar

chen chos kyi rgyal pos byang chub sems dpa' rtag tu ngu'i rnam par thar pa bzhin rnam thos sras bka' mi 'dra ba bco lnga tsam gyi chos skor gsan zhing / phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs
pa'i rgyun ma nyams pa rnams legs par thob pa la/ 'di nyid kyi gong gnon du phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi rjes gnang mdzad pa'i srol ltar mnos pa ni gong du smos
zin cing / slob dpon 'gro bzang snying pos rgyud dang man ngag la brten nas rgyal po ngal bsos po zhi ba nor du bsgrub pa dang drag byed mthu ru bsgrub pa'i cho ga sogs
mdzad pa las thog mar zhi ba bde byed ser po lha dgu zangs dkar ba nas brgyud pa stod lugs smad lugs kyi brgyud pa chu bo gnyis 'dres las/ phyag len gyi rim pa smad lugs
chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i bzhed srol gtso che bar mdzad la/ der ma zad rjes gnang lnga phrag gsum gyi cho ga so so'i lugs srol nyams pa med pa rdo
rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi phyag len bzhin/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis chog khrigs su mdzad pa'i nor 'dzin dpal mo'i rgyan phreng gi steng nas legs
par thos pa yin zhing / bsgrig rim thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi gsan yig gi go rim ltar bkod pa la/ rnam sras kun gyi rtsa bar gyur pa zhi ba bde byed
ser po lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba/ 1'di dang 'brel bar shin tu gnyan pa slob ma dam ldan bsnyen song re re tsam las mang por mi gnang ba'i drag po'i rjes gnang shin tu
gnyan cing bka' rgya dam pa/ zangs dkar ba'i gong khug sro ma can las byung ba'i

gsang sgrub ljang ser be con can/ yum padma gtsug phud ma ste/ yab yum gnyis kyi rjes gnang stod lugs las 'ongs pa/ 2slob dpon klu sgrub kyis sprang po nyi ma'i dngos grub
bsgral ba'i drag byed rta sngon bdud mo bzhis bskor lha lnga'i rjes gnang / rnam sras dmar po'i skor dang rnying ma bka' gter nas bshad pa rnams bla med du gtogs kyang 'dir
sde tshan gyi dbang gis phyogs gcig tu bkod do/ /3de nyid la cung zad kha bsgyur cing rgyal chen bzhi bsnan pa'i nang ma mo ltar bsgrub pa lha dgu'i rjes gnang / 4gnubs
kyis bsgyur ba'i bai shra wa Na kha rag khram thogs nag po'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i drag po mthu ru bsgrub pa'i nang nas drag byed seng zhon klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rjes
gnang / 5de nyid la cung zad kha bsgyur ba bzhon pa med pa'i drag byed rkang thang lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na mi gsal yang /
chog sgrigs gnyis ka na 'dug cing phyag len la'ang mdzad/6gsang ba gshin rje ltar bsgrub pa mdung dmar can lha bcu gsum gyi rjes gnang / kha rag khram thogs kyi rgyud na
mu stegs nyi ma sgrub pa dang bha ri ha'i grong khyer gzhom pa'i ched du slob dpon nA gArdzu na'i thugs nas rgyud bton par bshad pas sprang po nyi ma'i dngos grub bsgral
ba'i chos skyong yang 'di yin nam snyam/7bram ze su pa tos zhag gsum la mu stegs pa bco lnga bsgral ba'i yang gsang drag po srin po bzhis bskor gtso 'khor lnga'i rjes gnang
/ 8shu raM ga warma'i lugs kyi rnam sras mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa yum gyis 'khril ba gtso 'khor bco lnga pa'i rjes gnang / 9rnam sras dmar ser las mkhan mdung
dmar can dang bcas pa'i gtso 'khor gnyis kyi rjes

gnang / 10gar mkhan mchog gi rgyud nas sras gar mkhan mchog gur kum gzhon  'di la rjes gnang med/nu'i mdangs can zhal bzhi phyag bcu drug pa bstan pa'i shugs la slob dpon 'gro
bzang snying po dang kha che rin chen rdo rje sogs kyis bkral ba'i gar mkhan mchog ljang gu zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / 11de la cung zad kha
bsgyur ba gar mkhan mchog dmar smug zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad pa yum bcas kyi rjes gnang / 12rnam sras dkar po tshe 'phel lha dgu'i rjes gnang / 13lha sras mu tig btsan
po dang blon po zhang lha bzang klu dpal gnyis bha da hor gyi sgom gra bcom pa'i dmag la 'byon skabs dpal o DyAn chen pos gnang ba'i rnam sras zhi drag gnyis las zhi ba
ljang yul ma'am sprin gseb mar grags pa ser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang / 14drag po yang gsang mdung dmar can phyag mtshan bzhi pa las mkhan dang bcas pa'i gtso 'khor gnyis
kyi rjes gnang / 15rgyal ba stag lung pa nas brgyud pa'i rnam sras rigs chen brgyad du grags pa'i nang nas/ rnam sras dmar po gsung mchog lus ngan po snyan grags sgrub
kyi rjes gnang dang / stang lung pa'i yi ge'i steng nas a pa ra tsi ta dkar po dpa' gcig gi rjes su gnang ba rnams legs par nos nas rgyab brten lung gi skor la/ gnod sbyin
gyi sde dbon chen po gar mkhan mchog gi rtog pa/ (dbang )brtag pa gnyis dang le'u bcu drug pa kha che'i mkhas pa chen po dha na gupta dang rab zhi lo tsA bas lhun gyis
grub pa'i gtsug lag khang mtho gling

'dzam gling rgyan du bsgyur ba/ rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las sna tshogs sgrub pa le'u nyi shu rtsa bdun pa/ gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi rgyud rin chen 'byung
ba le'u bcu dgu pa rgya gar gyi paNDi ta kha che dgon pa ba dang lo tsA ba mnga' ris pa ye shes sdes bsgyur ba/ sna tshogs dag pa'i rgyud le'u sum cu pa slob dpon 'gro
bzang snying pos mdzad pa zangs dkar lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ 'di gleng gzhi'i skabs slob dpon gang gis mdzad na 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad ces dang rgyud kyi rdzogs mtshams
su mdzad pa po bshad pa mthun par byung yang skye rgyud kyi le'u'i skabs slob dpon 'gro bzang snying pos bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje la zhus par bshad pa cung zad
'gal ba ltar snang yang gsung ba po phyag na rdo rje dang 'gro bzang snying pos de'i bka' bsdus par mdzad pa'i sgra bshad pa 'dra'o/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di gnyis
kyi bar du sna tshogs dag pa'i rgyud le'ur nyer dgu pa dang 'gro bzang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gser 'od 'bar ba gnyis 'dug kyang dpe ma 'byor bas ma thob/ 'gro bzang
snying pos mdzad pa'i zhi ba bde byed lha dgu'i sgrub thabs gser 'od 'bar ba'i TI ka sems can dbul ba rnams kyi don du zhi ba nor sgrub las sbyor dang bcas pa bshad zin
to'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras drag byed seng zhon khros pa'i phrin las sgrub tshul bstan pa la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung bar gyur cig
gi mtha' can/ 'khor klu brgyad kyis ma bskor bar sgrol byed nag po/ khyab 'jug lha mo dpal tshul gnod sbyin gyi dmag dpung dang bcas pa snang ngo /des mdzad pa'i rnam thos
sras bde byed kyi rtog pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can paNDi ta te dza de wa dang

lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa shes rab kyis zhus shing bsgyur ba/ rnam sras ser chen phyag mtshan rin po che'i be con dang ne'u le 'dzin pa zhig snang /'gor bcom ldan 'das
dpal phyag na rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo dngos grub kyi 'byung gnas zhes yod pa shu raM ka warmas mdzad pa'i zhi ba bde byed ser po lha dgu'i man ngag yid bzhin (dbang )nor
bu'i sgrub thabs zhes pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ de'i TI ka slob dpon shu raM ka warmas mdzad pa'i sgrub yig 'di la gnyis te zhes pa 'gor yod pa la zab mo yin pas gsang
bar zhu'i mtha' can/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di gnyis kyi bar du bde byed kyi cho ga sna tshogs pa'i mdzod dang dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa'i lus ngan
po'i sgrub thabs thar lo'i 'gyur gnyis 'dug pa dpe ma 'byor bas ma thob/shog dril drug pa zhes pa nam mkha' mdzod kyi sgrub thabs la nang gses kyi sku gdung (kong )rgyal
mtshan gyi sgrub thabs te bsnyen pa'i cho ga gsung chos kyi dung sgrub (kong )pa'i cho ga tsitta rin po che thugs (kong )sgrub pa'i cho ga 'chi med yon tan (kong )sgrub
pa'i cho ga spu gris bsad (kong )pa phrin las sgrub pa'i cho ga bum pa bzang po'i dngos grub mthar thug bang mdzod sgrub (kong )pa'i cho ga rnams rgya gar shar phyogs kyi
paNDi ta te dza de was mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba/ de'i gsal byed zangs dkar lo tsA bas mdzad pa la sku gzugs kyi rgyal mtshan
(kong )la brten nas rgyal po zhal dngos su blta ba'i shog dril/ gsung dbyangs chos kyi dung la brten (kong )nas snyan grags kyi rgyun sgrub pa'i shog dril/ tsitta

rin po che thugs kyi sgrub pa la brten nas (kong )rgyal po dang tshangs pa'i bu mo'ang 'gugs pa'i shog dril/ yon tan shel gyi bum par brten nas 'chi med (kong )kyi tshe sgrub
pa'i shog dril/ phrin las drag po gnam lcags kyi spu gri la brten nas (kong )dgra srog myur du gcod pa'i shog dril/ mthar thug gter gyi bum pa la brten nas dgos (kong
)'dod kun 'byung nam mkha' mdzod bsgrub pa'i shog dril/ mjug tu gang las brgyud (kong )kyi lo rgyus nyung ngu dang 'khor lo bri tshul gyi yig chung dang bcas pa/ 'di gnyis
kyi bar du khro los kong bu ri pa la zhus pa'i shog dril drug gi yi ge zur pa zhig rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig tu thebs kyang dpe ma 'byor bas ma thob/ bsnyen pa'i gnad
snying du dril ba/ sgrub pa'i gnad snying du dril ba/ srog gnad la dbab pa ste don gsum gyi man ngag rnam sras snying dril lam snying dang 'dra ba'i gnad kyi yi ge khra
rgya gar du gtsigs po cher byas te rin po che sna lnga'i khu bas bris pas khra bo zhes pa'i ming thogs skad/bo/ 'di gnyis kyi bar na rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na gnod
sbyin brel phongs kyi mnan thabs gur ga de was mdzad pa 'dug kyang dpe ma 'byor bas ma thob/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba'i mgul khug  mgul khug sro ma can gyi kha gsal ma byung
yang dpe dang gsan yig zhus dag pher bas yid ches su byas so// sro ma can la rnam sras gser chen gyi gsang sgrub rin po che'i khang pa brtsegs pa zhes bya ba rdzogs byang
gi mtha' can/ rnam sras ljang ser be con ma'i thugs (dbang )sgrub gsang sgrub rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi gsang ba'i man ngag ces par nang gses kyi
dngos grub kyi gzhi bzung ba/ rten gzugs pa/ gsham bu bdun gyis

dngos grub bsdu ba/ tshe sgrub pa/ bse rag kha 'ching ba dang bcas pa 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa yin gyi mtha' can/ sna tshogs dag pa'i rgyud las gang la dmigs pa'i lingga

pa ra dzi ta'i dngos grub bsgrub pa la bar du gcod pa'i gnod sbyin lag

spun mnan pa/ mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di'i rjes su 'khor lo sogs kyi zhal gdams/ a pa ra gsum gyi dbye ba/ sgrub thabs mtshal min ngag dbang dgyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa
gsum 'dug pa dpe ma 'byor pas lung ma thob/cho ga phyag len gyi skor la/ 'gor bcom ldan 'das dpal phyag na rdo rje zhes yod pa'i zhi drag spel ba'i sgrub thabs mkhas pa
tsandra shrIs mdzad pa mjug tu thugs sras lo tsA ba'i ka bstod le tshan gnyis btags pa/ 'di rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na gsham gyi bstod pa'i mdzad byang la brten nas
thugs sras lo tsA bas mdzad gsung ba 'dug kyang 'di tsandra shrIs mdzad nges yin pa khyab bdag zhwa lu pa gsung /rnam sras zhi drag sbrel ba'i cho ka bklag chog (dbang )mkhyen
rab rje'i phyag len ltar chos rje bco brgyad pa 'jam dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ rnam sras rigs mi gcig pa lnga'i sgrub thabs (dbang )gsal bar bstan pa'i dgos pa kun tshang
gnyags dbon rin po ches mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i rnam sras zhi drag rnams mchod (dbang )pa'i cho ga rin po che'i gter zhes bya ba/ rnam sras zhi drag rnams kyi mchod
chog rjes gnang dang bcas pa skyor mo lung pa mkhan chen chos rgyal dpal bzang gi mchod g.yog nam mkha' seng ge sa mdzad pa  'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na nam mkha'
grags zhes snang ba yig skyon shor ram snyam/rnam sras ser chen gyi gtor chog mchod phreng bstod pa dang bcas pa stag tshang lo chen shes rab rin chen gyis mdzad pa/
'gor dngos grub chen po sgrub pa'i dus zhes yod pa'i rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi gsang mdos kha che dgon pa bas mdzad pa/ rnam thos sras kyi gsang mdos rgyas pa
kha che'i rigs kyi mkhan po gzi brjid lha dang paNDi ta

te tsa de wa dang bod kyi lo tsA ba zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyis kha che khri brtan du bsgyur ba/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na bar 'dir gsang mdos chung ba zhig 'dug
pa dpe ma 'byor bas ma thob/au DyAn chen po padmas khram thogs nag po'i rgyud dang yon tan 'byung ba'i rgyud la brten nas mdzad pa'i gnod sbyin rgyal po rnam thos sras
kyi gsang mdos sam stong mdos rgyal po'i dpung bzlog chen mo bal po ba su dha ra la gnang / des gnubs sangs rgyas ye shes la gnang ba nyug gi rdo rje sgrom bu la gter du
sbas pa/ phyogs bzhir drag po'i g.yal bzlog dmag dpon gyi mdos rnams/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di'i rjes su lus ngan po'i bzlog mdos au DyAn chen pos mdzad pa dang
dge slong dkon mchog ye shes kyis mdzad pa'i mdos rgyas pa zer ba 'dug pa dpe ma 'byor pas ma thob/tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i bkra shis khyab bdag rdor 'dzin
ma/ sa skya khri chen kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i zhi ba'i sgrub thabs gtso bor ston pa'i be bum dkar chag zab don nor bu'i me long / des mdzad pa'i rnam sras dbang
drag gi yi ge'i skor gtso bor ston pa'i dkar chag snyan brgyud gser gyi za ma tog mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i dpal chos skyong ba'i srung ma rnam
thos sras rigs mi 'dra ba lnga phrag gsum gyi rjes gnang gi cho ga nor 'dzin dpal mo'i rgyan phreng / mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa'i rnam sras lnga phrag
gsum gyi rjes gnang gi chog khrigs dngos grub 'dod 'jo/ stag lung pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i rnam thos sras rigs chen brgyad kyi rjes

gnang gi chog khrigs bstod pa dang bcas pa/ des mdzad pa'i a pa ra dzi ta'i rjes gnang gi yi ge dang bcas pa rnams legs par nos pa las/ zangs dkar lo tsA bas stod kyi phyogs
su thog mar gnang zhing gtum ston blo gros grags nas brgyud pa'i rnam sras stod lugs sam bya sder lugs su grags pa'i zhi ba bde byed ser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che dgon
pa ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ gtum ston blo gros grags/ gtum mgon po yon tan/ lung khu dgon pa/ mkhan po lung ston/ slob dpon legs pa'i shes rab/ bya
sder ba byang chub rin chen/ bya sder ba byang chub gzhon nu/ mang mkhar ba blo bzang dkar mo/ mang mkhar ba blo bzang grags pa/ bzang ldan mkhan chen shAkya blo gros/ 'bul
dpon rdo rje rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dpal dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje
'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rin chen mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang
lhun grub/ rmor chen mkhas grub kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen
la stsal to/ /yang na tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po

nas/ rin po che bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga rin po che mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra'o/ /!/ /zangs dkar
lo tsA bas smad kyi char g.yor po jo ston la gnang bas smad lugs su grags pa'i rgyal po chen po ngal gsos po zhi ba bde byed ser chen lha dgu dang drag byed bzhon pa
med pa klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rjes gnang bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i phyag len ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba yan gong ltar la/ de nas g.yor po jo
ston/ bcur bsod nams rin chen/ rje btsun btsong kha pa'i gsan yig na mi 'dug pas chad pa 'dra/'byed phu ba padma bkra shis/ stag pa lha rje jo bzang / khro phu lo tsA ba/
gnubs byams pa'i dpal/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug khro phu sems dpa' chen po/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras sems
dpa' chen po/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub dpal bzang / chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ sku zhang rin po che mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub dpal bzang / de las rje btsun
rdo ring pa chen po dang chos rje bkra shis dpal 'byor gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ de nas brgyud tshul le tshan rnams gong dang 'dra/
yang na mkhyen rab rin po che nas/ sku zhang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ 'jam dbyangs byang gling chos rje bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/
yang na byang gling rje nas/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab

thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal nas/ mkhas grub rin chen bsod nams 'phel/ stag tshang lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ rje btsun yab chos rgyal rin chen dpal bzang po/ tshar
chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na khro phu lo tsA ba nas/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa/ mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/
mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal ba phyag na/ mkhan chen kun dga' blo gros/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po man 'dra/ yang
na rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon kA ma ru pa/ slob dpon kahna pa/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang la rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa dge 'dun
bkra shis kyi gsan yig dang chog khrigs dngos grub 'dod 'jo na karna zhes pa 'dug slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che sadzdza na/ kha che
te dza de wa/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ zhu sa skya pa/ jo btsun grags pa seng ge rgya ston grub pa po/ sngags rams pa'i gsan yig na rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus zhes snang
rgyal dbang gsung /rgya ston grub mchog bla ma rdo rje dpal/ khro phu sems dpa' chen po man 'dra/ yang skyor mo lung pa'i phyag len ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon
'gro bzang snying po nas/ grub chen bhriM ga ra wa ti/ kha che dgon pa ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ g.yor po jo ston rdo rje rtse mo/ sbas ti dgra bcom pa sems

dpa' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab seng ge bsam yas pa tshul khrims dbang phyug se ba can pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa/
dga' ldan phug pa blo bzang grags pa/ de gnyis ka las mkhan chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ de nas paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dmar ba kun dga' tshe 'phel/ spyan snga shAkya
rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ rnam sras kyi rjes gnang lnga phrag gsum pa dngos grub 'dod 'jo ma gtogs pa'i rtags med pa'i lung yongs rdzogs
dang dbang gi rtags yod pa rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po yan gong du smos pa'i smad lugs kyi brgyud pa'i rnam grangs ltar la/ de nas mkhan btsun
grub pa'i dbang phyug mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ bstan pa'i srog shing spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dpal rdo rje kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams
mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun chen po bsod nams dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan
chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /dbang gi rtags yod pa'i brgyud lugs gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan nas/ khyab bdag zhwa lu pa man
'dra'o/ /kong gi rtags yod pa'i

lung brgyud ni/ kha che te dza de wa nas/ kaM po dzi/ su ma ti kIrti/ kong bu ri pa/ khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal man 'dra/ ra'i rtags yod pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen
kun dga' blo gros yan gong ltar la/ de nas paN chen bsod nams blo gros/ shambhar rin po che kun dga' sangs rgyas/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ 'brom gyi
rtags yod pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gsang ba'i bdag po/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ lo tsA ba dbas manydzu shrI/ la gsum rgyal ba byang chub/ de las paNDi ta kha che dkar pos
bod du zhus/ de nas zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ mchims yul smad kyi 'brom sde nyi ma/ dge bshes lo tsA ba/ sle'u mtshur ston/ sle'u ston pa/ dge bshes dbu gru ston smon lam/
phrin las jo sras nas rim par brgyud de/ shambhar rin po che kun dga' sangs rgyas/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ zhi ba bde byed ser po 'di dang 'brel pa'i drag
po'i rjes gnang shin tu bka' gnyan pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhyen rab chos rje nas/ sku zhang rin chen mchog grub/ 'jam dbyangs byang gling rje/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug

su len dgos tshul snang ngo / /yang drag po dang ma 'brel ba'i rnam sras ser chen smad lugs kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ mkhan chen kun dga' blo gros yan gong
ltar la/ de nas mkhan chen ngag dbang lhun grub bkra shis/ mkhan chen

tsA ba'i gong khug sro ma can gyi zab chos gsang sgrub ljang ser be con can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal yan rnam sras ser chen ltar

ni/ spyan snga chos kyi rgya

sras mthing kha lha bco lnga/ rnam sras dmar ser las mkhan mdung dmar can dang bcas pa/ gar mkhan mchog ljang gu zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad pa/ dmar smug zhal gsum phyag

gsum pa'i rjes gnang yongs su rdzogs pa chog sgrig nor 'dzin dpal mo'i rgyan phreng gi lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po yan gong du
smos pa'i smad lugs kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa'i rnam grangs ltar las/ de nas rje btsun bod mkhar ba chen po mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ snyan brgyud srog shing spyan
snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang chen po dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ lha khang mkhan chen don grub legs bzang / ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun
bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen dpal ldan

chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na a pa ra tsitta'i rjes gnang lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa rdo rje 'chang / gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/
rgyal po intra bhU ti/ jo bo nA ro pa chen po/ slob dpon dza wa ri pa/ slob dpon pra wa hasti/ bal po ba su dha ra/ jo bo rje a ti sha/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ pu
rang pa dge slong puNye dha ri/ rgya lcags ri gong kha pa/ chos rgyal zla 'od gzhon nu/ phag gru rdo rje rgyal po/ rgyal ba stag lung thang pa/ sku yal ba/ rje sangs rgyas
yar byon/ sangs rgyas dbon/ lha rin po che/ u rgyan mgon po/ ratna a ka ra/ grags pa'i mtshan can/ rje mi g.yo mgon po/ kun spangs grags pa/ 'jig rten mgon po/ padma
rgyal po/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ rje stag lung pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ 'dren mchog ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab
byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /nor chen rigs la nor bu bzang la sogs/ /'dzad
med dbyig gi rgyun du byin brlabs pas/ /sems can dbul ba'i sdug bsngal sel ba'i lha/ /rmugs 'dzin gnod sbyin zhi drag rnam pa mang / /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi
ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ nor can gyi rigs kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste bcu pa'o/ // /lnga pa rgyas pa'i rigs sam glang po che'i
rigs sam ban glang gi rigs

ni/ lngas rtsen dang 'phrog ma bu lnga brgya dang bcas pa dang / srin mo chen mo bzhi la sogs pa rnams ni ma byung ngo / /drug pa 'jig rten pa'i rigs ni/ lha dang lha ma yin
la sogs pa rnams te/ de rnams kyang 'dir thos pa med do/ /rgyas pa'i rigs la bu tsha 'phen pa dang / /longs spyod 'phel ba lngas rtsen la sogs dang / /'jig rten lha dang
lha min srog snying phul/ /ston pas byin brlabs bklags pas dngos grub ster/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ bya ba'i rgyud
kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim rnams song nas/ rgyud sde gnyis pa spyod pa'i rgyud kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim la/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub
pa las bstan pa'i lha rigs ni 'dir ma byung la/ rigs kyi bdag po ni 'jam dpal la sogs pa ste/ 'dir paN chen thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil
dang mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang dkyil 'khor gyi dbang gi brjed tho bklag chog yid kyi mun sel gyi steng nas/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs
a ra pa tsa na lha lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa/ gsang bdag phyag
na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ paNDi ta rab 'byor bskyangs/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon shes rab bskyangs/ slob dpon zhi ba snying po/ dge mtshan bshes
gnyen/ mkhas pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddhA ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen

bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos
kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ gan pa rin rgyal/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dol po kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ bla ma byang chub seng ge shar chen ye
shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo rje
'chang sangs rgyas seng ge de las thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang dang / mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i dbang phyug kun dga' chos 'phel/ mkhas btsun grub pa'i rtser son kun dga' bstan
'dzin/ bka' drin mtshungs med de nyid las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis mnos so/ /yang na mkhan chen bsod nams dpal ldan pa'i gsan yul gyi bla ma gang yin brtag bsod nams
dpal ldan nas/ thar rtse mkhan chen nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ 'jam dbyangs chos kyi bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ratna wardha/
lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra/ yang na lo chen rin chen bzang po nas/ dbus pa dge ser/ gnam kha'u pa/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po

che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ dga' ldan slob dpon mi pham pa/ khams chen rgan mo lhas pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' dpal/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma tshul
khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang / bla ma byang chub seng ge shar chen man 'dra'o/ /rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil dang / thar rtse pa dang mkhan
chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa gsum char gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i lung yang thos/ /!/ /paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge'i
steng nas 'jam dbyangs dmar ser a pa ra tsa na'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po 'jam dbyangs/ slob dpon chen po dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/
ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya
paNDi ta chen po/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ rje btsun rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de sras a  gong dkar ba'i gsan yig tu a kA ra siddhi zhes snang ngo / /kA
ra skye med grub pa/ brag kha ba grags pa seng ge bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub dang shar khang pa gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis char las brang
ti pa paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod

nams lhun grub/ ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje/ khri chen bsod nams brtan 'dzin dbang po/ chos rje bkra shis dpal ldan/ rje bla ma dam pa kun dga' rin chen/ mkhas grub dam pa
sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ 'jam dpal dbyangs dngos tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la lan gsum gyi bar du stsal to/ /yang na mkhan chen sangs rgyas
phun tshogs nas/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/ de las bdag gis mnos so/ /yang na mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub nas/ sa lo tsA ba/ sngags 'chang ngag gi
dbang po kun dga' rin chen/ de sras sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug ngag dbang kun
dga' bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis nas/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/
des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis nas/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal
ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ gu ge paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo tsA ba 'jam dpal
rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ khri chen pa man

'dra/ yang na ratna wardha nas/ lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse paN chen man 'dra/ yang na sa paNDi ta nas/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan
pa/ bla ma bsod nams skyabs/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen kun bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ mtshungs
med ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub pa man 'dra/ yang na 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge
paN chen man 'dra'o/ /'di'i sgrub thabs sa paN gyis mdzad pa dang / rjes gnang bya tshul rje btsun sangs rin gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rjes su gnang ba'ang mkhan
po chen po dpal ldan chos skyong las bdag gis tshar gcig mnos so/ /lus ngag spyod dang rtse gcig ting nge 'dzin/ /cha mnyam spyod pa la dga'i gdul bya'i ngor/ /legs par
gsungs pa ma rig mun sel lha/ /'gro ba smin byed dbang dang rjes gnang gnyis/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ spyod pa'i rgyud
kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste bcu gcig pa'o/ // /rgyud sde gsum pa rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la de nyid 'dus pa dang dpal mchog la sogs pa nas bstan pa'i
yi dam gyi lha mang du mchis pa las/ 'dir ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi brjid kyi rgyal po'i brtag pa dang pos dngos bstan/ bstan bya'i gtso bo rgyal ba gnyis
pa rje btsun kun dga' bzang po pas mdzad pa'i

gzhan phan mtha' yas dang / dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i mtshams sbyor blo gsal kun dga'i steng nas kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud
pa la/ A di bhU mi nA ya sya pa rampa raH/ bha ga wAM bai ro tsa naH/ gu hya pa ti badzra pA NiH/ rA dzA pra kA sha tsandraH/ A tsArYa pra bhU ti pA li taH/ ma hA siddho
nanda garbhaH/ ma hA paNDi ta pradznyA pA li taH/ A tsArYa shanti garbhaH/ ka lyA Na ni mitta mi traH/ A tsArYa su kha sya badzraH/ thog mar sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom
ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ slob dpon rab 'byor bskyangs/ grub chen kun dga' snying po/ mkhas pa chen po shes
rab bskyangs/ dge mtshan bshes gnyen/ slob dpon bde ba'i rdo rje/ ArYa shraddhA ka ra warmaH/ lo ka sya tsakShu ratna bha draH/ she lo pa ri gu Na shI laH/ lo tsA ba ma
ti kIrtiH/ shrI ma hA bhU mi paNDa rA nanda garbhaH/ bhaTTA ra ka ratna kIrti dhwa dzaH/ bhU mI paNDa ra paNDi tA nanda dhwa dzaH/ sambha ra bhA ba kA nanda shrIH/ ma hA
shru taM pu Nya sthi raH/ jo bo dad byed go cha/ 'jig rten gyi mig rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ dpal sa skya pa chen
po kun dga' snying po/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ ti shryA
nanda ma tiH/ sanggu ru puNya dhwa dzaH/ swA mya tri gu ha ka ma tisthi raH/ gu ru shrI wAnytsatshI laH/ dharmA swA mI dznyA na dhwa dzaH/ ma hA badzra dha rA nanda
bha draH/ ma hA sa twa ratna dhwa dzaH/ puNya siM ha/ to bha ya buddha ratnaH/ swA mA buddha singhaH

/ ma hA paNDi ta ga ga na shrI bha draH/ ti shrI kun  rmor chen pa'i gsan yig tu 'di ma byung /dga' blo gros/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje ri khrod pa blo gros
brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang chen po kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams seng
ge de gnyis ka las sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / swA myA kA sha buddhaH/ ma hA se na khaM shrI bha dra wA/ saddharma saM
kalpa siddhaH/ to bha yo pa dhyA ya buddha lakShmIH/ ma hA pUrba shA sa na dha raH/ badzra satwa mangga laM ni rA bho gaH/ te na nashshI la ratna ma wo tsa traH/ wA buddha
lakShmyAtma hA pUrba buddha shA sa na dha ra shtsa shA sa na dha ra ni rA bho ga dwA yA shU taM/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ se chen nam mkha' dpal bzang ngam/ dam chos
bsam 'grub/ gnyis kas mkhan sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ shar chen sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin/ rdo rje sems dpa' bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/
/yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ shar chen sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin dang bstan 'dzin lhun grub gnyis kyis gsan/ pashtsi ma shtsa mangga la ni rA bho ga dwA bhyaM/
ma ho pa dhyA ya buddha shrI bha dre Na shU taM/ ta to mA shru taM/ wA buddha lakShmyA ta/ A nanda shA sa na dha raH/ buddha shrI bha draH/ ta to mA/ wA bhaTTA ra ka buddha
ratnA ta/ manydzu gho Sha buddha singhaH/ ma hA pa Tu ga ga na shrI bha draH/ phyi ma dang bkra shis lhun grub gnyis ka las/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang pas gsan/
de las bdag gis so/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / de las bdag gis so/ yang na rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen

nas/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / ma hA pUrba mai tyA nanda mangga laM/ pUrba pradznyA saM bha wa/ pa Tu bha dantA nanda pA dhuH/ paNDi
ta siddho buddha lakShmI pashtsi ma pArba tsa sa mA naH/ wA ma hA ngor badzra dhA rA nanda bha drA ta/ A nande shwa raH/ nA ya kotti ma ratna wardha/ swa mi de wotta ma singhaH/
buddha singha pashtsi ma sA ma naH/ shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun kun dga' legs pa/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun
tshogs man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog seng ge buddha singha man
'dra'o/ /pu naHkaShmi ra ne ta sya tantra ni/ badzra satwaH/ a nu pa ma rakShi ta/ ratnA ka ra shAntaH/ a bha ya/ badzrA sa naM/ bi khyA ta de baH/ ma hA paNDi ta shAkya
shrI/ bi bhU ti tsandraH/ tsa ma ra se nA lo tsA puNya singhaH/ ratna shrI/ she la gu ha puNya shrI/ sha ba ra ma tisthi raH/ yang kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
sems dpa'/ dpe med bsrungs pa/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ 'jigs  rgyal dbang gsan yig tu bhaskar de bzhes byung ngo / /med rdo rje gdan pa/ rnam par bshad pa'i lha/ paNDi
ta chen po shAkya shrI/ rab 'byor zla ba/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba bsod nams seng ge dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ gu ru shrI
wanytsatshI laH/ dharmA sya swA mi dznyA na dhwa dzaH/ badzra dha rA nanda bha dra pashtsi ma pUrba sa mAnaH/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos kyi rje ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /chag lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig phyag na

rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ rdo rje gdan pa/ a bha yA ka ra/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ niShka laM kardo rje gdan
pa chung ba/ ra wendra/ chag lo tsA ba chos kyi dpal/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba bsod nams seng ge paNDi ta rdor she/ zhang dkon mchog dpal man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /yang na g.yag
sde lo tsA ba nas/ lo mchog bag ston/ tshul rgyal/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra'o/ /stod lugs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig rnam par snang mdzad/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ pradznyA pa lI ta/ pradznyA
bo dhi/ mukti ko Sha/ dharma pa la/ dI paM ka ra/ shrI dznyA na/ do pa sgom chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi 'od/ de'i sras snur badzra singha
/ snur byang chub 'od/ snur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rin chen shes rab/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge phyar bu ba zhwa ser rtse ring / thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen
grub/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /yang na snur nyi 'od nas/ gshen rdor
seng / glan chos 'byung / gtum ston shAkya 'bum/ bla ma 'dzim pa rin chen shes rab/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge man 'dra'o/ /yang na pradznyA pA li ta nas/ go mi dge
bsnyen/ shAkya dznyA na/ jo bo rje man 'dra/ yang na pradznyA pA li ta nas/ dharma pA la/ rab 'byor

bskyangs/ jo bo rje man gong ltar ro/ /yang na snur nyi 'od nas/ rtsa skya ston grags/ slob dpon ston 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ dge sdings pa chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen
'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che man 'dra/ yang na sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ ye shes rdo rje/ kun dga' snying po man gong dang 'dra/ yang na rnam
par snang mdzad/ dze tA ri pa/ kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ nA ya ka pa/ mai tri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ niShka laM kade wendra/ chag lo chos rje dpal/ g.yag sde
lo tsA ba bsod nams seng ge lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston man 'dra'o/ /smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon
kun dga' snying po yan gong ltar las/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdo rje/ shraddhA ka ra warmA/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ sum ston ye 'bar/
gnyal ston tshul 'bar/ thod pa dben tsha grags/ thod pa 'od zer/ ri lung phug pa chos mgon/ bla ma blo ldan seng ge bla ma 'phags 'od/ bod btsun dbu se/bu ston man sngar
dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa lha bcu gsum pa'i dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab

pa sgom chen zer ba'ang

byung /sgom chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi/ snur chen nyam 'od/ sras badzra singha / snur byang chub 'od/ snur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ snur ye rgyal/ snur chos 'phags rgyal
mtshan/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ slob dpon rgyal mtshan grags/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen buddha ratna/ sangs rgyas seng
ge ma hA paNDi ta ga ga na shrI bha dra/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ de las bla ma lhun grub bkra shis/ mnga' ris glo bo pa/de las mkhas
btsun kun dga' legs pa/ chu 'dus pa/mkhas grub buddha lakShmIM/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs

dga' chos 'phel gyis gsan nam snyam/ de las mkhas btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ kun dbang / 'dren mchog rje lha mchog
seng ge buddha singha man 'dra'o/ /!/ /thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i steng nas ngan song sbyong ba'i rgyud nas bshad
pa'i kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor/ 1shAkya thub pa sku'i dkyil 'khor/ 2tshe dpag med gsung gi dkyil 'khor/ 3phyag na rdo rje thugs kyi dkyil 'khor/ 4me ltar 'bar ba yon

bcas pa
