seng ge mr-i du swa ra ratna ni rA bho gaH/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/mokShA gra pa Tu siddha ga ga na shrI bha draH/ thar rtse pa mkhas grub nam mkha' dpal
bzang /bhU mi paNDra ka manydzu gho ShA nanda puNya ni rA bho ga maM ga

la kIrti dhwa dzaH/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan/ta to gu ru dwi tri mA tra a labdhe Na pu narnishtsi ta labdha shtsa
bandhaH/ tata shrI bhU mI paNDa ka wA gindrA nanda mangga laM/ ma ho pra dhyA ya mai tri shI la shrI bha draH/ mokShA gra ma ho pA dhyA ya ga ga na saM kalpa siddhaH/ ma
hA pra sA da sarba dznyA buddha shrI bha draH/ de nas bla ma gnyis gsum tsam ma rnyed pas slar nges par rnyed pa dang sbrel/ de nas dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga'
bkra shis/ mkhan chen byams pa tshul khrims dpal bzang / thar rtse mkhan chen nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ drin chen thams cad mkhyen pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / te nAtma dwande
shI la ratnaM pra da dAta/ bA ratna ni rA bho gA ta/ pUrba gr-i ha pradznyA dhwa dzaH/ mokShA gra pashtsi ma pUrba bta/ tsa pa ra ma de wa singhA ta/ pUrba gr-i ha pashtsi
ma sa mA naH/ bA ratna ni rA bho gAta/ swA mi buddhi singhaH/ mokShA gra pashtsi ma sa mA naH/ des bdag btsun pa tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na dkon mchog
lhun grub nas/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse pa man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na lha mchog seng ge nas/ shar khang pa man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub
nas/ rjes sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse pa man 'dra/ bi bhA Sha a bha yA ka rAta/ su tsA rA ka ra guptaH/ shu bha ka ra guptaH/ ratna rakShI ta/ ma tu la lo tsA siddha shrIH/
mkhas pa shAkya badzraH/ ma dhya buddha lakShaH/ lo ka tsakShu rutta ma bAM/ skyi shAsta pashtsi ma pUrba bta/ wA a bha yA ka rAta/ nA ya kaH/ yang na 'jigs med 'byung
gnas nas/ legs spyod 'byung gnas sbas pa/ dge byed sbas pa/ rin chen bsrung ba/ zhang 'jig rten du sgrog pa gru pa dpal/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs

rgyas 'bum/ 'jig rten mig mchog ldan/ skyi ston man snga ma bzhin no/ yang na 'jigs med 'byung gnas nas/ da  'dren pa stobs bcu'i dpal/sha pa la shrIH/ bi bhakSha ta de wa
pashtsi motta ma pa ta/ bA paNDi ta shAkya shrI yAH/ glan go dantaH/ gnyags badzra dha raH/ khams shAsta lho tshad pa ratna ratna/ lo ka tsakShu utta mAM nishtsa sa ma naH/
pu naHpanytsa maNDa la panytsa  mkha' 'gro lnga 'khor lo sgyur drug bsrung ba lnga rnams so sor phye bas te lnga/da shi ka bhe da mA le/ a bha yA ka raH/ rnam bshad lha
man gong ltar ro/ yang na mkhas pa shAkya dpal nas/ glan ba so ba/ gnyags rdo rje 'dzin pa/ khams ston lho tshad pa dkon mchog rin chen/ 'jig rten mig mchog ldan pa man
'dra/ yang dkyil 'khor lnga bcu rtsa lngar dbye ba'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jigs med 'byung gnas/ shAkya rakShi taH/ gau taM gu ruH/ bi bhU ti tsandraH/ go de wa shrIH/ kShanti
shrIH/ paNDi ta buddha shrIH/ paNDi ta nA thaH/ skyi shasta ni shtsa sa mA naH/ bA maNDa lAShTa biM shatsa  yang na dkyil 'khor nyer brgyad du bsdus pa'i brgyud pa ni/ma
hA ra Shya  kye rdor lha dgu ma bzhi dang bcu bdun ma bzhi bdag med ma gnyis bde mchog gsum phag mo gsum bdud rtsi bzhi rnams re re bsdus so/ /mA le/ shAkya bsrungs pa/ gau
taM bla ma/ grags 'byor zla ba/ sa lha'i dpal/ bzod pa dpal/ mkhas pa sangs rgyas dpal/ mkhas pa mgon po/ skyi ston man 'dra/ paNDi ta shAkya shrI yaH/ dakShi Na sarba
dznyAH/ de wa gr-i ha shukla/ yar klungs pa bha ga wAn khangga sya/ alpaHpradznyA pra Ni dhiH/ gu ru bo dhi singha nishtsa sa mA naH/ ga bi mA la shrI yaH/ lo ka tsakShu
ma ti sthi raH/ bo dhi singha nishtsa sa mA naH/ mkhas pa shAkya dpal nas/ lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ lha khang dkar ru ba/ yar klungs pa bcom ldan ral

gri/ gcung po shes rab smon lam/ bla ma byang chub seng ge man 'dra/ yang na dri med dpal nas/ /'jig rten gyi mig blo gros brtan pa/ byang chub seng ge man 'dra/ ma hA paNDi
ta darpan A tsArYa sya ne ma ta kri yA sa mutstshA nAM maNDal panytsa ma tsa tu riM sha dAM mA la/ badzra dha raH/ dznyA na DA ki nI/ paNDi ta darpaN A tsArYaH/ sa manta
bha draH/ dznyA na dzyo tiH/ shrI hA nu mantaH thar rtse pa'i gsan yig na dpal yid kyi 'gram pa zhes bsgyur snang /shrI manydzu bha draH/ shrI bha draH/ dharma dzyo ti
bha draH/ mkhas pa chen po slob dpon 'gro ba'i me long lugs kyi bya ba yang dag par bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro
ma/ slob dpon mkhas pa 'gro ba'i me long / kun tu bzang po/ ye shes kyi glogadapal myur ba'i mtha'am/ 'jam dpal bzang po/ dpal bzang po/ chos kyi klog bzang po/ ma na dzI
wa bha draH/ go taM shrI bha draH/ shrI bi dza ya bha draH/ shrI ma da na bha dra pA daH/ shrI lakShmI bha dra pA daH/ ga ga na bha draH/ u da ka dzI wa bha draH/ shrI
harSha bha dra pA daH/ bha ga warbha draH/ dza ga ta A nanda dzI wa bha draH/ yid 'tsho ba bzang po/ ngag gi dpal bzang po/ dpal rnam rgyal bzang po/ dpal myos byed bzang
po'i zhabs/ dpal phun tshogs bzang po'i zhabs/ nam mkha' bzang po/ chu'i 'tsho ba bzang po/ dpal 'phrog byed bzang po'i zhabs/ skal ldan bzang po/ skye dgu kun dga'i 'tsho
ba bzang po/ ta syai pu tra ma hA bo dhi/ de'i sras byang chub chen po/sa bzang ArYa ku mA ra ma ti nishtsa sa mA naH/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros man 'dra'o/
/!/ /mkhas grub chen po khyung po rnal 'byor gyis rgya  gsum bal  lan bzhi ste du lan bdun byon te/ spyir yongs grags kyi bla ma

brgya dang lnga bcu/ rtsa ba'i bla ma bzhi/ 'gran gyi do med ye shes kyi DA ki ma rnam pa gnyis dang / grub thob kyi bla ma bcu gsum po rnams las smin grol gyi gdams pa mtha'
yas pa gsan pa rnams bshad sgrub gnyis su 'dus/ de dag gi brgyud 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab kyang / snga bu bzhi'am lnga/ phyi bu gcig rnams kyis bstan pa bzung ba las/
snga bu zhang sgom chos kyi seng ge dang / phyi bu mnyam med rin chen brtson 'grus gnyis kyis bstan pa bzung ba'i sgrub brgyud kyi gdams pa mkha' 'gro ma ni gu ma dang su
ka siddhi gnyis kyi gdams pa zab cing rgya che bar bzhugs pa las/ dang po mkha' 'gro ma ni gu ma'i gdams pa thob pa'i skor la/ smin byed dbang dang byin rlabs kyi skor/
grol byed zab mo khrid kyi skor/ rgyab brten lung gi skor/ bka' srung ye shes kyi mgon po'i skor dang bzhi las/ dang po smin byed la/ chos drug spyi'i dbang khog phub/ rgyud
sde lnga'i gtso bsdus kyi dbang ngam sgyu lus dbang mo che zhes bya ba ngo bo gcig la ming gi rnam grangs bzhi dang ldan pa'i dbang bskur gdams pa dang 'brel pa/ gdams
ngag dbang bskur dang 'brel pas mtha' brgyan pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu ma/
mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog tsog pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyen ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ 'gro mgon sangs rgyas ston
pa/ mkhas grub gtsang ma shangs ston/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rdo rje

gzhon nu/ mtshan ldan nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ byang sems sbyin pa bzang po/ grub chen thang stong rgyal po/ brgyud 'dzin blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub dpal ldan dar po/
rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen/ paN chen ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas/ mang thos bsod
nams chos 'phel/ grub thob sangs rgyas bstan pa/ thugs sras sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /'di yan la rtsa ba'i brgyud pa zhes bya'o/
/khrid gzhung dang 'brel bar nyon mongs pa'i rtsa mdud 'grol bar byed pa gtum mo'i dbang / nyin par gyi 'khrul pa bzlog pa'i phyir sgyu lus kyi dbang / gnyid kyi 'khrul
pa bzlog pa'i phyir rmi lam gyi dbang / gti mug gi mun pa bsang ba'i phyir 'od gsal bde chen gyi dbang / btsan thabs su 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir 'pho ba'i dbang / srid pa
bar do dag pa'i phyir bar do'i dbang ste  'di yan sgos bka' drug go/ gzhung shing chen mo dang 'brel ba'i bde mchog dbang bzhi lus bsgrigs kyang khog phub kyi grangs su
bgrang / bka' brgyad/ phyag chen ga'u ma'i dbang / bla ma lam khyer gyi dbang / yi dam lam khyer gyi dbang / sgyu ma lam khyer gyi dbang / lus sems 'chi med kyi dbang ste
phyag rgya chen po'i bka' lnga rnams legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhas grub gtsang ma shangs ston yan gong bzhin las/ de nas mkhas btsun rgyal mtshan 'bum pa/ 'jags
chen byams pa dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs

blo gros dpal bzang / 'jags chen kun dga' dpal bzang / kun mkhyen chos rgyal dpal bzang / 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ rdo ring kun
spangs chen po/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags man sngar dang 'dra'o/
/yang na mkhas grub gtsang ma shangs ston yan 'dra ba las/ de nas mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu/ de gnyis ka las mus chen nam mkha'i rnal
'byor ram nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / bla ma chos rgyal bkra shis/ 'khrul zhig byams pa sher bzang / tshar chen blo gsal
rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs skal ldan bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man sngar 'jags ma lugs dang 'dra'o/
/khog phub kyi nang tshan bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang bzhi lus bsgrigs kyi byin rlabs/ bde mchog lha bzhi dril sgrub kyi dbang / bde mchog gsang sgrub kyi dbang / rnam
'joms gsang sgrub phyag rdor gsang sgrub sogs gsang sgrub skor lnga bzhugs pa'i gsang sgrub dang po gsum po dang dbang bzhi gnyis te bka' lnga po 'di rnams thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ ngag dbang chos grags yan bshad ma thag pa'i 'jags ma lugs ltar las/ de nas byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis/
mang thos bsod nams chos

'phel/ rong po sangs rgyas bstan pa man 'dra'o/ /mkha' spyod ma dkar mo'i dbang / mkha' spyod ma dmar mo'i dbang / mkha' spyod gsum phrugs kyi dbang ste bka' gsum thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni ngag dbang chos grags yan bshad ma thag pa'i 'jags chen lugs ltar las/ de nas ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal ba lhun grub/ spro lung pa
bsod nams chos 'phel man 'dra'o/ /mkha' 'gro ma su kha siddhi byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / su kha siddhi/ khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog cog pa/ skyer
sgang pa/ gnyen ston pa/ chos rje ston pa ste brgyud pa rin chen sna bdun dang / de nas lung bstan thob pa lnga ni/ gtsang ma shangs ston pa/ rgyal mtshan 'bum pa/ byams
pa dpal/ blo gros dpal/ kun dga' dpal bzang ba ste/ de las bka' drin can bsod nams bzang po/ des mkhas grub chos kyi nyi ma/ des rje btsun ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/
rje kun dga' chos grags/ bla ma nam mkha' chos dar/ rje byams pa ngag dbang kun dga' don grub/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen rgyal ba lhun grub/ spro lung pa bsod nams chos 'phel man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /spyan ras gzigs gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa spyan
ras gzigs dbang phyug grub chen rA hu la gupta/ jo bo dI paM ka ra/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag song ba/ ba yu ba shes rab tshul khrims/ lce sgom

shes rab rdo rje/ skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyan ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ dbon ston brtson seng / 'gro mgon tshul khrims 'bum/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / mus
chen nam mkha' dbang phyug mtshan ldan nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po nas ngag dbang
chos grags kyi bar gong gi 'jags ma lugs kyi brgyud pa dang 'dra/ yang na ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas man 'dra/
yang na mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ paN chen nam dbang / mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ dpal sa skya
pa chen po kun dga' bsod nams/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rnam rgyal bzang po/ 'jig rten dbang phyug tshul khrims
bzang po/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /rta mgrin
gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku khro rgyal rta mchog sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ gter ston snye mo zhu yas/
de gnyis char las skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge de nas gnyen ston chos kyi shes rab/ sangs rgyas ston pa brtson 'grus seng ge shangs ston tshul khrims 'bum/ khyung po tshul
khrims mgon po/ rje

sangs rgyas seng ge sprul sku sangs rgyas rdo rje/ pha rgod thar pa dpal bzang / drin chen sangs rgyas rnam rgyal/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug rta ra ba bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags man ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas bzhugs pa'i rtsa ba'i brgyud pa dang 'dra/ yang na ngag
dbang chos grags nas/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal dbang lhun grub/ spro lung pa bsod nams chos 'phel man 'dra'o/ /gnyis pa grol byed khrid kyi skor
la/ mkhas grub rgyal mtshan 'bum gyi khrid yig dang / grub chen rin po che thang stong rgyal pos mdzad pa'i gnad yig snying po kun 'dus kyi steng nas rtsa ba ni gu chos
drug gi khrid/ yal ga lam khyer rnam gsum/ 'bras bu lus sems 'chi med/ sdong po phyag rgya chen po ga'u ma'i khrid rnams brgyud pa'i phyag bzhes dri ma med pas brgyan nas
legs par thob pa'i snga ma gsum gyi brgyud pa'ang / gong gi rtsa ba'i brgyud pa dang mthun no/ /gdams pa de rnams 'chad thabs kyi yi ge la/ ni gu chos drug gi dbang chog
'jug sgo yon tan kun 'byung kun mkhyen gangs khrod pas mdzad pa dang / chos drug gi sgos bka' so so'i phyag len ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ lam khyer gsum gyi
yi ge rgya gzhung / phyag chen ga'u ma'i dbang chog ngag chos pas mdzad pa/ chos drug khrid yig grub chen rin po che thang stong rgyal pos mdzad pa dang / rgyal mtshan 'bum
gyis mdzad pa/ chos drug gdan thog gcig ma

ngag chos pas mdzad pa/ lam khyer gsum gyi khrid yig 'bras bu lus sems 'chi med kyi khrid yig ga'u ma'i khrid yig rnams grub chen rin po ches mdzad pa/ mkha' spyod dkar dmar
phrugs gsum gyi yi ge gsang sgrub skor gsum gyi byin rlabs chos tshan gcig ma tshang ba rnams ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ thugs rje chen po gsang sgrub kyi sgrub
thabs mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs bya tshul/ lha bzhi dril sgrub kyi byin rlabs dang nyams su
len tshul/ mkha' 'gro ma su ka siddhi'i byin rlabs kyi yi ge rnams ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs gnas sbyar ma khyung pos mdzad pa kha skong
dang bcas pa/ tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs kha skong dang bcas pa/ 'gyur med bde chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi dam lam khyer gyi dbang gi brgyud 'debs zung 'jug rgyal
srid ma kha skong dang bcas pa/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs sku gsum bdun ldan ma/ yang sku gsum bdun ldan chung ba rnams kyi steng
nas dbang dang byin rlabs khrid stsal ba mdzad cing / de rnams kyi lung yang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gong gi dbang byin rlabs khrid so so'i brgyud pa'i skabs ltar rtsa
ba'i brgyud pa chen po dang 'dra'o/ /gsum pa rgyab brten lung gi skor la gdams pa 'di brgyud pa gang las byung ba'i 'byung khungs bstan pa'i sgo nas yid ches bskyed pa'i
phyir brgyud pa'i rnam thar skor dang / brgyud pa de las byung ba'i gdams pa

dngos kyi lung nos pa gnyis las/ dang po ni sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar rmog cog pas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu ma'i rnam thar/ mkhas
grub khyung po rnal 'byor gyi rnam thar rmog cog pa sogs bzhis bsdebs pa/ de'i lhan thabs dang gsang ba'i rnam thar/ mnyam med rin chen brtson 'grus kyi rnam thar rje rang
gis mdzad pa dang / skyer sgang pas mdzad pa gnyis/ skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge'i rnam thar rje rang gis mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas gnyen ston gyi rnam thar dge slong gzhon
nu seng ge la gnang ba/ chos rje sangs rgyas ston pa'i rnam thar brgyud 'dzin rnams kyi don du bkod pa/ shangs ston tshul khrims mgon po'i rnam thar rje rang gis mdzad
pa/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal gyi rnam thar dge bshes smon lam pas mdzad pa/ mkhas grub rdo rje gzhon nu'i rnam thar gsol 'debs chos kyi seng ge sa mdzad pa/ mtshan ldan
nam mkha'i rnal 'byor gyi rnam thar dge slong rin chen dar gyis mdzad pa/ grub chen thang stong rgyal po'i rnam thar 'khor ba dong sprugs thugs sras rin po ches mdzad
pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa ni ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro mas mdzad pa'i chos drug rdo rje'i tshig rkang 'gor skad gnyis shan sbyar dang bcas pa'i rjes su/ gang zhig brjod bral lhun
grub 'dus ma byas/ /zhes yod pa lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba la slar yang rin chen bzang pos gtan la phab pa/ khyung pos mdzad pa'i thems yig tshigs
bcad ma/ des mdzad pa'i thabs lam/ sgyu lus/ rmi lam/ 'od

gsal/ 'pho ba bar do dang bcas pa'i sgos skabs kyi yi ge 'phyugs med bar do gsum gyi gdams pa khyung po'i nyams myong ma/ 'od gsal la 'char sgo ngos 'dzin don dam mngon gyur
gzhan don lhun grub shog gi mtha' can/ gzhi lam 'bras gsum gnad drug go drug sogs bstan pa phyag chen rdo rje'i tshig rkang 'gor skad gnyis shan sbyar dang / bde chen lhun
grub 'dus ma byas zhes dang / tha mal shes pa khyod la phyag 'tshal lo zhes pa'i mtha' can sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang chen gyis mdzad pa glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/
phyag chen gyi dbang gi yi ge dbang bzhi'i zin bris yin no'i mtha' can/ lam khyer rnam gsum gyi rgya gzhung 'gor skad gnyis shan sbyar dang / gang gi bla ma mchog bsten
dbang thob pas zhes yod pa/ ye shes mkha' 'gro mas mdzad pa glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'gor bde chen rgyal po lhun grub 'dus ma byas/ /tshad med thugs rjes sems can
smin grol mdzad/ /ces yod pa'i khyad 'phags lam khyer rnam gsum gyi gdams pa rtsa ba'i sa bcad bzhis bstan pa/ mjug tu/ e ma bka' brgyud rtsod med 'di/ /zhes sogs yod pa/
'gor rgyal ba longs sku drug pa rdo rje 'chang / /zhes yod pa'i rgyud sde lnga'i mngon rtogs bsdus pa lo gsum gyis mi 'grub pa mi srid ces yod pa/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i
zhabs btud nas/ /bcom ldan bde mchog lha lnga yi/ /zhes yod pa'i bde mchog lha lnga'i mngon rtog khyung pos mdzad pa/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'khor
lo sdom pa'i tshogs mchod byed par 'dod pas zhes

yod pa'i bde mchog gi mchod phreng tshogs mchod dang 'brel ba tshul khrims mgon pos bkod pa/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi gsang sgrub nyams su len tshul ni gu ma'i khyad par gdams
pa/ rnam 'joms bka' rgya ma zhes pa rang lus bum pa dang snying gar lha sgom tshul yod pa khrus chu'i gdams pa shin tu zab pa yin no'i mtha' can/ sgyu ma lam rim gyi skor
la/ 'gor skad gnyis shan sbyar dang / gdod nas rang bzhin 'od gsal ba/ /dgos 'dod ma lus 'byung 'gyur zhing / /zhes yod pa'i sgyu ma lam rim ni gu mas mdzad pa ye shes
kyi mkha' 'gro ma de nyid dang lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar dang / rgyal ba rgya mtsho rdo rje 'chang / /khyed zhabs bdag gis gus
btud nas/ /sgyu ma lam rim gsal byed don/ /mdo dang rgyud las gsungs bzhin bris/ /zhes yod pa'i sgyu ma lam rim gyi 'grel pa gnyis mdzad pa dang 'gyur byang gong dang 'dra/
sgyu ma lam rim gyi sa bcad khyung pos yi ge ra bkod pa/ sgyu lus 'byams gcod kyi bsdus don don tshan bzhis bstan pa/ sgyu lus 'dzin pa rang grol 'gor ye shes kyi mkha'
'gro ni gu ma sgyu lus la gsum bzhi zhes yod pa/ mkha' spyod dkar mo'i dbang bskur gyi yi ge mkha' spyod dkar mo'i rgya gzhung skad gnyis shan sbyar can dI paM ka ras mdzad
pa rin bzang gi 'gyur/ yang mkha' spyod dkar mo'i sgrub thabs a ti sha'i lugs/ yang mkha' spyod ma mdun du bsgom pa'i yi ge khyung po'i lugs/ yang mdun du bla ma dang
de'i smin mtshams su mkha'

spyod ma bsgom ste 'od zer gyi spro bsdu la brten te dam tshig gso ba'i nyams chag bshags pa/ mkha' spyod kyi ril bu sgrub thabs chig brgyud ma/ mkha' spyod ma'i 'pho ba bya
tshul/ khyung pos mdzad pa'i mkha' spyod dmar mo'i sgos bka' drug gi nang tshan 'pho ba'i dbang bskur/ 'chi med kyi rgya gzhung DA ki mas mdzad pa/ 'gor skad gnyis dang
/ rgyal ba longs sku rdo rje 'chang chen gyis/ /'chi med ye shes rang sgra 'di skad thos/ /zhes yod pa lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba la rin bzang gis bcos
pa/ rmi lam gyi dbang chog che ba DA ki ma'i gsung khyung pos bkod pa/ gzhi lam 'bras gsum gyi tho chung gcig khyung pos DA ki ma la zhus pa/ lam khyer gsum gyi dbang chog
mdzad byang med pa/ 'pho ba'i man ngag nyung ngu / 'chi med kyi dbang chog mdzad byang med pa/ thugs rje chen po gsang sgrub kyi dbang chog 'gor lo ka dbang phyug gi
bka' zhes pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ lus 'chi med kyi dbang chog sems 'chi med kyi khrid yig mthar 'di las zab pa rgya bod gnyis na med gsungs pa/ sems 'chi med kyi zhal gdams
sangs rgyas ston pa'i gsung / gnad 'phyugs med bar do gsum gyi nyams len khyung po'i yi ge 'byams gcod khyung po'i thugs bcud rmog cog pas mdzad pa/ khyad 'phags sdom
pa bco lnga pa rgyas bsdus gsum khyung pos mdzad pa/ dbu ma yi ge bdun ma nA ros ni gu la gdams pa/ rang grol rtsa ba DA ki ma'i gsung khyung pos zhus pa glan dar mas bsgyur
ba/ sgyu lus gdan thog gcig ma chos rje sangs rgyas ston pa'i

gsung / 'od gsal 'char sgo ngos 'dzin/ sgyu lus sbyang ba rnam gsum khyung po'i yi ge khyung po'i gnas drug ces bya ba sangs rgyas ston pa'i gsung bzhin bkod ces pa'i mtha'
can/ phyag chen bskyed rim rlung dang bsre ba ji ltar 'dod kyang bla ma'i snang ba dang mi 'bral zhes yod pa/ maNDal bka' rgya ma dang rab gnas bka' rgya ma gnyis khyung
pos mdzad pa/ 'gor skad gnyis shan sbyar phyag 'tshal dang bcas pa'i rjes su/ phyogs bcu dus gsum rgyal ba rgya mtsho yi/ /thugs rje phrin las phun sum tshogs pa yi/ /bdag
gis smon lam 'di dag thams cad kun/ /ji ltar btab pa bzhin du 'grub par shog/ ces yod pa'i smon lam bka' rgya ma khyung pos mdzad pa/ 'gor yon tan rab rdzogs gangs kyi
ri bo bzhin/ /zhes yod pa'i bkra shis bka' rgya ma khyung pos mdzad pa rnams dang / 'gor dus gsum sangs rgyas ngo bo nyid/ /bla ma'i sku gsung thugs la 'dud/ /'phyugs med
lam khyer rnam gsum gyi/ /zhes yod pa'i lam khyer rnam gsum gyi khrid yig dhwa dza lakShas gzhan phan blos bkod pa/ bla ma lam khyer gyi byin rlabs bya tshul/ de'i sham
du sgyu ma lam khyer gyi byin rlabs bya tshul gyi sa bcad tsam smos pa/ yang bla ma lam khyer gyi byin rlabs bya tshul gong ma de dang tshig rgyas bsdus tsam yod pa/ 'gor
mdo rgyud man ngag nyams myong gis/ /zhes yod pa'i 'chi med kyi zhal gdams ratna birWas mdzad pa/ 'gor nyin par snang stong lha sku la/ /zhes yod pa'i 'chi med rang grol
dharma singhas mdzad pa/ 'gor rang grol bde chen

'dus ma byas/ /dharma singha'i zhabs la 'dud/ /ces yod pa'i rang sems 'chi med rang grol gyi gdams pa dharma pradznyAs mdzad pa/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs pad la btud nas/
/'chi med rang grol dbang bskur bshad/ /ces yod pa'i 'chi med kyi dbang bskur bya tshul/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ dben pa'i gnas su 'gro zhing sems bskyed nas/ /rang bde mchog
tu bsgoms pa'i spyi bor bsgoms la zhes yod pa'i 'chi med kyi khrid yig 'di las zab pa'i gdams pa rgya bod gnyis na med gsungs pa/ 'gor bde chen rgyal po lhun grub 'dus ma
byas/ /longs spyod rdzogs sku rdo rje 'chang chen dang / /zhes yod pa'i 'chi med 'khrul 'khor sum cu rtsa gnyis pa'i gsal byed nyi ma'i 'od zer zhes bya ba bla ma'i phyag
len ltar birYa seng ge sa lhag chad med par bris pa'i mtha' can/ 'gor dus gsum shes bya'i rnam pa ma lus pa/ /sgrib pa med pas sa ler mkhyen gyur pa'i/ /zhes yod pa'i zhus
lan rin po che'i sgron me zhes bya ba chos rje dharma pra dznyA bIrYa singhas zhus pa/ 'gor mkha' ltar dag pa'i chos sprul/ /zhes yod pa'i nyams myong yon tan rgya mtsho
rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ 'gor dus gsum sangs rgyas rnams kyi thugs/ /bde gsal mi rtog dbyer med don/ /zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams rin po che 'od kyi phreng ba/ 'gor snang
zhing srid pas bsdus pa'i chos rnams kun/ /zhes yod pa'i mun sel nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sku gsum
ngo bo chos kyi rje/ /rdo rje 'chang chen khyod nyid

kyis/ /zhes yod pa'i zhus lan zla ba'i dkyil 'khor nyon mongs gdung sel rnams so/ /bzhi pa bka' srung ye shes mgon po'i skor la/ mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i rjes gnang thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / sha ba ri dbang phyug mnga' bdag mai tri pa/ rA hu la gupta/ grub thob khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog cog pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ skyer
sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyen ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ 'gro mgon sangs rgyas ston pa/ mkhas grub gtsang ma shangs ston/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rdo
rje gzhon nu/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ byang sems sbyin pa bzang po/ grub thob thang stong rgyal po/ brgyud 'dzin rin po che/ pu rong dpal ldan dar po/ zhe dgon
pa bsod nams rtse mo/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rgyal rtse ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med bstan pa rab rgyas/ grub dbang bsod
nams chos 'phel/ ngag dbang tshul khrims bzang po/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /bla ma mgon po dbyer med kyi khrid
rim shin tu zab pa thob pa'i brgyud pa'ang gong bshad ma thag pa ltar ro/ /phyag drug ye shes mgon po lha mang gi rjes gnang bar chad kun sel thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ sha ba ri dbang phyug nas gtsang ma shangs ston gyi bar mgon dkar gyi brgyud pa dang 'dra ba las/ de nas rgyal mtshan 'bum/ tshul

khrims mgon po/ ri khrod ras chen/ sangs rgyas rdo rje/ thar pa bzang po/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ ngag dbang chos grags
man gong dang 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas/ mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos grags rgya mtsho/ dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra'o/ /yang na tshar chen nas/
gnyen ston rnam 'phrul gzhon nu blo gros/ dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra'o/ /!/ /sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyi sa lo pa spyan snga rin po che ngag dbang chos grags
kyi phyag len zin bris mdzad pa'i steng nas rgya gar gyi grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba legs par nos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs
la/ grub chen lU hi pa/ 1dA ri ka pa/ 2DeM ki pa/ 3lI la pa/ 4birWa pa/ 5Dombi pa/ 6sha wa ri pa/ 7sa ra ha/ 8ko ka li pa/ 9mi na pa/ 10a nangga  go rakSha yang zer/badzra/

lo pa/ 23nA ro pa/ 24sha li pa/ 25tsa ta pa/ 26bha ta pa/ 27dho Shanti/ 28a dzu gi29sa ka la/ 30dhoM bi pa/ 31me ko pa/ 32ka ma ri pa/ 33dza landha ra pa/ 34rA hu la/ 35dharma

48ku ku ri

pa/ 49kudznyA li/ 50dha ma pa/ 51ma dhi la/ 52a tsInta/ 53bha la ha/ 54na li pa/ 55bhu su ku/ 56indra bhU ti/ 57lcam legs smin ka ra/ 58dza lendra pa/ 59ni gu na/ 60tsa pa
ri pa/ 61tsi pa ka62bhi Sha na/ 63til brdung pa/ 64ku mA ri pa/ 65du me pa/ 66ma Ni bha dra/ 67me kha la/ 68ka na kha69ka na ka70kanta li/ 71dha su ri pa/ 72u dha ri pa/
73ka pA li pa/ 74ki ra pa/ 75mtsho skyes rdo rje/ 76sarba bha ba/ 77nA ga bo dhi/ 78su ra li/ 79sa na ha/ 80ko ka li/ 81a na ka82sa mundra/ 83bya ri pa/ 84rnams kyi byin
rlabs dang rtogs brjod bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi/ mkha' 'gro ma ko ki la dang dharma de wa mched gnyis/ paNDi ta
sUrYa rasmi/ dpa' bo 'od gsal yang zer/bram ze'i paNDi ta ka ma la/ grub thob dza wa ri pa/ ma ga dha'i paNDi ta a bha ya dA na shrI/ mi nyag tsa mi lo tsA smon grub shes
rab/ rin po che yab sras/ ratna gu ru/ grub thob hU~M 'bar/rgan mo lhas pa'ang zer/ khams chen byang chub dpal/ stag ston che brag pa/ gzhon nu dar ma/ bag ston gzhon
nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma bde legs pa/ 'phags mchog bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ gnyug la
paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ tre bo chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin nyi zla bzang po/ gling stod chos rje kun dga' 'byung

gnas/ rmod pa grub chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ bco brgyad chos rje mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ bco brgyad pa mkhas grub mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad
mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan po chen po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa grub chen
so so'i shlau ka re yod pa rnams kyi lung yang thos so/ /smras pa/ gong 'og rgyud sde kun las btus pa'i lha/ /dngos grub 'byung gnas sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang / /ba ri
brgya rtsa snar thang brgya rtsar bcas/ /rdor phreng kri yA sa mutstsha sogs so/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ rgyud sde
gong 'og sna tshogs 'dres pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyis sarga ste bcu gsum pa'o/ // /rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos gsang chen rnying ma'i ring lugs las byung
ba bcom ldan 'das dpal chen rdo rje phur ba ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por/ chos rje bla ma'i mngon rtogs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum dang dkyil chog gi dgongs don bzhin
sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i bdag 'jug sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i slob ma dbang bskur gyi cho ga'i steng nas dbang bzhi yongs su
rdzogs pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang po bsrungs pa/ 'khon
rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon shes rab yon tan/ 'khon tshul khrims

rgyal po/ 'khon rdo rje gtsug tor/ 'khon dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong / 'khon ston bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/
bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rgyal
po 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal/ bu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ gan
pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje
glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po/ kun dga' rin chen/ grub mchog bsod nams dbang po/ sngags 'chang grags pa
blo gros/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams rin chen/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi bdag po badzra kI la ya chos kyi rje 'jam dbyangs chos dar/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na
chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa'i rjes su/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'

rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan nas/ sa lo tsA ba man 'dra'o/ /yang na rje btsun pa/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa dbang rin/ gan pa rin
rgyal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra'o/ /yang na rje sa paN/ glo bo lo tsA ba/ 'phags pa rin po che/ lo
tsA ba mchog ldan/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal man 'dra'o/ /!/ /bdag chen rgya gar bas mdzad pa'i phrin las kyi gzhung dregs pa zil gnon dang / sngags 'chang
kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i dbang chog mthong ba rang grol gyi steng nas/ rtsa ba thugs gter lho brag srin mo sbar rjes can gyi brag nas mnga' bdag nyang ral chen
po nyi ma 'od zer gyis spyan drangs pa'i gter kha gu ru drag po thod phreng rtsal drag po dmar chen gyi dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ mnga' bdag nyang ral chen po/ mnga' bdag sras chung
pa/ gu ru dharma ratna/ rtogs ldan chos nyid rang grol/ drin chen sangs rgyas lhun dbang / sprul sku kun dga' bkra shis/ gnubs/mkhas grub rgyal sras chos rje/ thugs mchog
rtsal gcung /sngags 'chang legs pa dpal bzang / 'khon rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba kun dga' bsod nams/ sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang
po kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs khri chen

bsod nams dbang po/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin stsal to/ /yang na brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas nas/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
lhun grub/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ de nas 'jam dbyangs kun dga' sangs rgyas kyis gsan
pa yin nam brtag de dbon 'jam dbyangs bkra shis phun tshogs/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /gu ru drag dmar mnga' bdag nyang lugs kyi rjes gnang mkhan ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad
pa'i yig cha go bde gsal ba'i sgron me'i steng nas legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhas grub rgyal sras chos rje yan gong dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba
dang 'dra zhing / de nas sngags 'chang legs pa dpal bzang / gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug grub mchog sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bkra shis dpal ldan/ mkhas btsun
kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande

tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ drin chen padma thod phreng rtsal dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/
/!/ /grub thob thang stong rgyal po'i lugs kyi tshe dbang 'chi med dpal ster ma'i dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ khro bo rta mgrin dbang gi rgyal
po/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ grub chen brtson 'grus bzang po/ rdo ring kun spangs chen po/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin nyi zla bzang po/ rje dbang phyug
dpal bzang / mkhan  yangs can chen ngag dbang chos grags/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ 'dren mchog nam mkha' dpal
bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ 'chi med dpal ster bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la lan mang du stsal to/ /yang na mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/
mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ tshe dpag med dngos dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo
rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub dang / kun dga' chos 'phel gnyi gas gsan/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs dang phyi ma gnyis te de gsum ga las bla ma bkra shis bzang po
dang / nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags nas/ rgyal sras ngag
dbang spyan snga kun dga' don

grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyugs skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen/
de las khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub dang / thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las bdag gis lan mang du legs par thob
bo/ /de dag gi yig cha phal che ba ni bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i 'chi med rdo rje'i rgya mdud kyi steng nas mdzad cing mkhan chen bkra shis lhun
grub pas skabs 'gar spyan snga ba'i yi ge ltar yang mdzad do/ /yang na grub dbang shug ra kun dga' dpal 'byor pa las spyan snga kun dga' don grub kyi yi ge'i steng nas
lan du ma'i bar du bdag gis thob kyang / grub chen de nyid kyi gsan yul bla ma shug ra gong ma yin nam/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs la sogs pa gang yin ma nges/
yang na rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog sdom brtson ngag dbang nyi ma/ lcags zam pa kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug bco brgyad byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ mkhas grub sangs
rgyas phun tshogs man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /!/ /mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge dang / mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa'i lhan thabs
dang bcas pa'i steng nas tshe dbang lcags sdong ma rig 'dzin rgod kyi ldem phru can gyi gter ma'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ sngags

'chang rdo rje dpal/ byams pa bshes gnyen/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / sngags 'chang chos rgyal bsod nams/ sngags 'chang chos skyong bsod nams/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rgyal mkhar rtse pa ngag dbang bsod  rje 'dis shes rab 'byung gnas la'ang
gsan no/ /nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje buddha ba/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ de nas bstan 'dzin lhun grub kyis gsan pa yin nam brtag de nas mkhan chen rdo rje
'chang bkra shis lhun grub pa dang / mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong pa gnyis kyis gsan nam/ bka' drin can gnyis ka las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par
thob bo/ /'di la brgyud pa'i tshul rgyas pa chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rgyal ba rigs lnga/ sprul sku phyag na rdo rje/ smug nag dbang gi mkha' 'gro/ tshangs pa'i
rgyal po gdong gsum pa/ rig 'dzin lha dbang brgya byin/ klu rgyal 'jog po/ skal ldan rgyal po dza/ mkhas pa shAkya pra bha/ padma bi ma la/ bal po shI la manydzu/ mkha'
'gro ye shes 'tsho rgyal/ rig 'dzin rgod ldem sogs/ 'di la rje dbang phyug rab brtan gu ru mtshan brgyad kyi gsol 'debs kyi gsung gdangs mdzad cing / tshe mda' la dar dmar
po btags pas g.yob par mdzad kyin 'dug  zhabs drung a mi lags kyi gsan yig na snang /gsung ngo / /!/ /gsol 'debs las/ grags pa gsum pa dbang phyug mtshan mtha' can/ /'bre
ban tshul bzang rnam gsum tshogs pa'i

gter/ /bla ma grum dang yon bdag nag po mkhar/ /gnyis tshogs gter sgo 'byed rnams la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa'i gter ston gsum tshogs ni rkyang po grags pa dbang phyug sum pa
byang chub tshul khrims/ 'bre shes rab bla ma gsum gyis yer pa se ba lung nas rta mgrin padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa khrag 'thung lha dgu'i rgyud sgrub thabs man
ngag rnams spyan drangs nas 'bru tshang gi gnyags ston la shog ser steng nas chos rgyun lan gcig tsam las spel rgyu ma byung bar gter rdur gyis rkyang po la mdze byung
/ sum pa 'das/ 'bre smyo bas shog ser rnams rta mgrin gyi grub thob zhu ston bya ba'i lag tu byung yang des zhu sa rtsad ma chod pas las 'phro gter brgyud kyi byin rlabs
bka' ma nyams pa yongs grags la med par yun ring 'byams/ ring zhig na grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po 'dar phya ru ba gtsang jo mo nags rgyal na bzhugs pa'i dus slob dpon chen
po padma 'byung gnas zhang tshe zla grags bya ba'i sngags pa zhig tu sprul nas dbang lung rnams rdzogs par gnang / sngags kyi oM de hrIHru bsgyur la sgrubs shig gsungs/
'dar phyar gyis bla ma rgya la gter brgyud kyang rtsad chod nas gsan pa'i bka' gter zung 'jug gi chos skor la/ thog mar ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba rgyal
ba'i dbang po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i padma yang gsang khros pa'i las byang gyer sgom 'jigs med rdo rje'i sgra dbyangs dang kun mkhyen dpal ldan seng
ge sa mdzad pa'i dbang chog bde chen myu gu la lha dbang gi lhan thabs

sbyar zhing / bla chen chos dpal bzang pos mdzad pa'i dbang chu ma dag pa'i dri ma 'khrud byed kyi steng nas zhib cha'i phyag len dang bcas dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa sngon du
btang ste bum pa la brten nas khrag 'thung rigs lnga'i rig pa'i dbang / lha dbang / dur khrod chas dbang / gtor dbang / gsang dbang / sher dbang / bzhi pa'i dbang dang bcas
pa rig 'dzin brgyud pa'i byin rlabs kyi bka' srol ma nyams pa yid ches khungs btsun du mnos/ dbus ston pa sogs sa dge'i mkhas rlom gzhan dag gis rig pa'i dbang lnga so
sor phral nas bskur bas mtshon te gsang 'dus dgyes rdor sogs rgyud sde gzhan gyi rgyas bkab rang bzo'i dri ma tsam yang ma 'dres pa yin no/ /'chi med tshe'i rdzong chung
gi dbang kun mkhyen chen po'i yig cha dang de'i gsal byed tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i nag po 'gro shes kyi steng nas tshe 'gugs 'ching / bsdu ba/ dbang dngos/
sba ba/ sbel ba/ tshe rdzas myang ba/ bsrung ba rnams smin rgyas/ bde gshegs 'dus pa'i byin rlabs dbang gi cho ga'i steng nas bum pa/ rta mgodur khrod chas/ bzlas lung
/ gtor ma la brten pa'i dbang / bka' srung gying lnga gza' gdong gi srog gtad kyi rjes gnang zab mo rnams kyang yid brtan du rung ba thob nas/ rgyab rten lung gi skor la/
spyir rtsa brgyud kyi steng du dril ba/ sgrub thabs byang bu'i steng du dril ba/ man ngag las tshogs kyi steng du dril ba'i tshul dang gsum/ dang po ni/ rgyud kyi le'u
drug pa yan gyis stod las byang chub sgrub pa rnams ston pas/ smin byed dbang gi

skor/ sgrub thabs las byang / bstod bskul/ rab gnas/ sbyin sreg zor sogs sgrub pa chen po'i cha lag tu nges par dgos pas smad las kyi char gtogs pa 'ga' zhig kyang der tshang
dgos la/ rgyud kyi le'u bdun pa nas bcu gnyis pa'i bar gyi smad las dgra bgegs sgrol ba mngon spyod drag po'i skor ni sgrub chen gyi le lag tu byung ba'i dmod pa kha sbyor
dbye ba sogs ma yin pa min na'ang / gtso bor sbas pa mig 'byed kyi le'u gsum pa man chad kyi skor dang / gtor ma'i las tshogs bcu bdun gyi nang gi mngon spyod kyi skor
sogs 'phrul shes par byas nas skabs gang dang gang du dgos pa de dang der len pa yin/ gnyis pa ni/ sgrub phrin sbyor dngos rjes tshang la brten nas rgyud dang man ngag
shog dril sogs skabs thob gang du dgos pa de bsnan nas nyams su len/ gsum pa ni/ sbas pa mig 'byed kyi skor te/ de yang rgyud ltar byed na le'u dang po dang gnyis pas stod
las rgyud le'u drug pa yan dang sbyar/ lhag mas smad las rgyud kyi le'u bdun pa man dang sbyor/ man ngag ltar byed na zhal gdams shog dril byang bu sogs stod las dang
thun mong gi las sgrub rnams smad las su sbyor/ man ngag rang rkyang du byed na sman sgrub dang lha sngags dmigs pa'i nges pa bstan pas stod las/ le'u gsum pa man chad kyi
smad las su sbyor dgos pas sdom 'di lta bu shes na chos lugs 'di la nang byan tshud par mngon no/ /de yang rtsa ba rgyud kyi skor/ sdong bu byang bu'i skor/ smin byed dbang
gi skor/ sgrub pa phrin las kyi

skor/ sbas pa mig 'byed skor/ bde gshegs spyi dril gyi skor/ thun mong las phran shog dril gyi skor/ thun mong ma yin pa mchog lam gyi skor dang brgyad/ dang po la/ padma dbang
chen yang gsang khros pa'i rgyud le'u (pha)bcu gsum pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can slob dpon chen pos mnga' bdag rje la gtad pa lo chen bai ros bsgyur ba/ dpal au DyAn
chen pos mdzad pa'i rgyud kyi skabs spyod (pha)don 'grel bai ro tsa na'i 'gyur/ rgyud kyi sa bcad dbang chen zhal gzigs kun mkhyen mus srad pa dpal ldan seng ge sa mdzad
pa piN ta tha rdzogs byang gi mtha' can rnams so/ /gnyis pa sdong bu lta bu byang bu'i skor la/ au DyAn chen pos mdzad pa'i dbang gi byang bu/ 'di rgyud kyi le'u gsum pa'i
dbang bgrod dam ldan slob dpon khur zhes pa'i skabs dang sbyor/sgrub pa'i byang bu/ le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/tshe'i byang bu/ sbyin sreg gi byang bu/ le'u bcu pa dang sbyor/rab
gnas kyi byang bu/ gsum pa dang 'brel/ gnas lung gi byang bu rnams so/ /gsum pa smin byed dbang gi skor la/ rtsa ba'i dbang byang mdzad pa po slob dpon chen po padma
bzang po yin pas slob dpon padma bzang po'i rnam thar lo rgyus zhes pa mdzad pa po/ rgyud/ phyogs/ dgos pa bsdus don te lnga'i sgo nas gtan la phab pa gsal ba'i mtha'
can/ le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/ chos khungs btsun pa brgyud pa'i rnam thar la grub thob 'dar bya ru ba rin chen bzang po'i rnam thar zur tsam bris pa bla med byang chub tu
'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje'i rnam thar tshig nyung don rgyas/ le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/chos rje nyan chen pa'i rnam thar

'gor 'khrungs yul dang mjug na gshegs tshul bstan pa legs par gda' 'o'i mtha' can/ sgrub chen gyi phyi'i sngon 'gro rgyan mchod pa rgyal mtho/ dam sri/ sgo byang dang bcas
pa sgo gong du gzhag go'i mtha' can/ le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/ rgyan dgod pa'i las byang mnga' brgyad ma dang bde stong dbyer med pa/ chag chag gdab pa drin chen dri chu ma/
le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/ thig 'debs stong gsum 'jig rten ma/ dbang chen sgrub pa'i tho yig bla ma'i phyag len bzhin rdo rje 'dzin pa seng ge'i mtshan can gyis bkod pa/
le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/ dam rdzas rnam pa lnga'i rtsa brgyad stong sbyar gyi ngos 'dzin/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan seng ge sa mdzad pa'i dbang chog bde chen myu gu le'u gsum
pa dang sbyor/dbang chog gi lhan thabs lha dbang dang rdzas dbang gi yi ge  le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/ rwa ban chos dpal bzang pos mdzad pa'i dbang chu (cha)ma dag pa'i dri
ma 'khrud byed/ rdzong chung tshe dbang gi yi ge rdo rje 'dzin pa dpal ldan seng ge sa bkod pa/ le'u gsum pa dang sbyor/tshe'i 'brang rgyas kyi bzang ngan brtag pa/ tshe

mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i tshe spel ba 'dir tshogs skal ldan ma rnams so/ le'u gsum pa dang sbyor// bzhi pa sgrub pa phrin las skor la/ dpal ldan seng ge sa mdzad pa'i brgyud
'debs dngos grub kyi gter mdzod/ le'u gsum pa bzhi pa lnga pa gang dgos la sbyor/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs smon lam

dang bcas pa/ rta mgrin dpa' gcig phyag gnyis pa'i mngon rtogs bla ma'i gsung ji lta ba bzhin bris pa/ le'u gsum pa bzhi pa lnga pa gang dgos la sbyor/ yab yum rkyang sgrub
kyi mngon rtogs bsnyen pa dang mjug tu gdon bgegs skrod pa'i sngags dmigs dang bcas pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i yab yum rkyang sgrub (dhI)kyi sgrub thabs
rgyun 'khyer dngos grub myur stsol/ le'u gsum pa bzhi pa lnga pa gang dgos la sbyor/ yab yum rkyang sgrub kyi mngon rtogs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa/ padma dbang

don spyi don gsum gyi sgo nas gtan la phab pa/ khro bo'i rgyal po padma dbang chen gyi phrin las ngag 'don mchan bur btab pa gnyags kyi bande rnam rgyal dpal bzang gis mdzad

pa/ le'u gsum pa

sar bsgyur nas/ lnga par sbyor/rje la gtad pa bai ro'i zhal khrigs zab pa'i gnad/ khyad par

gsad thabs gying lnga srog gcod kyi man ngag  bcu gcig par sbyor/ man ngag 'di gnyis la rgya gsum btab pa'i man ngag mnga' bdag gis bai ro la dung g.yas 'khyil sogs phul skad
do/ /gying lnga gza' gdong gi mngon (pha)('dar)rtogs yig rnying / bcu gcig par sbyor/ de'i mdos (pha)('dar)chogagying lnga gza' gdong gi gtor 'bul/ bcu gcig par sbyor/phrin
las myur 'grub tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ bcu gcig par sbyor/des mdzad pa'i gtor ma'i bca' thabs dang phan yon/ gying lnga gza' gdong gi rjes gnang gi yi ge rnams so/
bcu gcig par sbyor// brgyad pa mchog lam skor la/ bum dbang gi lam lha (pha)khrid sems bzung gi shog dril/ 'di man le'u gsum pa'i/ dbang bgrod dam ldan slob dpon bkuraHbrtson
'grus ldan pas rtse gcig sgrubaHces pa'i shugs bstan gyis dgongs par sbyor ro// lha 'grub mi 'grub brtag (pha)pa'i shog dril/ gsang dbang dang 'brel ba drod kyi gdams
pa gtum mo'i dmigs skor bco brgyad/ sher dbang zhal las shes par bya/ bzhi pa 'brel pa rta skad thengs cig (pha)ma'i dgongs pa dbu gtsug sprul pa ma/ dbang bzhi thun
mong gi lam dang 'brel ba bskyed (pha)rdzogs zung 'jug gi shog dril/ dngos grub (pha)spyod pa/ dug gsum (pha)lam slong / sdom pa (pha)dam tshigadangos (pha)grub/ yang dag
lta ba rnams (pha)kyi shog dril/ padma dbang chen gyi rdzogs rim ye shes gsang lam zab mo/ rdzogs rim padma gsang lam gyi nyams len gu rus chos rgyal la gsungs pa/ dpal
rta mgrin gyi dbang bzhi'i

khrid/ 'gor blo gros mnyam med dang zhes yod pa/ bla ma mkhas la bzod par mdzod ces pa'i mtha' can rwa ban chos dpal bzang po'i zin bris/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo
bzang rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i gyer sgom 'jigs med sgra dbyangs rnams legs par thob pa'i gying lnga gza' gdong gi dbang lung la/ bde gshegs spyi dril gyi gnas kyi rtags med
pa rnams dang sa bcad lnga pa yongs rdzogs rwa dhI 'dar gyi rtags yod rnams ma gtogs pa'i dbang lung yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku
padma dbang chen/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ lo chen bai ro tsa na/ mnga' bdag khri srong lde btsan/ gter ston rkyang po grags pa dbang phyug sum pa dbang phyug tshul
khrims/ 'bre shes rab bla ma/ 'brug tshar gyi zhang ston gzi brjid 'bar/ gsang mtshan dri med zla shar/rta nag gi bla ma rgya/ dpal ldan grub thob 'dar phya ru ba/ chos
rgyal bo dong rin chen/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ brag rams pa chos rgyal dpal bzang / kun mkhyen dpal ldan seng ge rnam grol ba rin chen bkra shis/ rtogs ldan yon tan
mgon po/ bla chen chos dpal bzang po/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mus chen rnam rgyal bzang po/ 'khrul zhig dkon mchog bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rigs brgya'i khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/
zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang grol/ rgyal

dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku rin po che padma phrin las/ rnam mang rigs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba chen po rdo rje
'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen du bod pa la stsal to/ /yang na rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub nas/ gnas gsar ba
ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhas btsun grub pa rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen du bod pa la'o/ /sa bcad lnga pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'di skor mnga' bdag gtso che ba tsam ma gtogs gter ston gsum tshogs la'ang byung ba sbas pa mig 'byed gter du sbas
tshul gyi lo rgyus kyis shes/mnga' bdag yan gong ltar la gter ston nyang ral/ she ma 'od 'byung / grub thob 'dar phyar/ brtson 'grus rdo rje/ nyan chen pa/ chos rgyal
dpal bzang / nye gnas chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma blo gros seng ge bla ma siddhi singha / bla chen chos dpal ba man gong ltar ro/ /rwa'i rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ bla
chen nas/ chos rje nor bu phun tshogs/ sngags 'chang sangs rgyas grags pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man gong ltar ro/ /dhI'i rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse nas/ 'phags mchog byams pa skal bzang / rje dbang rab man 'dra/ yang nye brgyud du byed na/ slob dpon padma las grub thob 'dar phyar gyis dngos su gsan pas/
slob dpon chen po nas grub thob 'dar phyar gyis kyang thus/ yang dbang dang

lung pha'i rtags yod pa rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan seng ge yan gong ltar la/ chos rje bsod nams bzang po/ rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po/ rje nam mkha'i rnal
'byor/ mus srad pa blo gros rin chen seng ge gnyal ston dpal 'byor lhun grub/ rje btsun chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bde legs nyi ma/ shar pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ chos
rje rin chen bshes gnyen/ bla ma phrin las lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa dpal 'byor lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ sprul
sku rin po che padma phrin las/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ bstan pa'i snang byed ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rdo rje 'dzin
dbang kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rje btsun chos rgyan nas/ yang dgon spyan snga ngag dbang rgya mtsho/ bla ma phrin las lhun
grub man 'dra/ brgyud lugs 'di'i sbas pa mig 'byed kyang chos rgyal dpal bzang nas dpal ldan seng ge la brgyud pas chog go/ rta mgrin bde gshegs gcig dril gyi dbang lung
yongs rdzogs dang 'dar gyi rtags can gying lnga gza' gdong gi srog gtad kyi brgyud pa ni/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan yan gong ltar la/ de nas mnyam med dkon mchog
dpal bzang / nub dgon pa byams pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ thugs sras byams pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub byams pa bzang po/ nub dgon sprul sku shAkya rgyal mtshan/
'dar nag rgyal sras bde ba bzang po/ des bdag

la'o/ /gying lnga gza' gdong gi srog gtad brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'khrul zhig dkon mchog bzang po yan gong ltar la/ de nas nub dgon pa nyi zla bzang po/ sngags 'chang kun bzang
nyi ma/ zur chen ngag dbang phun tshogs/ khyab bdag chos dbyings rang grol/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ mchog gi sprul sku padma phrin las/ rmor
chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhas btsun rdo rje 'dzin dbang
kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang bya tshul gyi yi ge'i steng nas grwa pa mngon
shes nas brgyud pa'i dzambha la dmar po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i rjes su gnang ba thob nas/ rgyab brten lung la bshes gnyen grwa pas bsam yas nas spyan drangs pa'i 'phags
pa dzambha la dmar po gsung gi sgrub skor la/ thod pa la brten nas khams gsum snying khrag sdud pa'i dbang / gtor ma rin chen 'bar bas 'dod dgu char 'bebs kyi dbang
/ chu sbyin dang lha sgom sngags bzlas kyi dbang mnos nas/ lung la/ 'phags pa dzambha la dmar po gsung gi sgrub thabs/ chu sbyin gtor ma la brten nas bsgrub pa/ ga'u la
brten nas bsgrub pa/ thod pa la brten nas bsgrub pa/ dzambha la'i sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa dbang du bya ba'i phrin las/ sbyin sreg la brten nas bsgrub pa/ tshogs mchod/
bstod pa bde

gshegs ma/ sgab 'dre mnan pa/ 'khor lo'i bri yig dzam dmar zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub pa/ dzambha la dmar po'i dbang bskur gyi yi ge rnams kyi lung dang rjes su gnang
ba bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon chen po padma ka raHmnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan/ grwa pa mngon shes dbang phyug 'bar/ gsan yig 'ga' zhig tu shes rab rgyal
ba zer ba'ang byung /grwa pa thugs rje 'bum/ slob dpon shu la tsandra/ slob dpon tshul rgyal ba/ mkhan po nyi ma/ slob dpon don bzang ba/ dbu ma  la lar dbu gru btsun zer
ba yod kyang rdo ring ba'i gsan yig na dkyus ltar snang gsung /pa grub pa brtson 'grus/ bka' bcu pa bkra shis bzang po/ bla ma blo gros bzang po/ rje btsun seng ge snyug
la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa/ sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen/ 'di nas bla ma 'ga' zhig btsal dgos/ de nas
mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris pa chos rje ye shes phrin las/ bla ma yon tan phun tshogs kyis de nas gsan nam brtag de nas rdo rje 'chang bkra shis bzang po/
des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na dbu ma pa grub pa brtson 'grus nas/ bka' bcu gzhon nu seng ge bla ma shAkya grub pa/ rdo ston bsod nams bzang po/ rje
rgyal ba dpal/ ya ma lag pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ gur rdzong pa
chos 'byor dpal bzang / rigs 'dzin gzhon nu don grub/ 'di nas bla ma gnyis tsam

gyi mtshan btsal te bri dgos/ de nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la sgrub skor gyi lung dang rjes su gnang ba chu
sbyin bcas legs par stsal to/ /yang na gter ston nas/ lce ston gsal ba'i shes rab/ tshe don gsal/ 'u yug dam pa shag po/ dam pa sher rdor/ bla ma bsod nams rin chen/ gzhon
nu seng ge man gong ltar ro/ /yang na gter ston nas/ gzhung pa rgyan legs/ rong pa chos mgon/ bla ma dbang phyug grags/ grwa dur pa/ mkhan po kun dga' rin chen/ rje rin
chen mchog dbu ma pa grub brtson man gong bzhin no/ /lung gi brgyud pa dang rjes gnang gi brgyud pa'i smad gcig gam ma yin cung zad blta'o/ /!/ /slob dpon rin po ches mdzad
pa'i sgrub thabs yig rnying dang / rjes gnang gi tho chung ngag dbang brtan pas mdzad pa'i steng nas/ slob dpon padma nas brgyud pa'i khyung dmar gyi rjes gnang thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung gnas nas rim par/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ byams pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje sogs
nas rim bzhin mkhan chen bsod nams dpal ldan/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang rdo rje 'chang shug ra kun dga'
dpal 'byor gyi drung nas kyang thob ste gsan yul gyi bla ma gang yin ma 'tshal to/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ chos rje bsod nams lhun

grub/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sogs nas brgyud pa'ang yod pa'i sbrel mtshams btsal bar bya'o/ /!/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen nyang ston
sgrub pos lho brag mkhar chu'i gter nas spyan drangs pa'i 'phags pa thugs rje chen po'i sgo nas mig gsal byed kyi gdams pa'i lung thob pa la/ lo rgyus dang gdams pa nyang
ston rang gis yi ge ra bkod pa/ sngags 'chang bkra shis stobs rgyal dbang po'i sdes mdzad pa'i de'i gsal byed kyi yi ge 'gor thugs rje chen pos rtag par 'gro kun la/
zhes yod pa'i dang por lo rgyus/ gnyis pa dngos gzhi nyams len/ gsum pa phan yon te skabs gsum gsal bar byed pa tshigs bcad ma/ des mdzad pa'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ yang
de'i lo rgyus dang nyams len tshig lhug pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ snang ba mtha' yas/ thugs rje chen po/ padma 'byung gnas/ nyang ston sgrub
pa po/ 'gro mgon shAkya bzang po/ rig 'dzin chos rgyal dbang po'i sde/ rig 'dzin ngag gi dbang po/ rje bkra shis rnam rgyal/ gling stod zhabs drung dkon mchog dpal 'byor/
sprul sku rin po che padma phrin las/ rje blo bzang don grub/ gnas gsar pa ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ des bdag
bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung nas/ mkhas btsun bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ chos kyi rje dam pa ting 'dzin rdo rje/ des bdag

la'o/ /smras pa/ 'khon ston las brgyud rdo rje gzhon nu'i dbang / /bla ma drag sgrub 'chi med sgrub skor gnyis/ /yang gsang dbang dang chos skor rmugs 'dzin sogs/ /snga 'gyur
gsang sngags thor bu'i thos tshul yin/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gsang sngags snga 'gyur gyi chos skor thos pa'i
brgyud rim gyis sarga ste bcu bzhi pa'o/ // /mkhas shing grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba rtsa gsum 'dus pa'i bdag nyid chen po mtsho las skyes pa'i rdo rje'i sgyu 'phrul drwa
ba'i zlos gar/ rig 'dzin sprul pa'i sku gter bdag gling pa 'gyur med rdo rje'i zhabs kyis/ bka' dang zab gter gyi bstan pa'i chu gter chen po las/ mchog dang thun mong
gi dngos grub thogs pa med par sgrub pa'i/ rtsa ba gsum gyi lhag pa'i lha'i 'khor lo'i rnam pa mtha' yas par 'byung ba rnams kyi sgrub pa'i thabs yongs su grags pa rnams
don du gnyer ba dang po'i las can rnams la nye bar mkho ba'i phyir dang / shin tu dkon pa 'ga' zhig ni rgyun mi chad par bya ba'i phyir dang / phyi 'gyur gyi sgrub thabs
'ga' zhig kyang nyer mkho'i dbang du byas nas phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa sgrub thabs 'dod 'jo'i bum bzang zhes bya ba nas 'byung ba'i lha tshogs rnams kyi dbang bskur byin
rlabs rjes gnang rig gtad/ bzlas lung la sogs pa'i bka' srol ma nyams par bzhugs pa'i cho ga'i rnam grangs tha dad pa'i tshul can ji snyed cig bzhugs pa rnams legs par thob

skor la/ bla ma gsang 'dus las thod phreng rtsal sgos sgrub kyi zlum po bzhi dbang / gsang 'dus gtor dbang gnad kyi shog gcig mar grags pa/ nyang gter bla ma yongs rdzogs kyi
gtor dbang rnams so/ /bla ma drag po'i skor la/ nyang gter drag dmar bde 'dus kyi dbang bka' rdo rje spyi blugs/ 'bring po me'i spu gri'i dbang chog che 'bring gnyis ka
dang 'brel pa'i byin rlabs lu gu brgyud/ brag dmar bka' ma 'o bran lugs/ byang gter drag po rtsal gyi byin rlabs thugs rje'i dbang bskur rnams so/ /!/ /tshe dpag med kyi
skor la/ tshe dpag med lung lugs sangs rgyas gsang ba'i man ngag chos dbang gi gter ma bla ma longs sku'i rdzong chen tshe dbang / byang gter tshe sgrub lcags sdong ma/
pad gling tshe sgrub rdo rje phreng ba'i tshe dbang sgrub khog las gsung rgyun bzhin phyungs pa/ grub thob thang stong pa'i gdams pa 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe sgrub rnams
so/ /!/ spyan ras gzigs kyi skor la/ thugs rje chen po rgyal po lugs phyag bzhi pa/ rgyal po lugs kyi bcu gcig zhal/ rgyal ba rgya mtsho bde gshegs bzhi sgril gyi sgrub
thabs rnams so/ /!/ 'jam dpal tshe bdag yang bzlog me'i spu gri'i rnon po nad gcod kyi dbang bka'o/ /!/ rta mgrin gyi skor la/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub shangs lugs/ nyang

las tshogs la brten pa/ byang chub gling pa'i

gnyis ma/ rdo rje phag mo don grub ma/ phag mo dbu bcad ma/ khros nag gi sgrub thabs rnams so/ /shes rab kyi lha'i skor la/ ma ti lugs kyi 'jam dpal dkar po/ dam pa sangs

ba ri lugs/ chos dbang lugs kyi drang srong loktri pA la/ rin chen gling pa'i nA ga raksha'i sgrub thabs rnams so/ /!/ bstan srung mgon po'i skor la/ dpal mgon legs ldan

/ re ti rang byung ma bka' gter gnyis ldan/ nyang gter gshog rgod ma/ las 'brel lugs lha mo srog sgrub ma/ las 'brel lugs gza' rgod dug gi spu gri/ las 'brel lugs gnod

skyong seng gdong can/ nyang gter dur khrod ma mo/ chos dbang gi brtan ma bcu gnyis/ nyang gter dkor bdag pe ha ra'i sgrub thabs rnams so/ /nor lha'i skor la/ rnam sras phyi

ni snga 'gyur bka' ma dang / stag zhon dang beng rang byung ma rnams ni bka' gter gnyis ldan dang / gzhan rnams ni zab gter sna tshogs las byung ba'i gdams pa sha stag go/

gu ru/ kun bzang dpal 'byor/ rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub/ sprul sku gter bdag gling pa/ rig 'dzin 'gyur med rdo rje/ rgyal sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ padma bstan 'dzin theg
