padma bzang po/ mkhan chen chos dbang / mkhan chen chos grub seng ge thugs sras kun rgyal/ tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse khu dbon gsum/ phrin las lhun grub
man 'dra'o/ /nang sgrub rta sngon can dang yang gsang gnyis la zangs dkar lo tsA ba nas brgyud de gsar ma'i 'dren tshul kyang yod do/ /gnod sbyin zhang blon la/ gsang
ba'i bdag po/ mgon po klu sgrub/ au DyAn chen po/ grwa pa mngon shes/ nye gnas ga dran/ pu ra ba bsod rin/ gnyis kas smon lam 'bar/ sha mi rdor rgyal/ dol pa badzra pA Ni/
rgya byang seng / brag dkar sman bla/ dkon mchog gzhon nu/ 'gar tshul gzhon/ chos dpal bzang po/ grags pa rgyal mtshan/ paN chen sku mched/ au DyAn rgyal po/ kun dga'
bkra shis/ bsod nams mchog ldan/ rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub man 'dra/ dzam dmar la/ au DyAn chen po/ grwa pa mngon shes/ grwa thugs rje 'bum/ shu la tsandra/ slob dpon
tshul rgyal/ mkhan po nyi ma/ slob dpon don bzang / dbu ma pa grub brtson/ bkra shis bzang po/ blo gros bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge

dpal/ paN chen byams gling pa/ lo chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rtse le rig 'dzin/ au DyAn bstan 'dzin/ karma gu ru/ chos dbang bstan rgyal/ chos dbang bsam grub/ rig 'dzin phrin
las lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /lha chen la/ snang mtha'/ thugs rje chen po/ au DyAn yab yum/ mchims rdo rje sbre chung / gter ston las 'brel rtsal/ rgyal sras legs pa/ karma
pa rang byung rdo rje/ g.yung ston pa/ rol dpal rdo rje/ mkha' spyod dbang po/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ sog dbon pa/ mthong ba don ldan/ dpal 'byor don grub/ khams pa grags
rgyal/ nam mkha' dpal ldan/ bla ma sprul sku/ chos bzang rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' lhun grub/ padma phrin las/ gsung sprul tshul khrims rdo rje/ rig 'dzin phrin las lhun grub/
rig 'dzin sprul pa'i sku gter bdag gling pa/ rgyal sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'gyur med theg mchog bstan 'dzin/ padma gsang sngags bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la'o/ /smras pa/ rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i mkhyen brtse nus so cog/ 'dus pa'i rang bzhin rtsa gsum lha tshogs kyi/ /dngos grub sgrub thabs dbang bskur rjes su
gnang / /gces btus 'dod 'jo'i bum pa bzang pos 'byor/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ rtsa gsum lha tshogs kyi sgrub thabs
'dod 'jo'i bum bzang zhes bya ba'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste bco lnga pa'o/ // /rgyud sde bzhi pa rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i phyogs su gtogs pa ni/ gdul
bya dbang po

rnon po'i mchog gi rigs can gyis/ rdo rje slob dpon sangs rgyas thams cad dang dbyer med du 'dzin cing thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rtsa ba yan lag dang bcas pa bsrung
ba lhur len pa la/ gzhan don du phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub tshe 'di'am bar do'am skye ba bdun la sogs pa nas 'grub par byed pa'i/ lam gyi rtsa ba bum pa'i
dbang mtha' dag gi steng du/ gsang ba dang / shes rab ye shes dang / dbang bzhi pa bcas yongs su rdzogs par bskur nas/ kye rdo rje las/ dngos po nyid kyis rnam grol zhing
/ /dngos po'i 'ching bas 'ching bar 'gyur/ /de yongs shes pas grol ba yin/ /dngos po med pa'ang yongs shes pas/ /dngos po bsgom 'gyur shes rab can/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/
'khor ba'i 'dra 'bag lam du byed pa'i tshul gyis rang nyid sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs dang dbyer med du bsgoms pas sbyang gzhi'i gtso bo tha mal gyi skye
'chi bar do'i gnas skabs su snang ba'i chos thams cad de/ de'ang lha'i ngo bor rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pas lhar 'gyur ba'i gzhi yin pa dang / tha mal gyi rnam rtog
gis de dag la tha mal du bzung nas 'khor bar 'ching ba'i rgyur byed pas sbyang dgos pa'i gzhi yang yin pa'i phyir ro/ /sbyang bya snang ba de dag la tha mal du 'dzin pa'i
rnam par rtog pa mtha' dgasbyong byed rnam par thar pa'i sgo dang byang chub kyi phyogs kyi cha dang / ye shes lnga la sogs pa chos kyi sku'i yon tan rnams dang / lha'i
rnam par bskyed cing bsdu ba la sogs pas gzugs kyi skur bsgom

pa rnams yin la/ sbyang tshul sbyang gzhi'i chos su snang ba thams cad sku gsum gyi lam du sgyur bar byed pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor nyams su blangs nas/ sbyangs 'bras
mthar thug sku bzhi zung 'jug gi go 'phang mngon du byed pa/ thabs ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par gong na med par spyod pa'i don du gsungs pa rnal 'byor bla na med pa ste/
de la dbye na/ tshul gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan las/ rnal 'byor che la thabs shes gnyis med gsum/ /zhes thabs kyi rgyud bla na med pa dang / shes rab kyi rgyud bla
na med pa dang / thabs dang shes rab gnyis su med pa'i rgyud bla na med pa gsum du phye ba'i khyad par yang / de nyid las/ de yi khyad par gleng gzhi'i yi ge dang / /bskyed
rim lha dang rdzogs rim rnam pa gnyis/ rjes spyod rnam dag rgyud kyi gdul bya rnams/ /rim bzhin mang nyung pho mo thabs shes te/ /gang gang gtso che thabs dang shes rab
ste/ /de de gnyis ka ldan na gnyis med rgyud/ /ces rags pa'i 'jog byed du gsungs shing / don la gsang ba 'dus pa sogs kyang gnyis su med pa nyid du byang chub sems dpa'i
'grel chen las bshad pa ltar nges dgos shing / 'dir 'jog byed de dag dang rjes su mthun par gtso bor pha rgyud dam thabs kyi rgyud de/ de la'ang zla gsang thig le'i rgyud
las/ 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug gis/ /rgyud kyang rnam pa gsum du 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gsum gyi/ dang por 'dod chags can gtso bor 'dul bar byed pa dpal gsang
ba 'dus pa'i skor la/ mi bskyod pa'i rigs su gtogs pa dpal

gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud las gsungs shing rgyal ba gnyis pa dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis legs par bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das mi bskyod rdo rje lha sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi
ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dngos grub rgya mtsho/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ye shes rgya mtsho/ gtor chog
'dod dgu'i rgya mtsho/ rdo rje sems dpa'i mchod chog tshogs gnyis rgya mtsho/ mchod phreng mchod sbyin rgya mtsho/ bkra shis dge legs rgya mtsho bcas dang / thams cad mkhyen
pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i 'dus pa 'phags lugs kyi sgrub dkyil zur 'debs mkhas pa'i yid 'phrogapaN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i dbang gi mtshams
sbyor dang bcas pa'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par nos pa'i brgyud pa la bka' babs bdun ldan du bzhugs pa'i thog mar 'gos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rngog lugs kyang zer/sangs
rgyas rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bhU ti/ klu las gyur pa'i rnal 'byor ma/ mkha' 'gro ma gri thod can/rgyal po bi su kalpa/ rgya gar shar phyogs
o Di bi shabram ze chen po sa ra ha/ dpal mgon/ rgyal bas lung bstan pa'i dge slong dpal ldan/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ de la slob ma'i mchog ArYa de wa/ shAkya bshes gnyen/
klu'i byang chub/ zla ba grags pa ste bzhis zhus/ de bzhi ka las slob pa'i rdo rje/ paN ser/de nas nag po spyod pa ba/ sa 'dres pa chen po/ paN phud rab byung /de las
mar me mdzad/ dI paM ka ra/de wa a ka ra tsandra/ paN dka' khyim pa'i rten

can/ mngon shes can gyi paNDi ta yin/bi dyA bha dra gsum gyis gsan/ sa 'dres pa'i slob ma lnga las shAnti pa dang / dpa' sras gnyis las ma gsan/ gzhan gsum ga las gsan par
bu ston gyis bshad do/ /gsum ga las 'gos khug pa lhas btsas kyis gsan zhing / sngags pa gos dkar co breg can yin/ deng sang rab byung gi chas 'dri ba ni rnam par ma brtags
pa'o/ /der ma zad za hor gyi mkhas pa btsun mo can/ paN dkar/bal yul ljongs kyi nA ga ko Ti bi kra ma la shI la'i thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis par grags pa dI paM ka ra/ paN
ser/rdo rje gdan gyi mkhan po nag po pa/ paN ser/kangka la'i mkhas pa chen po rgyal bu sprin  paN dkar/gyi shugs can/ zur gyis 'gos la mthu byung bar de'i gnyen por gshin
rje 'char ka zhus nas bsgyur ba'i 'char ka sprin shugs mar grags pa 'di las gsan pa yin no// rgyal po'i khab kyi mkhas pa chen po dza hU~M  gsan yig na dza hu zhes snang
/zhes pa zhi ba bzang po/ paN dkar/kha che khri brtan gyi mkhas pa chen po tsandra ha ri sogs paNDi ta bdun bcu/ paN dkar/mkha' 'gro'i bla ma gnyis dang bcas pa las lo
tsA ba 'gos kyis gsan/ 'gos lo tsA ba nas/ 'jad pa so rong gi mang ra ba  rje btsun btsong kha pa'i gsan yig na 'dzad bo dong gi zhes snang /seng ge rgyal mtshan/ rab byung
/'jad brag ltag gi rngog ye shes seng ge  rab byung /de'i dbon po rngog nyi ma seng ge  rngog mu ne rab tu byung ba'i mtshan/bres chu dbar gyi glan rtsad tsha nyi ma
lcam/ sngags pa gos dkar co bregde gnyis ka las rngog ArYa de wa/ rngog mu ni rab tu ma byung gong gi sras sngags dkar/de'i zhar chos pa skyi mkhar 'jug bres kha dben tsha'i
rtag pa rin chen grags/ rab byung /de las bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa chos sku 'od zer gyis rgyud 'grel

bshad bka' thob/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ rdo rje sems dpa'/mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod  zhwa lu'i ri phug gi byang nag phug gong
gi dgon pa tshes phug pa de yang tshong 'dus kyi nub dgon pa khyung po lhas kyi gdan sa thog gcig mdzad pas khyung lhas par grags/ gdung nas skyo/nams/ pa ri dga' chen/chos
rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ mus chen sangs
rgyas rin chen/ sa lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen/ 'dren mchog
dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ sngags 'chang bla ma kun dga' bkra shis grags pa
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bstan pa'i sgron me 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang chen po kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ bka' drin mnyam med mkhan chen sangs rgyas
dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ tshul khrims dpal bzang ngam/ tshul khrims lhun grub/ thar rtse pa mkhan
chen nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag la'o/ /yang na kun mkhyen nas/ paN chen dbang phyug grub pa/ 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun

dga' rin chen man gong bzhin/ yang na rje dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ zhabs drung a mi lags man sngar bzhin
no/ /yang na rngog ye shes seng ge dang glan rtsad tsha gnyis las/ snyi mo phug ka ba 'bum skyabs/ rong lha steng gi gtsong ston smra seng / nyang stod sribs chung gi
lce mdo sde seng ge de nas kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer man 'dra/ yang na brag ltag pa ye shes seng ge las/ bod btsun/cha gar mon mo brag gi mi nyag rdo rje sngags pa gos
dkar co breg can/ grags/ de nas lce mdo sde seng ge  gos dkar co breg can/dge sdings pa chos sku 'od zer man 'dra/ yang na glan rtsad tsha nas/ thang spe ba/ grub thob gser
sdings pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na dge sdings pa chos sku 'od zer nas/ lce blo ldan seng ge blo ma 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na 'gos lo tsA ba nas/ dbus
pa dge ser/ gnam kha'u pa/ rje sa chen/ kha'u pa rdo rje bdud 'joms/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug
pa/ ri khrod pa blo brtan/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gnyis pa mar lugs kyi brgyud par
nang gses kyi sgro 'dogs nang nas chod pa grub thob nyams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun btsong kha pa chen po'i gsan yig na 'di 'phags lugs min gsung /rdo rje 'chang / indra
bhU ti/ DA ki bde ba'i zhabs/ Dombi he ru kardo rje dril bu pa/ yan lag med

pa'i rdo rje/ kamba la pa/ nag po spyod pa/me tog dkar po'i thod can/ tai lo pa/ nA ro  nag po mi lpags gsol ba rgyan drug phyag DA thod/pa/ kun tu bzang po/ nam mkha'i snying
po ye shes dngos grub/ rtsa bshad pa/ snyan grags bzang po rnams mtshan gyi rnam grangs/mar lo chos kyi blo gros/ gos dkar lcang lo can/mtshur ston dbang gi rdo rje/
sngags dkar/'khon gad pa kIrti/ bod btsun/ 'khon bya khang pa bsod nams rin chen/ 'khon thur lha ba tshul khrims skyabs/ bod btsun/thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ gser sdings
pa gzhon nu 'od/ bod btsun/ dge sdings pa chos sku 'od  gsang mtshan mi bskyod rdo rje zer/zer man 'gos lugs dang 'dra/ yang na 'khon gad pa kIrti nas/ 'gar ston shes
rab rgya mtsho/ yar klungs zur ri dgon bsngags dkar/grang po khra bo la rtsar angku pa rin chen seng ge  la stod pa bod btsun/rong pa shes rab seng ge  rab byung /ston mo
lung pa ye shes 'bar/ bod btsun/kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / byang sems blo gros rin chen/ lha bu ser po chos 'chad kyi phyag
rgya/dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub/ gsang mtshan ma tanggi pa/ grub thob dmar smug ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya me tog gi thod can/tai lo pa man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gsum
pa mar lugs mkhas pa paNDi ta'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po klu sgrub yan 'gos lugs ltar la/ rje btsun btsong kha pa'i gsan yig na mi 'dren pa 'dra zhig 'dug kyang chu bo gnyis
'dres yin pas skyon du mi 'gyur/de nas 'jam dpal zhal mthong shAkya mi tra/ sgrol ma zhal gzigs nA ga bo dhi/ sa brgyad non pa ArYa de wa/ spyan ras gzigs zhal

mthong / ma tanggi pa ste klu sgrub kyi thugs sras bzhi/ sangs rgyas bskyangs/ legs ldan 'byed/ mkhas mchog dpa' bo ste nye ba'i sras gsum/ bdun po de'i nang nas ma tanggi
pa nas/ tai lo pa/ na ro pa/ mar pa'o/ /yang na klu sgrub kyis ma tanggi pa nas/ zla ba grags pa/ rig pa'i khu byug a wa dhU tI pa/ spyod pa'i rdo rje/ nag po'i zhabs/ dri
med blo gros/ nub lakShe tra'i gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i dpal ye shes snying pos lho brag mar pa lo tsA ba la gdams te/ mar pa la 'phags skor gyi rgyud 'grel pa dang
rgyud rkyang bshad rgyud lnga gzhung phran dang bcas pa dang / ye shes zhabs lugs sogs rgya gar nas 'grel pa nyer gsum/ jo bos nyer lnga tsam yang gsan par grags/ bod
na 'grel pa bdun zer yang mang du snang / mar pa la/ dza ya na/ tha ga na/ snyim tog gsum yod/ lo tsA ba 'dis rgya gar du lan gsum/ bal por lan bzhi ste lan bdun byon/ shar
nub lho byang kha che bal po'i paNDi ta dang ku sa lir grags tshad la bla ma brgya rtsa/ brgyud pa 'dzin nges lnga bcu rtsa brgyad/ snang ba 'gyur nges bcu gsum/ 'dus
pa la mkhas pa'i bla ma bdun dang bcas yod pa'i nang gi ye shes snying po 'di dbang brgyud man ngag gdams pa'i bka' thams cad babs pa'i gtso bor 'dzin no/ /bu bzhi'i nang
tshan mtshur dbang gi rdo rje/ gzhung gi rngog ston chos rdor dol gyi mtshur ston dbang nge / gtsang rong gi mes ston tshon po/ gung thang gi mid la ras pa/'khon ston gad
pa kIrti/ de las mi nyag thur lwa ba tshul khrims skyabs/ dbus pa 'gar dgegrub thob zhang zhung pa ste thugs sras gsum gyis gsan/ gsum ga las gangs par ser kha'i rin chen
gling pa tshul khrims mdzes/ btsong kha pa/ mkhyen brtse/ thar rtse/ sgrub khang pa bzhi'i gsan yig na 'di bzhin byung yang kun mkhyen bu'i gsan yig na gling pa tshul

khrims mdzes zur du mdzad 'dug pa brtag ces lnga pa chen po gsung ngo / /bla ma rgya rnal 'byor pho ba lung pa/ dge slong chos grags dpal bzang po/ bla ma shAkya gzhon nu/
bla ma blo ldan pa/ bla ma 'phags 'od man sngar ltar ro/ /yang na 'khon gad pa kIrti nas/ 'gar ston pa/ gnyan rtse ba/ go lung pa ye rgyal/ rong ston mkhan po/ phug ri ba
byang chub gzungs/ shong blo brtan/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na lo mchog pa nas/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul
khrims/ rje thog ston pa/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs bzhi pa jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rgyal po indra bhu ti che ba/ slob
dpon nA ga dzo ki bram zes ha ra/ slob dpon klu sgrub/ zla ba grags pa/ ku sa li che chung / jo bo chen po dI paM ka ra/ rong pa 'gar dgelha rje stod pa tshul khrims dpal/
sngags pa gos dkar lcang lo can/de sras che ba shes rab rgyal po/ chung ba shes rab gtsug tor/ lha rje chen po dharma tsakra/ thang stod chos kyi 'od/ bla chen klog skya
grags pa bzang po/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bu dang sngags rams pa'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang / thar rtse pa dang sgrub khang pa'i gsan yig na shes rab
rgyal mtshan zer ba 'dug pa dpyad/bla ma kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtshos gsan pa man 'dra'o/ bu thar rtse sgrub
khang shar pa bzhi'i gsan yig na bla ma sgom ye zer ba zhig 'dug kyang de'i brgyud pa gong ma tshigs bcad kyi stabs nas mi gsal lo// bka' babs lnga pa chag

lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ klu sgrub yan sngar ltar la/ de las slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen/ slob dpon ArYa de wa/ klu byang / zla ba grags pa ste sras kyi thu bo bzhis gsan/ ArYa
de wa nas/ 'phags pa rta dbyangs/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ dza landha ri pa/ dpe med dpal/ gambhi ra ma ti pa/ niska langka pa de wa/ paN
dkar/re wendra pa de wa/ chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal/ pod ka dkar po phyar bu dang zhwa rtse ring ser po/'u yug kung ra ba bla ma dpal/ phyar bu bse bo/bla ma grags chen/
don mo ri pa/kun mkhyen 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na slob dpon klu'i byang chub nas/ Dombi pa/ bI ra Di pa/ ma ti garbha/ rdo rje gdan pa/ paN dkar/re wendra/ chag lo
tsA ba man 'dra/ yang na slob dpon zla ba grags pa nas/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ skal ldan grags pa/ 'od zer 'byung gnas grags pa/ 'od mdzad lha/ chos kyi 'byung gnas zhi ba/ rnam
par grags pa'i lha/ rnyog med lha/ paN dkar/ gong gi niska langka ba de wa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ 'di gsum don gcig ming gi rnam grangs/re wendra/ chag lo man 'dra'o/ /bka'
babs drug pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ klu byang gi dkyil chog dang mthun pa'i brgyud par ngos bzung /rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ indra bhU ti/ klu las gyur pa'i
ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ rgyal po bi su kalpa/ bram ze chen po sa ra ha/ slob dpon klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ klu'i byang chub/ zla ba grags pa/ slob pa'i
rdo rje/ nag po spyod pa/ sa 'dres pa chen po/ birYa bha dra/ de wa A ka ra tsandra dI paM ka ra/ 'gos lo tsA

ba/ dbus pa dge ser/ bla ma gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ gnam kha'u pa rdo rje bdud 'joms/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje
sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ de gnyis ka las bla ma dpal
ldan tshul khrims/ de las grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man gong bzhin no/ /sa lugs brgyud pa phyi ma ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/
mgon po klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ zla ba grags pa/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ skal ldan grags pa/ 'od zer 'byung gnas grags pa/ 'od mdzad lha/ chos kyi 'byung gnas
zhi ba/ bi khyA ta de wa/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI bha dra/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'od zer shAkya/ kha'u pa dar ma shes rab/ se mo ra pa rin chen dpal/ bla ma ra gnyis
pa rgyal mtshan rin chen/ spro lung nags phug pa kun smon/ bla ma grags chen pa/ chos rje 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ 'phags pa rin po che/ shong blo gros brtan
pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal seng / mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / sngags rams pa'i
gsan yig na sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen dang mthun pa'i brgyud par mdzad/ shar pa'i gsan yig na dbang bka' gsar ma'i nye brgyud du ngos 'dzin/phyag na rdo rje/ klu
sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ ma tanggi pa/ sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes

gnyen/ bi khyA ta de wa/ kha che paN chen/ sa paNDi ta man 'dra/ jo bo lugs kyi dbang gi mjug na dpyal a mo ghas sbyar ba'i bum dbang cho ga'i dbang bka' 'di dkyil chog dpyal
ba'i dpe steng nas byas pa yin gyi/ dbang bka' jo bo'i bar ma chad pa yin no zhes 'byung ngo / /bka' babs bdun pa dpyal lugs kyi dbang gi brgyud pa ni jo bo dang 'dra'o
zhes zer ba bu ston rin po che'i gsan yig na snang yang / dpyal lo tsA bas kha che paN chen las gsan par snang bas/ kha che paN chen yan sa lugs dang 'dra ba las/ de nas
dpyal chos kyi bzang po/ rje btsun rgwa lo/ bla ma dpal gyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma don ri grags chen/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na 'gos lo tsA ba nas/
mang ra ba seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mgo pa dharma tsakra/ stag pa jo bzang / dpyal chos bzang man 'dra/ yang na dpyal chos bzang nas/ bod btsun/klog skya ba grags pa dpal/
klog skya bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ rdo rje chos/ indra
bhU ti/ padma'i zhabs/ rta mchogs ra ha/ klu sgrub/ klu byang / bal po phyag rdor/ ratna A ka ra shAnti pa shrI kIrti/ shrI legs smin/ shrI ku mA ra sha na/ bi nA ya karatna
badzra/ zhwa lu lo tsA ba chos kyi brtson 'grus/ she ston mar lam/ jo ston dkon seng / kun mkhyen chos 'od/ sri chung ba lce blo ldan/ 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na she
ston nas/ ya stod tshul bzang / dpyal nyi

ma/ chos sku 'od zer man 'dra/ yang brgyud lugs gcig la/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ dkon mchog rin chen/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs man 'dra'o/ /des na sngon gyi dus su lugs
srol so sor yod par snang yang / kun mkhyen bu ston sogs bla ma phyi ma rnams kyi dbang bka' thams cad gsan nas/ byin rlabs kyi chu bo kun 'dus phyag len kyang snying po
dril ba ste bka' drin che 'dug go/ dbang gi mtshams sbyor sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas mnos so/ /!/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po cher chos rje
bla ma dam pa'i gsung gis bskul nas mdzad pa'i khrid yig yid bzhin nor bu rin po che'i za ma tog dang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i yid bzhin
nor bu'i za ma tog kha 'byed pa'i lde mig ma bu sbyar ba'i steng nas pha rgyud bla na med pa'i snying po las kyang ches snying por gyur pa dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rtsa ba'i
rgyud dang bshad pa'i rgyud thun mong ma yin pa bzhis gsal bar byas pa'i don rgyal ba gnyis pa klu sgrub zhabs kyis thugs nyams su bzhes nas tai lo nA ro sogs paN grub
las nye bar 'ongs pa'i zab pa las kyang ches zab pa'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i rdzogs rim rim pa lnga'i dmar khrid zab mo nyams khrid du legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'di sngar
ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyis bris/yang

dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / byang chub sems dpa' blo gros rin chen/ lha'i bu mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i brgyud par 'byung ba dang gcig dpal mgon 'phags pa
klu sgrub/ mtshan gsang ba ma tanggi pa/ tai lo pa shes rab bzang po/ paN chen nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros/ mtshur dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kIrti/
'khon bya khang pa bsod nams rin chen/ mi nyag thur lha ba tshul khrims skyabs/ rgya mkhar thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ se sdings pa gzhon nu 'od/ mag dge sdings pa kun
mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam
rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen tshul khrims/ mkhan chen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ rje btsun rdo
ring pa chen po kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo
rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhan chen sku zhang rin chen mkhyen brtse mchog grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan
pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang khrid yig gnyis kyi
lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang dbang

phyug rab brtan nas/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ khu dbon gnyis ka las mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis gsan pa man 'dra'o/
/!/ mkhas shing grub pa'i slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyi legs par bkral ba'i gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i bdag nyid can gyi ras bris
kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sa mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kun tu bzang po'i nyi 'od/ dkyil chog ye shes rnam rol/ phyi rol tshogs bsags kyi
cho ga gtor chog phrin las rnam rol rnams dang / thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i mtshams sbyor bcas pa'i steng nas yi ge rnams kyi lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ bka' babs drug dang ldan pa las/ a bo tsa dA di ma hA lo tsA ne ta sya mA laH/ bka' babs dang po lo chen lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/manydzu shrI gho Sha tsA dwa ya wa
dhU tiH/ 'jam dpal dbyangs dang gnyis su med pa gnyis spangs pa/A tsArYa buddha dznyA na pA daH/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/shrI dI paM ka ra bha draH/ dpal mar
me mdzad bzang po/A nanda garbhaH kun dga' snying po/tha ga naH tha ga pa/ratnA ka ra shAntiH/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/shrAddhA ka ra warmaH/ dad byed go cha/padma
ka ra warmaH/ padma 'byung gnas go cha/to dwa yi ma hA lo tsA ratna bha dra Na pr-itstshaH/ de gnyis ka las lo chen rin chen bzang pos zhus/rka da po dharmma ma tiH/ rkyang
po chos kyi blo gros/ka lyA Na mi tra sha ra Na singhaH/ dge bshes skyabs seng / rje btsong kha pa'i gsan yig na skyabs se 'dug pa brtag badzra sA ra sthI raH/ rdo rje
sra

brtan/ratna dzwa laH/ dkon mchog 'bar/ka lyA Na mi tre shwa ra ratnaH/ dge bshes dbang phyug rin chen/dhA twa wa ni gu hi kaH/ khams pa sa phug pa/shAkya badzraH/ shAkya rdo
rje/nimnaM dharmma nA tha/ rong pa chos mgon/lo tsA wa rIH/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/gu ru shrI wAM singhaH/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge pu tra shAstA ratna siddhiH bu ston rin
chen grub/pa Tu siddhiHku mA ra puNyeH/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ khyung po lhas pa/dharmma swA mi dznyA nA dhwa dzaH/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ngorma hA badzra
dha rA nanda bha draH/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/yu ba rA dzA nanda shwa raH/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug sarba dznyA puNya singhaH/ kun mkhyen bsod
nams seng ge bhaTTA ra ka buddha ratnaH rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/bhU mi paNDi rA manydzu gho ShA nanda puNya kIrti dhwa dza shrI bha draH/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs
kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/mantra dha ra ya sho ma tiH/ sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/dharmmA swA mi pradznyA dhwa dzaH/ chos rje shes rab
rgyal mtshan/ma hA paNDi ta ga ga na shrI bha draH/ paNDi ta chen po nam mkha' dpal bzang /ratna shrI mA nArtha siddhiH/ rin po che dpal ldan don grub/manydzu gho Sha pUrba
pradznyA ka raH/ 'jam dbyangs shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ de'i sku dbon/manydzu nA tha pUrba dznyA na bha draH 'jam mgon shar pa ye shes bzang po/ma hA pa Tu siddho
buddha lakShmIH/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/badzra dha ra shA sa na dha ra ni rA bho gaH/ rdo rje 'chang bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ma hA pra sA da sarba dznyA
na mangga la ni rA bho ga kIrti rdhA dza shrI bha draH/ drin chen thams cad mkhyen pa bkra shis lhun grub grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ta to ma yA nande shI la
ratne na dwi phrashnaH/ de las bdag btsun pa tshul khrims rin chen gyis lan gnyis bar du mnos so// a pi ma ho pa dhyA ya mangga la ni rA bho gaH/ yang na mkhan chen bkra

shis lhun grub nas/rma ho pa dhyA ya manydzu gho Sha buddha shrI bha draH/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang /te na me pra da ta daH/ des bdag la stsal to//
yang na 'jam dpal/ ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ tha ga na/ bhu sha na pa/ ngag dbang grags pa/ bhi ma shAnti/ bhiM ga ra pA da/ shraddha ka ra warma/ lo tsA ba rin chen
bzang po/ rkyang po chos blo/ gcung po zhang khra/ gnyal pa skyogs ston/ khun tsi gzhon nu rin chen/ gtsang rong pa shes rab gzhon nu/ slob dpon dkon mchog 'bar/ g.yag
sde ba dbang phyug rin chen/ khams ston shAkya rdo rje man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gnyis pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal rdo rje/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ paN
grub mar me mdzad dpal bzang po/ dpal bde ba'i zhabs/ bi ma la gupta/ ratna badzra/ ratna kIrti/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ bla ma bandha pa/ gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/
bla ma gnam kha'u pa dar ma chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa
rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/
khams pa rdo rje dpal/ spang sgang pa grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gsum pa kha che lugs

kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad nas rim par brgyud de kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI/ kha che ga ga dha ra/ paNDi ta bi na shrI/
de la go pA la'i pho brang du khams pa rdo rje dpal gyis zhus/ de nas kIrtI shrI/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa man sa lugs dang 'dra'o/ /bka' babs bzhi pa gnyos lugs kyi brgyud
pa ni/ bi ma la gupta yan gong sa lugs ltar las/ de nas yi ge'i rnal 'byor ratna shrI/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ ba linta A tsArYa/ kha reg  de'i dbon yin/gi gnyos lo
tsA ba yon tan grags/ de sras gnyos rdo rje bla ma/ gnyos dpal le/ gnyos grags pa dpal/ gnyos gzi brjid dpal/ sangs rgyas ras chen/ rgyal ba lha snang / rtsa ri ras chen/
dpyal kha chos rje zhes pa rnams mtshan gyi rnam grangs yin/ston mo lung pa ye shes mkhar/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad
mkhyen pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /yang na gnyos rdo rje bla ma nas/ gnyos ston grags pa dpal/ gnyos lha snang ba/ rin po
che do pa/ mdog stod gser ma/ glas pa dpon rdo rje tshul khrims/ g.yas ru ba rngos ston rin chen rgyal mtshan/ spang khang pa grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs pa/ sa bzang
ma ti paN chen/ 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs lnga pa jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ sangs rgyas
ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ a nanda garbha/ tha ga na/ rin

chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ bar 'dir jo bo chen po mar me mdzad ces rgyal dbang lnga pa sogs kyi gsan yig na byung yang sngon ma 'di ye shes zhabs pa'i dngos slob kyi jo bo rje
yin dgos kyi/ 'dir 'ong don med pas yig skyon yin nam brtag rgya lcags ri gong kha pa/ rdzing bu kha pa/ span bug pa/ zhang ye shes/ gzi ba don grub/ bar thang pa yab sras/
bla ma dar ma shAkya/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ mkhas grub khyung
po lhas pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs drug pa rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ sangs rgyas ye
shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ dpal bde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ ratna badzra/ rin chen grags pa/ sa manta pra bha/ bha draH'ang byung /dznyA na shrI mi
tra/ ratna kIrti/ puNye shrI/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rdo rje sra brtan man 'dra'o/ /!/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sa mdzad pa'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
gyi mngon dkyil sogs dang / de'i mi 'dra ba'i khyad par gyi yi ge rnams kyi steng nas jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti shas legs par bkral ba'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jig rten dbang
phyug lha bcu dgu'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ jo bo rje dpal
ldan a ti sha/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/ 'am pa byang chub rdo rje/ rgya lcags ri gong pa/ rdzing bu

kha pa shAkya grags/ span phug pa dar ma grags/ zhang ye pa shes rab rdo rje/ gzi ba don grubmgon po/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ de sras chos grags/ bla ma dar ma shAkya/ bsod
nams dbang po/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ ngor
chen kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ gnyan chen
grags pa blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / de dbon nam mkha' rin chen/ hor nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/
mkhas btsun kun dga' chos 'phel/ chos rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jig rten dbang phyug bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs
kun dga' bsod nams/ grags pa blo gros/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ brang ti pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na gze pa don grub mgon po nas/ bar thang pa yab sras/ bsod nams
dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che man 'dra/ kun mkhyen chen po'i yi ge'i lung ni gong 'jam rdor gyi skabs bzhin no/ /smras pa/
rjes chags sgyu 'phrul bkod pas 'khor ba'i chos/ /yang dag lam byed thabs rgyud gsang ba 'dus/ /'phags pa'i lugs dang ye shes spyan ldan zhabs/ /mar me

mdzad bkral bka' srol che gsum thos/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim
gyi sarga ste bcu drug pa'o/ // /gnyis pa zhe sdang can gtso bor 'dul ba gshin rje gshed kyi skor la dmar nag 'jigs gsum las dang po la pha bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal
po thams cad kyi snying po'i yang snying rgyud dang man ngag gi dgongs pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan chos skyong
ngam birWa par zhes yongs su grags pa'i zhal snga nas legs par bkral ba'i dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs bdud rtsi'i bum pa/ shar chen gyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub
kyis mdzad pa'i bkra shis/ ngor chen dkon mchog dpal ldan gyis mdzad pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor dang / paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i mtshams sbyor sogs kyis
bsdus pa rnams kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa bka' babs gsum dang ldan pa las/ dang po chags lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed/ ye shes
kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa/ so ma pU ri/grub pa'i dbang phyug Dombi he ru ka na dha ki kagrub chen bi ra Di pa/ de bi ko Ta/ma ti
garbha/dza gaddhaH gambhi ra ma ti/ rdo rje

gdan pa chen po niShka langka de wa/ rnyog pa med pa'i lha/paN grub re  hI ma ya/wendra pra bhA/ chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal/ go lung pha mdo sde dpal/ shong lo tsA ba blo
gros brtan pa/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug bya sder ba byang chub rin chen/ ra ga brag pa/ shAkya seng ge rje btsun
jo nang pa phyogs las rnam rgyal/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab
kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje dbon nam mkha' sangs
rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bka' drin mnyam med rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la lan gnyis su stsal to/ /yang na mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' chos 'phel/ bstan pa'i srog zung bka' drin can bkra shis bzang
po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub nas/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/
/yang na ngor chen nas/ kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha man 'dra/ yang na mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ yongs 'dzin man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang yab sras
gnyis ka las/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug

dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge gnyis kas gsan/ de gnyis ka las ratna wardhas gsan/ yang na lha mchog seng ge shar khang pa/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na
ratna wardha/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa man 'dra/ yang na rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog dpal ldan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na rje
dkon mchog dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas man 'dra/ yang na chag lo nas/ rgyal mtshan dge ba/ shong lo tsA ba blo brtan/ lo mchog man
'dra/ yang na lo mchog dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na dpal ldan seng
ge kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang / ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa man 'dra'o/ /yang chag lugs brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ chag lo nas/ bla brang pa gzhon nu/ bla brang
pa blo gros dpal/ bla brang pa bzang po dpal/ bla brang pa nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bla brang pa bsod nams dpal 'byor/ bla brang pa chos dpal bzang po/ chag lo rin chen chos
rgyal/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse ba nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ bka' babs
gnyis pa dpyal lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i gshed/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug shrI birWa pa/ Dombi he ru kabI ra Di pa/ dge slong byi la'i sham

thabs can/ byi la pa yang zer/ma ti garbha/ gambhi ra ma ti/ niShka langka / dpyal chos bzang / rje btsun rgwa lo/ rong pa shes rab seng ge bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad
mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gsum pa dA na shI la lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam gsar/ rje btsun rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ rong pa shes rab seng ge skyi ston
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje kun mkhyen chen po/ jo nang pa phyogs las rnam rgyal/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man gong dang 'dra'o/
/!/ thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i gshin rje'i gshed dmar po'i shin tu spros med kyi khrid yig nges don rdo rje'i rnal 'byor them skas kyi steng nas/
gang zag mchog skal ba dang ldan pa cig car ba'i lam gyis bkri bar 'os pa'i don du gsungs pa shin tu spros pa med pa'i khrid kyi rim pa zab mo smin rgyas spros med kyi
byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi'i byin rlabs dang bcas pa legs par thob nas rgyab brten lung la/ thog mar rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pas mdzad pa'i gshin rje mthar byed dmar po
lha lnga'i mngon rtogs las tshogs dang bcas pa ston pa'i sgrub thabs che ba nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur ba/ de'i sgrub thabs chung ba
dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ gtor ma'i cho ga gnyis dang bskyed rim gyi gzhung gsum

dang / spros med rdo rje'i tshig rkang / rdzogs rim shin tu spros pa med pa de kho na nyid kyi man ngag darpan A tsArYa dang / glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur
ba/ des mdzad pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa'i man ngag 'od gsal 'char ba'i rim pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po re wendra dang / chag lo chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur ba ste rdzogs rim
gyi gzhung gsum/ gshin rje'i gshed kyi 'khrul 'khor gyi phreng ba dang / der mi gsal ba'i sngags btu dang / las so so'i sngags gsal bar ston pa/ gshin rje'i gshed kyi 'khrul
'khor gyi cho ga ste bi rU pa'i gzhung brgyad/ des mdzad pa'i bdud rtsi byin rlabs kyi rim pa darpan dang lo tsA ba zhe sdang rdo rje'i 'gyur/ de'i khrid yig glo bo lo
tsA bas mdzad pa/ spros med brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ spros med rgyun gyi nyams len yongs 'dzin gyis mdzad pa dang sa los mdzad pa rnams dang
/ gshin rje'i gshed dmar po'i rgyud le'u bcu dgu pa rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa legs par thob pa las/ rdzogs rim zab mo shin tu spros med kyi byin rlabs dang khrid thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i gshed/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa/ grub pa'i dbang phyug Dombi he ru kabI ra Di pa/ dge slong byi la'i
sham thabs can/grub pa'i 'khor los 'gyur ba bram ze dpal 'dzin/ sngon lha dang lha min 'thab pa'i tshe lha phrug gcig gi mgo chad par rang gi dbu sbyar bas gsos/ ma he shi
ba'i mgo rang la sbyar bas dge slong gi lus la ma he'i mgo can/blo bzang snying po/ paNDi ta darpan A tsArYa/ krI ya sa mutstsha mdzad pa po lo

dgu stong dang nyis brgya bzhugs pa/glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ sras bla ma sa pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad mkhyen
pa bu ston rin chen grub/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ jo nang pa phyogs las rnam rgyal/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus
chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje buddha singha / paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje nam
mkha' sangs rgyas/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rje btsun sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' chos 'phel/ rigs brgya'i
khyab bdag chen po bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na sems dpa' chen po nas/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / kun spangs
pa/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ rje bsod nams rgya mtsho
man 'dra'o/ /yang na bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan nas/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang
na bu ston nas/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ mkhas pa tsandra shrI ratna/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rje/ rdo ring pa man
'dra/ yang na thugs sras nas/ bsod nams don

grub/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rje man 'dra'o/ /birWa pa'i gzhung brgyad kyi bdud rtsi byin rlabs dang tshig rkang lung gi brgyud
pa ni/ gshin rje'i gshed/ birWa pa/ ma ti garbha/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ shAnta rakShi ta/ darpaN A tsArYa/ glo bo lo tsA sogs gzhan 'dra'o/ /yang nye brgyud byed na/ shar
chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mnal lam bzung nas sau ma pu rir rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa dang dngos su mjal nas gsan pas/ rdo rje 'chang / birWa pa/ shar chen man
sngar ltar ro/ /!/ rnam snang gi rigs su gtogs pa zhe sdang can gtso bor 'dul ba gshin rje'i gshed skor la rwa lo dge ba rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gshin
rje kun 'joms dang / dkyil chog gzhon nu rnam rol/ de'i zur 'debs mkhas pa bkra shis dpal ldan gyis mdzad pa'i steng nas/ rwa lugs kyi dpal gshin rje gshed dgra nag lha
bcu gsum ma ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi rdzogs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pradznyA rakShi
ta/ bal po menydza gling  ngor pa'i gsan yig 'gar menydze gling pa/ bal po thugs rje chen po zhes so sor byas 'dug pa thugs rje chen po/ sa dge ba'i mkhas grub mang po
bal po bha ro dang gcig par mdzad kyang 'di ye rang ba dang bha ro yam bu ba yin zhing thugs rje chen po ni dus 'khor phag mo sogs la shin tu mkhas/ bha ro ni gshin rje gshed
kyi grub pa thob pa tsam las mkhas par ma grags pas so sor ma 'dres par dgos par mngon no zhes rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po gsung ngo / /rwa chen lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/
rab

byung /rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge  sngags pa dkar chas lcang lo can/ rwa 'bum seng /sngags dkar co dreg can/ rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ thar rtse sgrub khang pa shar
pa gsum gyi gsan yig tu don yod rdo rje yin tshul 'dug pa gsang mtshan dang 'khrul lam dpyad/de sras rong pa shes rab seng ge  'di man rab byung /bla ma dpal ldan seng
ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ bla ma rin chen dpal grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab
chos rje/ mkhan chen rig 'dzin rgyal po/ bla chen chos rig rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsod nams dpal 'byor/ rje byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal
bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab 'byung gnas/ rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag bkra shis dpal ldan/ rigs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba rdo rje sems
dpa' bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs bdud 'joms snang ba/ dkyil
chog rab gsal snang ba/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor rnams kyi steng nas rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs ro langs chen po brgyad
kyis bskor ba'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi
mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ paNDi ta a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ grub chen padma

badzra/ dI paM ka ra/ bal po bha ro phyag rdum yang zer/rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rab byung /rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge  sngags pa gos dkar lcang lo can/rwa 'bum
seng / glog skya dbang phyug grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod
nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun
grub/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje buddha singha / rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/
bstan pa'i snang byed mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ dus dgra'i mgon po khyab bdag bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka'
drin du yang yang stsal to/ /yang na dbu mdzad phrin las rgya mtsho/ bka' drin mnyam med mkhan po chen po thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims
rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang
na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ dbu mdzad phrin
las rgya

mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na glo bo mkhan chen nas/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen man
'dra/ yang na paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rin po che dpal ldan don grub/ shes rab 'byung gnas man 'dra/ yang na sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje nas/ gnyen chen grags pa blo gros/
chos rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na rje nam mkha' dpal bzang las/ shar chen dang / nam mkha' sangs rgyas gnyis kas gsan/
de gnyis las rje dam chos pas so/ /snga ma gnyis char las gzar chen pas gsan/ de las rje dam chos pas so/ /yang na rwa 'bum seng nas/ rong pa rgwa lo/ rong pa shes rab seng
ge rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ mkhan chen rin rnam pa/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man gong dang 'dra/ yang na rong pa rgwa lo/
rong pa shes rab seng ge bag ston/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal/ bla ma dge ba rgyal mtshan/ bla ma shes rab zla ba/ sngags 'chang rin chen
rnam rgyal/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra'o/ /!/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa'i go don bdud rtsi'i
nying khu dang rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi khrid yig sku gsum lam byed snying gi thig le'i steng nas rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rdzogs rim rwa rtse sems 'dzin/ mtshan mo rgyu
ba/ mtshan ma gyen bsgreng rnams

thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gshin rje'i gshed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ la lI ta badzra/ 'jam dpal gshin rje/ a mo gha badzra che chung gnyis/ skyo ston 'od 'byung / skyo ston
ye shes 'byung gnas/ skyo ston bsod nams bla ma/ jo sras khams pa/ gnyen rin chen brtan/ gnyen 'od srungs/ gnyen chos rgyal/ 'dzim pa rin she/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/
shar pa 'jam dbyangs  'dis sa skya'i gdan sa lo bco brgyad mdzad/gzhi thog pa/ cha gan dbang rgyal/ klog skya grags chen/ klog skya dang grags chen so sor byas pa'ang snang
/kun mkhyen gongs pa/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / gu ge paNDi ta/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje
dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ dbon shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje nyang stod pa dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rmor
chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug bka' drin mnyam med rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal
to/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /sangs rgyas phun tshogs la gsan dus kyi khrid
yig mkhan chen legs 'byung gi gsung las rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas zin bris mdzad pa las thos so gsung / /!/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud dang rgya

gzhung rnams thos pa'i rnam grangs la/ sa ngor nas brgyud pa dang 'og nas 'byung ba gnyis phal cher zlos te 'byung yang dpe rgyun gyi sgrig rim mi 'dra ba dang / bla ma phyi
mas mdzad pa'i kha 'gengs mang nyung la sogs pa khyad par mchis pa rnams so sor ma bkod na/ rjes 'jug pa dag brgyud tshul tha dad pa'i khungs zhib par dpyod mi nus pa sogs
kyis rtogs dka' ba mchis par brten/ lung rgyun rgyas bsdus gcig go gcig chod du gyur na shin tu mi btub par snyam nas/ thog mar ngor nas brgyud pa ltar 'god pa la/ rtog
bdun thugs rje chen po dang rwa lo'i 'gyur/ yang rtog bdun mal los bsgyur ba la sa skya pas gsan pa'i lugs mchan 'byar ba/ rtog bdun gyi dka' 'grel chos kyi shes rab kyi
'gyur/ rtog pa gsum pa mchan 'byar ba/ slob dpon shrI bha dras mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rwa 'gyur/ a mo ghas
mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ bstod pa/ dbang chog sbyin sreg zhi ba las bdun dang drag po las bdun a mo gha chung bas mdzad par grags pa/ gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa mdzad byang
med pa/ gtor chog dang uShNI Sha'i srung 'khor bha ros mdzad pa/ tshogs 'khor shAnti pas mdzad pa rnams rwa 'gyur/ tstshun dha ra'i sgrub thabs dang / rtog pa zhi ba mo rwa
'gyur/ ya ma rA dza'i rtsa sngags lo tsA ba rdo rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ ma mo brgyad bskor gyi sgrub thabs 'jam dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ lha mo brgyad bskor gyi sgrub thabs
zhi ba ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'khor lo bskor ba'i las

drag po/ dpa' gcig che ba'i sgrub thabs dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa ba ri ba chos grags kyis bsgyur ba ste rgya gzhung de rnams kyi lung dang / rwa pod du grags pa'i chos kyi
rnam grangs ni/ rgyud kyi rgyal po rtog bdun la/ /nag 'grel mun pa'i mda' 'phen brtsams/ /dkar 'grel phyogs mthong 'bem la gtad/ /bcud kyi thigs pas phog par bsnun/ /gsod
pa'i mtshon de snying la gab/ /kha brgyud yi ge ra mthong ba bkod/ /bsnyen sgrub las gshin sbrel ma yod/ /mngon rtogs rim pa lnga yang yod/ /las bzhi'i sbyin sreg cho ga
yod/ /smin byed dkyil chog yig sna yod/ /dmar mo mda' gzhu 'gengs pa yod/ /'di dag rnams ni mi legs na'ang / /ban chung rwa yi lugs su snang / /nga yi rjes 'brang thams
cad kyis/ /bcos bslad ma byed nyams su long / /zhes pa ltar te/ de'ang thems yig nag 'grel gnyis/ dkar 'grel gnyis/ bcud kyi  lag len khrigs bkod zer ba yod/thigs pa/ ha
la'i shog dril/ de'i gsal byed rgya ston gyis mdzad pa/ mngon rtogs dri med snang ba/ phyag drug pa'i mngon rtogs khams gsum za byed/ phyag bzhi pa'i mngon rtogs dri med
chu rgyun/ phyag gnyis pa'i mngon rtogs rin chen don bsdus/ mngon rtogs yid bzhin gter mdzod/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg dbang chog chos rab kyi don du mdzad pa/ rma bya dug dbang
man ngag dang bcas pa/ las gshin gnad la dbab pa'i man ngag rnams rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis mdzad pa rnams dang / gzhan yang 'khrul 'khor gyi

man ngag sgrub pa'i zhal gdams bsnyen sgrub bsad gsum drag po'i sbyin sreg rnams mdzad byang med pa/ bsnyen sgrub kyi lag len dang spogs chog mdzad byang med pa/ yang gshin
rje nyi ma bzhi pa dang de'i man ngag 'bum seng ge sa mdzad pa/ rtog bdun gyi bsdus don rwa sher rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub kyi lag len rwa chos rab kyis mdzad pa/
phyag mtshan so gnyis kyi las tshogs zhes bya ba/ gri gug gis dgra gsad pa/ shAktis phung bar byed pa/ gtun shing gis rims dbab cing 'dre brdung ba/ chu gris grir 'gum
pa/ rdo rje rtse gcig pas gdon bsrung ba/ dgra stwas dgra bo tshar gcod pa/ mdung gis cho 'phrul gtang ba/ mda' gzhus sgrub thabs rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa gong du song
zin/ lcags kyus mtshan ma dgug pa/ dbyug tos nor bsgrub pa/ kha TwAM gas nyams chag sel ba/ 'khor los bgegs bsrung ba/ rdo rjes klu bsrung ba/ tho bas bar chad bsrung
ba/ ral gris dmag dpung bzlog pa/ cang te'us DA ki las la 'gyed pa/ thod pas nor bsgrub pa/ mgo bos 'gal ba cham la 'bebs pa/ phub kyis phyir bzlog pa/ rkang pa rlung gi
dkyil 'khor gyis skrod pa/ zhags pas lha dang mi'i bu mo dgug pa/ rwa'i mda' gzhus bi Sha gsad pa/ rgyu zhags kyis rims nad bzlog pa/ dril bus nyams chag bskang ba/ lag pas
phrin las bsgrub pa/ ro ras kyi 'khor los las kun bsgrub pa/ gsal shing gi ros ro langs bsgrub pa/ me thab kyis sbyin sreg cho ga bsgrub pa/ thod tshal gyis dgra bo gnad
la dbab

pa/ sdigs mdzub kyis 'gal ba cham la dbab pa/ 'phan rtse gsum pas 'gro ba dbang du sdud pa/ 'phyar dar gyis phyogs skyong ba bsdu ba rnams/ shar du 'khrul 'khor/ lhor sbyin
sreg nub tu tshogs 'khor/ byang du gtor ma la brten nas dgra bo bsgral ba'i man ngag uShNi Sha rwa lugs kyi yi ge rnying ma rwa los mdzad pa/ khro bcu'i srung bzlogasrung
bzlog gnyis kyi 'khor lo/ ming dang rnam shes sba ba sogs zhal gdams gnad kyi lde migabasad las dam nyams gsod pa'i mtshon cha/ srung bzlog gnyis kyi man ngag srung 'khor
gyi bstod bskul che chung gnyis rnams lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrIs mdzad pa rnams bla ma paNDi tas phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa dang / 'khor lo'i dpe chung rnams dang / rtog
bdun dang / rtog gsum gyi bsdus don re dang / de dag gi TI ka re dang / drug cu pa'i gtor chog rnams rgya ston gyis mdzad pa dang / yang ldong ston gyis mdzad pa'i las sna
tshogs dgra gshed gsal ba'i rgyan/ sku gsung thugs kyi byin rlabs/ drag po'i rgyan rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni yan chad dbang brgyud ltar la/ de nas rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po/ paN chen grags rgyal/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man sngar bzhin
no/ /yang dbus pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i rtog bdun gyi zhal shes man ngag lnga pa/ rtog gsum gyi 'khrul 'khor/ rtog gsum gyi sa bcad/ 'khrul 'khor gyi lung

sbyor/ bsnyen sgrub kyi lag len/ bzlas yig drag gcod zab mo/ zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg zhi ba'i las kyi cho ga rgyas pa'i las sgrub pa'i cho ga dbang dgug gi sbyin sreg dbang
dgug don yod zhags pa/ dgra phung ba'i man ngag de'i spogs chog sngags bzla tshul/ rdo rje'i mtshon cha 'bar ba/ dbye ba'i cho ga mnan bskrad rengs pa gsum/ srin pos 'dzin
pa/ rims nad/ 'khrug pa/ smyo ba'i cho ga ga'u sro ba'i man ngag gzugs brnyan sreg chog drag po'i gtor chog de ma 'grub na gnad 'bebs/ bsad pa'i sbyin sreg 'khor lo'i
dpe chung drug sngags spyi'i 'khor lo'i man ngag rtsa sngags kyi 'khrul 'khor/ bsad pa'i cho ga sngags btu/ 'khor lo rin po che'i mdzod/ las thams cad pa'i sbyin sreg rtog
gsum gyi rgyas 'grel/ drag shul spyod pa'i cho ga dug ha la ha la rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'bri khung dpal 'dzin/ sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal/ rje btsun sangs
rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge man sngar dang 'dra/ rje kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i zhi ba las bdun dang paN chen gu ge
ba grags rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i drug cu pa'i phyag len gyi yi ge'i lung yang thos so/ /!/ mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug rwa chen lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis mdzad pa'i mngon
rtogs yid bzhin gter mdzod dang dbang gi chu bo gnyis la rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i sgrub dkyil gsal byed lhan thabs nyi gzhon gsar pa'i dga' ston dang
/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang

phyug gis mdzad pa'i ngag 'don phreng chags nag po 'gro shes rnams kyis rnam par brgyan pa'i steng nas bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa lha
bcu gsum gyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal khros pa'i zhal lung
snying gi gzungs khrag mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs can gyi steng du rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa'i sngon 'gro lo rgyus sbyar ba dang bcas te/ dpal rdo

thob kyang de thob 'gyur gyis bris/ grub pa'i dbang phyug la lI ta badzra gyis mdzad pa'i khrid don gsal byed rgyal khams lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI dznyA nas mdzad pa'i yi

byed dpa' bo gcig pa zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i rjes gnang / rje shar khang pa'i yi ge'i steng nas phyag mtshan mda' gzhu la brten pa'i bi Sha bsad pa'i las tshogs dug
dbang rma bya rgyas pa/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i gtor chog rjes gnang gi yi ge la brten nas 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje dam can chos kyi rgyal po lha
bcu gsum gyi rjes su gnang ba/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i tho yig la brten nas las gshin dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes

gnang / tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i gtor chog rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i yi ge la brten nas las kyi gshin rje dmar po bse bya bzhis bskor gyi rjes gnang / des mdzad
pa'i gtor chog rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i yi ge'i steng nas gshin rje dmar po khrag mdog yab yum gyi rjes gnang rnams nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la rwa chen shes rab rgyal
mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i dkar chag na gsal ba'i chos skor/ der ma 'khod pa'i rgya bod kyi yig sna'i skor/ bod kyi mkhas pa 'bri khung dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i skor dang
gsum/ dang po la rwa lugs kyi gshin rje gshed nag po skor gsum du grags pa'i dkar chag rwa chen gyis mdzad pa'i tshigs bcad dang de'i rgyas bshad rwa dbon shes rab rgyal
mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ der gsal ba'i yig sna la/ rgyud 'bum pa las la lI ta badzra gyis phyung pa'i dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed khros pa'i rgyal po'am rtsa (rwa)(kun)ba'i

'byung ba'i a mo ghas mdzad pa'i dkyil chog 'gyur du bha ro'i mtshan smos pas kyang 'di gnyis tha dad par tshad mas grub bo/ /slob dpon chen po a mo gha badzra gyis mdzad
pa'i rdo rje 'jigs byed lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor (rwa)(kun)gyi cho ga dngos grub brnyes pa'i bla ma bha ro dang rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba/ rdo rje

/ des mdzad pa'i dkar (rwa)(rdo rje)(kun)'grel rtog pa bdun pa'i man ngag gi gnad du grags pa/ dpe la lar dka' gnad kyi 'grel pa'i brda dag bris yod 'dug kyang / dkar 'grel

sreg

(rwa)(kun)'dod pa kun 'phel/ dbang gi sbyin sreg (rwa)(kun)gnad kyi lcags kyu/ des sngags 'chang khro rgyal dang blo ldan gnyis kyi don du mdzad (rwa)(kun)pa'i drag po'i sbyin

gsum bstan pa/ bstan pa 'dzin skyong spel zhing nad gso ba (sher)la gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur ba/ rdo rje 'jigs byed dmar po'i mngon rtogs sngon por bsgyur yod do'i mtha'
can/ gu lang (rwa)(legs)gi mgo can la brten nas bzlas pa/ sngags kyi gnas pa/ dug brtag pa/ bsrung bya/ gso thabs rnams bstan pa (rwa)(legs)bi Sha bzhi skor/ bshal (rwa)(legs)bya
ba/ sngags kyis bi Sha phyogs med (rwa)(legs)thub pa kha ri su/ rdzas dgus (rwa)(legs)bi Sha phyogs med thub pa/ ser po (rwa)(legs)gsum sbyor/ rna ba mig sogs lus
kyi cha gang la babs pa (rwa)(legs)sngags rdzas gtar kha sman la brten nas 'chos pa/ phyag mtshan mda' gzhu la brten nas bi Sha bsad pa'i las bstan pa (rwa)(legs)lcags
rtse zlum po 'jib pa gnad yin gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ dug khyer yod pa'i mi dang nad pa'i brtag (rwa)(legs)thabs nag por song na bi Sha yin gyi mtha' can/ 'jigs byed glang
mgo can gyi bi Sha (rwa)(legs)gso bsrung badzra rakSha kIrtis A tsArYa la zhus pa badzra bhai ra'i rakSha'i mtha'

can/ sngags thems u pa (rwa)(legs)tadya thA/ bya ra bsrung ba/ khyab 'jug karko tra'i 'jug pa la (rwa)(legs)brten nas brtag thabs/ tho rengs kyi dri chur (rwa)(legs)brtag cing
bsrung ba/ dug (rwa)(legs)'breng / sngags (rwa)(legs)bshal/ khyi smyon gyis rmugs (rwa)(legs)par dug yod med blta ba/ be bum kha pa'i nang gi (rwa)(legs)shog dril gyi
gdams pa shin tu gces pa'i skor dpe la dam par mdzod kyi mtha' can/ dmar po mda' gzhu 'geng pa la brten pa'i dbang sdud skal med rnams la sba ba shis kyi mtha' can/ rdo

'gyur/ gtam rgyus kyi rtog pa dang las mkhan te'u lo pa chu bya'i rtog pa gnyis bha ros rgyud 'bum pa la gtugs te rgya dpe la phyis bsgyur ba/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson
'grus kyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen yon tan

tshul/ rgyud dang bla ma brgyud pa byon tshul gyi lo rgyus don gsum pa rgya ston gyi slob (shar)ma zhig gis mdzad pa/ rdzong lugs zab don bdud rtsi'i bcud (nub)kyi brgyud
pa'i gsol 'debs sku bzhi'i ngo bo/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal bas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs (nub)rab tu gsang ba yid bzhin gyi nor bu/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos

pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis
