pa A nanda ma tis rgya ston gyi yi ge la brten nas mdzad pa'i rwa pa'i man ngag (shar)thun mong ma yin pa lcags mkhar zur dgu pa'i 'jigs byed drug cu pa/ rdo rje 'chang
pha bong kha ba'i phyag len dang mi gcig par snang /bzlas pa'i man ngag dang gtor ma drug cu rtsa bzhi'i phyag len (shar)rgya ston dang 'dzam gling mkhas pa'i khyad bcas/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i (dpang )gtor ma drug cu rtsa bzhi zhal bsgyur ba'i man ngag yi ge bzhi pa la brten pa'i bsrung ba'i man ngag 'gor rang nyid 'jigs
byed dmar po shin tu khros pa zhes yod pa gsol ba gdab bo'i mtha' can/ yi ge bzhi pa la brten nas 'gong po gdug pa can gnod na bsad pa rta shi'i kha bzhin sdoms kyi mtha'
can/ 'gor rang nyid skad cig dran rdzogs la 'jam dpal khros pa zhes yod pa'i

srung bzlog bsad pa gsum gyi man ngag zab mo i thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor srung ba'i 'khor lo ni lte bar hU~M zhes yod pa/ 'gor mu khyud rdo rje phyed pa nang du 'khor lo rtsibs
brgyad ces yod pa'i bzlog 'khor/ 'gor yang lte bar hU~M gsham nas g.yon skor du zhes yod pa'i srung 'khor bri yig 'gor rang nyid 'phags pa 'jam dpal du bsgom zhes yod pa'i
yi ge bzhi pa'i srung bzlog bsad gsum gyi man ngag 'gor oM swasti/ sems bskyed pa ni bdag dang sems can thams cad mi dang mi ma yin zhes yod pa'i yi ge bzhi pa'i srung
(rwa)(nub)bzlog rbad pa zhal gdams dang bcas pa khyad par du 'phags pa'o'i mtha' can/ yi ge bzhi pa'i srung bzlog bsad mnan bsam gtan nyal (nub)chog gi gdams pa theg mchog
zla ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis bal po thugs rje chen po la gser srang lnga brgya phul (rwa)(nub)(rum)bar zhal gyis bzhes nas gnang ba'i
drag po bzhi'i srung bzlog yi ge ra mi 'dri ba'i bka' rgya can/ 'gor bdag nyid 'phags pa 'jam dpal zhes yod pa'i yi ge (nub)bzhi pa'i man ngag nyi ma dang sprad do'i mtha'
can/ 'gor rang nyid skad cig dran rdzogs la zhes yod pa'i yi ge bzhi pa'i (rwa)(nub)srung bzlog bsad gsum gyi man ngag zab mo'i mtha' can/ bha ya nA sa la brten pa'i byad
bzlog thams cad kyis tshugs par mi 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ btsan po'i mkhar du gzhug pa/ rno gsum mtshon la ngar btags pa/ gdos dang sha ba 'thab pa/ sgyogs rdo bar snang
la gcag pa ste rwa rgan

(shar)lo tsA'i khyad chos uShNI Sha'i srung bzlog mnan gsad rgya ston gyis bsgrigs pa/ des mdzad pa'i uShNI Sha'i (shar)gdams pa don lnga pa/ des mdzad pa'i man ngag thugs
kyi nying khu (shar)zhes par nang gses bsam gtan sgra'i bzlas pa/ phrin las rnam bzhi'i bzlas pa/ ting 'dzin gnad kyi man ngag gdug byed phur pas ngag bcing ba/ rmi lam ngan
pa bzlog pa/ mthu byed bsad pa/ ngag mnan dang bcas pa rwa lo'i man ngag byad ma phye mar 'thags pa (shar)rwa'i man ngag thod pa/ phur pa/ 'khor lo/ rang gshed la brten
nas bsad pa'i dus man ngag nyams su len pa'i (shar)rim pa zhes bsgom pa/ sngags/ yungs kar/ khragaphur bus bsad pa gza' rgyu ba dang bstun no'i mtha' can/ rgya ston kun
dga' brtson 'grus kyi dngos slob bod log dang star ma bye bzang gnyis kha mthun du byung ba'i man ngag (shar)dpal ldan grags pas tshigs bcad du bsdebs pa'i don gsal bar
bstan pa/ rdzas la brten pa'i gtad (shar)rul/ ting nge 'dzin la (shar)brten pa'i gtad rul/ ngag (shar)'grol 'gor/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed khro bo'i rgyal po la phyag 'tshal
lo/ /zhes (ma)yod pa'i uShNI Sha'i bsrung bzlog man ngag lag len dmar khrid phyogs med lo tsA bas gsal bar bkod pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'gor/ dpal khro bo'i rgyal po la phyag
'tshal lo/ /'dir bdag gzhan thams cad kyi lus (ma)srung bar byed pa zhes yod pa'i srung 'khor gyi bri yig des mdzad pa'i 'gor gnyis pa bzlog pa'i

'khor lo ni snga ma lta bu la/ ming spel gyi mthar zhes yod pa'i bzlog 'khor bri yig des mdzad pa'i 'gor Ni?Hdpal ldan khro bo chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /ming dang rnam shes
sba ba la zhes yod (ma)pa'i uShNI Sha'i srung 'khor rmi lam ngan pa bzlog pa byad ma mkhan gyi bsod nams nyams thabs byas pas mi tshugs pa dang bcas pa/ des mdzad pa'i
bzlog pa'i rnal 'byor khyad (ma)par can rngon pa nyi ma lde zhing gdos dang sha ba 'thab pa lta bu'i man ngag des mdzad pa'i uShNI Sha'i sgo (ma)nas dam nyams gsod pa'i
mtshon cha/ des brag dkar chos sdings su bkod pa'i bsrung bzlog (ma)gnyis kyi man ngag sngags pa nang 'gras dang bsad pa gzhan du gsal ba'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i uShNI
Sha'i bskul (ma)rnam dag zhi ba ma/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa (ma)thugs rje'i dbang khros ma/ las kyi gshin rje chos kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs la li ta badzra gyis mdzad
pa bal po thugs rje chen po dang rwa lo rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba/ ro ras dang thod pa la brten nas las gshin sgrub cing bsnyen sgrub bsad pa'i man ngag lo tsA ba phyi
mas yi ge ra btab pa/ las kyi gshin rje srid pa'i 'khor lo'i man ngag rwa chen gyis lcags sgom ras pa la gnang ba srid pa'i 'khor lo rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ dge 'dun
gtsug lag khang bsrung ba'i gshin rje srid pa'i 'khor lo bka' rgya dam po yod do i thi'i mtha' can/ las kyi gshin rje gnam lcags ur chung gi gdams pa zhes pa srung bzlog
bsad pa'i sngags bzlog pa yin na sngags bzla zhing bsad pa lhwam mthu ma

dang bcas pa sus kyang mi shigs pa'i man ngag lags so'i mtha' can/ las kyi gshin rje'i yig chung / drag sngags hur thum srog len dmar po snya nam pa'i man ngag yig chung zab
mo rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ dkon mchog gi bstan dgra ya ma rnams kyis 'dul bar khas blangs tshul/ 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje gnad la phab nas dgra bgegs sgrol ba'i yi
ge drag sngags kyi rgyan du dgos pa'i yig chung i thi'i mtha' can/ 'chi bdag sgrub (rgya)thabs gshes gnyen tshul khrims bla mas bskul ba'i ngor rgya ston gyis mdzad pa/
chos kyi rgyal po lha bcu gsum gyi mchod pa'i cho ga (rtsa)(bikShu)khrom yon nam mkha' lhun bzang gis mdzad pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos las dang po pa'i rig 'dzin
rnams la phan pa'i ched du mdzad pa'i (mkhan)las kyi gshin rje 'khor dang bcas pa la mchod gtor 'bul ba'i cho ga 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i dam
can gshin rje'i rgyal po'i mngon rtogs spyan 'dren (dbang )gtor 'bul bstod pa dang bcas pa'i chog sgrigs/ des mdo khams pa sbyin pa dpal bzang gi ngor mdzad pa'i 'chi bdag
(mkhan)()gshin rje'i dbang phyug chos kyi rgyal po'i thugs dam bskang ba mi bzad 'jam dpal ma/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad (dbang )pa'i las gshin gyi
bskang rdzas byin rlabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis bkod pa/ las gshin bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang gi yi ge thar gling (bikShu)ArYa de was bkod

pa/ las gshin dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes gnang gi tho (dbang )kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ gshin rje dmar nag gsum gyi rjes gnang gi (sa)cho ga'i lag len shin
tu gsal ba rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa/ gshin rje dmar po ma ru tse bzhis bskor du (dznyA)grags pa snying la brten pa'i phyi sgrub/ spyang thod la brten pa'i
nang sgrub/ nal gri'i thod par brten pa'i gsang sgrub/ ra spyang gi thod par brten pa'i gsang chen chig dril/ gtor chog bstod pa dang bcas pa rdo rje dbal ba'i don du
rgya ston gyis mdzad pa/ las kyi gshin rje khrag mdog yab yum gyi bsnyen sgrub (dpal)las gsum gyi man ngag rwa dbon shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa dge bas bstan pa
bsrung bar shog gi mtha' can/ de'i gtor chog rjes gnang dang bcas (dpal)pa'i cho ga rnams so/ /gsum pa bod kyi mkhas pa 'bri gung dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i skor la/ kun
dga' dbang phyug gis bskul pa'i ngor mdzad pa'i rtog pa gsum pa'i rgyas 'grel rin po che'i snye ma/ rtog pa gsum pa'i tshig gis mtshams bcad cing don gyi go rim bsdu ba/
dpal rtog pa gsum pa'i 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga khams gsum gyi 'khor los sgyur ba khrag skyugs kyi lo chos dkar nam mkha'i rdzong du mdzad pa/ de las drag shul spyod pa'i
cho ga zhib mo gud du bstan pa zad pa'i lo nag pa zla ba'i dkar tshes bzhi la mdzad pa/ rtog pa gsum pa'i man ngag gi zhal shes lnga pa zhes pa snyan brgyud yi ge med pa'i
zin bris mdangs dkar snying rje'i rdzong du mdzad pa/ rtog pa gsum pa'i

'khrul 'khor rdzong ri rtse dgu'i mgul du mdzad pa/ thar pa'i rgyal srid la gnas pa'i dge sbyong chen po'i bkas bskul ba la brten nas 'khrul 'khor gyi lung sbyor rin chen 'od
kyi sgron ma/ dpal rtog pa bdun pa'i 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga 'khor lo rin po che'i bang mdzod chos dkar nam mkha'i rdzong du mdzad pa/ de la mkho ba'i zin bris 'gor rtog
bdun gyi rgyas 'grel slob dpon mi bskyod pas mdzad ces yod pa rang bzo med par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bsnyen sgrub lag tu blang
ba'i rim pa snying gtam glen pa'i tshig tu btsun pa kun dga' dbang phyug la gdams pa/ rtags kyi yi ge zhib mo khrag skyugs kyi lo lhun gyis grub pa'i rdzong du mdzad pa/
rtsa ba'i sngags kyi bzlas pa'i tshul nges pa seng ge'i nga ro me byi mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ drag po'i las kyi bzlas pa rdo rje 'bar ba'i mtshon cha
me byi mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ 'di sngags sdebs yin 'dug pa gsar ma phyogs la grags chung bas dpal 'dzin rtsa ba gsang sngags rnying ma bar song gshis
snga 'gyur bka' gter gyi man ngag zab mo nas rku thabs kyi tshul du bris par mngon no/ /mdo khams tre shod pa rtogs ldan bsod nams dpal gyis bskul ba la brten nas thang skya'i
gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa'i las thams cad pa'i sbyin sreg dngos grub kyi gzi brjid rab snang / zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg nyes pa'i tshang tshing ma lus pa sreg par
nus pa bsod nams kyi nyi ma bdun 'bar mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ rgyud

rtog pa bdun pa'i 'khrul 'khor gyi skabs su khyim du bzhag na zhi bar 'gyur ro zhes pa'i man ngag zhi ba'i dngos grub bsgrub pa'i cho ga bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho/ de'i yan lag
'jigs pa zhi ba'i srung 'khor/ mtshon srung ba/ tshe sgrub dang bcas pa gtsang rong dmu lha shambhar gyi gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ yang gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i rgyas
pa'i las bsgrub pa'i cho ga yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che 'bar ba yan lag dang bcas pa/ dbang du bya ba'i cho ga don yod pa'i zhags pa rnam par g.yo ba/ de'i yan lag
'gugs pa'i cho ga lcags kyu 'bar ba/ bskyed rdzogs kyi rim pa gang rung gi lam gyi grogs su rig pa'i skyes bu 'gugs pa zhu ba'i bsam gtan rig ma mi bsrun pa 'dul thabs
bu mo rengs pa'i sbyor ba rnams me byi shambhar dpal gyi yang dgon du mdzad pa/ dbang dang 'gugs pa'i cho ga 'jig rten gsum rnam par gnon pa mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang
du mdzad pa/ drag po'i cho ga gshin rje'i gzugs la brten nas dgra sde 'phung bar bya ba'i man ngag 'jig rten gsum gyi bshan pa chen po rnam par rol pa skal ldan sbyin pa
rin chen gyi ched du mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gsum gyi bshan pa chen po rnam par rol pa ma grub na spogs pa'i cho ga 'jig rten gsum za ba me pho byi ba'i lor mdzad pa/ bsad pa'i
phrin las ga'u sro ba'i man ngag sa gsum rnam par 'joms pa'i 'khrul 'khor me byi mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ yang gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i sdig pa sbyong
ba'i cho ga sbyin sreg dang 'khrul 'khor sbrags pa 'jig rten gsum phung bar byed pa/ mdza' ba

dbye bar byed pa shambhar du mdzad pa/ yang gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i sdang ba yul nas dbyung ba bskrad pa'i 'khrul 'khor/ gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i g.yam pa la brten nas
rengs pa'i cho ga 'jig rten gsum rnam par g.yo ba/ gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i te'u lo pa'i pags pa la brten nas rengs pa'i cho ga 'jig rten gsum rnam par 'ching ba/ gnas
de nyid du mdzad pa'i yan lag mtshon gyis 'bugs pa'i man ngag 'jig rten gsum pham par byed pa/ srin pos 'dzin pa'i cho ga las kyi srin po zhes bya ba mtshur phur mdzad pa/
yang de nyid du mdzad pa'i rims nad gtang ba'i man ngag rims nad chen po 'khrug pa/ yang gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i smyo bar byed pa'i cho ga drag po'i bzhad gad chen
po/ drag shul spyod pa'i gtor ma drug cu rtsa bzhi'i cho ga sdig can sgrol ba'i mtshon cha ngar ma mdangs dkar snying rje rdzong du mdzad pa/ lugs srol 'di la lcags mkhar
mi rtsig pa'i phyogs su mdzad nas/ lcags mkhar zur dgu pa dang zur bcu drug pa sogs spro na byar rung gi 'on kyang rnying ma ba ltar blos btags nas byas pa yin pas rgyud
rgya gzhung gi khungs ni med la zhes zur za ba ni/ spyir kun rdzob kyi chos thams cad blos btags nas byas pa kho na yin pas gzhung lugs dang 'gal zhing rgyud rgya gzhung
gi khungs med bzhin du gsar ma ba rnams spro na byar rung ba'i dam bcar song bas ma thob pa'i gzhung cig 'dir shor bar gda'o/ /ma 'grub na gnad la dbab pa'i cho ga sa gsum
nges par 'joms pa me byi mtshur phur mdzad pa/ yang de nyid du mdzad

pa'i bsad pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga dus kyi me lce 'bar ba chen po'i phreng ba/ rtsa sngags kyi 'khrul 'khor bri ba'i zin bris bris pas chog go'i mtha' can/ rtog bdun 'khrul
'khor mchog gi man ngag rdzong ri rtse dgu'i mgul du brjed byang du mdzad pa/ las kyi gshin rje yab yum sbrags te bsgrub pa'i man ngag dug ha la ha la chen po zhes pa lhun
gyis grub pa'i rdzong du sbyar ba rnams so/ /'jigs byed kyi 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba zhes pa dang gtor ma'i cho ga'i lag len bsod
nams kyi 'od zer rnam par spel ba'i nyi ma zhes bya ba gnyis kyi lung rgyun deng sang mi 'dug gtor ma'i cho ga 'di la zhi rgyas dbang drag gi drug cu pa'i khyad par sogs
legs bshad ngo mtshar ba snang / 'di gnyis gshin rje gshed skor la shin tu mkhas pas rgya gar gyi slob dpon dpal 'dzin dang 'dra zhes gleng bar brten mtshan de ltar thogs
so/ /de ltar gong du smos pa'i smin grol rnams legs par thob pa las/ dbang gi brgyud pa dang po ni 'jam dpal dbyangs drag por khros pa dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed/ rgyal yum
rdo rje ro langs ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ rdo rje gdan pa/ don yod rdo rje/ paN grub ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ grub thob padma badzra/ bal po bha ro phyag rdum/
dI paM ka ra rakShi ta dang gcig mthu stobs dbang phyug rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa lo tsA ba chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa rgwa lo rnam rgyal
rdo rje/ khams pa rgwa lo'i skye bar grags pas de ltar du thogs/de sras rong pa shes rab seng ge bag ston gzhon nu tshul

khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang / rwa lo gnyis pa dge ba rgyal mtshan/ grwa thang pa shes rab zla ba'i dbang po/ rje btsun rdo ring
pa chen po kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ 'jam dpal dus dgra'i dbang po tshar pa chos rje/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang dgon gsar ba bsod nams chos 'phel/
rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang ngag
dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ gnas gsar ba ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po bla ma kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen
la stsal to/ /yang brgyud lugs gcig la/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang / 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug de las mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang bsod
nams chos 'phel/ rje bsod nams tshul khrims gsum gyis gsan/ yab sras lnga char las rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na rong pa sher seng
nas/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ spang khang pa grags pa dpal bzang / kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ de dbon sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ tshar
chen

rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /sa bcad dang po dang gnyis pa'i rwa rtags yod pa dang / rtags gang yang med pa rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan
yan dbang gi brgyud pa dang po dang 'dra la/ de nas rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan
chos skyong / de nyid kyi mkhyen brtse nus pas rjes su bzung ba bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ des bdag la'o/ /yang kun gyi rtags can gyi lung brgyud lugs gcig la/ rwa 'bum seng yan gong ltar la/ de nas rwa dkon mchog seng ge rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de sras
shes rab seng ge 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ brtse chen grub chen kun blo/ rig pa'i dbang phyug dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje rin chen rnam rgyal/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin
chen/ rje btsun kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ dbang brgyud gsum pa gong dkar ba'i lugs dang ldong rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ rwa 'bum seng
/ klog skya dbang phyug grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ shar gling pa rgyal mtshan bzang po/ sgo rum pa dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa
kun dga' rnam rgyal/ bla ma

bsod nams mchog ldan/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa
rin po che nas/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa chos rin/ gan pa rin rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa man 'dra/ yang dbang gi
brgyud pa lugs gcig dang / sa bcad dang po yongs rdzogs dang rigs kyi rtags can rnams kyi lung brgyud lugs gcig la/ rong pa shes rab seng ge nas/ mnyam med grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ chos rje dge legs bzang po/ bla chen chos dpal bzang po/ rtsa brgyad pa dbang ston bkra shis bzang po/ bya btang bsam 'grub rgyal
mtshan/ sngags 'chang rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / mang thos dpal ldan chos skyong / mchog gi sprul sku rig 'dzin legs ldan rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang dbang brgyud lugs gcig la/ rwa 'bum seng nas/ rwa dharma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa chen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ khams pa yon tan 'bum/ bla ma brtson 'grus bzang po/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ grub chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/
'brom pa 'jigs byed pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rwa chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na gu ge paN chen nas/ glo bo

mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge rwa chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ yang dbang brgyud lugs gcig la/ khams ston yon tan
'bum nas/ mchod rten dkar po ba sangs rgyas skyabs/ lha rin po che bsod nams rin chen/ jo gdan khrom yon nam mkha' lhun bzang / rje rin chen rnam rgyal/ chos rje nor bu
phun tshogs/ chos rje dpal ldan bkra shis/ chos lung shar gling pa 'khrul zhig kun bzang mthu stobs dpal 'bar/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang rwa khrid mkha' 'gro
snyan brgyud kyi nyams khrid dang rgya rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ rwa 'bum seng yan dbang brgyud ltar las/ de nas rwa dharma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhan chen dang ma ba brtson 'grus byang chub/ nyan po ba slob dpon kun dga' rgya mtsho/
dbur stod pa yon tan chos rin/ yer pa ba brtson 'grus rgya mtsho/ mal gro ba grub chen chos skyong rgyal mtshan/ mdo khams pa bla chen yon tan rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang
tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag gnas gsar
ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ dus dgra'i dbang po ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ de nyid kyis bdag
tshul khrims rin chen la nyams khrid smin rgyas su

stsal to/ /rnal 'byor bzhi rim gyi nyams khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ rwa 'bum seng yan dbang brgyud ltar la/ de nas rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/
mkhan chen dang ma ba/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ nyang stod ArYa de wa/ brtse chen grub chen kun blo/ ra lo gnyis pa dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje rin chen rnam rgyal/ mus
chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse pa chen po nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ 'khor lo'i mgon po mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/
des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang ma rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ slob dpon ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa nas/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ dbon chung bhU mi
shrI/ paN chen bi ma la shrI/ paNDi ta bi dya A ka ra/ paNDi ta sarYA shrI/ lo tsA ba shrI mAM bo dhi/ rgyal khams lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo
gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ 'gos ston rdo rje seng ge tshar chen rdo rje 'chang
chen po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra'o/ /!/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i rjes gnang dang sgo rtags can gyi lung brgyud
ni/ rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po

yan ngor chen brgyud par bzhugs pa'i dbang brgyud ltar las/ de nas 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug thub bstan mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug
rab brtan/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ bka' drin zla bral rmor chen ngag dbang kun
dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /nye brgyud ni/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed nas/ rje btsun sgo rum pa man 'dra zhing / rje dbang rab yan la bla ma
bzhi yod pas oM AHhU~M hoHyin gsung ngo / /yang na mkhyen brtse'i zhabs nas/ byams pa rab brtan/ 'dren mchog snying rje bzang po/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa
ngag dbang lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang dug dbang rma bya rgyas pa'i dbang dang / A'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ gtsug
tor 'khor los sgyur ba/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ dznyA na A ka ra gupta/ padma badzra/ bal po thugs rje chen
po/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rgwa lo yab sras gnyis/ mnyam med grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub gzungs kyi dpal
ba/ bla ma seng ge dpal/ mkhas grub dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje rin chen rnam rgyal/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge rje buddha singha / brang ti nam mkha'
dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo

rje/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na mus chen sangs
rgyas rin chen nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra'o/ /mkhan rtags can
gyi lung brgyud ni/ bo dong mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab man 'dra'o/ /rdo rje'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud gcig la/ rwa shar ba ltar na/
rwa chos rab nas/ rdzong chung ba'i gsan yig na rwa dharma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge shes rab rgyal mtshan gsum la rwa nub pa/de sras dharma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng
ge rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston  rwa tsho shar pa yin zer ba 'dug dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhas pa yon tan 'bum/ bsam yas mchod
rten dkar po ba sangs rgyas skyabs/ lha bsod nams rin chen/ khrom yon nam mkha' lhun bzang / rje dpal 'dzin bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa/ bla ma bsod nams mchog
ldan/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra'o/ /rwa nub pa ltar na/ rwa chos rab nas/ rdzong pa'i gsan yig na ye shes seng
ge dang 'bum seng gnyis la rwa shar pa/ rwa tsho nub pa zer ba 'dug sras ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rje btsun rgwa lo/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan
seng ge bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ zhang ston bsod nams grags/ 'bri khung dpal

'dzin gyi bla ma chos lung mkhan chen yin/gnyan ston rdo rje grags/ khrom yon nam mkha' lhun bzang man 'dra/ mus rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse yan dbang
brgyud thog ma ltar las/ de nas drin chen sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ rje btsun bka' 'gyur ba man 'dra'o/ /!/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog
lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje dam can chos kyi rgyal po lha bcu gsum gyi rjes gnang thun mong
ma yin pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ padma
badzra/ dI paM ka ra rakShi ta/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa rgwa lo/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan
seng ge bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ zhang ston bsod nams grags/ gnyan ston rdo rje grags/ jo gdan nam mkha' lhun bzang / sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal/ mus chen sangs
rgyas rin chen/ sa lo tsA ba kun dga' bsod nams/ ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mtshungs med dkon mchog dpal ldan/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje dam chos pa/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ dus dgra'i dbang po bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la
bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs

rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med 'dren pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /ngor pa dpon slob sangs rgyas tshul khrims pa las kyang thob bo/
/yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa/ brang ti pa/ shar chen khu dbon/ khu bo bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis/ dbon shes rab 'byung
gnas/rje dam chos sogs/ yang na brang ti pa/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ de las nam mkha' sangs rgyas dang shes rab 'byung gnas gnyis kyis gsan/ de man 'dra/ yang na
rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis man 'dra'o/ /!/ las gshin dpa' gcig yab yum gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo
rje 'chang chen/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro rdo rje ro langs ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa'i dpal/ grub thob padma badzra/ dI
paM ka ra rakShi ta/ bha ro phyag rdum dang gcig rwa lo tsA ba chen po rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rje btsun rgwa lo/ rong pa shes rab
seng ge bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang / chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ grwa thang pa shes rab zla ba'i
dbang po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje btsun mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel/
'jam dbyangs ngag dbang chos grags/ byams

pa ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhas grub
chen po sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mkhas pa bkra shis dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/
mkhas grub sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag la'o/ /!/ yang las gshin dmar po khrag mdog yab yum gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rwa 'bum seng yan dpa' gcig
yab yum ltar la/ de nas rwa dharma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhan chen dang ma
ba/ de nas thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ rin po che shes rab grags/ lung pa dkon mchog rdo rje/ khrom yon nam mkha' lhun bzang / brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ gong dkar
rdo rje gdan pa/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs pa drin chen tshe dbang bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug rdo rje 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rje bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags/ 'jam dbyangs ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ ri khrod pa bsod nams chos 'byor/ mkhas pa bkra shis dbang phyug dbang bla kun dga' bstan

'dzin/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ las gshin dmar po bse  ma ru tse bzhis bskor kyang zer/bya bzhis bskor gyi rjes gnang thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rwa 'bum seng yan dpa' gcig yab yum ltar la/ de nas rwa dharma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal
mtshan/ kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhan chen dang ma ba/ de nas rim bzhin rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rdo ring pa/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang / gnas gsar rje drung mkhyen
brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ ngag dbang chos grags/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang kun dga' bkra
shis/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ ri khrod pa bsod nams chos 'byor/ mkhas pa bkra shis dbang phyug dbang bla kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang
/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i las gshin rigs gsum gyi mchod gtor 'bul tshul rjes gnang gi tho dang bcas pa dang / tshar
chen gyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi chings kyi steng nas thos shing yig cha de dag gi lung yang thos so/ /rtse'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ mkhan chen dang ma ba yan
rwa khrid mkha' 'gro'i snyan brgyud ltar las/ de nas mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma ArYa de wa/ brtse chen grub chen kun blo/ khrom yon nam mkha' lhun bzang / rje dpal

'dzin bzang po/ mthu chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ rje bsod nams mchog ldan/ rje tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /sa bcad gsum pa dpal 'dzin nyi 'od
bzang pos mdzad pa'i glegs bam pod chung gi lung ni/ rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje yan dbang brgyud dang po ltar las/ de nas mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/
bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa zhang ston bsod nams grags pa/ gangs ri'i khrod kyi dpal 'dzin nyi 'od bzang po/ rgya mtsho
sprin gyi 'brug sgra glog gi phreng ba can yang zer/bla ma stag lung pa/ zhwa lu pa chen po/ stag lung pa ngag dbang grags pa/ mi nyag paN chen grags pa rdo rje/ mkhan chen
dkon mchog tshul khrims/ 'gos ston rdo rje seng ge tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mthu stobs dbang phyug dgon gsar ba bsod nams chos
'phel/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/
rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra/ rmor chen pas mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan gyi drung du zhus pa'i dus rwa pod sa skya'i phyag dpe'i nang ltar ma tshang ba
med par zhus pas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse khu dbon gsum brgyud par bzhugs pa thams cad/ de yan gsan yig ganggA'i chu rgyun ltar bris pa yin zhing / mkhan chen bzang rgyan
pas lung gsan dus kyang phyag dpe de kha yin 'dug gsung ngo / /smras

pa/ sdang bas zil mnan skye bo byang chub cher/ /bkri phyir khro bo'i rgyal por zlos pa'i gar/ /gshin rje mthar byed dmar nag 'jigs gsum gyi/ /dbang dang grol byed lam skor
phal cher mnos/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gshin rje'i gshed skor te pha rgyud kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi
sarga ste bcu bdun pa'o/ // /gsum pa gti mug can gtso bor 'dul bar byed pa rnam snang sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i smin byed nyid ni sngon du thos pa ma byung ngo / /!/ gnyis
pa shes rab bla na med pa'i rgyud kyis bstan pa'i skor la/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog sbyang gzhi sgong skyes sbyong byed ltar legs par bkral ba'i he ru ka'i rigs dpal 'khor
lo sdom pa lha drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sa mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang / 'dren mchog gis mdzad pa'i mchod phreng
/ rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i dkyil chog ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i gsal byed khyad par bzhi ldan dang / shar chen pa dang mkhan chen buddha
lakShmIs mdzad pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor rnams la brten nas brgyud pa'i bka' babs dgu ldan gyi dbang bzhi rdzogs par nos pa'i bka' babs dang pos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
ngor chen dang mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na bka' bab bdun las mi 'dug kyang jo bo lugs gnyis so sor bgrangs gnyos lugs bsnan pas dgu byung ngo / /khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang
/ dpal phyag na rdo rje/ bram ze chen po sa ra ha/ mda' bsnun/'phags pa klu sgrub/ grub chen

sha ba ri pa/ phag ro khur/slob dpon lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ bud med can/rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ kurma pA da/shrI dzA landha ra/ nag po spyod pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam
rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro ta pa/ kun tu bzang po/ nam mkha'i snying po/ snyan grags bzang po/ ye shes dngos grub/ rtsa bshad pa rnams mtshan gyi rnam grangs yin zhes
zer yang dpyad do/ /pham mthing pa gcen 'jigs med grags pa/ gcung ngag gi dbang phyug klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ pradznyA ku Ta/mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ rje btsun
brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo
gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor chen sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/
rje btsun dam chos bsam 'grub/ bstan pa'i sgron me sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i dbang phyug kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen can
la stsal ba'i chos kyi thog ma nyid do/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ drin chen mkhas btsun grub pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag
tshul rin la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas seng ge nas/ thar rtse pa nam mkha'

dpal bzang dang / mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ de nas nam mkha' sangs rgyas man 'dra/ yang na mus chen
yan gong ltar la/ de las kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pa dang grub chen dkon mchog blo gros gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis gsan pa man gong
ltar ro/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse pa man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas
rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs sa lo/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa brang ti paN chen/ shar
chen kun dga' bkra shis/ dbon shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje dam chos man 'dra/ yang na dpal ldan don grub las/ nam mkha' sangs rgyas dang shes rab 'byung gnas gnyis kyis gsan
pa man 'dra/ yang na rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ dmar chos rgyal/ mi nyag chos rgyal/ mi
nyag rdor grags/ lce mdo sde seng ge ston shAkalce blo ldan/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ bo dong rin po che/ khro phu rin po che/ bla ma dpal ldan
seng ge kun mkhyen bu man gong bzhin no/ /yang na sa paN nas/ bo dong rin po che/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod

nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan man gong bzhin no/ /yang na sa paN nas/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal
ba brag phug pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gnyis pa bskyed rim gtso bor
ston pa'i bshad rgyud a bhi dha na'i le'u sum cu rtsa gsum pa nas gsungs pa'i mar do lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bde mchog lU hi pa sbyangs pa'i yon tan lha bcu gsum ma'am bde
mchog la wa pa'ang zer/rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ lU hi pa/ DheM ki pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig tu lU hi pa dang 'di gnyis gcig par mdzad 'dug
paN grub dbang pa la wa pa/ rgyal po indra bhU ti/ ka tsa Ta pa/ bu ston dang rje btsun btsong kha pa'i gsan yig na ka tsa pa rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na ka tsa tra
pa zhes snang /grub chen dril bu pa/ bu rje btsong kha pa ngor gong dkar thar rtse shar pa rnams kyi gsan yig na mi gsal yang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'dir
rus sbal zhabs snang ba brtag dzA landha ri pa/ nag po spyod pa/ ku sha la nA tha/ bu dang gong dkar ba'i gsan yig tu 'di dang dge ba'i mgon po so sor 'dug pa rgya skad
bod skad kyi khyad par las don gcig pas yig skyon shor ba 'dra/ ngor mkhyen brtse thar rtse shar pa sogs kyi gsan yig dang dkyus mthun/tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ma na ka shrI
dznyA na/ bu'i gsan yig na ma na ka dang shrI dznyA na zhes 'dug pa yig skyon byung ngam snyam/bal po bha danta/ su ma ti kIrti dang gcig yin skad/ bu'i gsan yig na bha
ran dang / ngor chen gyi gsan yig tu bha tan zhes snang ba gcig la yig skyon byung 'dra/lo tsA ba mar pa do pa chos kyi dbang phyug gze pa blo ldan seng ge gze pa jo

bde/ rje btsun btsong kha pa rdo rje gdan pa thar rtse pa gsum gyi gsan yig tu bde mchog rdo rje zhes snang /slob dpon khu pa/ khams pa lho tshad pa kun dga' rin chen/ lo tsA
ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ rje sangs rin pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/
sangs rgyas seng ge de las thar rtse pa dang mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las sgrub khang dpal don pa man gong sa lugs dang 'dra/ yang na rdo
rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen la wa pa/ la ki mi pa/ 'bar ba'i gtso bo/ dge ba'i gtso bo/ ku sha la nA tha man gong ltar ro/ /yang na khyung lhas pa
nas/ chos rje bkra shis rin chen/ ngor chen man 'dra/ yang na gze pa blo ldan nas/ gze pa don grub ye shes/ sa phug pa shAkya rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan man 'dra/ bka'
babs gsum pa jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen lU hi pa/ slob dpon dha ri ka pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ratna A ka ra shAnti/
thar rtse pa'i gsan yig na 'di jo bo'i rjes su 'dug pa yig nor byung 'dra/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha/ rong pa 'gar dge dge bsnyen yin/lha rje stod pa tshul khrims
dpal/ sngags dkar/steng pa thugs rje zla gsal/ rje btsun btsong kha pa dang rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na steng shod zhabs gnyis zhes snang /shod nyi ma kha dro/ gcen shes
rab rgyal po/ 'di gnyis kyi tshab tu rje btsun btsong kha pa dang rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig tu rje che ba dang chung ba zhes pa 'dug cing zhwa lu

tsandra pa'i gsan yig tu rje che chung gi 'og tu so so'i mtshan brgyab 'dug pa don la gcig pa 'dra/gcung shes rab gtsug tor/ lha rje chen po dharma tsakra sngags pa se bo/thang
stod pa chos 'od/ rab byung se bo/zhing chen grags pa dpal/ bod btsun grwa ther se bo/bde gshegs dpal/ bod btsun/bla ma sgom  btsun pa/pa ye shes/ gyer phug pa sgom
ye dang gcig pa 'dra/bla ma grags chen/ btsun pa byar bu ba/bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ sems dpa' chen po/ sangs rin pa/
sangs rgyas seng ge de las thar rtse pa dang mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las sgrub khang pa man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs bzhi pa kha che lugs kyi brgyud
pa ni/ tsakra saM wA ra/ badzra wa ra hI/ grub chen lU hi pa/ ri khrod zhabs/ 'di gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na mi 'dug pa chad dam dpyad/kanta pa/ 'dren mdzad zhabs/ bikSha
ta de wa/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ bi bhU ti tsandra/ g.yag sde lo tsA bsod nams bzang po/ mnga' ris ze dmar ba sangs rgyas ye shes/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/
mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man jo lugs dang 'dra/ yang na bi bhU ti tsandra nas/ mnga' ris pa sangs rgyas
ye shes man 'dra/ yang na kha che paN chen nas/ spyi bo lhas pa seng ge dpal/ zhang phya ru ba/ 'bro lung pa/ rin po che khro phu ba/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu
ston man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ slob dpon dril bu pa/ dha ri ka pa/ dga' ba'i rdo

rje/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ a bha yA de wa pUrNa/ kha che paN chen man 'dra/ yang nye brgyud ni 'khor lo sdom pa/ paN chen shAkya shrI man gong bzhin no/ /bka' babs lnga
pa pu rangs lo chung lugs kyi dbang bshad gnyis ka'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ grub chen lU hi pa/ DheM ki pa/ dha ri ka pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ dza
landha ri pa/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa/ dge ba'i mgon po/ rus sbal zhabs/ gu hya pa/ rje btsong kha pa dang gong dkar ba sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa gsum gyi gsan yig na
bhu ba pa zhes snang /rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro ta pa/ ma na ka shrI/ pra dznyA rakShi ta/ pham mthing pa gsum/ 'jigs med grags pa/ ngag dbang grags pa/ bha danta/pu
rangs long chung grags mchog shes rab/ 'di las stod sribs kyi gad logs su lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du byon pa yin/dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris kyi ston
pa dkon mchog 'bar/ thur la ba tshul khrims skyabs/ thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston
rin po che/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man jo bo lugs bzhin no/ /yang na dmar chos rgyal nas/ mi nyag
chos rgyal/ mi nyag rdor grags/ lce mdo seng / bla ma ston shAkablo ldan seng ge 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na ma na ka dang pradznyA rakShi ta gnyis las ka na ka shrIs gsan/
de dang pham mthing pa gnyis ka las bha danta/ de nas pu rangs lo chung man bshad ma thag

pa ltar ro/ /bka' babs drug pa mar lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ gsan yig tshor 'di bzhin 'dug kyang mar lo sogs ma byung bas dmar lugs zer rgyu yin nam dpyad/pham mthing pa yan sa
lugs dang 'dra ba la/ de nas bal po bha danta/ lo chung grags mchog shes rab/ dmar chen po chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dbon po shes rab rdo rje/ thub pa shes rab/ brtson 'grus
rdo rje/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma shAkya gzhon nu/ lce blo ldan seng ge bla ma 'phags 'od/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes
rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man jo lugs dang 'dra/ bka' babs bdun pa dpyal lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ grub chen lU hi pa/ rgyal po dha ri ka pa/ mnga' bdag
mai tri pa/ nya ka pa/ kandha pa/ bikSha ta de wa/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ grub thob rdo rje gdan pa/ paNDi ta kShi ti garbha/ dpyal lo tsA ba chos bzang / rgwa lo rnam
rgyal rdo rje/ de sras shes rab seng ge gru ma chos skyong dpal/ khyung po lhas pa/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man jo bo lugs bzhin no/
/bka' babs brgyad pa sbal spang sna lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na 'di jo lugs brgyud pa'i rnam grangs su mdzad 'dug cing thar rtse dang shar pa'i gsan
yig na dkyus bzhin du so sor snang /sangs rgyas/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ slob dpon chen po tsandri ka pa/ bram ze chen po me ko pa/ slob dpon lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/
bram ze sdom pa bzang po/ jo bo rje a ti sha/ de las lo chen rin chen bzang po dang nag tsho lo tsA ba

gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las 'phan yul 'al pa ston mgon dang 'al pa jo btsun gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis las sgom  sngags dkar lcang lo can/pa mang sgom/ 'phan yul rgyal ba/sbal
spang  drang srong srin po ri pa/sna pa/ 'di gnyis sku mched yin/ me reg dar ma byang chub/ spang zho brag nag pa/de dbon rin chen rgyal po/ bla ma don ri ba grags pa
dpal/ bod btsun phyar bu ba/bla ma 'phags 'od/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ khyung po lhas pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man jo
lugs bzhin no/ /bka' babs dgu pa gnyos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ gsan yig 'ga' zhig tu 'di'i rjes su nag po pa 'dug gu hya pa/ rnam
rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ de las rakShi ta/ nag po lha las dad pa/ pham mthing pa ste gsum gyis gsan/ gsum ga las bal po bha danta/ de nas nag po lha las dad pa'i
slob ma/ gnyos lo tsA ba/ gnyos bla ma/ gnyos dpal le/ phug ka ba jo bo 'bum/ sngags dkar lcang lo can/ gtsang pa lha steng pa/sngags dkar lcang lo can/ lce mdo sde seng
ge bla ma ston shAka bod btsun/bla ma blo ldan/ sngags dkar lcang lo can/bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston  gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na'ang mtshan gsal mi 'dug rin chen grub/
mkhas grub khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man jo lugs dang 'dra'o/ /!/ grub pa'i khyu mchog
dpal ldan spyod pa'i rdo rje brtul zhugs grub pa'i zhabs

kyis dpal 'khor lo sdom pa rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi zab don sbyang gzhi mngal skyes ltar sbyong byed du bkral ba'i bde mchog lha drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor
du dbang bskur ba/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge dang mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs ma nor gsal ba'i sgron me/ rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i
nag po dkyil chog de'i gsal byed ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i gsal byed khyad par bzhi ldan/ shar chen dang mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad
pa'i bde mchog lU nag gnyis kyi dbang gi mtshams sbyor rnams la brten nas dbang bzhi legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rdo rje 'chang
/ phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba ri/ lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ grub chen rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ shrI dza landha ra/ grub chen spyod pa'i rdo rje/
nag po par grags pa gsum byon te/ nag po spyod pa ba/ nag po dam tshig rdo rje/ nag po lha las dad pa gsum gyi dang po gnyis la nag po pa che ba dang chung bar grags
pa las 'di nag po pa che ba kahna pa ste spyod pa bar grags so/ /slob dpon gu hya pa/ rnam par rgyal ba'i zhabs/ tai lo pa/ paN chen nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa gcen 'jigs med
grags pa/ gcung ngag gi dbang phyug klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ sngags pa gos dkar can/rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/
rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje paN chen/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan

pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / chos rje gzhon nu seng ge  rdul tshon gyi brgyud pa 'di man nas byung skad/rje
sangs rgyas dpal grub/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge de las brang ti paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang dang mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/
snga ma las dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis gsan/ de las rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po bkra shis bzang po/
des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na rje bkra shis bzang po nas/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims
rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na rje sangs rin nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa/ brang ti pa/ shar chen khu dbon/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub man 'dra/ yang na
brang ti pa/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ de las nam mkha' sangs rgyas dang shes rab 'byung gnas gnyis kyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na rje dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ dkon
mchog dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ kha char ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje sangs rgyas dpal grub man 'dra/
yang na ngor chen nas/ mus pa grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal

bzang / dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs man gong ltar ro/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ grub
chen dkon mchog blo gros man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ chos rje dge legs bshes gnyen/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang
man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ stag ston shes rab gzhon nu/ bla ma brag dkar ba/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ bu ston rin po che'i gsan yig dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses tshar chen dang grol mchog las gsan pa tshang mar rnal 'byor ma'i rjes su grub
chen dril bu pa 'dug na'ang / ngor chen rdo rje gdan pa thar rtse sgrub khang shar pa khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba rnams kyi gsan yig ltar na/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo
rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha wa ri pa/ lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ dril bu pa man mthun pa 'di bzhin no/ /!/ grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas
legs par bkral ba'i 'khor lo sdom pa'i zab don dril bu pa'i lugs kyi phyi dkyil ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya
mtshos mdzad pa'i dkyil chog gi steng nas dbang bzhi legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa/ langka li pa/ nag po
spyod pa/ dge ba'i mgon po/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ma

Na ka shrI/ 'di gnyis rmor gyi gsan yig na ma byung bar lnga pa'i gsan yig tu yod pas dgos mi dgos brtag ka Na ka shrI/ pham mthing pa 'jigs med grags pa/ bal po bha danta/
su ma ti kIrti yang zer/mar do lo tsA ba chos kyi dbang phyug  sngags pa gos dkar can/gze pa blo ldan seng ge gze pa jo bde/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ rong pa chos mgon/
lo tsA ba mchog ldan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ mkhan chen rin chen rnam rgyal/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun
grub/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags/ rmor pa grub chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/
ngag gi dbang phyug kun dga' lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i dbang phyug kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin
chen la'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ 'bar ba 'dzin/ kahna pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro
pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal gyo lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun chen po/ sa paNDi
ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ khro phu rin po 550che/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ bo dong rin chen brtson 'grus/ khro phu rin po che man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ tshogs
sgom pa/ khro phu ba man 'dra'o/ /!/ slob dpon dril bu pa'i bzhed srol dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi legs par nos pa'i bka' babs gnyis ldan gyi
dang po sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / yum rdo rje phag mo/ grub chen rdo rje dril bu pa/ rab byung gi mtshan blo gros snying po/kurma pA da/ 'bar ba 'dzin
pa/ kahNa pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ paN chen nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa gcen 'jigs med grags pa/ gcung ngag gi dbang phyug klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal
lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ rje btsun kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ bla ma rje btsun chen po/ chos rje paNDi ta/ de las 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal
'phags pa dang / tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ bo dong rin chen gsum gyis gsan/ 'phags pa nas zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin
chen/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ de las thar rtse

paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang dang mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rjes gsan/ de nas mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams
pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ 'khor lo sdom pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims
rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na mus chen nas/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/
she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rmor pa grub chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra'o/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/
ngor chen lha mchog seng ge dang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paN chen/ glo bo mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung
gnas/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra/ yang na sa paN las/ 'phags pa rin po che/ tshogs sgom rin po che/ bo dong rin po che gsum gyis gsan/
de gsum ga las khro phu rin po che bsod nams seng ge sa gsan/ de las bla ma dpal ldan seng ge dang yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge gnyis kyis gsan/ de gsum ga las thams
cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ de nas khyung po lhas pa/ gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang

kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ yang na khyung lhas pa las/ mkhas grub nor  'od zer ba'ang byung /bzang rin chen/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos
rje/ mkhan chen rig 'dzin rgyal po/ lcags sgog lung pa bkra shis dpal 'byor/ tshar chen gyis ku su li'i bla ma dang lam du mjal gsung ba de yin/byang gling pa rin chen bkra
shis rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ bka' babs gnyis pa kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ badzra dha ra/ badzra wA ra hI pa/ badzra ghaNDa pa/ dga'
ba'i rdo rje/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ a bha yA ka ra gupta/ de wa purNa/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ spyi bo lhas pa seng ge dpal/ zhang phya ru ba/ byang sems 'bre lung pa/
thar rtse pa dang shar pa'i gsan yig na zhang 'bre lung pa zhes 'di dang gong ma gnyis bla ma gcig tu mdzad 'dug kyang bu ston dang mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig tu dkyus ltar
so sor snang ngo / /khro phu rin po che/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ mkhas grub khyung po lhas pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje dril bu pa/ de wa pUrNa/ kha che paN chen man 'dra/ nye brgyud ni/ 'khor lo sdom pa/ kha che paN chen man gong bzhin no/ /!/ mkhan
chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis  byin rlabs 'di de sngon ma thob kyang thob rgyu'i dbang gis bris so/ /mdzad pa'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga dang khrid yig gi steng nas 'khor
lo bde mchog gi rdzogs rim shin tu zab pa dril bu rim lngar grags pa'i byin rlabs dang nyams khrid legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khro phu bsod nams seng ge yan gong
gi

dbang brgyud le tshan ltar las/ de nas yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bla ma gnyan mkhar ba bkra shis bzang po/ mkhas grub khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye
shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don
grub/ de dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rmor pa grub chen kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba rje btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhas grub chen po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /'gro ba'i mgon
po 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i rim lnga'i khrid kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa sa skya bka' 'bum dang 'dra la/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad
pa'i byin rlabs dang khrid kyi lung ni/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ mus chen bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po
rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba man 'dra'o/ /!/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa dus kyi 'khor lo dang mthun par bshad pa mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho lha stong
dang lnga brgya rig byed kyis  gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na lha stong phrag gcig dang brgya phrag dgur brgyad kyis lhag pa'i bcu phrag gcig yod par bshad cing / lo pa'i gsan
yig na stong dang bdun brgya zhes dang rgyal dbang lnga pas stong dang lnga brgya zhe lnga zhes

snang ngo / /lhag pa'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dngos grub rin po che'i mdzod/ des mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho
ga yon tan rin po che'i mdzod/ mchod phreng bsod nams rin po che'i mdzod/ sngags phreng ngor chen gyis zhus dag mdzad pa rnams mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad
pa'i gsung sgros phyag len yid kyi mun sel dang dbang gi mtshams sbyor dam pa'i zhal lung dbang gi dngos gzhi'i sdom bcas kyi dbang bzhi legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/
khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / yum rdo rje phag mo/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ grub chen sha wa ri pa/ mnga' bdag mai tri gupta/ rgya gar phyag
na rdo rje/ slob dpon ka ma la badzra/ paN chen gos dkar po/ paN grub dza ya sa na/ sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshanas skya
paNDi ta/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub gung
ru sher bzang / kun mkhyen go rams pa bsod nams seng ge byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ zhwa lu dang dpal 'khor chos sde'i gdan sa
pa/rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ jo nang mkhan po/thams cad mkhyen pa

mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug  zhwa lu'i mkhan po/rgyud sde'i mnga' bdag zhwa lu pa byang gling pa/ rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mus chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs nam mkha' dpal
bzang / rin po che dpal ldan don grub/ rdo rje 'chang dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ khams ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ chos rje mtshungs med don grub rgyal mtshan/
drin chen 'khor lo sdom pa bkra shis bzang po/ des skal ba dang ldan pa'i bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/
byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ tai lo
pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ dha byang chub sems dpa'/ jo bo rje'i dbon po yin/a bha yA ka ra/ mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na a bhya rakShi ta zhes gcig tu bsdoms 'dug kyang
gong dkar ba dang thar rtse pa'i gsan yig na dkyus ltar snang ngo / /ratna rakShi ta/ paN grub dza ya se na/ sum pa lo tsA ba man gong ltar ro/ /yang na sum pa lo tsA
ba nas/ mkhas pa sa mu dra/ seng ge rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen dang thar rtse pa'i gsan yig na grags pa dpal zhes pa dkyus su bris par rdo rje
yin nam 'di ma dag zer ba'i mchan 'dug kyang rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang ngo / /bag ston gzhon tshul man 'dra/ yang na sum pa lo tsA ba nas/ rgya thams
cad mkhyen pa/ srin po ri pa'am sbal spang sna pa/ bsgrad ston rdo rje dpal/ gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na sgrag ston zhes snang /mtshur phu ba tshul khrims rin chen/ rje
rang byung

rdo rje/ snye mdo kun dga' don grub man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ padma badzra che chung gnyis/ indra bhU ti/ lcam lakShmI ka ra/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/
rdo rje 'dzin pa/ a bha yA ka ra/ ratna shrI/ rgyal ba'i sde/ sum pa lo tsA ba/ rje btsun grags pa man gong bzhin no/ /yang na sum pa lo tsA ba/ sgang dar snying / gnyan
ras/ a kSho bhya badzra/ sgom pa shes rab/ bde ba can ye shes mgon po/ bsam gtan grub/ bla ma gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ 'dzam gling paNDi ta man 'dra'o/ /!/ gu ge paN chen
gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs phrin las mtha' yas dang dbang chog bdud rtsi ganggA'i klung rgyun gnyis kyi steng nas dpal 'khor lo sdom pa bong zhal can lha so bdun gyi ras
bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi legs par nos pa'i ring brgyud ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ 'jigs med 'byung
gnas sbas pa/ a nu pa ma rakShi ta/ darpaN A tsArYa/ kun tu bzang po/ ye shes kyi glogadapal yid kyi 'gram pa/ 'jam dpal bzang po/ dpal bzang / chos kyi glog bzang po/ yid
'tsho ba bzang po/ ngag gi dpal bzang / dpal rnam rgyal bzang po/ dpal myos byed bzang po'i zhabs/ dpal phun tshogs bzang po'i zhabs/ nam mkha' bzang po/ rgyal ba'i 'tsho
ba bzang po/ dpal 'phrog byed bzang po'i zhabs/ ye rang paNDi ta skal ldan bzang po/ skye dgu kun dga'i 'tsho ba bzang po/ de sras bal po ma hA bo dhi/ bla ma bsam gtan
'od zer/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal

mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ 'jam dbyangs sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ ngor chen sangs rgyas seng ge brang ti paN chen nam
mkha' dpal bzang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/
mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs grub pa bkra shis bzang po/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis mnos so/ /yang na nam mkha' bzang po/ de
sras byang chub chen po/ bla ma bsam gtan 'od zer/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ nye brgyud ni/ grub chen bsam gtan 'od zer gyis dbang gsan pa'i tshe brgyud pa
zhus pas ngas a pha/ de'i a phas tsakra saM wa ra dang yo gi gnyis las thob gsungs pa ltar/ bde mchog yab yum gyis byin gyis brlabs pa sha stag gi nye brgyud ni/ dpal 'khor
lo sdom pa/ yum rdo rje phag mo/ bal po ye rang gi paNDi ta skal ldan bzang po man gong bzhin no/ /!/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil
gyi steng nas dpal sgyu ma chen po lha lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi legs par thob pa'i jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi
mkha' 'gro ma/ ku ku ri pa/ grub thob khyi mo phyag rgyar bsten pa/jo bo nA ro ta pa/ shAnti pa/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sharong pa 'gar dgeklog skya ston pa/ stengs
pa thur

bsam/ 'phar lung pa rgyal sras/ rkyang po nyi she/ 'dar tsha dar rgyal/ 'dar tsha grags she/ spen phug pa bsod nams mdzes/ grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ thams
cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge
paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog
lhun grub/ rje byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ 'khor lo'i mgon po mkhyen rab bstan
'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ bka' drin mnyam med rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen
la'o/ /yang rngog lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ slob dpon ku ku ri pa/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ Dombi pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ paNDi
ta zhi ba bzang po/ mar pa lho brag pa chos kyi blo gros/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog jo sras mdo sde/ rngog chos sku/ rngog tsha dkon mchog dpal/ klog skya dbang phyug
grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhan po gzhon nu 'bum/ bla ma spang sgang pa grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs pa/ sa
bzang ma ti paN chen 'phags pa

gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra/ yang na chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa nas/ khro phu rin po che/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan
seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na rngog chos sku rdo rje nas/ sba lba ba can/ rngog
zhe sdang rdo rje/ gtsang lha steng pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ ngor chen man 'dra'o/ /'di'i mngon dkyil khrus khang lo
tsA bas mdzad pa'i steng nas mdzad song / /!/ nA lendra pa mkhan chen rin chen dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil gyi steng nas dpal 'khor lo bde mchog sangs rgyas thod
pa lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / dznyA na DA ki nI ye/ byang sems blo
gros rin chen/ dpal sa ra ha pa/ dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub/ grub chen sha ba ri dbang phyug mnga' bdag mai tri pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros/ rgya rnal 'byor
pa/ ro mnyam rdo rje/ yon tan grags/ khams pa sa phug pa shAkya rdo rje/ gnyal ba jo sras chos grags/ khams chen rgan mo lhas pa/ bla ma bsod nams 'phel/ bag ston gzhon
nu tshul khrims/ g.yung ston rdo rje dpal ba/ rin po che grags pa tshul khrims/ bla ma byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal

mkha' dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ 'khor lo'i mgon po ngag dbang kun dga' lhun
grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na rgan mo lhas pa nas/ bla ma ye shes rin chen/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ rgya ston thams cad mkhyen
pa/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ g.yung ston rdo rje dpal/ grags pa tshul khrims/ byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen man 'dra'o/ /yang na bla ma ye shes

phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ nag po zhabs/ de wa A ka ra tsandra/ a mo gha badzra/ mnga' bdag mar pa lo tsA ba/ mtshur dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad
pa kIrti/ yar klungs kyi snyigs dmar po/ 'gos ri khrod dbang phyug bal po dbang mgon/ rin chen bzang po/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma kun bsod pa/ bag ston gzhon
nu tshul khrims/ g.yung ston rdo rje dpal ba/ mkhan chen grags pa tshul khrims/ bla ma byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
chen po man

'dra'o/ /!/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs byin rlabs kyi yi ge'i steng nas kha che paN chen gyi thugs dam bzhi'i nang tshan bcom ldan 'das
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa dkar po lhan cig skyes pa'i byin rlabs/ bde mchog dkar po la brten nas byang chub bsgrub pa/ 'jam dpal dkar po la brten nas shes rab bsgrub pa/
yang dag me gcig thod gcig la brten nas ras grub pa/ dzambha la nag po la brten nas nor bsgrub pa'o/ /dpyal a mo ghas mdzad pa'i khrid yig gi steng nas bskyed rdzogs kyi
nyams khrid zab mo dang / rgyal dbang gis rdo rje 'chang dbang rab pas mdzad pa'i khrid yig yin gsung 'dug mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas
tshe khrid bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po/ rgyal yum rdo rje phag mo/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug lU hi pa/ dha ri ka pa/ mai tri
pa/ nA ya ka pa/ kandha pa/ kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI bha dra/ dpyal chos kyi bzang po/ dpyal a mo gha/ rong pa rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de sras rong pa shes rab
seng ge bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen ngag gi dbang phyug bla ma byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ ngor chen lha mchog
seng ge rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun

grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na kha che'i paNDi ta nas/ sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba bsod nams bzang
po/ grub chen ze dmar ba sangs rgyas ye shes/ mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ mkhan chen grags pa tshul khrims/ bya sder ba byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu
blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon
mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ glang thang spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan/
stong rwa ba kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ de dbon 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin
bzang po man 'dra'o/ /!/ mkhan chen sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang byin rlabs bya tshul gyi yi ge la brten nas rje btsun rdo rje phag
mo shes rab gsal byed kyi byin rlabs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / rgyal yum rdo rje phag mo/ grub thob kangka datta/ a bha yA ka ra/ su tsa
ri pA da/ ratna rakShi ta/ ma nA ka shrI dznyA na/ chag lo tsA ba

chos rje dpal/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan/ shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje bla
ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen mnyam med bsod nams lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang po/ ngag
dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na yan chad btsal dgos/ de nas mtshungs med kun dga' chos 'phel/ bka' drin rmad byung dbang bla kun
dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan nas/ dbang rnon rgyal ba mchog grub/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen
rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab
bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra/ yang na dpang lo tsA ba nas/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /!

/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs byin rlabs kyi yi ge la brten nas dpyal lugs kyi phag mo bden gnyis zhal/ phag mo dbu bcad ma/

bstan 'dzin bzang po/ bal po bha rendra ru tse/ dpyal kun dga' rdo rje/ zar ston A tsArYa/ gtsang yang dag rdo rje/ dbus pa shes rab rdo rje/ lce ston mdo sde seng ge lce
blo ldan seng ge lce btsun bsod nams dpal/ sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen dga' ba gdong pa chos rgyal dpal bzang / mkhan chen
'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje btsun rdo ring pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/

las zhang 'od de/ dbus pa gzi ston/ dbus pa shes rdor/ lce

mdo sde seng ge man 'dra/ yang na mar pa bsod nams rdo rje/ khams pa zhang ston/ phug ston/ lha steng pa 'byung gnas seng ge lce mdo sde seng ge man 'dra/ yang na zar ston/
snar ston/ grag pa tshul khrims/ mkhas btsun kun rdor/ bla ma tshul khrims dpal bzang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ khyung po gzhon nu bsod nams/ spos khang pa 'jam dbyangs
rin chen rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /!/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i rgyud mngon par brjod pa 'bum pa las gsungs
pa'i mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa lha gcig bum gcig tshe zan la brten pa rig 'dzin dbang mo grub pa'i rgyal mo'i lugs kyi byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba legs
par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa/ ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ti phu gsang sngags sdom po/ ras chung rdo rje grags pa/ mid la bzhad pa rdo rje/
dwags po lha rje bsod  sgam po zla 'od gzhon nu yang zer/nams rin chen/ bde gshegs phag mo  khams pa rdor rgyal/grub pa/ 'bri khung pa 'jig rten mgon po'am mtshan dngos rin
chen dpal/ spyan snga grags pa 'byung gnas/ yang dgon pa  thugs kyi rdo rje zer ba'ang byung /rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / thugs sras spyan snga rin ldan/ zur phug pa rin
chen dpal bzang / 'ba' rwa ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / 'di yang dgon pa'i sprul pa/chos rje bde legs rin chen/ gangs can pa kun dga' dpal bzang / dbu ma pa dpal ldan bzang

po/ chos rje dpal ldan mgon po/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga'
bkra shis/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ tshe dpag med dngos mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims
rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ sku dbon shes rab 'byung gnas/
mkhas btsun kun dga' legs pa/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ sa lo thams
cad mkhyen pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge 'dren mchog kun dga' lung rig sa/ nags dgon pa sbyin pa grags pa/ sa skya pa sngags 'chang
kun dga' bsod nams yab sras/ sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bka' drin zla bral bkra shis lhun grub/
des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na sa skya pa kun dga' bkra shis nas/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen/ mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub
man 'dra/ yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ 'chi med mgon po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/

/ yang na sa lo nas/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen/ sras 'jam dbyangs sku mched/ a mi lags man 'dra/ yang na sangs rin nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ she'u ri pa blo gros
rgyal mtshan/ sbyin pa grags pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na 'ba' rwa ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang yan gong ma ji lta ba bzhin la/ de nas grub chen rin chen 'phel ba/ zhwa lu mkhan
chen 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ byams
pa kun dga' chos grags/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya
mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na 'ba' rwa ba nas/ chos rje bde legs rin chen/ lha do rtogs ldan yang zer/nam snying pa rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa kun dga' dpal bzang / chos rje rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos

rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dpal rdo
rje bsod nams

dbang phyug sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ yab sras de gsum char las ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho man
'dra'o/ /mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub pas paN chen brang ti pas mdzad pa dang / sngags 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i yig cha so so'i steng nas ma 'dres par tha dad du gnang
byung ngo / /!/ rong ston chen po la ti phu pas dngos su gnang ba'i tshe sgrub zhag bdun ma'i nyams len zab mo'i gdams pa tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos gsal bar mdzad
pa'i 'chi med bdud rtsi'i bcud len dang brgyud 'debs dngos grub mchog stsol gyi lung dang dmigs khrid bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das mgon po tshe

kun spangs pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug 'di nas yin nam man chad cung zad brtag dgos/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/

grub/ spro lung bsod nams chos 'phel/ grub chen sangs rgyas bstan pa/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin
du stsal to/ /rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad

pa'i tshe sgrub zhag bdun ma'i yi ge'i lung yang thos so/ /!/ 'phags pa'i yul gyi ma hA paNDi ta A tsArYa dmar pos rje btsun sa skya pa chen po la gnang ba'i rdo rje nam mkha'
lding gser mig 'khyil ba 'byung po 'ur 'ded ces shin tu thugs gtsigs che ba'i zab chos kyi skor la/ yig rnying gi dgongs pa bzhin du mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs
kyis mdzad pa'i khyung nag gser mig 'khyil ba'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas legs par nos nas/ gdams pa shar sbu chu ba dpal ldan grags kyis mdzad pa'i lo
rgyus/ bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ las sbyor gyi nang gses khyad par gyi las sbyor ser ba dang char gcod pa/ mid 'byar 'chos pa/ dug bsrung ba/ dug 'bred pa/ sri'u gso ba/ gdon

ba shes rab kyang zer/ bod du lan gsum byon pa'i dang po khri srong lde'u btsan gyi dus/ bar pa bstan pa phyi dar gyi 'gorjes ma sa chen dang mjal ba ste sku tshe'i

mtshan/ chos rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ de las bdag

rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sa skya'i sngags 'chang a mi lags nas kyang zhabs drung bdag pos gsan pa man 'dra'o/ /!/ smras pa/ srid gsum ro gcig lhan skyes bde
ba che'i/ /'khor lor sdom pa'i dbang bskur gser ri'i grangs/ /tshe dang shes rab skyed byed byin rlabs dang / /tshe dbang grub rgyal lugs sogs legs par mnos/ /zhes dam
pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ rnal 'byor ma rgyud kyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste bco brgyad pa'o/ // /bstan

pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la dpal kye rdo rje'i bka' srol mi 'dra ba chen po bzhi babs pa la/ dpal kye rdo rje'i chos skor 'di rnams/ rnal 'byor ma rgyud
kye rdo rje/ /zhes pa'i dgongs don ltar ma rgyud du bkral ba dang / thabs dang shes rab gnyis med rgyud/ /ces pa'i dgongs don gnyis med du bkral ba'i lugs gnyis las ngor

pus min/ /thabs dang shes rab gnyis med pa'i/ /dges rdor 'di ni phyogs gcig min/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa rgyu mtshan du ma'i sgo nas thabs dang shes rab gnyis su med pa'i

kaa la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri
