kyis mdzad pa 'brog mis bsgyur ba/ mar me'i rtse mo  rmor chen pa'i gsan yig tu 'di ma byung ba brtag lta

bu'i rdzogs rim tshogs 'khor dam tshig lnga pa mtsho skyes kyis mdzad pa ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga mdzad pa gong 'dra/ bstod pa nyi shu pa mtsho skyes
zhabs kyis mdzad pa ga ya dha ra dang 'brog mis bsgyur ba/ de dag gi rgyab brten du dka' 'grel padma can mtsho skyes zhabs kyis mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po tri ti garbha
dang khu ston dngos grub kyis bsgyur ba/ skabs kyi 'grel chung brgyad du grags pa la/ gleng gzhi'i 'grel pa che chung nag po brtul zhugs spyod pas mdzad pa/ ga ya dha
ra dang 'brog mis bsgyur ba/ glu'i 'grel pa che chung slob dpon sgrol ma can gyis mdzad pa 'gyur gong 'dra/ yang glu'i de kho na gsal ba'i 'grel pa padma'i zhabs kyis mdzad
pa 'gyur gong 'dra/ rtsa'i 'grel pa  mngon par rtogs pa'i rim pa zhes byung brtag che chung 'gyur gong 'dra/ yang rtsa'i 'grel pa  kye rdo rje'i de kho na nyid kyi rim
pa zhes byung /mdzad byang med pa 'gyur gong 'dra/ dur khrod kyi 'grel pa che chung mdzad byang med pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po ratna shrI dznyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA
ba dge slong shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba/ dur khrod kyi 'grel pa che ba sampu Ta las bsdus par bshad snang ngo / /brda'i 'grel pa rnam par nges pa ye shes rgyal mtshan
gyis 'gyur bcos pa rnams so/ /gsum pa slob dpon dam tshig rdo rje'i rjes su 'brang ba nag po shAnta bha dra'i skor la/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nag po gzhung 'grel paNDi ta
nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba 'gos khug pa lhas btsas kyis bsgyur ba/ dpal kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid gsal ba nag po dam tshig
rdo rjes mdzad pa paNDi ta

de nyid dang nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba/ kye rdo rje phyag bcu drug pa dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang
'gos los bsgyur ba/ bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs mdzad pa dang 'gyur gong 'dra/ bar 'dir tshogs 'khor gyi cho ga 'gos 'gyur dang phyag gnyis pa dpa' gcig tshul khrims grags
kyi 'gyur zer ba gnyis sangs rgyas bstan pa'i gsan yig tu 'dug kyang dpe ma 'byor bas lung ma byung / rmor chen pa'i gsan yig na'ang mi 'dug pas ma dgos pa yin nam brtag
sbyin sreg gi cho ga mdzad pa dang 'gyur gong 'dra/ rab gnas kyi cho ga mdzad pa dang 'gyur gong 'dra/ gshin gyi cho ga nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa paNDi ta rgyal ba'i
gnyen dang thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis dben gnas thar pa gling du bsgyur ba/ ro sreg gi cho ga dang mchod rten gyi cho ga nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba ste gzhung
de rnams dam tshig rdo rje'i slob ma nag po shAnta bha dras mdzad pa rnams so/ /dka' 'grel 'di lung ma byung / rnal 'byor rin po che sbyor ba'i phreng ba nag po zhabs
kyis mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang 'gos khug pa lhas btsas kyis bsgyur ba rnams te/ de ltar gtso che ba'i chos sna so dgur grags pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
'chang yan chad gsan yig rgya mtsho ltar dang / de nas rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhas grub dpal
ldan rdo rje/ de gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ chos rje dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shes rab rgyal

mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams/ dpal sa skya pa kun dga' bkra shis/ 'khrul zad bsod nams chos 'phel/ khyab bdag sangs rgyas bstan
pa/ rigs kun khyab bdag sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin stsal to/ /!/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'am sgrub khang dpal ldan
don grub pas mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rje btsun ma sgrol ma lha bcu bdun gyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun
ma sgrol ma/ slob dpon nyi ma sbas pa/ tsandra garbha/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ wA gI shwa ra kIrti/ shraddhA ka ra warma/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ paNDi ta dA na shI
la/ manydzu shrI/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ khams pa ne tso sbal ston/ gnam pa rwa chos she/ mngon pa ba byang chub brtson 'grus/ paNDi ta
rdo rje shes rab/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ rgyal ba brag phug pa chen po/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
kun dga' bzang po/ paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun
grub/ rje btsun byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen
rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ g.yung drung

nas g.yung drung gi rtags bar 'di bas 'og ma 'di btsan/ rmor chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag
tshul khrims rin chen la stsal bar 'gyur ro/ /yang na mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa  'di mi 'dug chad dam snyam/ngag dbang lhun grub/ mtshungs med chos rje
kun dga' chos 'phel/ mkhas btsun chen po nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na mal lo nas/ pu cer lo tsA ba/ la stod dbang rin/
mchims chos seng / mchims blo brtan/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ bla ma ye shes rin chen/ bla ma mkhan chen pa/ bla ma klu byang pa/
lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na 'phags
pa rin po che nas/ bla brang pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ bla brang pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla brang pa bzang po dpal/ rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ ye shes dpal 'byor/ bzang
po'ang byung /rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje man 'dra'o/ /!/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i yi ge
la brten nas rdo rje gur nas gsungs pa'i las rgyas pa'i lha shes phyin dkar mo'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub pa'i dbang po/ badzra pA Ni/ dze
tA ri/ rdo rje

gdan pa che chung / ba ri rin chen grags/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom
kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ chos rje bsod nams skyabs/ rje gzungs kyi dpal ba/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse
nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ grub mchog kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag
tshul khrims rin chen la yig cha de nyid kyi lung bcas stsal to/ /!/ grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal pos 'jigs byed mun pa tshal gyi dur khrod du bram ze mchog sred
las mgon po'i rgyud dang man ngag rnams gsan zhing khyad par rdo rje gur nas bshad pa'i mgon po 'di nyid kyi rjes gnang gsan pa'i tshe/ nam srod kyi cha la sprin nag
du ba'i mdog can gyi dbus na zhabs pus man chad nub pa'i sku'i snang ba gsal bar bstan pas gur mgon sprin gseb mar grags pa'i rjes gnang ting 'dzin nyi zla bzang pos mdzad
pa'i dgra bgegs tshar gcod kyi yi ge bzhin thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen
po/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin nyi zla

bzang po/ de dbon ngag dbang nyi ma/ sprul pa'i sku mchog kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang drin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun
grub/ grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yig cha de nyid kyi 'gor/ na mo bIrYa bha drA ya zhes dang
/ dam med lag tu mi sbyin bka' rgyas thob saM mApta mi thi'i mtha' can gyi lung yang nos/ /!/ bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i shin tu thugs gtsigs che ba nor
gyi lha mo dbyu gu ma mched gsum gyi chos skor gyi lung man ngag phyag bzhes dang bcas legs par thob pa ni/ klu sgrub kyis sha za'i gnod sbyin mo mkha' 'gro kun nas 'khyil
ba'i rtog pa las phyung ba'i sgrub thabs bla ma rdo rje gdan pa dang ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa'i gnod sbyin mo kun nas 'khyil ba'i don bsdus
'grel pa ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba la slar pa tshab lo tsA bas 'gyur bcos mdzad pa/ de'i snying po sa paN gyis mdzad pa bla ma ba ri ba rgya gar du bzhugs dus shin tu
bkren par rdo rje gdan pas gnang nas zas gos nor gsum tshegs med du 'ong gsungs pa'i lo rgyus dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag chos brgyags su bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam
pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /man ngag 'di bla ma rdo rje gdan pas ba ri lo tsA ba la gnang ba'i zhes yod pa'i lo tsA ba bod du 'byon dus rdo rje gdan pas skyel thung mdzad
nas gnang ba'i thugs dam mkha' 'gro ma'i dngos grub lag bcangs i

thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes yod pa'i spun gsum gyi mngon rtogs gsal byed btsal sla ba yin no'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla
ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dbyu gu spun gsum gyi man ngag 'di zhes yod pa'i gtor ma gtang thabs phun sum tshogs par byed do'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams
la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bla ma rdo rje gdan pas bla ma ba ri lo tsA ba la gnang ba'i gdams pa zhes yod pa'i rten bca' thabs/ zab thig snying gi gdams pa i thi'i mtha' can/
'gor bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /man ngag 'di bla ma rdo rje gdan pas ba ri lo tsA la bu khyod bod du 'gro na zhes yod pa'i mkha' 'gro ma'i lag bcangs 'dra
min rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ 'gor rnal 'byor pa gang zhig ces yod pa'i bsgrub pa bya thabs rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ chang bu bsngo lugs dang tshigs bcad mkha' 'gro
chen mo la/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ 'jig rten 'dren pa phyag gi lhung bzed dbus/ /zhes yod pa'i brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ rten bca' thabs/ bsnyen sgrub las sbyor bcas ston pa'i man
ngag rgyas par bstan pa bla ma gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ de'i zhar byung du rab gnas bya thabs/ bla rdo bcangs thabs i thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo gu ru badzra DA ki ni/ dbul
ba sel ba'i gter chen mi zad pa/ /zhes yod pa'i man ngag bla rdo bcangs thabs dang bcas pa rgyas par bstan pa bkra shis sogs bya'o'i mtha' can/ sa skya pa chen po sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis dge tshul

byams pa bzang po'i don du mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs bsam don kun 'grub/ shAkya'i dge slong ratna'i mtha' can gyis bskul ba'i don du tsakra la brten pa'i dbang sdud zab mo'i lag
len gsal bar bkod pa bsam 'phel nor bu rnams thob pa las/ rgya gzhung yig rnying rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ dze tA
ri/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags pa/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/
'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ bla ma khang ston pa/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ jo nang kun mkhyen chen po/ bla ma byang chub seng ge shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun
grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams/ mkhan chen nam mkha' rin chen/ grub brtson
kun dga' bzang po/ khams ston sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ chos kyi rje kun dga' chos 'phel/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des
bdag la'o/ /yang na sa skya pa kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i yig cha rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ yan chad rgya gzhung ltar las/ de nas sa skya pa kun dga' bsod nams

nas/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag la'o/ /yang na bod gzhung rkyang pa'i lung ni/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs par 'dra/ de nas bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen
bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan/ tshogs
sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ rgyal ba brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma blo bzang pa/ bla ma seng ge dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rje bsod nams seng ge de sras bya btang rje/
'jam dbyangs nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje chos kyi dbang phyug mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /!/ bla ma g.ya' bzang pa nas brgyud pa'i gza' srung thos pa/
gnubs 'dul 'dzin chen po rgyal ba g.ya' bzang par drang srong gzas dngos su phul ba'i gza' nyi ma mdung gang ma'i skor la/ rang skor man ngag la dgos pa'i sgom lung / rang
gi skor le tshan gnyis/ g.ya' bzang yang dkon gyi skor/ sham po rtsal gyi skor/ gzims chung ma'i skor dang drug dang po phyag rdor sgom  sgom lung zur du 'bogs pa zhig
ma byung yang lung gis thus sam/lung sogs/ brgyud pa rgyal ba g.ya' bzang pa/ chos smon lam 'od pa/khams sgom bya bral nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ thar pa bde rgyas pa don yod
dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal

mtshan/ mdo stod pa brtson 'grus dpal/ gtsang nyeg pa rin chen  zhwa lu'i phu shar bsam gtan sgang nas yin/rgyal mtshan/ dben pa bla ma rin chen dpal grub/ zhwa lu'i phu nub
pa/chos rje ston dge ba/ srad pa/chos rje bka' bcu dar bzang / snar thang pa/chos rje don grub grags pa dpal bzang / srad pa/slob dpon bka' bcu bsod nams grags pa/ lo chen
chos skyong bzang po/ bar 'dir bla ma gcig gnyis shig ma rnyed/ byang gling pa dbang rab la sogs/ yang na gtsang nyeg pa rin chen rgyal mtshan nas/ snar thang byang chen
pa bsod nams blo gros/ chos rje don grub grags pa/ bka' bcu bsod grags man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa/ gtsang nyeg pa man 'dra/ skor rnams mi 'dra ba mang du snang /
yang na g.ya' bzang pa nas/ nyi ma rgyal mtshan don yod dpal/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen byang seng / theg chen chos rje/ bla ma chos grags pa/ rin chen bzang po/ gangs can
kun dga' dpal/ rin chen legs 'phel/ o rgyan dpal 'byor/ g.ya' bzang pa rin chen phun tshogs/ rin chen dar rgyas sogs/ yang theg chen nas/ mar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/
brag nag pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ lha btsun grags pa byang chub/ kun spangs rin chen/ khrab chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / nam mkha' sangs rgyas/
chos dbang phyug mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ a mi lags/ tshogs gsog pas 'di nas gsan nam brtag tshogs gsog pa nas rje buddha ba/ mkhas grub

sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ gtsang gsar chos rje/ gter dbon bsod nams lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /smras pa/ rtsa bshad rgyud kyis nyer bstan kye rdo rje/
/bka' babs rnam gsum gur dang kha sbyor dbang / /shes rab pha rol phyin ma mgon rkyang bcas/ /kun 'khyil la sogs bkas gnang skal ba sbom/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi
ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ thabs shes gnyis med dgyes pa rdo rje'i rgyud gsum gyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste bcu dgu pa'o/ // /gnyis
su med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dang po'i sangs rgyas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i skor la/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyi ma'i gnyen nyid shing pho rta'i lo sa gas nya ba'i tshes
la zag pa med pa'i bdud rtsi mchog brnyes pa'i go 'phang bla na med pa mngon du mdzad nas bgrang gzhi bzhi bcu rtsa drug 'das pa lcags 'brug nag pa'i zla bar shrI dha
nya ka Ta ka'i mchod rten gyi nang gi steng du dpal ldan rgyu skar gyi dkyil 'khor spros te sprul pa'i chos rgyal zla ba bzang po la sogs pa skal ldan gyi gdul bya rnams
smin par mdzad/ de'i phyi lo chos rgyal zla ba bzang pos dus 'khor rtsa ba'i rgyud bsdus/ byang phyogs sham bha lar chos rgyal drug dang rigs ldan bcu bdun 'das shing rigs
ldan rnam gnon gdong lnga'i dbang pos sgeg pa'i chos kyi khrir phebs shing / dam pa'i chos bstan nas lo sum cu rtsa lnga pa/ me mkha' rgya mtsho la 'das lo drug cu skor
bdun dang nyag ma lnga bcur slebs pa/ rab byung bcu gsum pa'i khyu mchog co zhes pa'i gnam lo shar

ba/ sgrol byed bu mo dbos nya ba'i zla ba/ dkar po'i phyogs kyi rdzogs pa gsum pa'i tshe sa ga la bar/ res gza' pa sangs/ skar ma phug ron/ sbyor ba las bzang / byed pa snga
cha biShTi/ phyi cha gdab pa rnams shar ba'i dus su mdo khams phyogs kyi dbyig 'dzin thig le shrI se na shu bha'i rigs kyi chos ldan gyi sa'i tshangs pa chen pos phun tshogs
stobs kyi 'khor los legs par bsrungs pa'i gdan sa chen po lhun grub steng gi gtsug lag khang chen por khams gsum 'gro ba'i bla ma khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po dang
po'i sangs rgyas kA la tsakra nyid ngur smrig bla gos gsar pa'i lang tshos mngon par sgeg pa'i blo gsal kun dga' ster byed phun tshogs mdzad pa'i chu gter skyong ba gang
de dus kyi 'khor lo'i ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs pa'i rdo rje'i slob dpon chen po gang gis dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil
'khor chen por thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i mngon par rtogs pa rgyas pa dngos grub 'dod 'jo/ dkyil chog yon tan kun 'byung / mchod phreng mchod sprin
rgya mtsho/ mkhyen rab rjes mdzad pa'i zin bris bkra shis rab rgyas/ gzhan yang slob ma yang slob dang bcas pa'i zin bris thor bu bzhugs pa rnams kyi steng nas rdo rje'i
slob bu ngag dbang tshul khrims rin chen du bod pa la byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun gyi dbang bskur ba la brten nas 'og min srid pa'i mthar thug pa'i 'jig rten pa'i dngos
grub 'grub pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bden pa nyid kyi bsod nams

dang ye shes kyi 'bras bu thob pa'i slad du lung bstan cing rjes su gnang ba dang / zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor mchog gi nges don gyi dkyil 'khor rnams su dbang gong ma bzhi
gong chen dang bcas pa bdag po chen po'i dbang rnams brgyud pa'i bka' babs bzhi dang ldan pa legs par nos pa'i dang po 'bro lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag dang po'i
sangs rgyas/ chos sku rdo rje 'chang / longs sku dus kyi 'khor lo/ sprul sku shAkya thub pa/ chos rgyal zla ba bzang po/ lha'i dbang po/ gzi brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha'i
dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan te chos rgyal bdun/ rigs ldan 'jam dpal grags pa/ padma dkar po/ bzang po/ rnam rgyal/ bshes gnyen bzang po/ phyag na rin
chen/ phyag dmar ba yang zer/khyab 'jug sbas pa/ nyi ma grags pa/ shin tu bzang po/ rgya mtsho rnam rgyal/'di nas me mkha' rgya mtsho'i dbu tshugs/ rgyal dga'/ nyi ma/
sna tshogs gzugs/ zla ba'i 'od/ mtha' yas/ sa skyong / dpal skyong / grub chen dus 'khor zhabs pa che chung / che ba tsor yang sha'i pho brang du 'khrungs/ chung pa nA lenda
pa/rgyal sras nA lenda pa/ bu ston rje btsun btsong kha pa gong dkar thar rtse lo pa spyan snga sgrub khang pa rnams kyi gsan yig na mi 'dug kyang mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags pa'i gsan yig na kha che zla mgon dang gcig par mdzad/ ngor chen/ rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa/ rje mkhyen brtse gsum gyi gsan yig na dkyus ltar snang ba dpyad
do// kha che zla ba mgon po/ paN dkar/'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags/ grab sgom dkon mchog srung / 'phan yul ba bod btsun/rnal 'byor bzang po sgro ston rnams la brtsegs/
sngags dkar co

breg can/grub chen yu  btsun rgan mo  bu ston rje btsong kha pa ngor chen gong dkar thar rtse ngag chos lo pa rnams kyi gsan yig na mi snang bas dpyad/dad pa  gsang mtshan
mi bskyod rdo rje/rgyal po/ sras chos kyi dbang phyug  sngags dkar co breg can/grub thob nam mkha' 'od/ sprul sku jo 'bum/ se mo che ba nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam gsar
shes rab 'od zer/ phyam rtse ba/kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ se ston kun rig gi skye bar grags/ bod btsun yin/byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/
'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ shar pa ye shes rgya mtsho/
rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub/ chos rje don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling 'jam dpal bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen tshe dbang lhun grub/ khyab bdag klu sgrub rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med smon
lam lhun grub/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang brtson 'grus bzang po/ stobs bcu mnga' ba mchog gi bstan pa rin po che'i snang byed/ gsang chen dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdagaganas
gsar mkhan po ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po nga / khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po dpal ldan dang po'i sangs rgyas ngur
smrig 'chang gi rnam par rol pa'i dus 'khor ba rdo rje slob dpon chen po

kun dga' phun tshogs pa/ des bdag bande shI la ratna'i ming can la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na 'jam gsar nas/ rje btsun rong pa rgwa lo/ de sras shes rab seng ge skyi ston
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na 'jam gsar nas/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ byang sems rgyal
ba ye shes/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs shAkya gzhon nu/ gzhon nu
rdo rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ gnyags phu ba bsod nams bzang po/ paN chen byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal
ba/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ dam chos gling pa ye shes dbang po/ nyi ma gling pa
tshul khrims bkra shis/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang chen po kun bzang padma phrin las/ kun mkhyen bstan pa'i sgron me ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/
/yang bu lugs kyi 'bro'i brgyud pa ltar na/ 'phags 'od yon

tan rgya mtsho yan gong ltar las/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ shar pa ye
shes rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ sku zhang rin po che bsod nams mchog grub/ yang na kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer nas/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/
bu ston man 'dra/ thar lo lugs kyi ring brgyud ni/ 'jam gsar ba yan gong ltar las/ de nas nyeg po chos ldan/ go lung pa gzhon nu dpal/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bu ston
rin po che man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / dpe med 'tsho/ dpal 'dzin/ 'od byed lha/ chos 'byung zhi ba/ nyi ma dpal ye shes/ rin chen 'tsho/ bi bhU ti/ ko grag pa bsod
nams rgyal mtshan/ go lung pa gzhon nu dpal man 'dra/ yang nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / sha ba ri/ bi bhU ti/ ko grag pa man 'dra/ yang shong lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
se mo che pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan nas/ bo dong rin chen rtse mo/ stag sde ba seng ge rgyal mtshan/ shong lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ shong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan
pa/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa man 'dra/ yang na bo dong rin chen rtse mo nas/ 'dzim pa rin
chen shes rab/ shar pa dus 'khor ba ye shes rin chen/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ chos rje bu ston rin po che man 'dra'o/ /yang na
bu ston rin po che nas/ bla ma dharma shrI snar thang lo tsA ba sanggha shrI/ gzad pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ mkhas
grub rin chen rnam rgyal/ yangs pa can pa shAkya kun dga'/ dam chos gling pa ye shes dbang po/ mtshungs med nyi ma gling pa man 'dra/ yang na bu ston rin po che nas/ thugs
sras rin chen rnam

rgyal/ zhwa lu khang rnying slob dpon bsod nams chos 'phel/ stag tshang lo tsA ba sogs las brgyud pa'ang yod do/ /bka' babs gnyis pa rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dang po'i sangs
rgyas/ chos rgyal zla ba bzang po/ chos rgyal sum cu gnyis/ gsan yig rnams su 'di ltar 'byung yang tsi lu pa'i dus rigs ldan yan ma gtogs de min dpyad gzhir snang /'jam
dbyangs sprul pa tsi lu paNDi ta/ pi to pa/ gong dkar ba dang thar rtse ba'i gsan yig na paNDi ta A tsArYa zhes pa 'dug dus zhabs pa che chung / manydzu kIrti/ sa manta
shrI/ rwa lo tsA ba chen po chos rab/ ne'u me tog gdan du 'khrungs/rwa ye shes seng ge  khu lung se byi ru/rwa 'bum seng / khu lung chos shing dgon pa/rje btsun rgwa lo
rnam rgyal rdo rje/ rong dman dmar ba/bla ma rong pa shes rab seng ge  rong shambhar du/skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan man gong bzhin no/ /bu lugs rwa brgyud ltar na/ dam
pa dang po'i sangs rgyas/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo/ rgyal ba shAkya thub pa/ zla ba bzang po/ lha dbang gzi brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha'i dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i
dbang ldan/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ padma dkar po/ 'jam dbyangs sprul pa/ tsi lu paN chen/ rwa pa rnams 'di dang dus zhabs pa tha dad du bzhed/pi to A tsArYa/ dus zhabs
pa che ba/ dus zhabs pa gnyis pa/ manydzu kIrti/ sa manta shrI/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de sras shes rab seng ge
bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na rong pa shes rab seng ge nas/ rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ bu

ston rje man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gsum pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje snying po/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ tsi lu paNDi
ta/ dus zhabs pa che ba/ dus zhabs pa gnyis pa/ a nu pa ma rakShi ta/ sA dhu pu tra/ chos kyi 'byung gnas/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ bi kShA ta de wa/ ma hA paNDi ta shAkya
shrI/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ rgyus pa gzhon nu seng ge dol po ye shes mgon po/ kun spangs kun tu bzang po/ kun mkhyen 'phags
'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs bzhi pa ma hA paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rigs ldan rnam rgyal yan
gong ltar las/ de nas dus zhabs pa che chung / shAkya seng ge rgyal mtshan/ nyi ma'i 'od/ gau tam dpal/ rin chen bkra shis/ rgyal ba'i rgyan/ blo ldan rje/ shAkya bsrungs
pa/ rje chen po legs skyes/ dpal sangs rgyas dbyangs/ ma hA paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa man sngar bzhin no/ /!/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyas
'grel rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad pa/ stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od le'u lnga pa 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags
kyis bsgyur zhing / slar shong ston gyis dpal ldan sa skyar dag par bsgyur ba la bu ston thams cad mkhyen pas dka' ba'i gnas la gsung mchan zhib par mdzad pa bcas pa'i lung
yongs su

rdzogs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rong pa shes rab seng ge yan dbang brgyud bu lugs kyi rwa lugs dang 'dra zhing / de nas bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu
ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po rin chen rnam rgyal/ mkhas pa ratna shrI/ mkhas pa zla ba dpal rin/ tsandra shrI/'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/
rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ byang gling pa rin chen rgyal po/ 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ dge 'khor ba
rin chen dkon mchog lha 'o pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mngon dga' ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ don grub chos gling pa mtshungs med bstan
pa dar rgyas/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ gnas gsar ba kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas man 'dra'o/ /dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la thun mong gi las sgrub pa'i lha gsum
yod pa'i dang po rje sgo rum pas mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rdo rje'i tsher ma 'brum nad kyi gnyen po bcom ldan 'das ma sna tshogs yum gyi rjes su gnang ba thun mong
ma yin pa phyag len ltar dang sgo rum pas mdzad pa'i yi ge'i lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dang po'i sangs rgyas/ rigs gsum mgon po/ dus zhabs pa che chung / rgyal
sras nA lenda pa/ paN chen zla ba mgon po/ 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags/ sgom pa dkon mchog srung / sgro ston gnam la brtsegs/ 'phan yul sgro rings pa/yu mo dad pa rgyal
po/ sras dharme shwa ra/ rje nam mkha' 'od/ ma gcig sprul sku jo 'bum/ se

mo che ba nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam gsar shes rab 'od zer/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ mkhas btsun yon tan
rgya mtsho/ dol po kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje bsod nams sangs rgyas/
rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa rin chen
bsod nams mchog grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na rdo ring rin po che nas/ rje btsun
sgo rum pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang na sgo rum pa nas/ de dbon ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra'o/ /yang na
shrI kA la tsakra/ ma hA paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen/ khrims khang lo tsA ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde/ bla ma gnyis gong 'og nor 'dug kyang ras chung pas mid la la tshe
dbang phul ba ltar yin nam zhes gsan yig tu snang /'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs
man 'dra'o/ /!/ gnyis pa klu dang sa bdag gi gdon 'joms pa mkha' lding rdo rje khyung khra bo'i skor la/ rje sgo rum pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rgyud 'grel dang mthun
par sbyar ba'i yi ge'i steng nas rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje

'chang / chos rgyal zla ba bzang po/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ padma dkar po/ dus zhabs pa che chung gnyis/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ mkhyen brtse thar rtse
sgrub khang gsum gyi gsan yig na mi gsal yang rdzong lugs kyi gsan yig na 'di'i rjes su glog skya shes rab brtsegs 'dug pa chad dam snyam/mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags/ sa
chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga' ldan
pa kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ gu ge paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga'
bsod nams lhun grub/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bkra shis dpal ldan/ chos rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub chen po
sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bka' drin mnyam med rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /sgrub thabs gong du smos
pa dang / rjes gnang sgrub thabs rgya mtsho ltar mdzad do/ /!/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pas mdzad pa'i rjes gnang dang de'i zur 'debs le'u mkhan chen byams pa ngag dbang
dpal bzang gis mdzad pa gnyis la brten nas dus kyi 'khor lo'i

bsdus rgyud kyis zin cing paNDi ta nA ro pa'i man ngag rje btsun sa skya pa chen po'i zab chos dpal rdo rje khyung khra'i sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi byin rlabs byab
bsrung dang 'brel ba nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ mnyam med bzang po rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i chos skor gyi dkar chag thub bstan mi mjed ma/ byis pa'i gdon chen
bco lnga'i nang nas bya mig gi bcos thabs zhes pa brtag thabs/ gso thabs/ phyir 'phro gcad pa dang bcas pa sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal bas mdzad pa la snying po'i zhal
shes rnams go bde phyir shrI bsam rtser pha la'i ming can gyis bris pa/ tshim par byed pa bya mdos kyi yi ge bya rgyud dang mthun par rdo rje khyung khra'i las mtha' gzungs
kyi ming can gyis mdzad pa/ khyi smyon gyi brtag pa/ gso ba'i thabs/ rang srung rjes gcod dang bcas pa sngags 'chang gzungs pas mdzad pa zhal shes rnams go bde phyir bsnan
te shrI bsam rtser pha la'i ming can gyis bris pa/ gza' nad la dang por brtag pa/ bar du gso dpyad/ phyir mi ldog pa rjes kyi bya ba dang gsum gyis bstan pa sngags 'chang
gzungs dpal gyis mdzad par slar yang zhal shes kyis brgyan pa shrI bsam rtser pha la'i ming can gyis bris pa/ dkar phra men brtag thabs kyi zhal shes/ gza' bcos kyi
lag len dang shog dril khyung rgya ma zhes par ming dang 'gyu dus/ phyi ru rten 'brel brtsi ba/ gza' brgyad kyi sngags/ rA hu la'i byad 'grol dang bcas pa gzungs pas rdzong
chung bla brang du mdzad pa/ las mde gshed skor zab mo/ sbrul

lpags la brten pa'i bsrung ba/ gza' mdos kyi cho ga 'bring po rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ dug nad gso ba bai DUrYa'i phreng ba zhes pa brtag pa/ 'chos thabs/ 'bring bsdus zab
mo sngags 'chang gzungs pas mdzad pa/ dug bsrung brtag pa'i man ngag zab mo zur du bris pas blta bar bya'o'i mtha' can/ las sbyor drug pa zhes pa bong nga'i bcud len gnyan
gyis so btab pa gso ba/ dug bsrung dug khong du song ba bzlog pa/ nad phyogs med 'joms pa/ de'i ge gas sel dang dmigs pa'i khyad par rnams bla ma'i gsung bzhin 'phags
pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ nA ro paN chen nas brgyud pa'i rdo rje khyung khra'i las sbyor brgyad pa/ zhes pa bong nga la brten nas grang ba snying rlung tshad pa sel zhing
bcud len gyi mchog tu 'gyur ba/ g.yos dug dbyig dug sbyar dug bsrung ba/ rgyu ba'i dug rnams kyis so btab pa zhi ba/ gre nad sel ba/ gnyan tshad las grol ba/ nad brgya sman
gcig nad spyi dang khyad par mdze dreg grum gza' nad sel ba/ bum chog gtor chog dang bcas pa sngags 'chang gzungs pas rdzong chung bla brang du mdzad pa/ dreg 'don pa'i
man ngag bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la dreg byung ba'i dus dpal gyi ming can gyis sa skyar bkod pa/ dreg sel ba sdig pa chung pa bka' rgya ma/ mdze 'chos pa brtag thabs gso
thabs rjes gsum gyis bstan pa lus la btags so'i mtha' can/ bsnyen pa 'khyol nas thog bsrung ba 'phags pas shing kun tu mdzad pa/ khyung gi las mtha' ge gas sel gzer lnga'i
snyan brgyud gzungs kyi ming can gyis rdo rje khyung

khra'i las mder sbyar ba/ rgyal mo chu sbyang ba 'og rlung 'bebs so'i mtha' can/ rigs gsum 'dus pa'i drag sngags phyag cha rang la bskor ba skyin thang bsrung ba/ ser ba bsrung
ba/ lo chog dang lo phud kyi lag len zhes pa sngon 'gro dang dngos gzhi la nam mkha'i mthongs su sprin nag gi gur bshig pa/ ri thang mtshams su ser ba'i rkang bcag pa/
bar snang khams su 'khyags pa chur bzhu ba/ sa gzhi'i steng du rlung gi gzhu bcag pa/ drag po 'brug gi ngar skad bcag pa rnams bstan pa/ kha ba bsrung ba/ 'phags pa rin
po ches mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga des mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge des mdzad pa'i bstod pa rigs lnga'i klu 'dul/ A nanda ma ti bha dras mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/
sngags 'chang gzungs pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs nang bzhin las 'don mjug cung zad kha bskang ba/ mkhan chen byams pa ngag dbang dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i byin rlabs zur 'debs
kyi yi ge dang bcas pa rnams legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ drug pa rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ paN chen nA ro pa/ bal po pham mthing pa sku mched/
gcen 'jigs med grags pa/ gcung ngag dbang grags pa/klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo blo gros grags/ dpal sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ chos rje sa paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang gzungs
kyi dpal

ba/ chos rje dge legs dpal bzang / rdzong chung pa A nanda ma ti bha dra/ chos rje sangs rgyas bzang po/ rig 'dzin chos blo gros/ rig 'dzin chos dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen byams
pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ mkhan chen byams pa ngag dbang dpal bzang / rdo rje 'chang zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ gnas gsar pa mkhan chen
'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa wA gIndra shA sa na lakShmI/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos
skyong / de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis nos so/ /yang na las tshogs kyi lung rkyang gi brgyud pa ni yan chad sngar bzhin la/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong
/ de las bdag gis legs par nos so/ /yang na sngags 'chang gzungs pa nas/ mnyam med bzang po rgyal mtshan/ sems dpa' chen po rgyal mtshan dkon mchog rus kyi ming yin/
rtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgyud gsum smra ba shes rab rin chen/ rdo ring kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ sgye chu mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal
'byor man 'dra/ yang na A nanda ma ti nas/ mkhas grub byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang rjes gnang dang bya khyi rnam gsum bcos thabs kyi lung brgyud lugs gcig
ni/ 'bum chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas bkra shis/ byams pa ngag dbang dpal bzang man 'dra/ /!/ gsum pa lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs
dang

rjes gnang gi yi ge la brten nas char dbab gcod byed pa khro bo'i dbang po rdo rje shugs kyi rjes su gnang ba nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / dus kyi 'khor lo/ shAkya
thub pa/ chos rgyal rigs ldan so lnga/ dus zhabs pa che chung / kha che zla ba mgon po/ 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags/ lha rje sgom pa pa/ sgro ston gnam la brtsegs/ yu
mo mi  dad pa rgyal po zer ba'ang byung /bskyod rdo rje/ sras chos kyi dbang phyug se chen nam mkha' 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'jam gsar ba/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ zhang thugs
rje brtson 'grus/ byang sems rgyal ye/ mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen dol po shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ mkhas grub nya dbon/ grub chen
kun blo/ mkhan chen dkon mchog  dpal 'khor chos sde'i mkhan po/bzang po/ zhwa lu lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ lo chen ratna bha dra/ lo chen 'gyur med bde chen/ rje
a wa dhU tI pa/ spyan snga rin po che kun dga' don grub/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga'
lhun grub/ de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis mnos so/ /'dir rmor chen pa'i gsan yig tu/ yang ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi
ge'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ zhwa lu lo chen nas/ she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po
man 'dra'o/ /gong gi yi ge gnyis kyi rjes

gnang gi chings ni shin tu mi 'dra mod kyang brgyud pa gcig pa'i phyir na gcig go gcig gis chod dam snyam mo zhes gsungs/ bdag gis ni yig cha snga ma'i steng nas thob bo/ /smras
pa/ gsang rgyud gzhan las bshad tshul khyad par ba/ /dus 'khor dbang bdun gong ma gong chen bcas/ /thun mong dngos grub sgrub pa'i lha gsum gyi/ /rjes gnang thos pa'i
rna lung ma dog tsam/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste nyi
shu pa'o/ // /rnal 'byor mchog gi dbyar skyes 'dzam bu las/ shing rta che srol snye ma yongs lhung ba/ /mkhas dbang mkhyen pa'i ma dros rtsis bsgyur ba'i/ /zab chos bum
pa brgya skyes mnos pa'i tshul/ /spyi don lnga pa gser chos skor la/ dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa byon dang 'byon 'gyur 'byon bzhin pa mtha' dag gi lam po che/ mdo sde
dang rgyud sde mtha' dag gi man ngag thams cad kyi bcud phyung ba/ 'phags yul paN grub kun gyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa 'jigs bral dpal ldan chos skyong ngam grub
pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa chen po la rje btsun rdo rje bdag med mas dngos su gnang ba'i gdams pa lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa/ 'bras bu
lam dang bcas pa/ gcig shes pas mang po shes pa/ skyon yon tan du blang ba/ bar gcod dngos grub tu blang ba/ ltas ngan g.yang du 'gugs pa/ ting nge 'dzin ngo shes pas bsam
gtan gyi ge gas sel ba/ bar gcod ngo shes pas bdud kyi

gegs sel ba/ sde snod gsum gyi de nyid shes pa gser 'gyur gyi rtsi lta bu/ mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub kun gyi 'dod pa 'jo ba'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu/ gsung ngag rin
po che zhes mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug mtha' dag zung 'jug tu gshegs pa'i them skas chen po 'di nyid ni/ lo tsA ba rnams kyi nang nas nyi zla ltar phyogs kun tu yongs
su grags pa 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyis/ 'phags yul paN grub kun gyi gtsug rgyan du gyur pa'i ma hA paNDi ta gha ya dha ra mnyes pa gsum gyi sgo nas mnyes par mdzad
de legs par zhus shing gtan la phab/ lo tsA ba chen po de la slob ma bgrang gis mi ldang ba'i tshogs dpag tu med pa byung ba'i nang nas gtso bor gyur pa/ gzhung rdzogs pa/
gdams ngag rdzogs pa/ grub pa thob pa'i slob ma gsum sogs byung bar grags shing / gdams pa rdzogs pa'i slob ma'i nang nas rab tu thob pa se mkhar chu ba kun rig de'i slob
ma zhang ston chos 'bar nas bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la bka' babs pa/ de'i srol 'dzin ngor rdzong gong dkar ba tshar pa la sogs pa'i mkhas shing
grub pa ston ka'i mkha' dbyings dag pa'i ngos su sgrib pa med par rgyu skar gyi tshogs bkrag tu che ba ltar grangs su mi chod pa byon pa'i nang nas/ rgyal ba nyi ma'i
rtsa lag chen po rang gi lung rtogs kyi bstan pa rin po che'i snang byed chen por padmo'i gnyen nam bsil sbyin mkhan gyi dkyil 'khor ltar bsngags shing nges pa grub pa
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po zhes yongs su grags pa'i skyes bu chen po

de nyid kyis rgyal tshab chen po'i spyod pa rmad du byung ba ci rigs pas mdo sngags kyi chos thams cad la mkhas pa'i bgyi ba gsum gyi bgyi ba yang dag par bgyis pa'i nang nas/
lhag par sampu Ta las/ bstan bcos tshad ma slob dpon dang / /lung gi rjes 'brang de nyid rig / gsang ston de nyid dngos po yang / /gcig nas gcig brgyud shes par bya/
/bla ma rab kyi zhal las blangs/ /zhes dang / tshad ma snyan brgyud bzhi yis spros pa bcad/ /ces pa ltar lugs srol 'di la tshad ma bzhi dang / snyan brgyud bzhi zhes gsungs
pa'i dang po rje btsun chen pos/ chos kun tshad ma bzhi yis gtan la dbab/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ bla ma tshad ma/ nyams myong tshad ma/ bstan bcos tshad ma/ lung tshad ma
bzhi'i sgo nas gtan la 'bebs par mdzad pa'i tshul gyis legs par phye zhing log par smra ba gzhan gyi klan ka'i gnas rnams yang dag pa'i lung dang rigs pa dang man ngag
gi sgo nas dgag sgrub kyis legs par gtan la phab pa ni/ bdag cag gi ston pas kyang ji skad du/ bsreg bcad brdar ba'i gser bzhin du/ /legs par brtags la nga yi bka'/ /blang
bar bya yi gus phyir min/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'i tshul gyis sprin bral nyin mor byed pa'i dkyil 'khor ltar ches cher gsal bar byed pa po ni rdo rje 'chang chen po de
nyid de/ slar yang de nyid kyi zhal slob yang slob tu bcas pa rnams kyis deng sang gi bar du 'chad nyan gyis gtan la phab cing thugs nyams su bstar bar mdzad pa'i zab pa
las kyang ches zab pa 'di nyid mkhas par rlom pa gzhan gyi

spyod yul du ma gyur pa yin pas/ ji skad du/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ gsung ngag gnad kyi snying po ni/ /gnyis las gsum byung gdams ngag yin/ /kun gyi spyod yul ma
yin pa'i/ /man ngag shes pa bla ma'i drin/ /zhes pa ltar gyi lam srol chen po de nyid kyi nyams khrid zab mo lan gsum gyi bar du thob pa'i chos kyi rkang grangs la/ thams
cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i gdams ngag gi gzhung shing rgyas pa gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i lam gyi sngon 'gro'i khrid yig snang gsum mdzes
par byed pa'i rgyan gyi steng nas bkri ba'i 'gor/ khog phub bshad thabs la/ gsung ngag bstan pa rgyas pa'i nyi 'od/ kha skong kun mkhyen go rams pas mdzad pa dang / kun
mkhyen gung rus mdzad pa gnyis/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i chos 'byung rnams kyi steng nas bshad pa'i rnam grangs ci rigs pa len par mdzad/ thog mar chos spyod
po ti'i lung gi skor la/ 'phags pa dkon mchog gsum rjes su dran pa'i mdo'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas thub pa/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ ma hA paNDi ta/ jo bo dpal ldan a ti sha'abrom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ pu to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan
grags/ gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ rgyang ro byang chub 'bum/ mchims blo bzang grags/ yol ston bsod nams lhun grub/
slob

dpon grags pa rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ rgya ston tsandra de wa/ ri khrod pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo
rje/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ de las rje dkon mchog dpal ldan dang brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis
ka las 'jam dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub dang shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las rje dpal ldan don grub/ de las rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/
bstan pa'i snang byed sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ de las bande tshul khrims
rin chen gyis lan gsum gyi bar du nos so/ /yang na khri chen 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub las/ 'dren mchog nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje btsun nam mkha' dpal
bzang / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ 'phags pa phung po gsum pa'i mdo'i
brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang kun dga' bo dang rakShi ta/ /kr-iShNa'i gos can sha na'i gos can dang / /nyi ma gung pa rgyal rigs thams cad mkhyen/ /'phags pa klu sgrub ArYa
de wa dang / /'jam dbyangs grags pa chos 'byung zhi ba dang / /rdo rje gdan pa che 'bring chung gsum rnams/ /paN chen shAka shrI lho pa thams cad mkhyen/ /kong nag ral gri
jo gdan zas gtsang

dang / /shangs pa grags seng zhal snga bsod rin dang / /mkhan po gzhon ye se ston 'byung ldan pa/ /mang mkhar byang sems kun dga' 'od zer ba/ /bag ston gzhon tshul kun spangs
chos grags dpal/ /ma ti paN chen sa bzang 'phags pa dang / /ngor chen kun bzang rgyal tshab kun dbang pa/ /ratna wardha dkon mchog lhun grub zhabs/ /dkon mchog dpal ldan
paN chen gnyis kyis gsan/ /gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub dang / /shar chen byams pa bkra shis gnyis las gsan/ /gnyis kas rjes bzung dpal ldan don grub pa/
/de las 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ /bstan pa'i snang byed sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa/ /bka' drin tshad med tshul khrims lhun grub zhabs/ /de las thos pa tshul
khrims rin chen no/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub nas/ /nam mkha' sangs rgyas nam mkha' dpal bzang pa/ /de las mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs zhabs/ /gang
des rjes bzung tshul khrims lhun grub las/ /legs par nos pa bande tshul rin no/ /yang na thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs/ zhi ba lha/ e la dha ri/ dpa' bo'i
sde/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ 'brom ston pa/ pu to ba/ sha ra ba/ chu mig pa/ gro ston pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ ze'u grags brtson/ grags pa shes rab/ mchims blo bzang
/ mkhan chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ yongs 'dzin dkon

mchog 'phel man 'dra'o/ /!/ thub pa'i dbang po'i bstod pa mdo sde rgyan las phyung ba sems can rnams la brtse ba can zhes sogs yod pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags pa byams pa/ 'phags pa thogs med/ mkhas pa dbyig gnyen/ slob dpon blo gros brtan pa/ paN chen gang ba spel/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze sadzdza
na/ pa ra hi ta/ blo gros grags pa/ mar pa jo gdan/ mchims don grub/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyi ston shAkya 'bum/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ dol pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/
rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje dkon mchog lhun grub man gong gi dkon mchog rjes dran brgyud pa dang 'dra'o/ /!/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying
po'i mdo'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ jo bo rje/ a ti shade'i dbon po dA na shI la/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ dbang bka' gdams
pa/ skyer sgang pa ye shes seng ge  chos kyi seng ge 'ang zer/sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon/ kun mkhyen
bu ston/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog

'phel/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub man gong ma rnams dang 'dra'o/ /mchims nam mkha' grags kyis mdzad pa'i mdo sgrub thos pa'i brgyud pa'ang de dang 'dra'o/ /!/ 'phags pa bzang
po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi mdo dang / byams pa'i smon lam gyi brgyud pa ni/ shes bya kun gzigs thub pa'i dbang po/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ rakShi ta/ kr-iShNa'i gos can/
sha na'i gos can/ nyi ma gung pa/ rgyal rigs thams cad mkhyen pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ chos 'byung zhi ba/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan
med pa'i dpal/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ jo bo puNya shrI/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ dpyal chos bzang / dpyal padmo can/ dpyal a mo gha/ dpyal gzhon nu ye shes/ rong pa shes
rab seng ge bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ kun spangs chos grags/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rgyal ba'i rgyal tshab kun dga' bzang
po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel man gong ma rnams dang 'dra'o/ /!/ yang bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam rkyang pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub/ slob dpon Dombi pa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan
med pa'i dpal/ 'bring ba don yod rdo rje/ chung ba puNya shrI/ so ma shrI/ rwa hu la bha dra/ bi ma la shrI/ be na dha ri/ paN chen shAkya shrI bha dra/ khro phu lo tsA

ba byams pa dpal/ lho pa kun mkhyen rin chen dpal/ spang sgang grags pa rgyal mtshan/ shangs pa grags pa seng ge zhal snga bsod nams rin chen/ dpyal gzhon nu ye shes/ shes
rab dpal/ dge slong kun nyi/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ kun spangs chos grags/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ rgyal ba kun dga' bzang po man sngar dang 'dra'o/
/!/ pha rol tu phyin pa bcu'i smon lam gyi brgyud pa ni gong byams pa'i smon lam dang 'dra'am snyam pa dpyad do/ /!/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dang po'i
sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor lo/ chos rgyal rigs ldan/ dus zhabs pa che chung / kha che zla ba mgon po/ 'bro lo tsA ba/ grags mkhar ba dkon mchog srung / sgro ston gnam la
brtsegs/ grub chen yu mo/ sras dharme shwa ra/ sprul sku jo 'bum/ khang gsar ba nam mkha' 'od zer/ se mo che pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs gsar ma/ de gnyis char
las bo dong rin po che/ de las 'dzim pa rin chen shes rab/ glo chen sangs rgyas sras/ mkhan po rgyal bzang ba/ gangs pa grags pa dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags
pa/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ chos rje dkon mchog
dpal ldan man 'dra'o/ /yang na mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ rwa ston yon tan dpal bzang / mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo

tsA/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ sgrol ma'i phyag 'tshal nyer gcig yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad chen pos mdzad pa
sgrol gsol dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ slob dpon nag po pa/ wa gu paNDi ta/ khu rnal 'byor pa/ zur khang pa gzhon
nu dbang / dge slong bsod nams lo mchog glo chen sangs rgyas sras/ mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun
dga' bzang po man sngar dang 'dra'am snyam ste dpyad do/ /yang na rje btsun sgrol ma nas/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ nyi ma gung pa/ sha na'i gos can/ kr-iShNa'i gos can/ nyi
ma sbas pa/ rA hu la shrI/ bo dhi da shrI/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ khro phu lo tsA ba/ rin chen 'bum/ bla ma sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ glo chen sangs rgyas sras
man 'dra/ yang na mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po nas/ byang seng ba/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na sha na'i gos can/ kha
che thams cad mkhyen pa/ nyer sbas/ rgya mtsho bskyangs/ slob dpon dze tA ri/ ngag dbang grags pa/ kha che ma Ni kamal lo tsA ba/ la stod dbang rin/ mchims chos

seng / mchims blo brtan/ 'jam gsar/ chos 'od/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ don grub/ rgyal mgon/ bkra shis rin chen/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ de dag ni brgyud pa dmigs bsal
dgos pa cung zad bris pa yin la/ chos spyod pusti dngos kyi rkang grangs ni/ dkon mchog rjes dran/ byang chub ltung bshags/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya'i rgyal po la mdzad pa bcu
gnyis kyi sgo nas bstod pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad par grags pa/ thub bstod sems brtse ma mgon po byams pas mdzad pa mdo sde rgyan las phyung ba/ thub dbang rgyan drug mchog
gnyis sogs la bstod pa zhi gdong ma 'phags pas mdzad pa 'dogs 'brel dang bcas pa/ mkhan po bo ddhi sa twa/ chos rgyal mes dbon/ lo paN rnams la thun mong du bstod pa
rnams chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i rgyal rabs gsal ba'i me long gi mchod brjod du mdzad pa rnams dang / jo bo yab sras kyi bstod pa shlau ka re re/ jo bstod phun tshogs
bhangga ma nas 'byung ba rnams so/ /de nas snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi'i dang po bla ma tshad ma'i skor la/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i gsung ngag bla
ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs 'gor rnam dag dkyil 'khor bzhi zhes yod pa/ sa skya pa chen po la rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa gtso 'khor lngas mngon sum du zhal bstan pa'i
dus su mdzad pa'i bstod pa 'gor a la la ste zhes yod pa/ sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i birWa pa'i bstod pa dad pa'i chu las ma/ sa chen gyi bstod pa tshangs dbang ma/ slob dpon
rtse mos mdzad pa/ rje bsod nams rtse mo'i rnam thar

bstod pa khyod nyid dam pa can dang / tshangs par spyod pa'i dge bsnyen ma gnyis rje btsun rin po che grags pas mdzad pa/ rje btsun grags pa'i bstod pa yon tan rgya mtsho ma
sa paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ sa skya paNDi ta'i rnam thar bstod pa chos rgyal ma chung ba yar lung pa byang chub rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ 'phags
pa rin po che la bstod pa sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs rje ma gtsang nag phug pa 'jam dbyangs shes rab 'od zer gyis mdzad pa/ yang 'phags pa'i bstod pa grags ldan ma shlau ka
gcig rgya nag rgyal pos  mi nyag paN chen grags pa rdo rje'i bka' 'bum na'ang 'dug pa des mdzad dam brtag mdzad par grags pa/ bla ma dam pa'i bstod pa bsod nams ye shes
ma shlau ka gcig rgyal sras thogs med pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa las phyung ba/ rje kun dga' bzang po la bstod pa mdo rgyud kun gyi rgya mtsho can shlau ka gcig mus chen gyis
mdzad pa/ rong ston shes bya kun rig la bstod pa mang thos ma/ rje mus chen la bstod pa dkon mchog dges pa ma/ 'jam dbyangs shes rgyal la bstod pa shes bya kun la thogs
med ma/ rgyal tshab dam pa la bstod pa rgyud sde kun gyi de nyid ma/ gung ru sher bzang la bstod pa shes bya'i mkha' la sogs mnga' ris tshul 'od pas mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen
chen po la bstod pa rgya chen bsod nams ma shlau ka gcig rje de nyid kyis mdzad pa/ mkhas grub dpal rdor ba la bstod pa mtha' yas rgyud sde ma kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa/
rje yongs 'dzin/ rje sangs rin/ rje lha mchog pa rnams la bstod pa shlau ka re re

ba rnams dang / rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la bstod pa rab dkar ma rong ston gyis nA lendrar mdzad pa/ rdo rje 'chang la bstod pa sde snod ma mus chen gyis mdzad pa/
yang de la lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i sgo nas bstod cing gsol ba 'debs pa dad pa'i rba rlabs zhes bya ba 'jam dbyangs chos rje shes rab rgya mtshos glo bo smon thang gi
thub bstan dar rgyas gling gi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba/ rong ston chen po'i bstod pa gsung rab rgya mtsho ma rje nyid kyis mdzad pa/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi
bstod pa thub bstan gser gyi khang pa ma bdag chen chu mig pas mdzad pa/ yang sems dpa' chen po'i bstod pa dkon mchog gsum gyi ngo bo ma gung rus mdzad pa/ 'jam dbyangs
shes rab rgya mtsho'i bstod pa mtha' yas shes bya ma bdag chen chu mig pas mdzad pa/ rgyal tshab dam pa'i bstod pa dpal ldan kun dga' ma kun mkhyen go rams pas mdzad pa/
kun mkhyen gyi bstod pa bsod nams ye shes ma mi nyag grags rdor pas mdzad pa/ yongs 'dzin la bstod pa rgyal ba rigs bdag ma glo bo mkhan chen gyis mdzad pa/ yang yongs
'dzin la bstod pa phun tshogs dngos grub ma rje dkon mchog lhun pas mdzad pa/ rje sangs rin gyi bstod pa sangs rgyas kun gyi ngo bo ma sa los mdzad pa/ yang rje sangs rgyas
rin chen gyi bstod pa sangs rgyas kun gyi ngo bo nyid sogs shlau ka gcig glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la bstod

mdzes ma rje rang gis mdzad pa/ rje lha mchog seng ge'i bstod pa bla ma rnams dang lhag pa'i lha sogs shlau ka gcig yang de la bstod pa lhag pa'i lha mchog ma mkhan chen legs
