ge ltar bla ma rin chen 'byung ldan gyi byin rlabs/ paN chen gyi yi ge'i steng nas rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis brtse chen snying po'i zhabs la dngos su gnang ba'i phyi'i
bar gcod srung ba rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi srung ba thun mong ba'i byin rlabs/ ngor

chen rdo rje 'chang dang ngag dbang chos grags pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi srung ba nang ma'i byin rlabs/ de dang 'brel ba'i bir srung gi bsrung ba'i dmigs
rim dang yig rnying / sngon chad zhal shes kho nar bzhugs pa'i bir srung gi cha lag zab mo'i dmigs khrid/ rje ngor chen gyi yi ge'i steng nas bla ma don grub kyi bla
ma'i rnal 'byor bye brag pa tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor du byin gyis brlabs pa/ paN chen ngag
dbang chos grags kyi yi ge ltar brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sa mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs/ man ngag rnams
yongs su rdzogs pa'i mthar brda chig brgyud kyi byin rlabs/ gsung ngag stan thog gcig tu nyams su blang ba'i tshul ston pa lam bsdus te sgrub pa'i lung sbyin pa/ lam yongs
su rdzogs pa'i mthar gsang ba bcus rgyas gdab pa'i byin rlabs/ kun mkhyen go rams pa dang ngag dbang chos grags pa'i yi ge ltar bstan pa gtad cing bka' bsgo ba'i tshul
du lam 'bras pa'i mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang dang bzhi/ chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge la brten pa dang bcas pa rnams legs par thos so/ /gnyis pa de rnams kyi rgyab brten
du bstan bcos tshad ma dang 'brel ba'i lung thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ thog mar gsung ngag glegs bam pod ser ma zhes pa ste/ de'i rgyu mtshan na bza' ser pos dril bas de
ltar du grags so zhes gsungs te/ der bzhugs pa'i chos tshan gyi rnam grangs

la/ 'phrang brag dmar ba dang / dkar shAkya grags sogs kyis bsgrigs pa cung zad mi 'dra tsam du ma 'dug kyang 'dir rje btsun mchog gis bsgrigs pa 'phyugs med kyi rkang grangs
tshigs bcad du brjod na/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang rnam 'grel  sa dpyad gcig yod/gnyags ma dang / /gsal byed kun gzhi rgyu rgyud gdan sogs dang / /lus dkyil 'chi bslu bum
dbang 'da' ka ma/ /thig le'i rnal 'byor phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid dang / /bzhi pa'i 'da' kha bar do'i gdams ngag dang / /lam dbang tshad ma bzhi dang gdams ngag drug / rten
'brel lnga dang grib sel yi ge gnyis/ /thig le bsrung dang yig brgya'i 'don thabs dang / /rlung sbyor bha ga'i yi ge 'khor bzhi'i rgya/ /dbang phyug don brgyad sa phyed
mngon rtogs dang / /don bsdus ma ste nyi shu rtsa bzhi ni/ /rtsa ba nyid kyi steng du bshad bya'o/ /de dag las 'phros gud du gsungs pa'i chos/ /'khor 'das dbyer med dbang
bzhi'i man ngag gnad/ /mchog dbang bskur tshul bskyed rim bsdus pa dang / /ril bu'i sgrub thabs yum gyi byin rlabs dang / /gegs sel bzhi dang dbang chu sgrub thabs gsum/
/rtsa ltung 'khrul spong tshogs 'khor sbyin sreg ste/ /'phros te gsungs pa'i chos sna bcu bdun las/ /phyi ma bdun po logs su bzhugs kyang rung / /'bring gsum lam gnyis
gzhung shing chen po bzhi/ /rtogs bskyed chos lnga lam zab bla ma dang / /lung sbyor bzhi dang brgyud pa'i lo rgyus gnyis/ /man ngag phra mor bcas pa drug cu'o/ /zhes te
drug cu pa 'dir man ngag phra mo la ngos

bzung ba ltar snang yang don la gzhung rtsa ba 'dren pa 'thad par bzhed/ de yang tshad ma bzhi dang sbyor tshul ni/ /bla ma tshad ma rgya bod rnam thar gnyis/ /nyams myong
tshad ma khrid kyi gzhung shing bzhi/ /rtogs bskyed chos lnga ge gas sel yi ge bzhi/ /dbang dang dam tshig gsum gsum lta ba'i gcig / bskyed rim lnga dang yum gyi byin rlabs
dang / /gzhung shing dang po sbyar ba'i chos bcu gsum/ /'bring bsdus lam gnyis lam zab bla ma dang / /nyi shu rtsa dgu nyams myong tshad ma'i skor/ /gnyags ma gsal byed
nyer gnyis don bsdus ma/ /nyi shu rtsa bzhi bstan bcos tshad ma'i skor/ /lung gi tshad ma lung sbyor rnam bzhi ste/ /man ngag phra mos kun la phan 'dogs byed/ /gzhung shing
rgyas par sbyar bya'i chos bcu gsum/ /'phros te gsungs pa'i chos sna bcu bdun las/ /gegs sel gdams ngag bzhi spang bcu gsum mo/ /zhes pa ltar tshigs su bcad pas mdor
bstan nas/ de dag so sor phral te bstan pa ni/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i glegs bam gyi dkar chag rje btsun  'di glegs bam gyi dbur bzhugs kyang chos
sna drug cur mi gtogs so/ /chen pos dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ gsung ngag rin po che'i rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang / 'di rje btsun chen po'i glegs
bam dkar chag na mi gsal bar brten rjes 'brang mang po zhig glegs bam gyi grangs su mi 'dren pa ni 'khrul par bzhed do/ /gzhung chung yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che/ dge
ba'i bshes gnyen gnyags bzhi rab pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan gyis zhus pa'i ngor dpal ldan sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa'i rnam 'grel gnyags

ma/ rnam 'grel bcu gcig tsam yod pa'i nang nas 'di gzhung nyung la don rgyas pa'i khyad du 'phags zhes dkar chag tu snang ngo / /dkar chag las mi gsal ba gsal bar byed pa la
zhal las shes so zhes smos pa dgu las med kyang gsal bar byed pa'i yi ge nyi shu rtsa gnyis yod de zhes gsal byed kyi yi ge nyi shu rtsa gnyis don bsdus ma dang bcas pa
las kun gzhi'i yi ge don bsdus pa/ gdan sogs kyi yi ge lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi yig chung / bum dbang gi 'da' kha ma'i skabs su 'chi ltas 'khrul 'khor 'chi bslu dang bcas
pa snang ba bsgyur ba'i 'da' kha ma ste bum dbang gi yig chung chos sde gcig tu 'dren pa/ gsang dbang gi thig le'i rnal 'byor/ shes rab ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid/
bzhi pa'i 'da' kha ma bum dbang dang thun mong du yi ge sa sgo dgag pa dang bcas pa'i yig chung 'di ni bum dbang dang thun mong ba yin no'i mtha' can/ bar do bzhi'i
yig chung / lam dus kyi dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi yig chung / tshad ma bzhi'i yig chung / gdams ngag drug gi yig chung / rten 'brel lngar bstan pa'i lam gyi yig chung
/ grib sel dang gnas sbyong 'byams gcod kyi za byed mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg  klu sgrub pa'i khog 'bubs su 'di sAtstsha'i mjug tu 'dug gi yig chung / gdon gyi grib ma
khrus kyis sel ba'i yig chung / grib ma sAtstshas sel ba'i yig chung / thig le 'dzag pa bsrung ba'i yig chung / yi ge brgya pa gdon thabs kyi yig chung ste 'khor 'das thun
mong gi skabs dgos pa bcu bdun/ rlung gi sbyor ba bdun/ bha ga'i yi ge bcu bzhi ste 'khor lo

'cham pa la gnyis/ gsang dbang gi skabs su 'khor bzhi'i rgya/ bzhi pa'i dbang phyug gi don brgyad/ mthar phyin pa'i sa bcu gsum phyed 'og ma'i mngon rtogs te 'das lam gyi skabs
su gsum gyi gsal byed nyi shu rtsa gnyis so/ /byang chub sems dpa' a seng gis zhus pa'i ngor sa skya pa chen pos gnang ba'i 'grel pa thams cad kyi don bsdus kyi tshigs
bcad rnam 'grel a seng mar grags pa nyi shu rtsa bzhi  glegs bam 'di nyid tshad ma bzhi dang sbyar na 'di yan gyi chos tshan nyi shu rtsa lnga po bstan bcos tshad ma/ni
bstan bcos 'di nyid kyi steng du bshad par bya ba yin no/ /de dag las 'phros pa'i gud du gsungs pa'i chos skor la/ kun gzhi rgyu rgyud las 'phros nas snying po'i don lta
ba 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi rtsa ba tshig le'ur byas pa rin po che'i snang ba shlau ka nyi shu pa 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ thabs rgyud gdan sogs las 'phros pa dbang bzhi'i
cho ga mtha' dag mdor bsdus pa'i man ngag gi yi ge 'am rgyu dus su dbang gi chu bo ma nub pa'i man ngag gi gnad/ gdan sogs las 'phros pa mchog dbang gsum grol lam la brten
nas bskur ba'i man ngag lam sogs nyi shu las 'phros nas phyi bskyed pa'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa'i gnad ces pa rgyas 'bring mi 'dra ba'i khyad par bstan pa'i mjug tu bsdus
pa la bsod nams tshogs gsog sogs gsal bar bstan pa/ dam tshig las 'phros pa bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub tshul/ gsang sngags snyan brgyud sogs ma chad pa las 'phros nas rdo
rje bdag med ma'i byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pa'i tho yig brtse chen snying po'i zhabs kyis mdzad

pa/ dkar chag tu byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pa ni logs su rtogs par bya'o gsung ba 'di yin la phra mo'i chos sder yang gtogs so/ /bsrung ba sum cu dang man ngag gi gnad
bdun cu las 'phros nas ge gas sel gyi yi ge bzhi byung ba las thog mar bsam gtan 'dor ba'i 'phrang bdun gyi ge gas sel thabs/ byung rgyal du mi gtong ba'i gnad bzhi/
lus 'khrugs rlung dang spyod lam gyis sel ba/ rnal 'byor gyi phrin las sum cu rtsa gnyis te dgu po 'di glegs bam du dngos su bzhugs shing / las dang po pa dang thun mong
du dgos pa'i chos bdun po deng sang glegs bam 'dir mi bzhugs pas gong du smos zin na'ang don du de dag thams cad rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang las 'phros pa'i skor yin/ dkar
chag tu glegs bam 'di na gnas kyang 'gal ba med la las dang po pa dang thun mong du dgos pa'i phyir logs su 'dug kyang nyes pa med do zhes so// lam rgyas 'bring bsdus
gsum gyi rgyas pa gong du bshad ma thag pa ltar dang / 'bring po rtsa ba med pa'i lam 'bras 'bring du bsdus nas gang zag gcig gis lam 'bras bu dang bcas ma tshang ba med
par ston pa/ rang gi gzhung cung zad yod pa sgrub pa'i lung sbyin pa'am 'bogs pa lam bsdus pa/ de ltar lam rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum mtha' dag rnal 'byor pas nyams su blang
ba'i phyir gzhung shing chen po bzhi las thog mar gzhung ji lta bar bkri ba'i khrid yig jo lcags mar grags pa lho brag pa dkar ston jo sras lcags kyi rdo rjes lan mang
du gsol ba btab pa la brten nas mdzad pa/ dkar chag dang rin po che klu sgrub pa'i khog 'bubs su 'di ltar 'dug cing / rje mkhyen brtse'i khog 'bubs na

gzhung shing dang rtogs pa bskyed pa bsdoms pa'i chos tshan dgu po ge gas sel gyi 'gor 'dug pa tshad ma bzhi dang sbyor ba'i dbang du byas so// man ngag gi gnad drug gis bkri
ba'i khrid yig khyad par can/ brtson 'grus can man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig gis bkri ba'i khrid yig gang zag dbang po rab 'bring gsum bkri ba'i khrid yig dang bzhi/ de ltar
nyams su blangs pa las byung ba'i rtogs pa bogs dbyung ba'i phyir rtogs pa bskyed pa'i chos lnga la/ thog mar lam 'jug ldog mgyogs byed pho nya'i lam phyag rgya 'jug ldog
shes pas phan 'dogs pa'i man ngag bdun/ 'khor 'das kyi lam thun mong du bsre ba dang / 'gros bzhi dang bcas pa'i yi ge phyi nang gi mdzad pa bcu gnyis/ rtogs pa bsal
ba'i phyir  dkar chag dang klu sgrub pa'i khog 'bubs kyi dngos bstan las bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi phyag dpe'i dpe ris rnams cung zad mang bar snang ngo / /'chi ltas brtag
pa rgyas pa'i dpe chung / ma nges pa'i 'chi ltas kyi dpe chung / de gnyis dang 'dra min re/ rtsa ba'i dpe ris rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ gsung ngag dkyus dang sras don
ma'i lugs kyi bha ga'i yi ge bcu bzhi'i dpe chung so so/ yang bha ga'i dpe chung lugs gcig nyams skye tshul dang bcas pa/ rnal 'byor gyi phrin las sum cu rtsa gnyis dpe ris/
gegs sel gzhan gyi dpe chung gnyis/ lam sbas bshad kyi rigs drug skye ba brtag pa'i dpe chung rnams rnam grangs gcig tu 'dren no/ /gang zag dbang po rab bla mas grol
bas lam gzhan la ltos mi dgos pas de'i cha rkyen lam zab 'bring gsum las lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor bla ma chen po'i dbu snyung ma  'di

yan la rtogs pa bsal ba'i skor ma gtogs dngos bstan gyi yi ge rnams kyi steng du dbang chu/ sgrub thabs yan lag bzhi drug bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs/ sbyin sreg rnams bsnan
pa'i chos sna sum cu po rnams nyams myong tshad ma yin no/ /tshad ma bzhi pa bka' yang dag pa'i lung tshad ma dang sbyor bar lung tshad ma gsung ngag rin po che 'di nyid
dang mdor bsdus te sbyar ba lam phyi ma gnyis kyang de bzhin du shes par bya'o'i mtha' can/ gsung ngag rin po che lung mtha' dag dang mdor bsdus te sbyar ba gsung ngag tshad
ma lung dang sbyar ba'i gdams ngag go'i mtha' can/ rje btsun brtse ba chen pos mdzad pa'i gsung ngag rin po che lung 'di nyid dang zhib tu sbyar ba/ dkar chag tu lung
'di nyid dang zhib tu sbyar ba ni logs su shes par bya'o gsung ba 'di yin pas/ dpe la lar dmar gyis mdzad tshul 'dug pa ni mchan bu lta bu dmar gyis mdzad pa yod srid pa
la 'khrul lam snyam mo/ /phra mo'i chos sder yang snang ngo // gleng gzhi dang gleng bslang ba dang rgyud kyi yan lag rgyas par dbye ba dang sbyar ba gsum gyi sgo nas bstan
pa  lung sbyor gsum po 'di lung tshad ma/mtshon gyis bsrungs la mkha' 'gros bzod par gsol gyi mtha' can/ bla ma tshad mar sbyar ba'i skabs kyi bla ma brgyud pa rgya gar
ba'i lo rgyus zhes pa rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi rnam thar/ 'di gnyis bla ma tshad ma'o// bla ma brgyud pa bod kyi lo rgyus zhes pa 'brog mi lo chen nas sa skya pa chen
po'i bar gyi rtogs brjod mdor bsdus/ 'di yan gyis lam 'bras glegs bam chos sna drug cu zhes pa tshang ba yin la/ rjes 'brang la la dag rdo rje'i tshig rkang dang rtog bsal
dor nas yi ge med pa'i lung sbyor rgyas pa dang phra mo'i dkar chag gnyis 'dren

pa dang / 'ga' zhig rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi tshab tu man ngag phra mo gzhan rnams gcig tu 'dren pa dang / rdzong pa'i bzhed par rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi tshab tu dkar chag
'dren pa 'dug go/ deng sang yongs grags la glegs bam du nges par bzhugs dgos pa bzhi bcu zhe dgu  dgar chag la snga rtsom phyi rtsom gyi khyad nas la lar 'khor 'das dbyer
med rtsa 'gral med 'dug pa de'i dbang gis zhe dgur ngos bzung ngam snyam mo// zhes grags na'ang dkar chag gi tshig gis zin pa lnga bcu nga gcig logs su bzhugs pa byin rlabs
kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pa dang lung 'di nyid dang zhib tu sbyar ba gnyis/ glegs bam 'dir bzhugs kyang rung zhing ma bzhugs kyang rung ba'i yig sna bdun dang bcas pas
chos sde drug cu tham pa/ yang chos sde drug cur dngos su mi gtogs par glegs bam du bzhugs pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' yang dag pa lung gi tshad ma lung 'di nyid dang sbyar
na mthar thug rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi bka'i dbang du byas te/ gleng gzhi'i mdo dang gleng bslang gi mdo rgyud don rgyas pa dang sbyar ba slob dpon rin po ches
mdzad pa/ phra mo'i chos sder yang the/mjug na 'di ni bdag cag spun gnyis dang bka' lung pa dang rmog ston dang bzhis zhus pa lags zhes sogs yod pa/ rje sa skya pa chen
pos gsung ngag 'di la zhu ba po so so'i don du mdzad pa'i rnam 'grel bcu gcig tsam yod pa'i nang nas shin tu zab cing rgyas pa rigs kyi sras slob dpon rin po che sku mched
gnyis kyi don du mdzad pa'i rnam 'grel sras don ai we 'di dang pod nag ma gnyis de sngon ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyi dbang gis bris so// mar grags pa rdo rje'i tshig
rkang

yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che'i bshad pa zhal nas zhal du brgyud pa'i gdams ngag rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i
glegs bam pod e we nag tu grags pa'i skor la/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba/ phyi dkyil gyi mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa/ lam dus kyi smin byed mchog gi
dbang bskur ba'i tshul zab pa las kyang ches zab pa/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs lam dus dbang gi nyams len dge bshes kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyi ngor mdzad pa/ bla ma la brten
nas dngos grub rnam gnyis sgrub pa'i rnal 'byor yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan dang bla ma sras pa'i don du mdzad pa/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi yan lag
mdo stod pa chos rgyal 'od zer gyi ngor mdzad pa/ lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i khrid yig sbas don gsal ba/ gnad drug gis bkri ba'i khrid kyi
gsal byed gnad kyi lde migagand bcu gcig gis bkri ba'i khrid kyi gsal byed gnad kyi sgo 'byed/ dbang po rab 'bring tha gsum bkri ba'i khrid kyi gsal byed nyung ngu rnam
gsal/ lam 'bras 'bring du bsdus nas snang ba gsum du gang zag gcig la dgos pa phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs nas rjod byed kyi sgra la ma ltos par brjod bya'i don gtso bo'i dbang
du byas nas ma tshang ba med par bstan pa'i snyan brgyud/ lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag rnam par bshad pa man ngag gi mdzod rnams so/ /gsung ngag rin po che'i
po ti smar chung ngam pod dmar du grags pa'i lam

'bras kyi yi ge'i skor la/ ring brgyud kyi skor tshad ma bzhi dang sbyar te bshad pa dang / nye brgyud kyi skor tshad ma bzhi dang sbyar te shes par bya ba la/ dang po ni/
bla ma tshad ma brgyud 'debs kha skong dang / /sa bir mjal tshul nyams myong tshad ma ni/ /zhu lan spyan dang aShTa'i bzlas lung bshad/ /bdud rtsi dbang dbye rga gdams maNDal
gsum/ /lus sbyong lus gnad bdag med gtum mo gnyis/ /gegs sel dgu dang phrin las sdom bcas dang / /dbang bzhi ngo sprod rtsa 'grel lung sbyin dang / /gsang ba bcu yi
rgyas gdab rnams yin no/ /gnad chen rten 'brel lnga dang lcags kyu dang / /phyag chen 'khor bzhi'i rgya dang tshogs sbyor lam/ /lam bsdus bshad pa bstan bcos tshad ma'i skor/
/lung gi tshad ma lung sbyor gsal byed de/ /dgon pa ba las brgyud pa'i rnam grangs so/ /gnyis pa ni/ lam zab rin 'byung bir srung byin rlabs skor/ /birWas sa chen dngos
la brgyud pa'o/ /brda don gsal ba rtsa 'grel dang bcas pa/ /tshad ma sbyar tshul bsgres te shes par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ de rnams kyi kha skong rje yab sras kyis
mdzad pa la/ rje btsun 'gro kun dga' mdzad bcu phrag gcig / dkon mchog mkhyen pa'i gter chen rnam grangs brgyad/ /ces sdom gyis bsdus pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs so sor gsal
bar 'god pa 'di lta ste/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i dkar chag rin po che'i phreng ba/ bla ma tshad ma'i skabs su/ rje btsun rin po che grags pas
mdzad pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs bla ma rdor 'dzin ma  phra mo na'ang

yod/de'i kha skong shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i gangs khrod ma/ de'i zhar byung kha skong du ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i shar chen dang buddha shrI'i gsol 'debs/
sa chen yab sras dang birWa pa mjal ba'i lo rgyus sga theng la bskur ba/ nyams myong tshad ma'i skabs su/ bra ston blo gros kyis zhus pa'i gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du
bkri ba'i khrid yig tshigs bcad ma rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa/ phra mor 'jug pa shlau ka gcig med pa zhig 'dug brtse ba chen pos mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas spyan ma'i rnal
'byor dbang dus su rmi lam ngan pa bzlog pa dang thun mong 'chi ba thub pa yang ngo'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i aShTa'i bzlas lung bla ma'i phyag len mdzad pa bzhin bris
pa'o'i mtha' can/ phra mo'i de 'di dang mi gcig pa 'dug sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i rtsa ba'i sngags kyi rnam par bshad  phra mo na'ang yod/pa snying po don gsal/ bdud rtsi ril
bu sgrub pa'i phyag len bdud rtsi 'byung ba zhes pa 'phags pas mdzad pa/ phra mo na'ang yod/dbang gi rab dbye rje btsun grags pa'i gsung bzhin zhang btsun gyis bris pa/
rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis byi lo nag zla'i tshes bcu la sga ston rdo rje grags la spring yig  phra mor yang yod/skyu ra'i dbon po dpon g.yog gis gsol ba btab
pa la brten nas sa paN gyis bsam yas su mdzad pa'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi maNDal/ de'i kha skong shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i pags pa gser gyi sa gzhi
ma/ 'gor dang po lag bkru lta bu ste/ zhes yod pa'i lus sbyong nyi shu'i gsal byed mdud 'grol zin bris nor bzang pas mdzad

pa/ lus gnad la dbab pa'i gdams pa tshigs bcad ma sa paN gyi zhabs la spyi bos rab tu btud pa'i dpal ldan phug pa dmar gyis zin bris kun dang thun mong ma yin pa/ bdag med
ma'i byin rlabs brgyud pa ma nyams pa'i lag len gyi tho yig rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa/ phra mor 'dug pa sa chen gyis mdzad par bzhed/'gor bshang sgor yaM las rlung gi
dkyil 'khor zhes yod pa'i 'khor lo bzhi'i rgya sa chen gyis mdzad pa thugs kyi nying khu lags so'i mtha' can/ dpal yang dag par sbyor ba'i rgyud las byung ba'i rang byin
gyis brlabs pa'i dmigs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu ba zhar byung rlung gi rnal 'byor gtso bor bzhed pa bla ma'i zhal shes zhes pa'i ge gas sel dang bcas pa/ rje sa skya pa chen pos
lho brag dkar ston la gnang ba'i phyi nang gsang ba'i bar gcod gsum sel/ phra mo na'ang yod/'gor rtsa dag par bya ba ni zhes yod pa'i bla ma sa chen gyi nyams chung pa
bar pa dang mtha' ma la sogs pa'o'i mtha' can/ phra mor yang yod/'gor spyir srog 'dzin pa snying gar rengs pa'i tshul bzhi zhes yod pa'i bla ma sa chen gyi nyams chen mo/
phra mor kun gzhi byin rlabs dang me mnyam gyi rlung rengs tshul sogs kyang chos tshan gcig tu bzhed/mthar dri chen rdo lta bu skam po 'byung ngo'i mtha' can/ khyad par
gyi rlung rengs pa lnga 'chos pa sogs kyi thabs bla ma'i zhal la ltos pa khrag de nyid bskol te spod kyis sbran nas gtang ngo'i mtha' can/ phra mor thig le bsrung ba yan
las mi 'dug lho pa dkar ston gyis zhus pa'i gzhan la med pa'i ge gas sel gsang bdun ma/ phra mor yang yod/'gor 'khor 'das kyi chos thams cad bskyed pa'i sa bon zhes yod

pa'i ge gas sel gling bzhi ma ri bong gi ril ma 'dra ba chu dang bcas nas stan thog tu byung bas sel lo'i mtha' can/ phra mo na nyams chen po dang sbrel nas 'dug cig sgom chen
rdo rje 'bar lus ma bde ba man mi 'dug 'byung ba lus 'khrugs sogs sel ba'i thabs ge gas sel ces gnad du grags pa 'di dag thams cad nyams myong rjes su dran pa'i tshad
ma las shes par bya'o'i mtha' can/ dmar chos kyi rgyal pos zhus pa'i ge gas sel bka' rgya ma/ phra mor yang yod/'di khams pa lnga dang rje btsun sku mched gnyis la gnang
zhing dzang gis rje btsun sku mched sbran pas dzang 'di nged la shin tu drin che gsung ba mjug na snang / 'gor gzhan dbang rten 'brel zhes byas ting nge 'dzin gyi ge gas
sel ston zhes yod pas ge gas sel bzhi'i zhal shes 'di la goms nas mtshan sum cu so gnyis thob gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ 'gor dza landha ra zhes yod pa'i phrin las so gnyis
kyi sdom tshig zhal shes buddha shrIs mdzad pa/ de'i zhal shes 'gor lag gnyis bsnol ba zhes yod pa re mos rdog gi mtha' can/ sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa'i dbang bzhi ngo
sprod/ phra mo na'ang yod/de'i 'grel pa/ 'gor rje btsun thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa zhes yod pa'i brda don gsal ba'i rtsa ba sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ phra mor yang yod/de'i
rang 'grel rtsom pa dam bcar/ rdo rje'i tshig 'byed brda don gsal ba 'di/ /dbus gtsang mtshams su bla ma rje la gnang / /zhes yod pa/ de'i gsal byed lho pas gsung bzhin
zin bris su mdzad pa/ phra mo na'ang yod/bstan bcos tshad ma'i skabs su bskyed

rim/ rlung / byin rlabs/ phyag rgya ma/ phyag rgya chen po/ rten 'brel te gnad du che ba drug gi gdams pa sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ 'di phra mor lam skor khrod du bgrangs 'dug
sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i rten 'brel lngas lam yongs su rdzogs pa/ 'di phra mo na'ang bzhugs/'gor g.yas pa'i khu tshur brkyangs byas te zhes yod pa'i dmar gyis mdzad pa'i lam
bsdus pa 'dod pa'i lcags kyu lam 'bring po bya ba yin gsung ba'i mtha' can/ phyag rgya chen po'i dbye ba dpal ldan sa skya paNDi ta'i mnal lam bsam yas su byung ba/ mjug
gi shlau ka gcig ma tshang ba zhig phra mo na'ang yod/des mdzad pa'i 'khor lo bzhi'i rgya/ 'di gnyis phra mor yang yod/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pas mdzad pa'i
tshogs sbyor gnyis kyi mngon rtogs/ lam bsdus pa'i bshad pa mdo tsam du bstan pa bla ma rin po che'i gsung la brten nas sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ lam bsdus te sgrub pa'i lung
sbyin pa sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ phra mor yang yod/rje sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab/ nyam pa'i 'phrang la yid bzhin nor bu ltar/ /gsang bcud ldan pa'i spyod
pa mtha' ru bskyal gyi mtha' can/ lam zab bla ma'i khrid yig sa paN gyis dpal ling chu rtse'i khab kyi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba/ phra mo na'ang yod/bla ma rin chen
'byung gnas kyi rnal 'byor sa skya paN chen gyi gsung bzhin chos rgyal dmar gyis yi ge ra bkod pa/ lam sbas bshad kyi yi ge sa skya paNDi tas mdo smad du sbyar ba/ phra
mo na'ang yod/'gor lam sbas te khrid na zhes yod pa'i pho brang lnga la brten pa'i sbas bshad 'bras bu rim par rgyas pa gzhung du gsal lo'i mtha' can/ 'gor

mkhal 'degs rigs gsum spyi'u tshugs dang / zhes yod pa'i lam sbas bshad kyi 'khrul 'khor rtsa ba rje dpal ldan tshul khrims kyis mdzad pa/ de'i rang 'grel chos rdzong du yi
ge ra bkod pa/ 'gor rdo rje lce yi sbyor ba dang / zhes yod pa'i grub chen bcu dang phra mo brgyad kyi rtsa ba/ 'di gnyis phra mo na'ang yod/ de'i 'grel pa 'gor dpal ldan
rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i zhal gyi gdams pa zhes yod pa sa skya paNDi ta'i thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams pa/ de'i gsal byed snyom las pa buddha shrIs brjed byang
du bris pa/ phra mor la lar buddha shrIs mdzad zer ba mi 'thad tshul dang bcas pa snang ngo / /'gor rdo rje'i tshig rkang las srung ba'i 'khor lo zhes yod pa'i bir srung
swa dheM swA hA'i mtha' can/ phra mor 'phags pa'i yi ge'i gsal byed du bgrangs 'dug go/ 'gor dpal ldan mthu stobs dbang phyug ces yod pa'i bir srung spyan sngar dpe 'di gtugs
so'i mtha' can/ 'gor ra ga ta dza phaT/ ces yod pa'i bir srung mi tshugs so'i mtha' can/ 'phags pas shin tu zhib par bkod pa'i bir srung dang / 'di phra mor yang yod/byin
rlabs bya tshul/ phra mor byin rlabs 'di sa chen gyis mdzad par bzhed/'gor rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa nas byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma chad pa/ zhes yod pa'i rnam
'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs bya tshul bar ma chad pa'o'i mtha' can/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs la sa paN gyis mchan mdzad pa/ de'i gsal byed sa paN gyis mdzad
pa'i rnam par bshad pa bdud rtsi spel ba/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i rgyud don nyams su blang ba'i cho ga nub pa rig 'dzin grags kyis

mdzad pa/ rje btsun chen pos dbang phyug 'od zer gyi ngor btsong kha dgon par mdzad pa'i tshar gsum khug pa'i man ngag  phra mor dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i khrod du yod/'gor
spyir yi ge brgya pa phyir bzlog tu 'gro ba dang / zhes yod pa'i yig brgya'i man ngag sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ 'gro ba'i gtso la bdag skyabs mchi/ /zhes brjod do'i mtha' can/
'brog mis paNDi ta drug las chos gsan pa'i sgo drug chos 'brel du grags pa la shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pas gdon/ dznyA na shrI lus 'khrugs/ rin chen rdo rjes sems kyi
bar chad bsrung ba gsum chos tshan gcig tu byas pa/ phra mor yang yod/nA ro pa'i phyag rgya chen po sdug bsngal gsum sel gyi gsal byed rje btsun gyis mdzad pa zhar byung
bzhi pa man chad rlung dang bstun tshul/ phra mor yang yod/ ngag dbang grags pa'i gnyug ma dran gsal/ phra mor yang yod/de'i dbang bzhi stan thog gcig tu blang ba zhang
'phags pa lhas yang yang bskul nas rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa/ phra mor bla ma brgyud pa yan las de man gyi zhang 'phags pa lhas bskur tshul sogs mi 'dug gzhung rnams legs
par tshar nas shAnta pas gnang ba'i mdo rgyud bsre ba snying po'i don rang grol du grags pa/ phra mor yang yod/rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa'i lam 'bras
bu dang bcas pa bshad thabs kyi gdams ngag gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ des mdzad pa'i rgyud gsum lam gyi rim pa'i bsdus don/ des mdzad pa'i lam zab nang ma'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor/
des mdzad pa'i rgyu dus kyi dbang gi rtogs pa bskyed pa'i rim pa/ bir srung gi man ngag bar chad kun sel/ des mdzad

pa'i birWa pa'i sku'i rnam 'gyur drug gi dbye ba/ des mdzad pa'i bir srung gi thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul tshigs bcad ma/ des mdzad pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i
bir srung nyams su blang tshul/ dkar chag tu mi gsal ba des mdzad pa'i bir srung gsar ma srung bzlog gi gdams pa khyad par can rnams so/ /de dag tu ma gtogs pa lam skor
lhag ma brgyad kyi chos tshan kha shas bgrangs 'dug pa ni phal cher glegs bam du bzhugs pa shas che/ de thams cad la nye bar mkho ba'i gnad drug ces pa bskyed rim rlung
/ pod dmar na lam 'bras kyi chos sder bgrangs 'dug mkha' 'gro'i byin rlabs/ phyag rgya ma/ phyag rgya chen po/ rten 'brel te drug ston pa/ lam skor byung tshul zhes pa'i
yig chung lam dgu po bla ma bzhi las gsan gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i lo rgyus bla ma sa skya pa chen po'i gsung sgros ji lta ba bzhin rang gi slob ma'i
ngor dkar ston chos 'od kyis dbri bsnan med par bris pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i byin rlabs bla chen 'brog mi las rang gis thob pa ltar brjed byang du bris pa 'di ni yab
yum dbang rdzogs thob par gdams te byin pa/ 'di 'brog mi'i dngos slob gcig gis yin tshul dkar chag na 'dug bar ston gyi lam skor zin bris la/ mchod rten drung thob/ bsam
mi khyab/ padma badzra gyi lam/ lhan cig skyes grub/ gtum mo lam rdzogs rnams kyi zin bris chos tshan gcig tu bsdebs pa/ thog mar rtsom pa'i dus 'di rnams 'khor 'das dbyer
med kyi 'gor bris yod 'dug gnyags snying po rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i phyag rgya chen po

yi ge med pa nyams su len pa'i khrid/ mdzad byang na hri da dhwa dza zhes rgya skad du bris 'dug 'gor bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gdams ngag 'di la zhes yod pa'i zin bris chen
mo lta ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa lngas rgyu dus su gtan la phab ste lam dus su lus ngag yid gsum sbyangs nas 'bras bu lung bstan pa'i phyag rgyas mtshams sbyar bas gnas 'gyur
gyi sku gsum yan lag bdun ldan 'grub par byed pa'o'i mtha' can/ gsung ngag rin po che'i bstan pa 'dzin pa rnams kyis mdzad pa'i yig sna thor bu'i skor la/ rnam 'joms
bir lugs lha bdun cu rtsa lnga'i sgrub thabs nub pa rig 'dzin grags kyis mdzad pa'i dbu'i phyogs nas phyung ba rnams/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs kun mkhyen bsod nams
seng ge sa mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i ga ya dha ra nas brgyud pa'i gur mgon gyi rjes gnang bya tshul/ rje mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i gsung ngag rin po
che'i khrid yig dngos grub 'byung gter kha skong dang bcas pa/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i gsung ngag rin po che rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa'i bla
ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa byin rlabs myur 'jug gi pho nya bcas pa/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len/ gsung ngag rin po che'i dmigs rim dang mthun pa'i
gsol 'debs zab don snying po/ de'i lam khyer gyi smon lam bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ man ngag gi brda 'phros zab don snang ba/ dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed/ man ngag lugs
kyi slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi yi ge sa chog mdor bsdus/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub

thabs bsnyen sgrub yan lag bzhi ldan/ mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa'i mdzes rgyan/ lus dkyil mdzes rgyan/ bdag med ma'i sgrub dkyil gyi tho/ lam 'bras rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi
bsdus don tshang bde nyung gsal/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du bkri ba'i lam gyi sngon 'gro'i khrid yig snang gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ des mdzad pa'i lam gyi dngos gzhi'i
khrid yig rgyud gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ des mdzad pa'i dpal kye rdo rje'i dbang gi tshig don rnams legs par bshad pa lung dang man ngag gi gter mdzod/ des mdzad
pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor snying po bsdus pa/ des mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga lag len gsal ba'i me long / de la ltos pa rgyas pa'i sbyin
sreg gi tho/ kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa lugs dang mtsho skyes lugs dang nag po lugs rnams kyi sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog tshul dang po gsum gyi don nyung ngus ngag gi sgo nas
ston pa tshul gsum gsal bar byed pa'i rgyan/ rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa'i don gsal bar byed pa ljon shing mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ legs par bshad pa gong ma'i dgongs
rgyan la sogs pa dang / thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi cho ga lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len/
bla ma rin 'byung gi byin rlabs bya tshul/ bir srung thun mong ba'i byin rlabs bya tshul/ sgrub pa lung byin/ brda chig brgyud/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ brda don gsal ba rnams
kyi byin rlabs bya tshul gyi cho ga bla ma

mchod pa'i cho ga thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa bya ba'i lag len/ rje dpal ldan don grub kyis mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i las bzhi'i sbyin sreg gi rnam bshad ye shes me dpung
rnams so/ /paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i gsung ngag gi yi ge'i skor la/ slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi phyag len nyams su blang bde ba/ aShTa'i bzlas lung byed
tshul lugs gnyis/ brgyud pa khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga dam pa'i bzhed srol sems nyid ngal gso'i bdud rtsi/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul
gsang chen chos kyi rnga chen/ lam dbang gi mtha' dpyod zur 'debs kyi gnad/ rdo rje bdag med ma'i byin rlabs bya tshul legs byas gtam gyi bdud rtsi/ lam zab bla ma'i
rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs bya tshul mkhas la nye bar mkho ba/ bla ma rin 'byung gi nyams len byin rlabs dang bcas pa'i yi ge 'dod dgu'i dpal 'byor ma lus pa 'byung ba'i gnas
legs byas kyi rnga bo che/ lam zab nang gi rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs bya tshul mkhas la nyer mkho/ bir srung thun mong gi byin rlabs rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa la
zur 'debs cung zad dang bcas pa/ bir srung thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul zur 'debs dang bcas pa/ brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs bya tshul la gnyis las gsum
byung gi go don dang bcas pa/ lam sbas bshad kyi byin rlabs bya tshul bklag chog tu bkod pa/ brda chig brgyud kyi byin rlabs bya tshul lag len go bde bklag chog tu bkod pa/
sgrub pa lung sbyin dang gsang bcu rgyas gdab kyi phyag len go bde bklag chog tu bkod pa

mtha' dpyod dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung dang / gzhan yang 'di dag gi skor rgyas pa ni sa skya pa'i rje btsun gong ma lnga dang / ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras la sogs pa'i
gsung rab la bzhugs pa thos pa'i brgyud pa rnams ni so so'i lung gi skabs su 'chad par 'gyur la/ 'dir rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba dang byin rlabs dang khrid dang glegs
bam rin po che phal cher gyi lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ samyaksaM buddha badzra dha raH/ bhaTTA rA ka badzra nai ratna/ A tsArYa yo ge shwa ra shrI madbirWa/
ShaShabhU mi shwa ra ma hA siddha pUrba dika hNaH/ rA dznyAHkU la DA ma ru pa/ bhaTTA rA ka a wa dhU tiH/ ma hA paNDi ta ga ya dha raH/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma/ slob dpon rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa/ sa drug gi dbang phyug grub chen shar phyogs nag po pa/ rgyal
rigs DA ma ru pa/ rje btsun gnyis spangs pa/ mkhas pa chen po sprin 'dzin/ ma hA lo ka tsakShu 'brog mi shAkya dznyA naH/ gu ru se ku Dyalpa sarbba bi traH/ gu ru ka
kA ra Nya ka dharmma dzwa laH/ bhaTTA rA ka ma hA bhU mi paNDu ra nanda garbhaH/ A tsArYa ratna puNyA graH/ bhaTTA rA ka ratna kIrti dhwa dzaH/ ma hA paNDi ta bhU mi paNDa
rA nanda dhwa dza shrI bha draH/ 'jig rten gyi mig chen po 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ bla ma se mkhar chung pa kun rig bla ma zhang dgon pa ba chos 'bar/ rje btsun sa skya
pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta chen po kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po/ dza ga nA tha dharmma rA dza/ ratnArYa ma ti dhwa dzaH/ gu ru ka ka ratna shrIH/ ma hA siddha she

la kau Tya ka puNya shrI/ sarba dznyA puNya dhwa dza shrI bha draH/ dharmma swA mi shrI matstshI laH/ ma hA siddha buddha shrI/ ma hA ngor badzra dha rA nanda bha draH/ 'gro
ba'i mgon po chos kyi rgyal po/ 'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla ma zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod
nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen sangs rgyas dpal/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ ma hA satwa ratna dhwa dzaH/ tau
yu bha yA bhyaM sangyu wa rA dzA nande sho rashtsa sarba dznyA puNya si dhau yu bha yA bhyaM shru taM/ pishtsu ma tri bhyaHpa ri dha ra ratna wardhaH/ tasmAtpU mi paNDa
rallo tsA manydzu swa rA nanda puNya na shru taM/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis ka las rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug dang kun mkhyen bsod
nams seng ge gnyis kas gsan/ phyi ma gsum char las yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ de las sa skya lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams kyis gsan/ tau yu bha yA bhyaM
sarbba dznyA ratna ni rA bho ge na shru tam/ tasmAtabha TTA ra ke wa mi ratna shrI wAnytsa/ bhaTTA rA ka ga ga na shrI bha dra dI bhyaM shru taM/ tau yu bha yA bhyammanydzu
swa rA nanda ni rA bho ge na shru taM/ tasmatsarbba dznyA shya gra dhwA dze na shru taM/ de gnyis ka las thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsan/ de las rje
btsun e waM pa dkon mchog dpal ldan dang / rje btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub kyis gsan/ de las thams
cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyis gsan/ tasmadmanydzu gho Sha buddha lukShmyA shru taM/ tasmAtpra sa dAtabhU ta ma hA badzra dha rashshI la ni rA bho ga mangga
la kIrti dhwa dza shrI bha dre na shru taM/ ta twa sya dznyA na kr-i sA nu bha wai ra

nu dha ra ka syAtma bande shI la ratnaM wa tsa na wA gratna syA bhi She ka nA ya nau pa ri pUrNaN stri NAnytsa/ de las 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis gsan/ de las
bka' drin rmad byung rdo rje 'chang ba chen po tshul khrims lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos gsan/ de nyid kyi mkhyen brtse nus pas rjes su bzung
ba'i bdag btsun pa tshul khrims rin chen la gsung ngag rin po che'i dbang khrid yongs su rdzogs pa lan gsum dang / he tu wA panytsa ma pra da ti/ wA ma hA pa Tu siddha
buddha lakShmyA tra/ a pa mA Na puNya shrI wAM/ ma hA badzra dha rashshI la ni rA bho ga ma tho kIrti dhwa dza shrI bha draH/ tasmA dAtma bande shI la ratne na su praptaH/
rgyu dbang lan lnga'i bar du stsal to/ /yang na mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ rdo rje 'chang ba chen po tshul khrims
lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ de las bdag btsun pa tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par thob bo/ /yang na shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas nas/
mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub nas/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/
nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang dang byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub dpal
ldan don grub gsum ga las/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis gsan/ de las hor nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ mkhas pa'i
dbang po dpal ldan don

grub/ de las 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyis gsan pa man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog
rgyal mtshan man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na paN chen brang ti pa nas/ rje dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na
rtse gdong khri chen/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub gsum char las/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas kyis so/ /yang na yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel
dang rje sangs rgyas rin chen gnyis ka las rje lha mchog seng ge de las rje dkon mchog lhun grub dang / rje sangs rgyas seng ge gnyis char gyis gsan/ de gnyis char las
rje dkon mchog dpal ldan dang / paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis char gyis gsan/ de gnyis char las 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub dang / shar chen byams pa
kun dga' bkra shis gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis char las rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyis gsan no/ /yang na rje dkon mchog dpal ldan las/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa
kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub gsum char gyis/ de gsum las rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge mus
chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang las/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho

dang mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel man 'dra/ yang na sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dang 'jam dbyangs
shes rab rgya mtsho gnyis char las/ mkhas grub dpal rdor man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ lha mchog seng ge dkon mchog lhun grub gsum char las/ 'jam dbyangs
sangs rgyas seng ge sa gsan/ de las rje btsun dkon mchog dpal ldan dang rje nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ lha mchog seng ge dkon
mchog lhun grub gsum char las shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis gsan/ de las rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pas gsan no/ /yang na sangs rgyas rin chen dang lha mchog pa
dang dkon mchog lhun grub gsum char las/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtshos gsan/ de las rje dkon mchog dpal ldan gyis so/ /yang na sems dpa' chen po dang kun mkhyen gnyis
ka las/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ de las sa lo dang rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na sems dpa' chen po nas/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje man
'dra/ yang na sems dpa' chen po nas/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen man 'dra/ yang na rgyal tshab kun dbang nas/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/
de las rje sa lo dang dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na sa skya paNDi ta nas/ tshogs sgom pa kun dga' dpal/ nyan

chen bsod nams brtan pa/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal man 'dra/ yang na nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa nas/ dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims man
'dra/ yang na brag phug pa bsod nams dpal nas/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen rin po che nas/ paN chen dbang phyug grub
pa/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na rje dkon mchog 'phel nas/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang na sa lo tsA
ba nas ngag gi dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' dbang phyug dkon mchog rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na rje dkon mchog rgya
mtsho nas/ rje btsun byams pa rab brtan/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen rin po che bsod nams seng ge dang / kong ston dbang phyug
grub pa gnyis char las/ 'jam dbyangs chos grags rgya mtshos gsan/ phyi ma gsum char las mkhas grub blo gros rab yangs dang / mkhas mchog bkra shis brtan pa gnyis kyis
gsan/ de gnyis ka las rje blo gros 'byung gnas kyis gsan/ de las rje byams pa rab brtan pas so/ /yang na kun mkhyen rin po che/ lum pa grags 'byor shes rab/ rje blo gros
'byung gnas man 'dra'o/ /yang na sa lo tsA ba dang rje dkon mchog lhun grub gnyis las sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen pas gsan/ sngags 'chang rin po che dang 'jam dbyangs
dkon

mchog rgya mtsho rje dkon mchog dpal ldan gsum las 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang pos gsan/ de las 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub kyis gsan pa man sngar bzhin no/
/yang na mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang man
sngar bzhin no/ /yang nye brgyud ni/ brtse ba chen po mnga' ris gung thang du bzhugs skabs dug byung ba'i ro ma g.yas ru'i grong chu dgon par bzhugs dus longs pa'i skyon
gyis chos rnams mnyel bas 'jam dbyangs phug tu sku mtshams bsdams te gsol ba btab pas/ zhang dgon pa ba mnal lam dang dngos su byon nas gdams pa rnams gsungs/ de rjes rnal
'byor gyi dbang phyug chos 'khor gyi phyag rgya can sa skya'i 'bal grog mon grog gi bar skyil krung gcig gis khebs pa gtso 'khor lnga pa zhig zhal gzigs/ de nas dbu rtse
rnying mar zla ba gcig gi bar du mngon sum du bzhugs nas gsung ngag rin po che dang lcags ri mi 'da' ba'i gser chos bzhi dang rgyud sde bdun bcu rtsa gnyis la sogs pa
gsungs te/ de'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen
po kun dga' snying po man gong bzhin no/ /de rnams ni gsung ngag gi brgyud pa gtso che ba'i rnam grangs yin la/ rgyu dbang rkyang pa thob pa'i brgyud pa'i rnam grangs la/
chos kyi rgyal po

'phags pa yan gong bzhin lam 'bras rgyu dbang lhan cig pa ltar las/ de nas zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ri khrod pa blo
gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis ka las rgyal
tshab kun dbang dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ de las sa lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ de gnyis ka las thams cad mkhyen pa
dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub
sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen shes bya bzang po/ de gnyis ka las shug ra he ru ka dpal kun dga' dpal 'byor gyis gsan nam gsan yul gang yin cung zad brtag de las bdag
tshul khrims rin chen gyis so/ /yang na mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan nas/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs thams cad mkhyen pa bkra shis lhun grub/ chos rje rdo rje
'chang kun dga' chos 'phel/ de bzhi char las drin chen rdo rje 'chang bkra shis bzang pos gsan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na brag phug
pa nas/ lam 'bras pa ye shes dpal/ sa skya pa rin chen dpal/ chos kyi rje paNDi ta man 'dra/ yang na chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims las/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan

dang / grub chen buddha shrIs gsan/ de gnyis las rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun grags pa nas/ gcung dpal chen 'od po/ sa paN/ zangs tsha
bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa/ 'di gnyis kyi bar na bla ma zhig dgos nges su 'dug pa dam pa kun dga' grags yin min dpyad/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ bla ma
dam pa man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ tshogs sgom pa kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen
bsod nams brtan pa/ dkar po brag pa rin chen seng ge chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rje rdo rje 'chang / mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje man 'dra/ yang
na 'phags pa nas/ paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab/ bla ma 'phags rgyal ba/ bla ma rin chen dpal bzang / 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na zhang dkon mchog
dpal nas/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal ba brag phug pa man 'dra/ yang na nyan chen pa nas/ bang mo zhu pa gzhon nu dpal/ bla ma dam pa man 'dra/ yang na rje sa
paN nas/ tshogs sgom rin po che/ gnyags snying po rgyal mtshan/ bar ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rdo rje tshul khrims/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ sa skya bu
ston dbang phyug dar/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ kun mkhyen rong ston chen po/ mkhas grub gung ru sher bzang man 'dra/ yang na sa skya'i zhal ngo nang brgyud ni/ 'phags
pa

nas/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos rje kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/
sa lo sngags 'chang chen po/ khri chen bsod nams dbang po/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ yab sras gnyis char las mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan pas gsan no/ /yang
na brag phug pa bsod nams dpal nas/ brag phug pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ sa skya bu ston dbang phyug dar man 'dra/ yang na dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nas/ sngags 'chang gzungs
kyi dpal ba/ chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med rgyal mtshan dkon mchog rdzong chung pa byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan
man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paNDi ta/ rje ri ti skyog pa/ rje dpal ldan pa/ rje nam dpal ba/ rje yon tan chos rgyal/ rje legs pa'i shes rab drug gis gsan/
drug ga las glo bo mkhan chen pas gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ dpal ldan rdo rje/ kun dga' mchog grub man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen dang sems dpa' chen po gnyis
las/ shes rab rgya mtsho/ kun dga' dbang phyug dpal ldan rdo rje/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge bzhis gsan/ mus chen man gyi bla ma lnga ga las ratna wardhas gsan pa man
'dra/ yang na sems dpa' chen po las/ kun mkhyen go bo/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ rje dkon mchog 'phel gsum gas gsan/ gsum ga las rje sangs rgyas rin

chen gyis gsan/ dkon mchog lhun grub man gong ltar ro/ /yang na ngor chen yab sras/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje nas/ mi nyag paN chen grags pa rdo rje/ sa lo tsA ba/ rje dkon
mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ mkhas pa gzhon nu seng ge de gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba lha 'bri ston pa shes rab rdo rje/ mi nyag paN chen man gong
bzhin no/ /yang na ngor chen dang mus chen gnyis las/ spyan snga rdo rje kun dga' dang / mkhas grub gung ru sher bzang gis gsan/ gnyis ka las mi nyag paN chen gyis gsan no/
/yang na sa paN nas/ grub thob yon tan dpal/ la ru ba bsod nams seng ge kun mkhyen gangs pa grags pa dpal/ spang khang pa yang zer/ma ti paN chen/ theg chen chos rje/
nyi lde pa gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po/ dpal ldan rdo rje/ mi nyag paN chen grags pa rdo rje man gong ltar ro/ /yang na bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims nas/ de dbon nam mkha'
dpal bzang / gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po nas/ rje ngag dbang grags pa/ bdag chen rgya gar ba shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo man 'dra/ yang na 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ nya dbon kun dpal/ grub chen kun dga' blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po/ rgya gar
shes rab rgyal mtshan man gong dang 'dra/ yang na 'gro mgon chos rje/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge theg chen chos rje/ grub chen kun dga' blo gros

sogs sngar dang 'dra'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po nas/ bdag chen rgya gar ba man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na sangs rgyas seng ge dang / brang ti pa nam mkha' dpal
bzang gnyis las/ shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ de dbon rje btsun shes rab 'byung gnas man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na sangs
rgyas seng ge nas/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen pa man gong ltar/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ shar pa kun bkras pa man 'dra/
yang na thar rtse pa nas/ rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/
rtse gdong khri chen man 'dra/ yang na bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug nas/ mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan/ rtse gdong khri chen man 'dra'o/ /zhes gsan yig 'ga' zhig tu 'di
ltar byung yang rgyu dbang gi brgyud pa la'ang lam 'bras kyi brgyud pa 'dres pa'ang 'byung ba sogs zhib par gong ma so so'i rnam par thar pa la legs par dpyad pas rtogs
par 'gyur ro/ /aShTa'i bzlas lung gi brgyud pa ngor lugs ni/ chos rje rdo rje 'chang yan lam 'bras ltar la/ de nas mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin
chen/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ de dbon dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ de
gnyis

ka las dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ de las mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bzang po dang / tshul khrims lhun grub gnyis
char gyis gsan/ snga ma las 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang bas gsan/ de las bdag gis so/ /yang na mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan pa nas/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen
pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul rin la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog dpal ldan nas/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog
pa man sngar bzhin no/ /rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa chen yan chad yab
dang 'dra/ sa skya pa chen po nas ne tso sbal ston/ slob dpon  slob dpon bye ma lung pa zhes pa 'dir sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa'i gsan yig na byung yang thar rtse paN chen
dang rmor chen sogs kyi gsan yig na med pas dgos sam ma yin brtag bye ma lung pa/ bla ma shes rab grags/ gnam pa rwa chos kyi shes rab/ mngon pa ba dbang phyug brtson
'grus/ de las 'phags pa rin po che dang paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis las zhang dkon mchog dpal/ de nas na bza' brag phug pa bsod nams dpal ba/ de
las bla ma

dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang ri khrod pa blo brtan gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de las chos rje shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan dang grub
chen buddha shrI gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis gsan/ de nas sems dpa' chen pos gsan/ gnyis ka las rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug dang kun
mkhyen bsod nams seng ge gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ grub mchog bsod
nams dbang po/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ drin chen rdo rje
'chang bkra shis lhun grub grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen zhes bgyi bas legs par mnos so/ /yang na mngon pa ba/ 'phags pa
rin po che/ sgang ston shes rab 'bum/ dkar po brag pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims pa man 'dra/ yang na 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel nas/ rje lha mchog seng ge de gnyis ka las
rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ a mi lags sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra/ yang na 'dren mchog dkon
mchog 'phel nas/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas brgyud pa ngag dbang chos grags las/ a mi lags kyis gsan

no/ /yig cha rnams ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ dkyil chog mtshams sbyor rnams kyi steng nas thob bo/ /!/ rdo rje slob dpon chen po'i zab mo lus
kyi dkyil 'khor du lam dus kyi dbang bskur ba lan du ma'i bar du thob pa'i brgyud pa rgyas pa ni gong gi gsung ngag yongs rdzogs kyi dbang khrid kyi brgyud pa ji lta ba
bzhin yin zhing / 'dir yang rgyu dbang dang lam dbang gnyis ka'i brgyud pa so sor ma phye bar tshigs su bcad pa'i sgo nas rtogs bde bar brjod na/ thog mtha' med pa'i sangs
rgyas rdo rje 'chang / /ma skyes mi 'gag shes rab bdag med ma/ /stobs bcu'i dbang phyug dpal mgon dmar ser zhes pa me sbrul lo la sau ma pU rir bltams nas rnam 'byung
sa 'brug la grub pa brnyes/ bi rU pa/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug shar phyogs nag po  rgya gar shar phyogs su sku 'khrungs/pa/ /rten 'brel zab mo'i don gzigs DA ma  rgyal rigs
yul dbus su sku 'khrungs/ru/ /gzung 'dzin kun spangs a wA ra NA sIr sku 'khrungs/ wa dhU tI pa/ /mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa ratna  gha ya dha ra'i mtshan gyi rnam grangs
te bhaM ga lar sku 'khrungs/shrI/ /sgra bsgyur rgyal po shAkya  mang mkhar du sku 'khrungs/ye shes dang / /snyan brgyud gdams pa kun mdog sma che 'gram du sku 'khrungs/
rig rje btsun se/ /zab don chos kyi snang ba  sag thang sdings su sku 'khrungs/zhang chos 'bar/ /aM bag yod ces pa chu mo glang gi lo dpal sa skya btab nas lo bcu dgu
'das par brom stod kha 'ur/ gir chu sprel lor 'khrungs sa skya pa/ /rnga chen chu khyi lor 'khrungs  yab lnga bcu pa'i dus gzims spyil dkar por/rje btsun rtse/ /rab byung
me yos  de las

lngas gzhon pa sgo rum mgon khang mdor/'khrungs pa grags pa'i zhabs/ /dge byed chu stag lor 'khrungs  de las sum cu rtsa lngas gzhon pa sgo rum tshogs khang phur/paNDi ta/
/myos byed shing lug lor 'khrungs  de las lnga bcu nga gsum gyis gzhon pa klung khud du/'phags pa'i zhabs/ /kun ldan lcags  de las lngas gzhon par ra sa mtshal khud du/byi
lor 'khrungs dkon mchog dpal/ /dbang phyug me glang lor 'khrungs  de las lo so bdun gyis gzhon pa ra sa mtshal khud du/brag phug pa/ /yongs 'dzin chu byi lor 'khrungs 'gro
mgon rje/ de las so lngas gzhon pa zhwa lu khang gsar du/agni de las bzhis gzhon pa/ me 'brug lor 'khrungs ri khrod pa/ /dpal gdong chu bya lor 'khrungs  de las bcu bdun
gyis gzhon pa 'bras khud sgang skya ru/dpal ldan pa/ /myos ldan sa yos de las drug gis gzhon pa mdog gi phur/ lor 'khrungs buddha shrI/ /rnga chen chu khyi lor  de las
zhe gsum gyis gzhon pa sa skya'i byi khung sgor/'khrungs rdo rje 'chang / /rnam byung sa 'brug lor  de las drug gis gzhon pa mus stod gling skyar/'khrungs mus pa rje/ /khro
bo shing glang lor  de las bdun gyis gzhon pa sa skya'i gu rar/'khrungs dkon mchog 'phel/ /dmar ser me sbrul lor  de las nga gnyis kyis gzhon pa dpal sa skya'i gnyan
bla brang du/'khrungs dkon lhun rje/ /myos byed shing lug lor 'khrungs  de las so brgyad kyis gzhon pa sa skya'i mdo brjod bkra shis gling du/brang ti pa/ /skyes bdag lcags
lug lor 'khrungs  de las so drug gis gzhon pa/sa  'jam dbyangs kun gda' bsod nams lhun grub/skya pa/ /gdong ngan me sprel lor 'khrungs  de las nyer lngas gzhon pa bzhad
kyi khyel du/sher 'byung gnas/ /mig dmar shing byi lor 'khrungs  de las nyer

brgyad kyis gzhon pa shar mi nyag gi yul 'dun par/lhun grub dpal/ 'gal ba sa glang lor  de las nyer lngas gzhon pa mnga' ris smad kyi tre'i 'brog gseb tu/'khrungs buddha'i
mtshan/ /agni me 'brug lor 'khrungs  de las lo nyer bdun gyis gzhon pa yul dar rtse mdor/tshul lhun zhabs/ /rnam gnon lcags 'brug lor skyes de las nyer bzhis gzhon pa ldan
yul sa dkar du/ bdag la'o/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ /phur bu sa sprel la  de las bcu dgus gzhon pa mdo mkhar chos sder/'khrungs bkra shis lhun/
/de yis rjes bzung tshul khrims rin chen  de las so gnyis kyis gzhon pa ldan phrug go/ no/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ /shing yos lor  de las nyer drug
gis gzhon pa mi nyag rab sgang du/'khrungs tshul khrims dpal bzang dang / /zhi ba sa bya'i bsod dpal  de las drug gis bgres par phyug gzhung spes rgyar/gnyis kyis gsan/
/gnyi gas rjes su bzung nas legs stsal ba/ /sna tshogs chu rta'i dpal ldan chos skyong  phyi ma las so gsum gyis gzhon pa gtsang ngor gyi spe'i rong du/ste/ /de yis rjes
bzung bande tshul rin  de las gsum gyis bgres pa 'bri klung gser dang ldan ma'i 'gram ngogs sa dkar du/no/ /yang na mkhan chen bsod nams dpal ldan nas/ /dkar po sa sbrul
la  de las nyi shus gzhon pa gtsang rong gling ma mkhar du/'khrungs bsod nams bzang / /de las myos ldan sa yos dpal  de las bcus gzhon pa 'bri klung gser ldan ma'i 'gram
gyi bya rar/bzang pa/ /de las rgyu lam dbang thob tshul rin no/ /yang na ngor chen yab  rdo rje 'chang dang sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/sras gnyis char las/

/ khro mo shing  phyi ma las so drug gis gzhon pa sa skya ru/'brug rgyal tshab kun dbang dang / /zhi ba sa bya'i go rams  de las lngas gzhon par mdo khams 'bam gyi yul du/gnyi
gas gsan/ /gnyi ga las thob dkon mchog 'phel  de las bcu drug gis gzhon pa/'phel ba'o/ /de las dpal  de las brgyad kyis gzhon pa mus stag mo gling skyar/gdong chu bya
sangs rin pa/ /gnyi gas rjes su bzung ba'i sras kyi mchog / kun 'dzin sa byi lor  sangs rgyas rin chen las bco lngas gzhon pa sa skya ru/'khrungs lha mchog seng / /gnyi
de las nyer dgus gzhon pa/gas rjes bzung dkon mchog lhun grub dang / /mig dmar shing bya'i sangs rgyas seng ge gnyis/ / de las bdun gyis gzhon pa// gnyi gas rjes bzung mi
zad me khyi  phyi ma las nyer gnyis kyis gzhon pa sa skya'i gnyan khang gsar du/ba/ /dkon mchog dpal ldan pa dang brang ti pa/ / de las dgus gzhon pa/gnyi gas sa rtar 'khrungs
phyi ma las nyer gsum gyis gzhon pa sa skya'i gu ra ru/pa kun bkras par/ /de las sgyur byed sa de las zhe gnyis kyis gzhon pa gcan lung mkhas sngar/ phag dpal mchog
las/ /sangs rgyas phun tshogs man chad gong de las lnga bcus gzhon pa/ bzhin no/ /yang na ngor chen yab sras gnyis ka las/ /sa byi lor phyi ma las nyi shus gzhon par
gtsang chu mig gi bya 'dab grong du/ 'khrungs 'jam dbyangs sher rgyam las/ /bong bu lcags yos dpal rdor  de las gsum gyis gzhon pa dpal sa skyar sku 'khrungs/man chad 'dra/
/yang sa skya'i zhal ngo nang brgyud ni/ 'phags pa nas bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ de las bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis gsan pa nas/ theg chen chos rje kun
dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs nam

mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo sngags 'chang chen po/ khri chen bsod nams dbang po/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams yab sras gnyis char las/ mkhan
chen lhun grub dpal ldan pas gsan no/ /yang rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung nas lam dus lus dkyil gyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa slob bshad ltar na/ ngor chen rdo
rje 'chang yan chad sngar bzhin la/ de nas sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rdo ring pa chen po
kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma blo ldan shes rab kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams
pa ngag dbang lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen can la bka' drin du stsal to/ /brgyud pa thun mong tsam ni zhang dkon mchog dpal nas/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla
chen kun dga' blo

gros/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun sgo rum pa/
'jam mgon mkhyen brtse man sngar ltar ro/ /yang na mus chen nas/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge paN chen dbang phyug grub pa/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug bdag chen kun
dga' bsam 'grub/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen las/ mus chen/ rgyal tshab rje/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhas
grub dpal ldan rdo rje las gsan/ de lnga char las mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ de dbon dkon mchog
dpal ldan/ de las shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis dang / khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan pa'i
rdo rje/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ lam dbang gi skabs su mdzad pa'i he ru ka'i yi ge brgya
pa'i bzlas lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni gong gi lam dbang gi skabs brgyud pa'i 'gros gcig pas des shes shing / 'dir mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa'i gsan yig tu/
rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas yan gong ltar las/ de nas rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun

grub/ des bdag la'o/ /rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ni/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas yan sngar bzhin las/ de nas mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/
mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /lam zab
mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhal brgyad bcu drug phyag can du bsgom pa'i khrid dang byin rlabs bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rnal 'byor
dbang phyug birWa pa/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom kun
dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ de las ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa dang bla ma dam pa gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las bla ma dpal
ldan tshul khrims/ de las shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan dang grub chen buddha shrI gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos gsan/ de las
sems dpa' chen po/ de gnyis ka las rgyal tshab dam pa kun dbang dang kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge gnyis kyis gsan/ phyi ma gsum char las rje dkon mchog 'phel gyis gsan/
sems dpa' chen po las grub chen dkon mchog blo gros kyis gsan/ sems dpa' chen po dang / kun mkhyen dang / grub chen gsum char las sangs rgyas rin chen pas gsan/ phyi ma

las rje dkon mchog 'phel dang sangs rgyas rin chen gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las sa lo tsA ba dang / lha mchog pa dang dkon mchog lhun grub gsum gyis gsan/ sa lo tsA ba
las rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsan/ rje lha mchog pa dang dkon mchog lhun grub gnyis char las/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge dang shar khang pa gnyis kas gsan/ dkon mchog lhun
grub dang / sangs rgyas seng ge dang shar khang pa gsum ga las rje brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang pas gsan/ de nas rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub dang
mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyis gsan/ de las mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis gsan/ de las thams
cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub kyis gsan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis so/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub las/ rje dkon mchog dpal
ldan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje byams pa rab brtan/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po dang bzhis gsan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang las/ shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra
shis kyis gsan/ rtse gdong khri chen dang byams pa kun dga' bkra shis gnyis las/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas kyis gsan/ de las rje dam chos bsam 'grub pas gsan/ de
las mkhan grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis gsan/ de las mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub kyis gsan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin

chen gyis lan gsum bar du legs par nos so/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis so/ /yang
na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ shes bya bzang po dang rje bsod nams dpal ldan gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyi ga las 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na sangs
rgyas phun tshogs nas/ byams pa tshul khrims dpal bzang dang / mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las byams pa bsod nams bzang po dang / thams
cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong gnyis kyis gsan/ phyi ma de las bdag gis thob bo/ /yang na rje bsod nams bzang po dang bkra shis lhun grub gnyis ka las/ mkhan chen
'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par thob bo/ /lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor nang ma'i byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya
paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ na bza' brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ kun mkhyen bsod nams

seng ge lnga kas rjes su bzung ba 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sa
skya pa zhabs drung a mi lags/ bdag chen bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan pa/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/
'jam dbyangs bkra shis lhun grub grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub nas/ rdo rje
'chang dpal ldan chos skyong dang 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par thob bo/ /bla ma don yod grub
pa la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs zab mo thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ dpal birWa pa/ grub chen kahNa pa/ rje
btsun DA ma ru pa/ gnyis spangs zhabs/ paN chen ga ya dha ra/ lo chen/ 'brog mi/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/ rje btsun brtse ba
chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ lung phu ba nam mkha' bsod nams/ bkras lung pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu don grub/ zhang ston byang chub
shes rab/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ chos kyi rje ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ rgyal tshab kun
dbang pa/ kun mkhyen bsod

nams seng ge 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa pradznyA'i mtshan can/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong khri
chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ bco brgyad pa mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin/ de dbon byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ sprul sku rin po che padma phrin las/ mkhas grub chen
po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ de nas bla ma gzhan yod dam mus pa'i dge bshes tshul khrims kyis gsan pa yin nam brtag drin chen rdo rje 'chang chen po tshul khrims lhun grub/
de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis mnos so/ /yang na rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan nas/ dbang phyug 'od zer/ mkhan po rong pa/ lung phu ba man 'dra/ yang na
sa skya paNDi ta nas/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla
ma dpal ldan tshul khrims man 'dra'o/ /bla ma rin chen 'byung ldan gyi byin rlabs zab mo thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ lo chen 'brog mi yan snga ma rnams dang 'dra ba las/ de
nas mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma gsum/ sa skya paNDi ta/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu don grub/ zhang
ston byang shebla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / gung ru shes rab bzang po/ mkhyen rab rje/ lo pa ngag dbang chos
grags/ bco brgyad pa

mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ de dbon byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ sprul sku rin po che padma phrin las/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/
mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul rin la'o/ /yang slob bshad pa las brgyud pa'i lugs ltar na/ ngor chen rdo
rje 'chang yan chad sngar bzhin las/ de nas sems dpa' chen po/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab pa/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ sprul sku padma
phrin las/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs man 'dra'o/ /bir srung thun mong ba'i byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa rtse gdong khri chen dang byams pa kun dga' bkra shis
gnyis yan chad ni lam zab zhal brgyad bcu drug phyag can pa'i byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa dang 'dra ba las/ de gnyis ka las shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas kyis gsan/ de
las rim par rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis lan gsum gyi bar du mnos so/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas phun

tshogs nas/ 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ shar chen sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin/ rje bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/
/yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag
la'o/ /yang na rje nam mkha' dpal bzang pa yan lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs dang 'dra/ de nas 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub dang mkhas grub dpal
ldan don grub gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ de las 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs man gong bzhin no/ /bir srung thun mong ma yin
pa'i byin rlabs man ngag dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen/ kun dbang pa/ 'dren mchogs skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo
rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'di nas brgyud rim gyis tshul gang yin gyi bla ma 'ga' zhig btsal dgos pa yod/ de nas mus pa'i dge bshes
tshul khrims/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong pa'i gsan yig
ltar yan chad btsal/ de nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang ba chen po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog rje lha mchog seng ge rdo
rje 'chang buddha singha man 'dra'o/ /yang na mus chen/ grub chen dkon

blo/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa skya lo tsA ba man 'dra/ yang na rgyal tshab kun dbang / mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang
buddha singha man 'dra'o/ /!/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i don thams cad bsdus pa brda don gsal ba byin rlabs khrid tho gnad zab mo du ma dang bcas
pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / dpal bi rU pa/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ chos kyi rje sa paNDi ta/ bla ma lung phu
ba nam mkha' bsod nams/ bkras lung pa/ mkhas btsun gzhon nu grub/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ de las bla ma dam pa dang blo gros brtan pa gnyis
kyis gsan pas de gnyis gang rung / gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen
dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba rgyal tshab kun dbang / de nas yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog
lhun grub/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun rin/ khri chen bsod nams dbang po/ sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug
mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ bstan pa'i sgron me sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rigs kun khyab bdag mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/
/yang na dkon mchog lhun grub

nas/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ khri chen kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na rgyal
tshab kun dbang nas/ kun mkhyen go rams pa/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo tsA ba man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag
phug pa man 'dra'o/ /brda chig brgyud kyi man ngag byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje bla ma dam pa yan gong dang 'dra/ de nas ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma
dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rje sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje
sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang la sogs pa nas rim par btsal/ de nas mtshungs med
bstan 'dzin lhun grub yin nam/ de nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen du
bod pa la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ rgyal tshab kun dbang / 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge
des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen/ kun dbang / 'dren mchog rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rdo rje 'chang buddha singha / des bdag la'o/ /lam sbas bshad kyi byin rlabs kyi

brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan nye brgyud ltar la/ de nas tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ ri khrod pa blo brtan/ gnyis ka las dpal tshul ba/ buddha shrI/
ngor chen/ rgyal tshab pa/ dkon mchog 'phel/ sa lo/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan man brda don gsal ba'i ngor lugs bzhin
no/ /rdo rje rnam par 'joms  'di de sngon ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyis bris/pa birWa pa'i lugs kyi dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du legs par nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug dpal ldan chos skyong / dpal sa skya pa chen po/ rje bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi ta/ skyo
ston dri med/ zhang dkon mchog 'phel/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal tshul ba/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen
