tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub yin nam brtag thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /sgrub pa lung sbyin
gyi byin rlabs zab mo

thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen nas rgyal tshab kun dbang / 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ gling stod zhabs drung dkon mchog dpal 'byor/ sprul sku rin po che man 'dra/ yang na 'dren mchog rgyal
ba lha mchog pa/ rdo rje 'chang buddha singha man 'dra/ yang na rgyal tshab kun dbang / kun mkhyen go rams pa/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog
lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /rje btsun chen pos gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i khrid yig tu/ lus sbyong rgyas bsdus ji rigs pas lus 'byong 'byong bya'o/ /zhes gsungs pa'i lus
sbyong bsdus pa ni yan lag lnga'i sbyong ba dang / rgyas pa ni lung sbyong nyi shu pa ste de'i gsal byed mdud 'grol lam 'bras pa nor bzang gis zin bris mdzad pa dang /
'khrul 'khor gyi dngos gzhi rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor gyi phrin las sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi yi ge dang / de dag gi gsal byed bla
ma phyi rabs pa'i zin bris las 'byung tshul bshad pa/ snyigs dus bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung rgyun zin bris las 'byung tshul bshad pa/ gzhan
yang mkhas pa gzhan gyi gsung rab las 'byung tshul bshad pa gsum gyi sgo nas gsal bar bshad pa'i lam 'bras 'khrul 'khor rnams kyi lag len rnal 'byor kun dga' zhes bya ba
sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad

pa'i yi ge'i steng nas/ lus sbyong rgyas bsdus dang phrin las sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi 'khrul 'khor rnams kyi lag len gyi khrid rgyug 'bul dang bcas pa ste legs par thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yan lam 'bras khrid kyi brgyud pa dang 'dra zhing / de nas mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhas
grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ de las rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen dang / sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen
pa dkon mchog lhun grub gsum gas gsan/ phyi ma gnyis las sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis gsan pa nas/ rim par 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ sngags
'chang grags pa blo gros/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ de gsum ga las 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams kyis gsan/ de nas 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug sngags 'chang
ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ e waM pa mkhan chen tshul khrims dpal bzang / mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mi nyag mkhas btsun sangs rgyas tshul khrims/ des bdag
bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan yan gong bzhin las/ de nas bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun
rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ sa
skya pa ngag dbang kun

dga' bsod nams man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug nas/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra'o/ /zhabs drung kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i lung gi brgyud pa ni rje tshul khrims dpal bzang pa yan 'dra/ de nas mtshungs med
bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /lam 'bras kyi bstan pa gtad pa'i tshul du mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yan chad lam 'bras dang 'dra zhing / de nas rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal
ba lha mchog seng ge de gnyis ka las thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ zhabs drung sngags 'chang
kun dga' bsod nams/ bdag chen bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan chen
'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul rin la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub yin nam/ mkhan
chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na rgyal tshab pa dang kun mkhyen gnyis ka las rje sangs rin dang ratna wardha

gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis las sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ de gsum char las dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ chos
rje blo gros rin chen/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang / mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ rje ngag dbang chos grags/ zhabs
drung a mi lags man 'dra'o/ /'di'i rjes gnang gi yi ge kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa ltar dang / rjes gnang gi tshe thun mong ma yin pa'i gsol gdab mdzad cing / zhabs g.yas brkyang
can du mdzad/ thugs la rigs 'dra bstim nas lta ba ngo sprod mnyam par gzhagagazhan dkyus bzhin no/ /'dir gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab ni ma thos so/ /!/ bla ma 'brog mis
chos rnams rdzogs pa'i mthar bi kra ma shI la'i mkhas pa sgo drug las chos 'brel du gsan pa'i sgo drug chos 'brel du grags pa/ shAnti pa'i mdo rgyud bsre ba shes rab 'byung
gnas sbas pa'i gdon gyi bar chad sel ba/ dznyA na shrI'i 'byung ba lus 'khrugs/ rin chen rdo rjes sems kyi bar chad sel ba/ nA ro pa'i phyag rgya chen po sdug bsngal gsum
sel/ ngag dbang grags pa'i gnyug ma dran gsal te drug las/ de dag gi brgyud pa ni shAnti pa/ dznyA na shrI/ shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pa/ rin chen rdo rje/ ngag dbang
grags pa/ jo bo nA ro pa drug las 'brog mis gsan/ de nas bar chad gsum sel  gdon sel ba 'byung ba lus 'khrugs sems kyi bar chad sel ba gsum/gyi brgyud pa sgom chen se reg
gnyis/ des gnyos yer pa sgom seng / grub thob lha

'bar/ kha reg bsgom pa/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu grub/ byang chub shes rab/ chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de
las shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan dang buddha shrI gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gnyug ma dran gsal gyi brgyud pa ni/ rje
btsun sgrol ma/ ngag dbang grags pa/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma shangs pa/ sa chen/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/
zhar byang chub shes rab/ bla ma dam pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de las shar chen dang buddha shrI/ gnyis ka las ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / nA ro pa'i sdug bsngal gsum sel
gyi brgyud pa ni/ nA ro pa/ 'brog mi/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che/ lung phu ba/ bkras lung pa/ mkhas
grub pa/ zhang byang she/ bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mdo rgyud bsre ba'i brgyud pa ni/ shAnti pa/ 'brog
mi/ se ston/ zhang dgon pa ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ lung phu pa/ bkras lung pa/ gzhon nu grub/ byang she/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/
bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / de man cha da gong gi brda don gsal ba ltar so sor phyin pas chog go/ !/ rje ngor chen gyis lam 'bras
la sogs

lam skor dgu zhes pa'i gdams pa paN grub brgyad kyis mdzad pa lam skor brgyad dang chos kyi rnam grangs dgu yod pas lam skor dgur yang grags pa bla chen 'brog mi la bka' babs
pa'i chos skor la/ dpal ldan tog tse pas sampu Ta la brten nas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gdams pa mdzad/ de nyams su len pa la bsam mi khyab lnga'am byin rlabs kyi brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rta mchog zhabs/ mda' chen zer/pi na pA da/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di ltar 'dug kyang rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na bi na pa ti
dang thar rtse ba'i der pI na pa zhes pi waM 'dzin pa yin zhes snang ngo // rgyal po indra bhU ti/ legmi pA da/ thar rtse ba'i der phun tshogs zhes bsgyur 'dug cing lcam
lakShmI ka ra zhes sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa'i der byung gzhan du zur chag 'di bzhin 'dug lI la badzra gundha ri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa dang thar rtse ba'i der sgeg pa'i
rdo rjer bsgyur/padma badzra/ dharmmA pa/ gong dkar ba dang thar rtse ba'i der chos kyi pha zer ba 'dug bha dra pA da/ gong dkar ba dang thar rtse ba'i der bzang po'i zhabs
su bsgyur 'dug grub chen tog tse pa/ sta mo'am 'jor 'dzin pa'i don/bhu Sha Na pa/ gong dkar ba'i der ghu sha na 'dug dha ma pa/ gong dkar ba'i der padma pa zer/kahna pa/
gong dkar ba'i der karNa zer/bI ra badzra/ 'brog mi lo chen/ rdo rje gdan pa'i der ga ya dha ra la yang bod du gsan zer/se ston kun rig zhang dgon pa ba/ brtse ba chen
po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa dang ri khrod
pa gang rung / bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal

mtshan/ zhwa lu pa chos rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ mtshungs med dkon mchog dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' bkra
shis/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ rje dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin
chen la'o/ /yang na rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ rje nam
mkha' sangs rgyas/ de gnyis ka las rje dpal mchog man 'dra/ yang na rje rdo rje 'chang / mkhas mchog kun dga' blo gros/ mkhas btsun dpal ldan rgyal po/ mus chen nam mkha'
dpal bzang / rje dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ paNDi ta ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud dang brtag pa gnyis pa'i dgongs pa dang rje btsun
ma sgrol ma'i gsung la brten nas yan lag bdun pa dang bzhi pa snang bar byed pa la sogs pa'i bstan bcos mdzad pa'i lam nyams  Dombi he ru ka'i bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs
bdud rtsi 'od kyi snying po nyams su len pa'i ched du'ang yin/su len pa la phyag rgya chen po yi ge med pa'i gdams pa las byung ba'i byin rlabs dang de'i gsal byed rje
btsun chen po grags pas dge slong blo gros brtan pa'i don du mdzad pa nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun sgrol ma/ paN grub ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/
de wA ka ra tsandra/ de gnyis

ka las jo bo a mo gha badzras gsan/ de las bla chen 'brog mis gsan pa man gong ltar ro/ /dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis gsang ba 'dus pa la brten nas byang chub sems 'grel
mdzad/ de nyams su len pa la mchod rten gyi drung du sems thag bcad pa'i gdams pa'i gsal byed rje btsun chen po grags pas mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag
na rdo rje/ bram ze sa ra ha/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon ArYa de wa/ dge slong nag po'i zhabs/ slob dpon tsandra kIrti/ rdo rje gdan pa dang thar rtse pa'i gsan yig
na zla ba grags pa zhes bsgyur/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na ga ya dha ra zer ba 'dug pa bla chen gyis rgya gar du dpa' bo rdo rje dang
bod du ga ya dha ra las gsan pa'i khungs mdzad 'dug 'brog mi man gong bzhin no/ /slob dpon nag po spyod pas sampu Ta dang sdom 'byung la sogs pa bde mchog gi rgyud la
brten nas nag po pa'i chos drug mdzad/ de dag gi nang nas o la pa ti mngon par rtogs pa'i sdom gyi nyams len gsal byed rje btsun chen po grags pas mdzad pa'i gtum mo lam
rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ kurmmA pA da/ thar rtse pa'i der rus sbal zhabs
su bsgyur/dza landha ra/ rdo rje gdan pa'i der 'dis rdo rje rnal 'byor mar gsan zhes snang /kahna pa/ thar rtse ba'i der nag po spyod pa ro la zhon pa zhes byung /bram ze
dpal 'dzin/ paNDi ta ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba man gong dang 'dra'o/ /slob dpon u tsi ta 'chi ba med pas dpyid kyi thig le'i rtsa ba'i sdom nyams su len pa la yon
po bsrang ba

'khor ba lu gu rgyud du gcod pa'i gdams pa nag po pa'i gsung bzhin rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang chen po/ lha dbang phyug chen po/ nag
po  'chi ba med pa/u tsi ta/ grub chen nag po spyod pa/ slob dpon dpal 'dzin/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa'i der bram ze rin chen zhes byung /paNDi ta ga ya dha ra/ 'brog
mi lo tsA ba man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /mi dbang indra bhU tis rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud sde mtha' dag la brten nas dbang yon tan gyi rim pa mdzad/ de nyams su len pa
la phyag rgya bzhi rdzogs kyi lam ma gor/ lhas byin gyis ni rta byas la/ zhes pa dang / lo rgyus dang bcas pa bstan zin to'i mtha' can rgya gzhung ma'i brgyud pa ni/ dang
po dpal sde'i zhal snga nas/ /de bzhin du yang tshangs pa dang / /bram ze mo ni rdo rje grub/ /shrI badzra rdo rje rgyal/ /de yi slob dpon de'i phyi ma/ /gos bral zhal
snga de bzhin no/ /dpal ldan dznyA na bo dhi rgyal/ /de bzhin shrI yo bo dhi dang / /slob dpon padma badzra dang / /Dombi zhal snga de bzhin no/ /yan lag bar pa dpal lha
mo/ /bung ba'i padma de bzhin no/ /dur khrod du na kI lar bzhugs/ /lha lcam legs smin de bzhin no/ /bdag kyang dang po grub pa yin/ /zhes pa ltar/ kun mkhyen rdo rje 'chang
chen po/ indra bhU ti che ba/ rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na dpal bde ba zhes byung ba tshigs bcad ltar na dpal bde ba dang indra bhU ti che ba gnyis gcig pa 'dra/brahma
pA da/ tshangs pa'i zhabs zhes bsgyur/bram ze mo grub pa'i rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bhU ti bar pa/ slob dpon u pa ma'i zhabs/ ni utta pA da/ rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig
na

slob dpon gong bral zhabs zhes 'dug pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig rgya skad ma dang mthun yang thar rtse pa'i der gcer bu'i mchan dang bcas gos bral du bshad 'dug
pa dpyad/rgyal po dznyA na bhU ti/ shrI yo bhU ti/ slob dpon padma badzra/ Dombi he ru kaa nangga antarbha/ rdo rje gdan pa dang thar rtse pa'i der yan lag bar ma'i zhabs
zhes bsgyur/lha mo bung ba'i padma/ lcam lakShmI/ thar rtse pa'i gsan yig tu legs smin zhes zur chag 'dug rgyal po indra bhU ti chung ba/ bram ze ratna badzra/ kha che
shes rab gsang ba'am/ a tsArYa dmar por grags pa/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /nye brgyud ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / indra bhU ti che ba/ lcam legs smin/
paN chen shes rab gsang ba man 'dra'o/ /slob dpon padma badzra gyis rdo rje gur la brten nas sgrub thabs mtsho skyes mdzad pa'i don nyams su len pa la zab mo'i tshul
dgu'i lam gyi gsal byed sbal ston dar ma 'byung gnas kyis zhus pa'i ngor rje btsun chen po grags pas mdzad pa/ mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dpal kye rdo rje mar me'i rtse
mo lta bu'i man ngag rgya gzhung ga ya dha ra dang 'brog mi'i 'gyur gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / grub chen bi lA
sya badzra/ a nangga badzra/ rdo rje gdan pa dang thar rtse pa'i der yan lag med pa'i rdo rjer bsgyur/grub chen padma badzra/ de gnyis na mtsho skyes rdo rjer bsgyur/rgyal
chen indra bhU ti/ lcam lakShmI ka ra/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ paNDi ta ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba man gong dang  rdo rje gdan pa'i der rgya
gar du dpa' bo rdo rjer yang gsan zhes snang /'dra'o/ /slob dpon Dombi he ru kas kye rdo rje'i rgyud brtag

gnyis la brten nas lhan cig skyes grub mdzad/ de nyams su len pa la lhan cig skyes pa gsum gyi lam nyams len dbu na/ de la Dombi he ru kas/ zhes dang / zhag gsum de gnyis kyi
bar nas gang tsam la sgom/ gzhan yang shes par bya'o'i mtha' can gyi brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen rdo rje 'chang chen/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen Dombi he ru kaa
la la badzra/ slob dpon nags khrod pa/ bA ra si pa zhes pa'ang byung ngo / /grub chen garbha ri pa/bsod snyoms par bsgyur/ pinda pa/ slob dpon  mi thub zla bar bsgyur/durga
tsandra/ dge slong pradznyA indra ru tsiH rdo rje gdan pa'i der bI ra badzra dang thar rtse pa'i der dpa' bo rdo rje zhes 'dug pa dpyad/'brog mi lo tsA ba  rdo rje gdan
pa'i der bod du yang shes rab gsang bar gsan zer ba 'dug man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /smras pa/ gang zhig thos pas las bzang sdong po bskyed/ /thos don dpyad pas shes bya'i
lo 'dab rgyas/ /dpyad don bsgoms pas bla med byang chub kyi/ /snye ma g.yur za rgyal kun bgrod gcig lam/ /bdag med mkha' 'gro'i zhal lung rgya bod kyi/ /mkhas grub dbang
po du ma'i gshegs shul 'di/ /lan re thos pa'i blo ldan de nas bzung / /phyogs re'i gdams pa bsrel la gus pa lhod/ /snyan brgyud tshad ma'i 'dab stong dga' tshal las/ /ma

ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gser chos gsung ngag rin po che'i chos skor
